“哞！哞！” 
曼先生听到他家的牛在田里大声叫着。他连忙跑出门，看到有个东西闪着火光快速地飞过天空。那个东西直接冲向了他的农场。 
“啊，不好了！” 曼先生惊慌大叫。
"Moo! Moo!"
Mr. Mann heard his cows mooing in the field. He ran outside and saw something flash across the sky. It shot straight toward his farm.
"Oh no!" cried Mr. Mann.
“呃！” 杰克厌烦地说。“今天午饭是牛肉酱面包。” 
这是美罗城小学的星期一早晨。学生们正准备去上课。
"Yuck!" said Jack. "We're having sloppy joes for lunch today."
It was Monday morning at Metro City Elementary School. The students were on their way to class.
“我最讨厌牛肉酱面包了。” 玛拉说。“又恶心，酱汁又滴得到处都是。” 
“要是火箭女孩儿在就好了。” 特勒尔说。“她一定可以把我们从牛肉酱面包解救出来。” 
"Sloppy joes are the worst," said Mara. "They're so gross and they drip everywhere."
"I wish Rocket Girl was here," said Terrell. "She could save us from those sloppy joes."
“没错，火箭女孩儿无所不能。” 杰克说。 
“火箭女孩儿是美罗城最厉害的超人。” 玛拉说。“她会飞，力气也很大，还能从眼睛里射出激光呢！另外，她还有许多其他的超能力！” 
"Yeah, Rocket Girl can do anything," said Jack.
"Rocket Girl is the number-one superhero in Metro City," said Mara. "She can fly, she's really strong, and she can shoot lasers out of her eyes. She has lots of other super powers too!"
“上个星期，她成功阻止了一个想要踏平我们学校的大怪物。” 特勒尔说。
“还有一次，火箭女孩儿打败了巨型机器人，保护了美罗城。” 玛拉说。
"Last week she stopped a big monster from stomping the school," said Terrell.
"Rocket Girl once saved Metro City from giant robots," said Mara.
“记得上次月球人打算炸毁地球吗？” 杰克说。“火箭女孩儿飞到月球，一下子摧毁了他们的地球炸弹呢！” 
"Remember when moon men were planning to blow up Earth?" asked Jack. "Rocket Girl flew to the moon and destroyed their Earth Blaster!"
“你们总是在说火箭女孩儿。” 罗西说。“但是她也并不完美，我觉得她也无法从牛肉酱面包日中解救出我们。” 
"You guys are always talking about Rocket Girl," Roxy said quietly. "But she's not perfect. She can’t save us from sloppy joe day."
“你在开玩笑吗？” 玛拉说。 
“罗西，我看你一定是在嫉妒她。” 特勒尔说。 
“嫉妒？” 罗西反问道。 
"Are you kidding?" asked Mara.
"I'll bet you're just jealous, Roxy," said Terrell.
"Jealous?" asked Roxy.
“是啊。” 特勒尔说。“因为每次火箭女孩儿出现，你都不在，所以你很嫉妒。说不定，你还在心里偷偷希望你就是火箭女孩儿呢。” 
“我？火箭女孩儿？” 罗西笑了。“这是个荒唐的想法！” 
"Yes," said Terrell. "You're jealous because you're never around when Rocket Girl shows up. You probably wish you were Rocket Girl."
"Me? Rocket Girl?" Roxy laughed. "That's a ridiculous idea!"
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。手表的声音设得非常小，只有罗西才可以听到。 
“我不想再跟你们说关于火箭女孩儿的事了。” 罗西说。“我去看看潘校长有没有需要我帮忙的地方。” 
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. It was only loud enough for Roxy to hear, and no one else.
"I'm tired of talking about Rocket Girl," Roxy told her friends. "I'm going to see if Principal Penn needs help with anything."
罗西走到空无一人的走廊，确认周围没有人。然后她按下了手表上的一个按钮。一个小小屏幕亮了起来。美罗城的市长布洛姆出现在屏幕上。他看上去并不开心。 
Roxy walked down an empty hallway and made sure no one was around. Then she pressed a button on her watch. A small screen blinked on. Mayor Bloom, the mayor of Metro City, appeared on the screen. He didn't look happy.
“出什么事了，市长？” 罗西问。 
“一个奇怪的东西降落在曼先生的农场里。” 市长说，“我们觉得可能是一艘宇宙飞船。” 
“宇宙飞船？外星人乘坐的宇宙飞船？” 罗西问。 
"What's wrong, Mayor?" asked Roxy.
"A strange object landed at Mr. Mann's farm," said Mayor Bloom. "We think it might be a spaceship."
"A spaceship? With aliens?" asked Roxy.
“我们还无法确定。” 布洛姆市长说。“不管它是什么东西，我们都需要调查清楚。我已经跟潘校长说好了。她说你可以离开学校，去解决这件事情。就靠你了，火箭女孩儿。” 
“我这就出发。” 罗西说。
"We're not sure," said Mayor Bloom. "But whatever it is, we need to find out. I talked to Principal Penn. She said you can leave school until we solve this case. We're counting on you, Rocket Girl."
"I'm on my way," said Roxy.
罗西跑进一个空房间。过了一会儿，她变身成为了火箭女孩儿！
有时候罗西觉得隐瞒自己的身份很对不起自己的朋友们。但是罗西决定暂时只把秘密告诉布洛姆市长和潘校长。
Roxy ran into an empty room. A moment later she was Rocket Girl!
Sometimes Roxy felt bad that her friends didn't know she was actually Rocket Girl. But Roxy had decided to tell her secret only to Mayor Bloom and Principal Penn.
只有这样她才能够过上普通女孩儿的生活。嗯……其实说普通也并不普通。有多少八岁的孩子需要每天拯救世界呢?不过现在没有时间想这些了，火箭女孩儿有任务在身！
罗西跑过走廊，跑出教学大楼。
That way she could still have a normal life. Well, sort of normal. How many eight-year-olds had to save the world every day? But now was not the time to worry about that. Rocket Girl had a job to do!
Roxy ran down the hall and out of the school.
“好了。” 她说，“现在我该去看看究竟是什么落在了曼先生的农场里。” 说完，罗西飞上了天空。 
“快看窗外！” 玛拉大声叫道。 
“是火箭女孩儿！” 特勒尔说。
"Okay," she said. "It's time to figure out what landed at Mr. Mann's farm." Then Roxy blasted into the air.
"Look out the window!" cried Mara.
"Rocket Girl!" said Terrell.
很快，罗西就到达了曼先生的农场。她看了看周围。有一些玉米杆儿已经被切断。然而罗西没有看到宇宙飞船。 
就在这时，玉米地里有什么东西在移动。一个人影走向了罗西。
Soon Roxy was at Mr. Mann's farm. She looked around. Some of the corn had been cut down. Roxy didn't see the spaceship though.
Just then something moved in the cornfield. A figure stepped toward her.
“天啊！” 罗西笑着说，“是个外星人侦探！” 
“现在没空跟你开玩笑。” 史密斯侦探皱着眉头说。史密斯侦探是美罗城的第一侦探。他非常严肃，从来不开玩笑。
"Oh no!" Roxy laughed. "It's an alien detective!"
"This is no time for making jokes," said Detective Smith with a frown. Detective Smith was Metro City's head detective. He was a very serious man. He never joked.
“好吧。” 罗西说，“那么这里究竟发生了什么？宇宙飞船在哪里？” 
“我也不知道。” 史密斯侦探说，“我已经四处找过了。但是哪里也找不到。” 
“曼先生看到它飞到哪里了吗？“罗西问。
"Fine," said Roxy. "So what happened here? Where's the spaceship?"
"I don't know," said Detective Smith. "I looked all over for it. I didn't see it anywhere."
"Did Mr. Mann see where it went?" asked Roxy.
“没有。” 史密斯侦探说，“他太害怕了，马上跑回屋里。他说自己躲在了床底下。等他重新出来时，宇宙飞船已经不见了。一些玉米也不见了。” 
"No," said Detective Smith. "He got scared and ran into his house. He told me he hid under his bed. When he came back out, the spaceship was gone. So was the corn."
“外星人为什么要拿走玉米呢？” 罗西感到诧异。 
她看了看周围。她看到一棵折断的大树，就飞了过去。
"Why would the aliens take the corn?" Roxy wondered.
She looked around. She saw a tree with a broken branch and flew over to it.
‘看上去像是有什么东西撞到了这棵树。’罗西想。 
附近有一个被损坏的围栏。罗西把目光从树移向围栏，然后越过围栏看去。她看到了一条树木被毁坏的痕迹。
"It looks like something crashed into this tree," thought Roxy.
Nearby, a fence was also broken. Roxy looked from the tree to the fence. Then she looked past the fence. She could see a trail of damaged trees.
‘我猜这一定是宇宙飞船干的。’罗西想，‘但是为什么宇宙飞船没有从这些树的上方飞过？它飞到哪儿去了？’
罗西飞得更高以便看得更清楚。
"I bet the spaceship did that," thought Roxy. "But why didn't the spaceship fly over all the trees? And where did the spaceship go?"
Roxy flew up high to get a better view.
那条痕迹通往……
罗西吓了一跳。“天啊！我知道宇宙飞船去哪儿了。是美罗城！” 
The trail led straight toward . . .
Roxy gulped. "Uh-oh! I know exactly where the spaceship went. It's headed toward downtown Metro City!"
“火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探叫道，“你要去哪里？” 
“我要回到市中心去！” 罗西叫道，“宇宙飞船飞到那里去了！” 
罗西努力飞得更快。 
"Rocket Girl!" called Detective Smith. "Where are you going?"
"I'm going back to downtown!" yelled Roxy. "That's where the spaceship went!"
Roxy flew as fast as she could.
到达美罗城的时候，她看到人们在跑。  
“啊！外星人来攻击我们了！” 一个高个子男人喊道。 
“快跑啊！” 有人叫道。 
“快救救我们，火箭女孩儿！” 一个蓝头发奶奶喊道。
When she reached downtown Metro City, she saw people running.
"Agh! Aliens are attacking!" shouted a tall man.
"Run for your life!" someone cried.
"Save us, Rocket Girl!" yelled an old woman with blue hair.
罗西看到大家都很惊慌。
但是她没有找到宇宙飞船。
‘宇宙飞船到哪里去了？’她想。
Roxy saw lots of scared people. But she didn't see the spaceship anywhere.
"Where did the spaceship go?" Roxy wondered.
一群人跑了过来，他们都穿着超市的工作服。
‘啊！’罗西想，‘宇宙飞船一定在超市里。’
A large group of people ran by. They were all wearing Shop Well Supermarket uniforms.
"Aha!" thought Roxy. "The spaceship must be at the Shop Well Supermarket."
罗西飞到了超市。她在那里看到了一艘宇宙飞船。那艘飞船撞进了超市的前门。为什么宇宙飞船总是在撞东西呢？ 
Roxy flew to the Supermarket. And then she saw it—the spaceship. It had crashed into the front of the store. Why did the spaceship keep crashing into things?
两个绿色的外星人从商店里面走了出来，罗西赶紧藏在一辆卡车后面。这两个外星人拿着西红柿汤罐头。罗西看着一个外星人打开了飞船侧面的一扇小门，然后把西红柿汤倒了进去。
Two green aliens came out of the store. Roxy hid behind a parked truck. The aliens had cans of tomato soup. Roxy watched one alien open a small door on the side of the spaceship. The alien poured the the tomato soup into a hole.
另外一个外星人钻进了飞船，并试图启动发动机。飞船从地面离开了一秒钟。但有烟雾从里面冒了出来。轰！飞船撞上了一辆停着的卡车。
The other alien got into the spaceship and tried to start the engine. The spaceship lifted off the ground for a second. But then smoke puffed out of it. Boom! The spaceship crashed into a parked truck.
‘嗯。’罗西想，‘也许飞船用食物作燃料。’ 
又有一个外星人拿着苹果酱从商店里面走了出来。他把苹果酱倒入了飞船上的那个洞。
"Hmm," thought Roxy. "Maybe the spaceship runs on food."
Another alien came out of the store with jars of applesauce. It dumped the applesauce into the hole in the spaceship.
外星人又一次尝试着启动飞船。这次它飞了一会儿，紧接着又撞上了一个邮箱。
‘看起来食物并没起什么作用。’罗西想，‘为什么呢？’
Again the aliens tried to start up the ship. This time it flew for a moment, and then crashed into a mailbox.
"The food doesn't seem to be working though," Roxy thought. "I wonder why."
外星人开始相互交谈。一个在挥舞着他的胳膊，另一个开始叫嚷。
‘哎呀。’罗西想，‘外星人看起来很不开心。’
The aliens started talking to each other. One was waving its arms around. Another was beginning to yell.
"Uh-oh," thought Roxy. "The aliens don't look happy."
一个外星人看到了一辆比萨外卖车经过，他就用一个很小的设备瞄准了那辆货车。 
嗖！
One of the aliens spotted a pizza delivery truck driving by. The alien pointed a small device at the truck.
Shlurp!
一股紫色的黏液冒了出来。货车的轮子瞬间就粘在了马路上。 
“救命啊，火箭女孩儿！” 司机大叫道。
A stream of purple slime shot out. The truck's wheels instantly stuck to the road!
"Help, Rocket Girl!" the driver shouted as aliens surrounded the truck.
罗西向外星人跑去。但是在她跑过去的时候，罗西看到一个外星人正拿着那个枪瞄准她。 
嗖！
Roxy raced toward the aliens. But when she ran over, Roxy saw one alien point the gun at her.
Shlurp!
罗西低头看去。紫色的粘液把她的脚紧紧粘在了地面上。
“呀啊！” 罗西用她的超能力用力地扯，用力地扭。终于——哧！——她的双脚自由了。
Roxy looked down. The purple slime made her feet stick to the floor!
"Grr!" Roxy used her super strength. She pulled, heaved, and twisted until—shloop!—her feet came unstuck.
但是外星人已经打开了比萨外卖车的门。
“啊！” 司机叫道。
“快停下！” 罗西冲着外星人们飞去并喊道，“我不会让你们伤害他的。” 
By now the aliens had opened the door of the pizza delivery truck.
"Yikes!" the driver shouted.
"Stop right there!" Roxy shouted as she flew toward the aliens. "I'm not going to let you hurt him."
“我们不会伤害任何人。” 一个外星人说道，“我叫布里姆。我们需要给飞船补充燃料。飞船用食物作燃料，但是这些食物都没用。” 
"We aren't going to hurt anyone," said one alien. "My name is Brim. We need to refuel our spaceship. It runs on food, but none of this food is working."
“为什么没用？” 罗西问道。
“这些食物种类都不对。” 布里姆说道，“我们需要又厚又黏的食物。” 
“又厚又黏？” 罗西问道，“嗯……” 
"Why not?" asked Roxy.
"It's not the right kind of food," said Brim. "We need something really thick and gloppy."
"Thick and gloppy?" said Roxy. "Hmm . . ."
“啊！” 玛拉说，“我把牛肉酱沾到袖子上面了！” 
“真糟糕。” 杰克说道。
紧接着布里姆和别的外星人一起走进了食堂。
“外星人！” 有人喊道。
"Ugh!" said Mara. "I got sloppy joe on my sleeve!"
"This is awful," said Jack.
Just then Brim and the other aliens walked into the cafeteria.
"Aliens!" someone shouted.
“快跑啊！” 有人叫道。
火箭女孩儿飞了进来。
“不要惊慌。” 她说，“这些外星人很友好。他们只是需要一些牛肉酱来作燃料启动飞船。” 
"Run for your life!" shouted someone else.
Rocket Girl flew in.
"Don't panic," she said. "These guys are friendly. They just need your sloppy joes so they can refuel their spaceship."
在火箭女孩儿解释了一切之后，大家不再害怕了。
“噢！你可以拿走我的牛肉酱！” 杰克说道。
Rocket Girl explained everything, and no one was scared anymore.
"Oh! You can have my sloppy joe!" said Jack.
“把我的也拿走吧！” 玛拉说道。
“还有我的！” 特勒尔说道。
“请大家拿着午餐跟我们来。” 火箭女孩儿说道。
"Mine too!" said Mara.
"Take mine!" said Terrell.
"Everybody, grab your lunch and follow us," said Rocket Girl.
“现在来试一下，布里姆。” 罗西说道。
布里姆尝试着启动飞船，飞船完美启动了。
“谢谢大家。” 布里姆说，“这些牛肉酱真是我们飞船的完美燃料。” 
"Try it now, Brim," said Roxy.
Brim started up the spaceship. It worked perfectly.
"Thank you, everyone," said Brim. "Those sloppy joes are the perfect fuel for our spaceship."
孩子们向飞走的飞船挥手。
“我很开心我们摆脱了那些牛肉酱。” 特勒尔说，“但是我们现在要吃什么呢？” 
The kids waved good-bye as the spaceship flew away.
"I'm glad we got rid of those sloppy joes," said Terrell. "But now what will we eat?"
“快看窗外！” 玛拉说道。
“比萨！” 杰克叫道。
布洛姆市长走进了食堂，他手里面端着一大摞比萨。
"Look out the window!" said Mara.
"Pizza!" said Jack.
Mayor Bloom came into the cafeteria. He had a tall stack of pizzas.
“谢谢你们为了拯救美罗城而放弃了午餐。” 他说，“我请大家吃比萨。” 
学生们都欢呼起来。过了一会儿，罗西走进了食堂。
“罗西！” 玛拉喊道。“你错过了火箭女孩儿！” 
"Thanks for giving up your lunches to save Metro City," he said. "I have pizza for everybody."
The students all cheered. A moment later Roxy entered the cafeteria.
"Roxy!" said Mara. "You missed Rocket Girl!"
“还有外星人！” 杰克叫道。
“什么？” 罗西说道，装作一副很惊讶的样子。
“你去哪儿了？” 马拉问。
“哦，我在帮助潘校长做一些……办公室的工作。” 罗西说。
"And aliens!" said Jack.
"What?" asked Roxy, pretending to be surprised.
"Where were you?" asked Mara.
"Oh, I was helping Principal Penn with . . . office work," said Roxy.
特勒尔怀疑地看了看罗西。“你知道吗，罗西？你错了。火箭女孩儿真的把我们从牛肉酱面包里解救了出来。” 
罗西什么也没说。她只是笑了笑，静静地拿起了一块比萨。
Terrell looked at Roxy suspiciously. "Well, you know what, Roxy? You were wrong. Rocket Girl was able to save us from sloppy joe day."
Roxy didn't say anything. She just smiled and quietly reached for a slice of pizza.
凌晨，乳梦冰淇淋店的店长迪佩尔小姐来到了店里。她打开了门，然后打开了灯。她吓了一大跳。
“我的冰淇淋不见了！” 
It was early morning at Dairy Dream Ice Cream Parlor. Miss Dipper, the owner, arrived at the store. She unlocked the door and turned on the lights. She gasped.
"My ice cream is gone!"
“我快要融化了！” 玛拉擦着额头说。
“不要说话。” 杰克说，“那样只会让你觉得更热。” 
美罗城小学的空调坏了。艾普卡特老师班上的同学们正忍受着炎热。
"I think I'm melting!" said Mara, wiping her forehead.
"Don't talk," said Jack. "It only makes you feel hotter."
The air-conditioning at Metro City Elementary School wasn't working. The students in Miss Apricot's class were miserable.
本来是安静阅读的时间，但是没有人可以把注意力集中在阅读上。
“太热了，我都不能思考了。” 特勒尔说。
“我也是。” 杰克说，“我希望我们可以去游泳。” 杰克闭上眼睛，想象着自己跳进一个凉爽的泳池。
It was Quiet Reading Time, but no one could concentrate on reading.
"It's so hot, I can't even think," said Terrell.
"Me neither," said Jack. "I wish we could go swimming." Jack closed his eyes and imagined jumping into an ice-cold pool.
“我希望我们可以吃冰淇淋。” 玛拉说，“那样我们就可以凉快下来。” 
“如果火箭女孩儿在这儿就好了。” 特勒尔说，“她可以帮我们摆脱炎热。” 
"I wish we could have ice cream," said Mara. "That would cool us off."
"If only Rocket Girl was here," said Terrell. "She could do something about this heat."
“也不是特别热呀。” 罗西说。
“你在开玩笑吧？” 特勒尔问，“你不热吗？” 
“当然热。” 罗西说，“但是我有一个秘诀可以让自己凉快一些。” 
"This heat isn't so bad," said Roxy.
"Are you kidding?" asked Terrell. "Aren't you hot right now?"
"Of course," said Roxy. "But I have a secret power I use to keep cool."
特勒尔一脸好奇。其他人也是。
“是吗？” 杰克问，“快告诉我们！” 
杰克还有玛拉把身子凑了过来。
Terrell looked interested. So did everyone else.
"You do?" said Jack. "Tell us!"
Terrell, Jack, and Mara leaned closer to hear about Roxy's secret power.
罗西看起来很严肃。“我可以告诉你们，但是你们要保证不会告诉任何人。” 她说。
“我们保证。” 大家屏住呼吸说。
Roxy looked very serious. "I'll tell you. But you all have to promise to never tell anyone," she said.
"We promise," said her friends, hardly breathing.
“好的。” 罗西小声说，“其实很简单。当天非常热的时候，我....” 她停了下来。
“你什么？” 玛拉问，“你怎么做？” 
"Okay," Roxy whispered. "It's very simple. When it's really hot, I . . ." She paused.
"You what?" asked Mara. "What do you do?"
罗西看了看四周，确保没有人在听。她小声说：“我就尽量不去想它。” 说完之后，罗西咯咯地笑了。
杰克抱怨道：“我以为你真的要告诉我们什么好办法呢！” 
Roxy looked around to make sure no one else was listening. She whispered, "I try not to think about it." Roxy giggled.
Jack groaned. "I thought you were going to tell us something good!"
艾普卡特老师坐在教室前面。她抬起头看了看。
“我知道现在很热。” 她说，“但是请保持安静。” 
“我还是觉得火箭女孩儿可以帮我们摆脱炎热。” 特勒尔小声说。
Miss Apricot looked up from the front of the room.
"I know it's very hot," she said. "But please be quiet."
"I still think Rocket Girl could stop this heat," whispered Terrell.
就在这时，罗西听到她的手表响了。
‘是市长。’她心想。
“艾普卡特老师。” 罗西说，“我可以去一下厕所吗？” 
Just then Roxy heard her watch beeping.
"It's the mayor," she thought.
"Miss Apricot," said Roxy. "May I go to the restroom?"
罗西到了女厕所。
“布洛姆市长。” 她看着手表的屏幕说，“有什么事吗？” 
A moment later Roxy was in the girls' room.
"Mayor Bloom," she said, looking at the screen on her watch. "What's the problem?"
“火箭女孩儿，我们需要你的帮助！” 布洛姆市长说。“真实储蓄银行被抢劫了。我已经跟潘校长说过了，在事情解决之前，你可以不用去学校。” 
“我马上过去。” 罗西说。
"Rocket Girl, we need your help!" said Mayor Bloom. "True Savings Bank is being robbed. I spoke with Principal Penn. She said you're excused from class until we solve the case."
"I'm on my way," said Roxy.
罗西很快就变身为火箭女孩儿。她从学校跑出去，然后飞上了天。
“看！” 玛拉说，“是火箭女孩儿！” 
Roxy quickly changed into Rocket Girl. She ran out of the school and shot up into the air.
"Look!" said Mara. "It's Rocket Girl!"
“她这是去哪里呢？” 杰克问。
“罗西还没有从厕所回来。” 特勒尔说，“怎么这么长时间？” 
"I wonder where she's going," said Jack.
"Roxy's still not back from the restroom," said Terrell. "What's taking her so long?"
当罗西到达真实储蓄银行的时候，她本来想找到抢劫犯。但是她却看到了一群人。他们全部都被冻住了！
When Roxy arrived at True Savings Bank, she expected to find the bank robber. Instead she saw a crowd of people. And they were all frozen!
“哇！这里发生了什么事？” 罗西思索着，“为什么他们被冻住了？” 
史密斯侦探冲进了银行。他跑得上气不接下气。
"Whoa! What happened here?" Roxy wondered. "Why are all these people frozen?"
Detective Smith rushed into the bank. He was out of breath from running.
“火箭女孩儿。” 他说，“我以最快的速度赶到了。刚才我在乳梦冰淇淋店。” 
“您知道吗，侦探，您真的不应该把冰淇淋当早餐！” 罗西笑着说。
"Rocket Girl," he said. "I came as fast as I could. I was at the Dairy Dream Ice Cream Parlor."
"You know, Detective, you really shouldn't eat ice cream for breakfast!" Roxy laughed.
史密斯侦探皱了皱眉。“我没有吃冰淇淋当早餐。” 他说，“冰淇淋店被偷了，所以我们现在有两个抢劫案要破。” 
Detective Smith frowned. "I wasn't eating ice cream for breakfast," he said. "The ice cream was stolen. So we have two robberies to solve."
‘嗯。’罗西想。乳梦冰淇淋店被偷了，然后这些在银行的人被冻住了。罗西觉得这有些蹊跷。
“我觉得这两件案子是同一个人做的。” 罗西说。
"Hmm," thought Roxy. Dairy Dream had been robbed. And there were frozen people at the bank. Roxy found this very suspicious.
"I think both robberies were done by the same person," said Roxy.
“你为什么这么想？” 史密斯侦探问。
“冰淇淋店被盗了，这里的人又被冰冻了。” 罗西说，“这两件案子必定是有关联的。” 
"Why do you think that?" asked Detective Smith.
"We have stolen ice cream and frozen people," said Roxy. "The crimes must be connected."
“我不这样认为。” 史密斯侦探说，“银行抢劫犯不会去偷冰淇淋的。” 
“好吧，我们现在需要给这些人解冻。” 罗西说，“我来用我的热感视力。” 
"I don't think so," said Detective Smith. "Bank robbers don't usually rob ice cream parlors."
"Well, we have to unfreeze these people right away," said Roxy. "I'll use my heat vision."
“热感视力？” 史密斯侦探问，“我以为你的眼睛只能放射激光。” 
“两个都会。” 罗西说，“您最好还是退后一点，侦探先生。” 
"Heat vision?" said Detective Smith. "I thought your eyes shot lasers."
"They do that too," said Roxy. "You'd better stand back, Detective."
罗西紧紧地盯着其中一个被冻住的人。一束橙色的光慢慢从罗西的眼睛射了出来，把冰融化了。冰块儿一块接着一块地融化了。很快，大家就都被解救了出来。
“好冷！谢谢你，火箭女孩儿。” 一个女人说。
Roxy stared hard at one of the frozen people. An orange beam slowly radiated out of Roxy's eyes, melting the ice. She melted one ice block after another. Soon all the people were free.
"Brr! Thank you, Rocket Girl," said a woman.
“你可以告诉我们这里发生了什么吗？” 
女人颤抖着。“我来存款。” 她说，“接着，一个男人走进来，用冰冻射线冻住了所有的人。呃！” 
"Can you tell us what happened here?" asked Roxy.
The woman shivered. "I came in to deposit a check," she said. "Then a man came in and started blasting freeze rays at everyone. Brr!"
“冰冻射线？” 罗西问。
就在这时，史密斯侦探的手机响了起来。
“喂？” 他说。史密斯侦探看起来很严肃。“真的吗？什么时候？哦，不好。太糟糕了。是的，马上就去。” 
"Freeze rays?" said Roxy.
Just then Detective Smith's phone rang.
"Hello?" he said. Detective Smith looked very serious. "Really? How long ago? Oh no! This is terrible. Yes, sir. Right away, sir."
“什么事？” 罗西问。
“另一家银行正在遭遇抢劫！” 侦探回答。
"What's wrong now?" asked Roxy after Detective Smith had hung up.
"Another bank is being robbed!" said the detective.
“是哪家银行？” 罗西问。
“美罗城中心银行。” 史密斯侦探说，“我们要快……火箭女孩儿？” 
"What bank is being robbed now?" asked Roxy.
"Metro City Central Bank," said Detective Smith. "We have to hurry—Rocket Girl?"
一分钟后，罗西到了美罗城中心银行的外面。这是美罗城里一座很大的建筑，它建在一个又长又陡的山坡上。
A minute later Roxy was outside Metro City Central Bank. It was a large building in downtown Metro City. It was at the top of a long, steep hill.
罗西可以看到大家正在里面哭喊着跑来跑去。
“他正在发射冰冻射线！” 
“好冷啊！” 
Inside the bank Roxy could see people running around and crying out.
"He's shooting freeze rays!"
"I'm so cold!"
“快来救我们，火箭女孩儿！” 
罗西看着那个坏人。他穿着银色的靴子和白色连身衣，冰柱挂在他银色的胡须上。
“是冰冻弗雷迪！” 罗西说。
"Save us, Rocket Girl!"
Roxy saw the villain. He was wearing silver boots and a white jumpsuit. Icicles hung from his silver beard.
"It's Freddie Freeze!" said Roxy.
弗雷迪正拿着一个很大的冰冻喷气枪，枪连着弗雷迪背后的大罐子。他正在向银行的保险箱走去。
罗西用她眼睛发射的x射线看到罐子内部。罐子里面装满了冰淇淋。
Freddie was holding a Big Freeze Blaster. It was attached to a large tank on Freddie's back. He was walking toward the bank's safe.
Roxy used her x-ray vision to look in the tank. It was filled with ice cream.
“啊哈！” 罗西恍然大悟。
“冰冻弗雷迪利用冰淇淋来给冰冻喷气枪补充能量！” 
罗西飞进了银行。
"Aha!" Roxy realized. "Freddie Freeze is using the ice cream to power his Big Freeze Blaster!"
Roxy flew into the bank.
“快住手，弗雷迪！” 她大声叫道，“你抢银行的日子结束了！” 
冰冻弗雷迪很快转过身来，他满眼惊讶。
"Hold it right there, Freddie!" she shouted. "Your bank-robbing days are over!"
Freddie Freeze quickly turned around. His eyes widened in surprise.
“火箭女孩儿！” 他说，“你不能阻止我！” 
弗雷迪向罗西发射冰冻射线。
砰！
"Rocket Girl!" he said. "You'll never stop me!"
Freddie blasted a freeze ray at Roxy.
Fwoosh!
罗西快速躲开，跑到了外面。弗雷迪紧追不舍。罗西跑下山坡。
“我要把你变成冰块儿！” 弗雷迪大叫道。
Roxy jumped out of the way and ran back outside. Freddie followed her. Roxy ran partway down the hill.
"I'm going to turn you into an ice pop!" shouted Freddie.
砰！
罗西旁边的树被冰冻住了。
“你永远不可能射到我的！” 罗西说，“你太慢了！” 
冰冻弗雷迪用冰冻喷气枪射出一个又一个的冰冻射线。
Fwoosh!
The tree next to Roxy was frozen solid.
"You'll never hit me!" said Roxy. "You're too slow!"
Freddie Freeze shot blast after blast of freeze rays.
罗西矫捷地躲过一次又一次的攻击。她比弗雷迪快多了。
“放弃吧，弗雷迪。” 罗西说，“我比你的傻瓜冰冻射线快多了。” 
Roxy darted back and forth and up and down. She was much too quick for Freddie.
"Just give up, Freddie," said Roxy. "I'm too fast for your dumb freeze rays."
罗西站在小坡的边缘。弗雷迪再次瞄准了她。
砰！
罗西跳了起来。
Roxy was now standing at the edge of the hill. Freddie aimed his Big Freeze Blaster and fired at her.
Fwoosh!
Roxy jumped.
“哈哈！” 罗西笑道，“你又射偏了！” 
弗雷迪的最后一击把整个街道都冻住了。这是一个很长，很陡的山坡，罗西快速地滑了下去。
“哇！” 罗西叫道。
"Ha-ha!" Roxy laughed. "You missed me again! Whoa!"
Freddie's last freeze ray had frozen the entire street. It was a long, steep hill, and Roxy was sliding fast!
"Whoa!" cried Roxy.
罗西想用她的热感视力融化那些冰。但是她滑得太快了，并且一直打转。她抬头一看，发现弗雷迪正用他的冰冻喷气枪瞄准她。
罗西咽了一下口水。“哎呀！” 
Roxy tried to melt the ice with her heat vision. But she was sliding too fast and spinning all over the place. Looking up, she could see Freddie aiming his Big Freeze Blaster at her.
Roxy gulped. "Uh-oh!"
冰冻弗雷迪扣动了冰冻喷气枪的扳机。但是什么也没发生。
“该死！” 弗雷迪咒骂道，“为了打中那个讨厌的火箭女孩儿，所有能量都用完了！
Freddie Freeze pulled the trigger of the Big Freeze Blaster. Nothing happened.
"Drat!" said Freddie. "I used up all the freeze power dealing with that pesky Rocket Girl.
还是不要管火箭女孩儿了，我得找到更多的冰淇淋。我今天还要抢劫更多的银行。” 
到了坡底，罗西终于停下了。
But never mind her—I need to get more ice cream. I have a lot of banks to rob today."
Roxy finally stopped sliding when she reached the bottom of the hill.
“咻！” 她吐了口气，站了起来。罗西飞回山坡顶端。弗雷迪已经不在那里了。
‘弗雷迪一定是去找更多的冰淇淋了。’罗西想。
"Whew!" she said, standing up. Roxy flew back to the top of the hill. Freddie was gone.
"Freddie must have gone to get more ice cream," thought Roxy.
‘他已经把乳梦冰淇淋店盗空了。美罗城里面还有什么地方有很多冰淇淋呢？’
罗西皱着眉头想了一会儿，突然她吓得吞了吞口水。“哦，不好！美罗城小学的食堂！” 
"He already robbed Dairy Dream. What other place in Metro City has a lot of ice cream?"
Roxy thought for a moment and then gulped. "Oh no! The Metro City Elementary School cafeteria!"
“啊！食堂居然比我们的教室还热。” 玛拉说。
所有的学生都刚刚坐下来吃饭。今天的午餐是热肉丸三明治。
"Ugh! It's hotter in the cafeteria than in our classroom," said Mara.
All the students had just sat down to eat. Today's lunch was hot meatball sandwiches.
“呃。我真的不想吃热的食物。” 杰克说。
突然间食堂的门被撞开了。
“火箭女孩儿！” 一个男孩儿叫道。
"Eww. Hot food is the last thing I want right now," said Jack.
Suddenly the doors to the cafeteria flew open.
"Rocket Girl!" shouted a boy.
“大家听好了！” 罗西站在冰箱旁边说，“我们没有太多的时间，现在你们需要开始吃冰淇淋，吃得越多越好！” 
"Listen up, everyone!" said Roxy, landing next to the ice cream freezer. "We don't have much time. I need you to start eating lots and lots of ice cream!"
整个食堂变得很安静。然后一个男孩儿说话了。“我们需要吃很多的冰淇淋？” 他问道。
“是的！” 罗西说，“而且必须要快！” 
她开始向学生们扔冰淇淋。
The whole cafeteria became silent for a second. Then a boy spoke up. "We need to eat lots of ice cream?" he asked.
"Yes!" said Roxy. "And quickly!" She started throwing ice cream to the students.
“为什么？” 另一个学生问。
“为什么管这么多？” 特勒尔说，“我们吃就是了！” 
冰淇淋甜筒，冰淇淋三明治还有冰棍儿都在空中飞着。
"Why?" asked another student.
"Who cares why?" said Terrell. "Let's just eat!"
Ice cream cones, ice cream sandwiches, and ice cream pops flew through the air.
很快，大家就都在吃冰淇淋了，甚至老师们也加入了吃冰淇淋的队伍里。
“哇！” 特勒尔叫道，“真是太棒了！我终于感到凉爽了。” 
Soon everyone was eating ice cream, even the teachers.
"Woo-hoo!" shouted Terrell. "This is great! I'm finally cooling off."
“我爱冰淇淋！” 杰克说。
当冰冻弗雷迪冲进食堂的时候，所有的冰淇淋都已经被吃掉了。
“啊！” 弗雷迪大叫。
"I love ice cream!" said Jack.
When Freddie Freeze burst into the cafeteria, all the ice cream was gone.
"Aargh!" cried Freddie.
罗西笑了。“弗雷迪，你再也不需要冰冻喷气枪了。你要被关进监狱了！” 
罗西把弗雷迪送到派出所之后，立刻返回了学校。孩子们在外面休息。
Roxy smiled. "Freddie, you're not going to need that Big Freeze Blaster anymore. You're going to jail!"
After Roxy took Freddie Freeze to the police station, she headed back to school. The kids were outside for recess.
“罗西！你去哪儿了？” 玛拉问。
“我在帮助潘校长做学校的网站。” 罗西回答道。她坐在一个秋千上荡了起来。
"Roxy! Where have you been?" asked Mara.
"I was helping Principal Penn work on the school website," said Roxy. She got on a swing and started swinging.
特勒尔怀疑地看着罗西。“你不在的时候火箭女孩儿来了。” 他说。
罗西只是微笑着把秋千荡得很高很高。
Terrell gave Roxy a suspicious look. "Rocket Girl came while you were gone," he said.
Roxy just smiled as she flew high in the air.
傍晚，潘校长和其他的教师们到达了美罗城格兰德酒店。一个叫做思维普斯的神秘男人邀请他们去参加一个特别的会议。
It was early one evening. Principal Penn and the teachers were arriving at Metro City Grand Hotel. A mysterious man named Mr. Sweeps had invited them to a special meeting.
‘也许他要给学校捐些款。’潘校长想。
“欢迎你们。” 思维普斯先生说，“请拿一个胸针。” 
"Maybe he's going to donate money to the school," thought Principal Penn.
"Welcome," said Mr. Sweeps. "Please take a button."
潘校长把一个星星模样的胸针别在了夹克上面，然后坐了下来。
“现在。” 思维普斯先生说，“让我来告诉你们，为什么会邀请你们来到这里……” 
Principal Penn pinned a star button onto her jacket. Then she sat down.
"Now," said Mr. Sweeps. "Let me tell you why I invited you here . . ."
这是一个美丽的秋天早晨，罗西和她的朋友们正向学校走去。
“天气一直都是这样就好了。” 杰克说，“我们班下周组织一起去动物园。” 
It was a beautiful fall morning. Roxy and her friends were walking to school.
"I hope the weather stays like this," said Jack. "Our class has a field trip to the zoo next week."
“我已经等不及要去看蛇了。” 特勒尔说。
“我担心我们去不了。” 玛拉说，“我妈妈告诉我，我们学校现在很需要钱。也许去动物园的活动会被取消。” 
"I can't wait to see the snakes," said Terrell.
"I'm worried we won't be able to go to the zoo," said Mara. "My mom told me our school needs money. The field trip to the zoo might be canceled."
“那就太糟糕了！” 杰克说。
“我们需要做点什么来帮助我们的学校。” 
“我们能做什么呢？” 玛拉问，“我们又没有钱。” 
“也许火箭女孩儿可以帮忙。” 特勒尔说。
"That would be awful!" said Jack. "We should do something to help."
"What can we do?" asked Mara. "We don't have any money."
"Maybe Rocket Girl can help," said Terrell.
“我可不这么认为。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿也没有钱。” 
“没有什么是火箭女孩儿办不到的。” 特勒尔说，“她是最棒的超级英雄！” 
罗西耸了耸肩。
"I don't think so," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl doesn't have money."
"Rocket Girl can do anything," said Terrell. "She's the greatest superhero ever!"
Roxy shrugged.
很快，罗西和她的朋友们到达了学校。罗西向停车场望去。
“老师们的车怎么都不在？” 她自言自语道。
Soon Roxy and her friends reached school. Roxy looked at the parking lot.
"Where are all the teachers' cars?" she wondered.
“学生们，欢迎你们！” 一个站在学校门口的男人说。他正在发放星星模样的胸针。“我是思维普斯先生，是你们的代理校长。潘校长……嗯……在忙别的事情。” 
"Welcome, students!" said a man at the school entrance. He was handing out star-shaped buttons. "I'm Mr. Sweeps, your substitute principal today. Principal Penn is . . . um . . . busy doing other things."
罗西怀疑地看着思维普斯先生。这个代理校长有些奇怪。
“好的！谢谢您给我这个胸针。” 杰克说。
Roxy looked at Mr. Sweeps suspiciously. Something about the substitute principal seemed odd.
"Cool! Thanks for the button!" said Jack.
思维普斯先生把一个胸针递给了罗西。“这是你的，小姑娘。” 他说。
“谢谢。” 罗西小心翼翼地看着胸针说。
“快，把它带上。” 思维普斯先生说。
Mr. Sweeps handed one to Roxy. "Here you go, young lady," he said.
"Thanks," said Roxy, carefully looking at the button.
"Go ahead, put it on," said Mr. Sweeps.
就在这时，罗西听到了她手表的响声。她把胸针放进了口袋里面，然后快速地离开了学校大门。
罗西按下手表的按钮。“布洛姆市长。” 她说，“有什么事吗？” 
Just then Roxy heard her watch beep. She put the button in her pocket. Then she hurried away from the school's entrance.
Roxy pressed a button on her watch. "Mayor Bloom," she said. "What's wrong?"
“我们有麻烦了，火箭女孩儿。” 市长说，“潘校长失踪了，我想让你查查看她发生了什么事儿。” 
罗西看了看思维普斯先生。
“不要担心。” 罗西说，“我会找到潘校长的。” 
"We have a problem, Rocket Girl," said the mayor. "Principal Penn disappeared. I want you to find out what happened to her."
Roxy looked over at Mr. Sweeps.
"Don't worry," said Roxy. "I'll find Principal Penn."
罗西确认了没人在看她以后，悄悄跑到学校教学楼的后面。就在一瞬间，她变身成为了火箭女孩儿！
“是时候去找出潘校长失踪的原因了。” 罗西说。
Roxy made sure no one was watching her. Then she sneaked around the school building. In an instant she was Rocket Girl!
"It's time to find out what happened to Principal Penn," said Roxy.
她飞向空中。
“看！是火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉叫道。
“她这是去哪里呢？” 杰克说。
特勒尔看了看四周。
“你们知道罗西去哪里了吗？” 他问道。
She blasted off into the sky.
"Look! It's Rocket Girl!" said Mara.
"I wonder where she's going," said Jack.
Terrell looked around. "Does anyone know where Roxy went?" he asked.
罗西在警察总局落了下来。她找到了史密斯侦探。他正坐在桌子前，盯着他的电脑。
“您这是在看电视节目吗？” 罗西笑道，“您不应该在破案吗？” 
Roxy landed at Police Headquarters. She found Detective Smith. He was sitting at his desk, watching something on his computer.
"Are you watching a TV show?" Roxy laughed. "Aren't you supposed to be solving crimes?"
史密斯侦探皱了皱眉。“我没有在看电视节目。我在看一段交通录像。” 
“布洛姆市长给我打电话了。” 罗西说，“他告诉我，潘校长失踪了。” 
Detective Smith frowned. "I'm not watching a TV show. I'm watching video from a traffic camera."
"I got a call from Mayor Bloom," said Roxy. "He said Principal Penn disappeared."
“她没有失踪。” 史密斯侦探说，“她离开了小镇。事实上，美罗城小学所有的老师都离开了小镇。你看。” 
"She didn't disappear," said Detective Smith. "She left town. In fact, all the teachers from Metro City Elementary School left town. Watch this."
罗西看了看交通录像。录像里面有很多汽车和公交车经过。
“嘿！那是潘校长！” 罗西说。
“接着看。” 史密斯侦探说。
Roxy watched the video from the traffic camera. The video showed lots of cars and buses driving by.
"Hey! That was Principal Penn!" said Roxy.
"Keep watching," said Detective Smith.
接下来是艾普卡特老师。紧接着是格林老师。罗西学校的老师们一个接着一个，开着车经过。
“那是西大街。” 史密斯侦探说，“通往美罗城外的山上。” 
Next Miss Apricot drove by. Then Mr. Green drove by. One after another, all the teachers from Roxy's school drove by.
"That's West Street," said Detective Smith. "It leads out of Metro City and into the mountains."
“所有的老师开着车去山上了？” 罗西说。
“我猜是的。” 史密斯侦探说，“这说不通啊。为什么所有的老师会在工作日去山上呢？他们现在应该在教书！” 
"So all the teachers drove to the mountains?" asked Roxy.
"I think so," said Detective Smith. "But it doesn't make any sense. Why would teachers do that on a school day? They're supposed to be teaching!"
罗西又看了一遍录像。这次她发现了什么。所有的老师们胸前都别着一模一样的星星胸针！而且所有的胸针都在发着光。
Roxy watched the video again. This time she noticed something. All the teachers were wearing the same star buttons! And the buttons were glowing.
“我见过这些胸针！” 罗西叫道，“思维普斯老师，那个代理校长，他把胸针都发给了学生们！” 
“你确定吗？” 史密斯侦探问，“那太值得怀疑了。我们需要……火箭女孩儿？” 
"I've seen those buttons before!" cried Roxy. "Mr. Sweeps, the substitute principal, was giving them to all the students!"
"Are you sure about that?" asked Detective Smith. "That is very suspicious. We'll have to . . . Rocket Girl?"
罗西一瞬间就到达了美罗城小学。她冲进大门。
“思维普斯老师在哪里？” 罗西喊道。
In a flash Roxy was back at Metro City Elementary School. She burst through the front doors.
"Where's Mr. Sweeps?" Roxy demanded.
走廊是空着的。
“有人在吗？” 罗西叫道。
没有人回答。
The hallway was empty.
"Hello?" Roxy called.
No one answered.
罗西冲进了教室里。没有人在。校长室里面也是空着的。罗西很快意识到，整个学校都是空着的。
Roxy ran into her classroom. No one was there. No one was in the principal's office either. Roxy soon realized the whole school was empty.
“大家都去了哪里呢？” 她思索着，“我需要用我的超级听力了。” 
几秒之后，她听到了什么声音，并且是非常奇怪的声音！
"Where did everyone go?" she wondered. "I'll use my super hearing."
A second later she heard something—something very strange!
咚……咚……咚……
唧！唧！罗西靠超级听力听到很多学校里寻常的声音。她听到画室里面水槽滴水的声音，以及幼儿园教室里面蟋蟀鸣叫的声音。
Drip . . . drip . . . drip . . .
Chirp! Chirp! With her super hearing, Roxy heard lots of usual school sounds. She heard water dripping from the art room sink. She heard a cricket chirping in one of the kindergarten rooms.
但是她也听到了一个不寻常的声音。一个低沉的嗓音从学校地下传来。
“干活儿！干活儿！干活儿！” 有人咆哮着，“快点儿！” 
But she also heard something unusual. It was a deep voice coming from under the school.
"Work! Work! Work!" growled the voice. "Move faster!"
“那是思维普斯的声音！” 罗西想，“我就知道不能够信任他！” 
罗西飞快地跑到了地下室。她来到一扇被锁的大门前面。
"That's Mr. Sweeps!" Roxy thought. "I knew I shouldn't trust him!"
Roxy ran down the stairs to the basement. She came to a pair of locked doors.
罗西紧紧地盯着这扇门，激光从她的眼睛里面射出。
嗞轰！
大门被炸开了，罗西马上冲了进去。
Roxy stared hard at the doors. Lasers shot out from her eyes.
Whiz-hoo!
The doors blew apart, and Roxy ran through the opening.
地下室是空着的。罗西瞅了瞅四周，发现一个地板门。她跑了过去，打开了地板门。罗西跳了下去，落在了一个大洞穴里。
The basement was empty. Roxy glanced around and spotted a trapdoor. She rushed over and opened it. Roxy jumped down, landing in a large cavern.
在那里，罗西看到所有的学生们都在做苦工。一些在用铁锹凿石头墙，一些在推着小推车。
There, Roxy saw all the students doing hard labor. Some were chipping away at the rock walls with pickaxes. Others were pushing wheelbarrows.
“这难道是一个矿井？” 罗西想。她看了看四周，发现一个学生正在从墙里面拉出一块闪闪发光的东西。
“哇！” 罗西深吸了一口气。“这是一个钻石矿井！” 
"Is this a mine?" Roxy wondered. She looked around, and saw one student pull something sparkly from the wall.
"Whoa!" gasped Roxy. "This is a diamond mine!"
所有的学生都带着思维普斯给的星星胸针。没有人看到火箭女孩儿。他们都在忙着干活儿。
“这真是太奇怪了。” 罗西自言自语道。
The students were all wearing the star buttons from Mr. Sweeps. Nobody saw Rocket Girl. They were all too busy working.
"This is totally weird," Roxy said to herself.
她看到了特勒尔。“这里发生什么了？” 罗西朝他喊道。
但是特勒尔并没有回答，他甚至都没有看她一眼。
“他被催眠了！” 罗西恍然大悟。“大家都被催眠了！这都是因为那些星星胸针。” 
She saw Terrell. "What's going on here?" Roxy called to him.
Terrell didn't answer. He didn't even look at her.
"He's hypnotized!" Roxy realized. "Everybody is. It's because of those star buttons."
突然间，杰克和玛拉从后面抓住了罗西。她本来想用力挣脱他们，但是马上觉得这并不是什么好主意。她不想伤害她的朋友们。
Suddenly Jack and Mara sneaked up from behind and grabbed Roxy. She thought about fighting them off. But Roxy knew that wasn't a good idea. She didn't want to hurt her friends.
思维普斯出现了。“你以为可以阻止我，是吧？” 他说。罗西发现他的手上戴着一个闪闪发亮的星星戒指。
“这里发生了什么？” 罗西质问道。
Mr. Sweeps appeared. "Thought you could stop me, did you?" he said. Roxy noticed he was wearing a glowing, star-shaped ring.
"What's going on down here?" Roxy demanded.
“你们学校的地下有很多的钻石。” 思维普斯说，“我想拥有它们！我催眠了所有的老师，让他们离开小镇。之后我又催眠了你的同学们，让他们为我挖钻石。” 
"There are lots of diamonds here under your school," said Mr. Sweeps. "And I want them! I hypnotized your teachers and made them leave town. Then I hypnotized your schoolmates so they could mine the diamonds."
思维普斯咯咯一笑。“我要变成富翁了！” 
“你逃不掉的！” 罗西说。
思维普斯笑了。“哦，那可不一定！” 他看了杰克和玛拉一眼。“把这个犯人带过来！” 
Mr. Sweeps let out a cackle. "I am going to be rich!"
"You'll never get away with this!" said Roxy.
Mr. Sweeps grinned. "Oh, not necessarily" He looked at Jack and Mara. "Bring the prisoner this way!"
杰克和玛拉把罗西推进了一个监狱。
思维普斯先生笑了。“现在你再也阻止不了我了。” 他把铁门重重地关上。罗西听到他把门锁了起来。
Jack and Mara pushed Roxy into a cell.
Mr. Sweeps smiled. "Now you'll never stop me." He slammed the heavy iron door. Roxy heard him lock it.
罗西思考着思维普斯先生戴着的那个戒指。‘他是在用那个戒指控制着大家，我要把那个戒指毁掉。’
罗西看了看监狱的四周。‘我可以把那扇门撞碎。’她想。
Roxy thought about the ring Mr. Sweeps was wearing. "He's using that ring to control everyone. I need to destroy it."
Roxy looked around the cell. "I could break down that door," she thought.
‘但是思维普斯先生会听到的。我需要想一个可以悄悄溜出去的办法。’
罗西跺了一下脚，想知道这个地板有多硬。“我有办法了。” 
"But Mr. Sweeps will hear me. I need to find a way to sneak out."
Roxy kicked at the rock floor to see how hard it was. "I think I have an idea."
思维普斯先生正在仔细观察一块钻石，突然他听到一声巨响。
“火箭女孩儿正在想办法越狱。” 他叫道，“大家快去守住门。” 
Mr. Sweeps was examining a diamond when he heard a crash.
"Rocket Girl is trying to break out of her cell," he yelled. "Everyone, guard the door!"
所有的学生们都扔掉手里的工具。他们全都聚集在监狱的门口。砰！传来了一阵巨响。整个洞穴都在震动。
All the students dropped their tools. They gathered in front of the cell door. Boom! There was a deep rumbling sound. The entire cavern shook.
“如果火箭女孩儿逃脱出来，就马上抓住她！” 思维普斯先生命令道。
突然间——砰！石头飞散开来。罗西从大家身后的地板下蹦了出来。
"As soon as Rocket Girl comes out, capture her!" commanded Mr. Sweeps.
Suddenly—kaboom! Pieces of rock flew everywhere. Roxy blasted through the cavern floor behind everyone.
思维普斯先生想躲开，但是他不够快。嗞轰！
罗西的眼睛里发射出激光。戒指爆炸了。
“我的戒指！” 思维普斯先生叫道。
Mr. Sweeps spun around, but he wasn't fast enough. Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams. The ring exploded.
"My ring!" cried Mr. Sweeps.
瞬间，学生们身上的胸针就失去了光芒。
“我们这是在哪儿?” 杰克问。
“发生了什么事，火箭女孩儿？” 玛拉问。
Instantly the students' buttons stopped glowing.
"Where are we?" asked Jack.
"What's going on, Rocket Girl?" asked Mara.
“你们都被思维普斯先生催眠了。” 罗西回答，“他并不是真的校长，他强迫你们来帮他挖学校地下的钻石。” 
"You were all hypnotized by Mr. Sweeps," answered Roxy. "He isn't really a principal. He was forcing you to mine diamonds here under the school."
“没错。” 这时，史密斯侦探走了进来。“现在，思维普斯就要进监狱了！” 
眨眼之间，火箭女孩儿就消失了。
过了一会儿，罗西出现了。她穿着平常的衣服，还有一个星星胸针别在上面。
"That's right," said Detective Smith, who had just walked into the cavern. "And now Sweeps is going to jail!"
In a flash Rocket Girl disappeared. A moment later Roxy appeared. She was wearing her regular clothes and her star button.
“发生了什么事？” 她装作一副也被催眠过的样子嘟囔道。
特勒尔满脸怀疑地看了她一眼。
"What happened?" she mumbled, pretending she'd been hypnotized too.
Terrell gave her a suspicious look.
第二天早晨，潘校长和其他的老师们都回来上班了。
“看上去一切都恢复正常了。” 玛拉说。
“我真高兴。” 杰克说，“比起在钻石矿里面干活，我还是更喜欢学习。” 
The next morning Principal Penn and the teachers were back at work.
"It looks like things are back to normal," said Mara.
"I'm glad," said Jack. "I'd rather learn than work in that diamond mine."
“你们知道吗？” 玛拉说，“我们可以去动物园了！我妈妈告诉我，学校现在有足够的钱了。” 
“从哪里来的钱啊？” 特勒尔问。
"You know what else?" asked Mara. "We can go to the zoo! My mom told me our school has money for field trips now."
"Where did the money come from?" Terrell asked.
“潘校长要把钻石卖掉！” 玛拉说。
“哇！” 特勒尔说，“我说过，火箭女孩儿什么都可以解决的。是她帮助我们学校得到了钱。” 
罗西什么也没有说。
"Principal Penn is going to sell the diamonds!" said Mara.
"Wow!" said Terrell. "I told you Rocket Girl can do anything. She helped our school get money!"
Roxy didn't say a word.
电视台的每个人都在忙碌着。一个女人把摄像机打开了，一个男人把话筒搬了过来。他们正在准备开拍新一集的《大力士》。
Everyone at the TV station was busy. A woman turned on a camera. A man carried a microphone. They were getting ready to film a new episode of Mighty Man.
“大力士在哪儿？” 有人问。
“我在这儿呢。” 一个穿着超级英雄服装的演员说。
突然间——砰！一个男人出现在烟雾中。
"Where's Mighty Man?" asked someone.
"Here I am," said an actor in a superhero costume.
Suddenly—poof! A man appeared in a puff of smoke.
他戴着一顶高高的帽子，嘴上留着细细的胡子。他穿着礼服，肩膀上有一只猴子。
这个男人邪恶地笑着。“今天会上演一出新的节目！” 
He had a tall hat and a thin moustache. He wore a tuxedo. A monkey sat on his shoulder.
The man had an evil grin. "There's going to be a new show today!"
“快点儿！” 杰克说，“十分钟后《大力士》就要开始了！” 
罗西和朋友们在去杰克家的路上。他们要去看《大力士》，是一个关于超级英雄的电视剧。
"Hurry up!" said Jack. "Mighty Man is on in ten minutes!"
Roxy and her friends were on their way to Jack's house. They were going to watch Mighty Man, a TV show about a superhero.
“我很好奇大力士今天会干什么。” 玛拉说。
“上周一个行星马上就要撞到地球了。” 杰克说，“所以，今天大力士会阻止它。” 
"I wonder what Mighty Man will do today," said Mara.
"Last week an asteroid was about to crash into Earth," said Jack. "So today Mighty Man is going to stop it!"
“大力士真的是太酷了。” 玛拉说。
“还可以吧。” 特勒尔说，“他并不是特别厉害。” 
杰克和玛拉愣了一下。
“你是什么意思？” 杰克问。
"Mighty Man is so cool," said Mara.
"He's okay," said Terrell. "But he's not that great."
Jack and Mara were stunned.
"What do you mean?" asked Jack.
特勒尔耸了耸肩。“大力士不是真的。他只是一个电视剧里面的演员。” 
“我们知道。” 杰克说，“但是如果他是真的，那他就是最棒的超级英雄。” 
Terrell shrugged. "Mighty Man isn't real. He's just a character in a show."
"We know that," said Jack. "But if he was real, he'd be the best superhero ever."
“那是不可能的！” 特勒尔说，“火箭女孩儿比大力士酷多了！对吗，罗西？” 
大家都看着罗西。
"No way!" said Terrell. "Rocket Girl is much cooler than Mighty Man! Right, Roxy?"
Everyone looked at Roxy.
“罗西。” 玛拉说，“你是怎么想的？” 
罗西想了想。
“我同意特勒尔的想法。” 她说，“火箭女孩儿比大力士酷多了。大力士有点儿……傻。” 
"Well?" said Mara. "What do you think, Roxy?"
Roxy thought for a moment.
"I agree with Terrell," she said. "Rocket Girl is definitely cooler than Mighty Man. Mighty Man is kind of . . . silly."
四个朋友到了杰克的家，进了房子。杰克拿了一些零食，然后大家坐在了沙发上。杰克打开了电视，但是《大力士》并没有开始。取而代之的是一个奇怪的男人在表演。他戴着一顶高高的帽子，嘴上还有细细的胡子。
The four friends got to Jack's house and went inside. Jack grabbed some snacks, and everyone flopped onto the sofa.
Jack turned on the TV. But Mighty Man wasn't on. Instead a strange man was on the set of the TV show. He had a tall hat and a thin moustache.
“大家好。” 那个男人说，“《大力士》被取消了。我将为大家表演一个新的节目。这是一个魔术表演，我是明星！我会变得非常有名的！” 
“那是谁呀？” 特勒尔问。
"Hello, everybody," said the man. "Mighty Man has been canceled. I have a new show for you. It's a magic show, and I'm the star! I'm going to be famous!"
"Who is that guy?" asked Terrell.
罗西知道那个男人是谁，但是她没有办法告诉她的朋友们。‘那是邪恶的魔术师普雷斯托！’她想。
罗西的手表响了。
Roxy couldn't tell her friends, but she knew who the man was. "That's the evil magician Mr. Presto!" she thought.
Roxy's watch beeped.
她冲到杰克家的厨房，按下了手表上的按钮。
“火箭女孩儿！” 布洛姆市长说，“普雷斯托占领了整个电视台！” 
“我知道。” 罗西小声说，“不用担心，我会阻止他的！” 
She rushed into Jack's kitchen and pressed a button on the watch.
"Rocket Girl!" said Mayor Bloom. "Mr. Presto took over the TV station!"
"I know," Roxy whispered. "Don't worry. I'll stop him!"
罗西要查出普雷斯托到底想要干什么。
“嘿，朋友们。” 她对朋友们说，“我才想起来我要帮我妈妈做一些家务活。我马上就回来。” 
Roxy had to find out what Mr. Presto was up to.
"Hey, guys," she said to her friends. "I just remembered I have to help my mom with chores. I'll be back soon."
罗西在电视台看到了史密斯侦探。他正在看一些设备。
“普雷斯托在哪儿？” 罗西问。
“我不知道。” 侦探说，“我到的时候，他已经走了。” 
Roxy found Detective Smith at the TV station. He was looking at some equipment.
"Where's Mr. Presto?" Roxy asked.
"I don't know," said the detective. "He was gone before I got here."
罗西笑了。“我很惊讶，大力士居然没有阻止他。” 
“哈哈。” 史密斯侦探假装笑道，“大力士不像你，他可不是真的超级英雄。” 
“我们得查出普雷斯托在干什么。” 罗西说。
Roxy smirked. "I'm surprised Mighty Man didn't stop him."
"Ha-ha." Detective Smith pretended to laugh. "Mighty Man isn't a real superhero like you, Rocket Girl."
"We need to find out what Mr. Presto's doing," Roxy told him.
史密斯侦探点了点头。“是的，我想……” 
“救命！” 一个声音从门后传来。
罗西向四周望了望。“那听起来像是……” 
“大力士！” 史密斯侦探说。
Detective Smith nodded. "Yes, I think—"
"Help!" A voice cried out from behind a door.
Roxy looked around. "That sounded like . . ."
"Mighty Man!" said Detective Smith.
罗西跑到门口。门被锁上了。嗞轰！罗西用眼睛里射出的激光把门炸开了。
大力士和节目工作人员都被关在了里面。
Roxy ran to the door. It was locked. Whiz-hoo! Roxy blasted it open with her eye laserbeams.
The Mighty Man actor was inside a small room. The TV crew was with him.
“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿。” 大力士说。
“不客气。” 罗西说。
“你知道普雷斯托去哪儿了吗？” 史密斯侦探问。
"Thank you, Rocket Girl," said the actor.
"No problem," Roxy said.
"Do you know where Mr. Presto went?" asked Detective Smith.
“不知道。” 另外一个人回答，“他偷了一台摄像机，然后就逃跑了。但是我们有办法知道他在干什么。” 
男人打开了一台显示器。
"No," said another man. "He stole a camera and left. But we can find out what he's doing."
The man turned on a monitor.
普雷斯托出现在了显示器上。他一只手拿着魔杖，另一只手拿着麦克风。背景是美罗城银行。
Mr. Presto appeared on the screen. He held a wand in one hand and a microphone in the other. Metro City Bank was in the background.
普雷斯托向一个女人走去。这个女人戴着一条钻石项链。
“您好!” 普雷斯托说，“请问您的名字是什么？” 
“莫莉。” 女人说。
Mr. Presto walked over to a woman. The woman wore a diamond necklace.
"Hello!" said Mr. Presto. "What's your name?"
"Molly," said the woman.
“多好听的名字啊！” 普雷斯托说，“我来给你表演一场魔术，莫莉！” 他挥舞着他的魔杖。“一，二，三……变！” 
砰！莫莉的项链消失了。
普雷斯托看着摄像机。“大家觉得我的节目好看吗？” 
"What a lovely name!" said Mr. Presto. "I'm going to show you a magic trick, Molly!" He waved his wand. "One, two, three . . . Presto!"
Poof! Molly's necklace disappeared.
Mr. Presto looked at the camera. "Is everyone enjoying my show?"
接下来，普雷斯托走向一个男人。
“先生，您好！” 普雷斯托说，“哦，您戴着的这块手表看上去很不错。” 
“嗯，谢谢。” 男人说。
Next Mr. Presto walked over to a man.
"Hello, sir!" said Mr. Presto. "Ooh! That's a very nice watch you're wearing."
"Uh, thank you," said the man.
“您喜欢魔术吗？” 普雷斯托先生问。
“是的。” 男人说。
“看这个。” 普雷斯托说。他挥舞着他的魔杖。“一，二，三……变！” 
砰！手表不见了。
"Do you like magic?" asked Mr. Presto.
"Yes," said the man.
"Watch this," said Mr. Presto. He waved his wand. "One, two, three . . . Presto!"
Poof! The watch was gone!
罗西也不见了。她必须阻止普雷斯托继续偷东西！
史密斯侦探还在看着显示器。“火箭女孩儿，我们需要采取行动了。普雷斯托他……火箭女孩儿？她去哪里了？” 
And so was Roxy. She had to stop Mr. Presto from stealing things!
Detective Smith was still watching the monitor. "Rocket Girl, we need to do something. Mr. Presto is . . . Rocket Girl? Where did she go?"
“这个节目真是糟糕透了。” 特勒尔说。
特勒尔，玛拉，还有杰克一直看着普雷斯托的节目。这个魔术师刚刚把一个老爷爷的拐杖变没了。
“大力士在哪儿？” 杰克问。
"This show is terrible," said Terrell.
Terrell, Mara, and Jack were still watching Mr. Presto. The magician had just made an old man's cane disappear.
"Where's Mighty Man?" asked Jack.
突然玛拉叫了起来。“火箭女孩儿在电视里！” 
史密斯侦探和节目工作人员都盯着显示器。
“哇！” 扮演大力士的演员说，“火箭女孩儿！” 
Suddenly Mara shouted. "Rocket Girl is on TV!"
Detective Smith and the TV crew were still watching the monitor.
"Whoa!" said the Mighty Man actor. "It's Rocket Girl!"
普雷斯托正想要把一个小女孩的棒棒糖变没。
“一，二，三……” 
“住手，普雷斯托！” 罗西喊道。
普雷斯托转过身来，那个小女孩趁机跑了。
Mr. Presto was about to make a little girl's lollipop disappear. "One, two, three . . ."
"Stop right there, Mr. Presto!" Roxy yelled.
Mr. Presto spun around, and the little girl ran away.
“火箭女孩儿！” 普雷斯托说，“我一直盼望着你的出现。现在我的节目变得更精彩了！” 
“你的节目就要结束了！” 罗西说。
"Rocket Girl!" said Mr. Presto. "I was hoping you would appear. Now my show will be more exciting!"
"Your show is over," said Roxy.
普雷斯托笑了。“哦，不会的，不会结束的。我马上就会表演我最精彩的节目。我会让美罗城银行里面的钱全部消失！” 
“不，你不会得逞的。” 罗西说。
Mr. Presto smiled. "Oh no, it's not! In a moment I'll perform my most amazing trick. I'm going to make all the money in Metro City Bank disappear!"
"No, you're not," said Roxy.
普雷斯托挑了挑眉毛。“不会得逞？谁能阻止我呢？” 
“我能。” 罗西说。她向普雷斯托跑去。
Mr. Presto raised an eyebrow. "I'm not? Who's going to stop me?"
"I am," said Roxy. She ran toward Mr. Presto.
普雷斯托挥舞了一下他的魔杖。“变！” 
一面墙出现在罗西的面前。砰！罗西撞到了墙上。
普雷斯托大声地笑着。“这个节目真是越来越有意思了！” 
Mr. Presto waved his wand. "Presto!"
A wall appeared in front of Roxy. Bam! Roxy crashed into it.
Mr. Presto laughed. "This is turning out to be such a great show!"
“哎呀！” 罗西疼得大叫，揉了揉自己的额头。她跳过那面墙，落在了普雷斯托的面前。她想抓住他。
“变！” 魔术师说。砰！他消失了。
"Grr!" Roxy growled, rubbing her head. She jumped over the wall and landed in front of Mr. Presto. She tried to grab him.
"Presto!" said the magician. Poof! He disappeared.
罗西看了看四周。“普雷斯托去哪儿了？” 她心想。她走了几步，小心翼翼地看着四周。突然她感觉到有人戳了戳她的肩膀。
Roxy looked from side to side. "Where did Mr. Presto go?" she wondered. She took a few steps, looking carefully. She felt someone tap her on the shoulder.
“我在这儿！” 普雷斯托说。
罗西转过身。
砰！普雷斯托又消失了。
"Here I am!" said Mr. Presto.
Roxy spun around.
Poof! Mr. Presto disappeared again.
罗西找不到魔术师。“嘿！” 她叫道，“普雷斯托！你为什么不出来面对我？你害怕了吗？” 
砰！普雷斯托在附近出现了。
Roxy couldn't find the magician anywhere. "Hey!" she yelled. "Mr. Presto! Why don't you come out and face me? Or are you too scared?"
Poof! Mr. Presto appeared nearby.
“我是世界上最棒的魔术师！” 普雷斯托说，“我才不会害怕一个傻乎乎的小女孩儿呢。” 
罗西瞪着普雷斯托。“一个傻乎乎的小女孩儿？你会为你说的话而感到后悔的！” 
"I'm the world's greatest magician!" said Mr. Presto. "I'm not scared of a silly little girl."
Roxy glared at Mr. Presto. "A silly little girl? You're going to regret saying that!"
罗西像一支火箭一样冲向普雷斯托。
“变！” 普雷斯托说。一个黑色的大盒子出现在他的面前。罗西飞得太快了，没有办法停下来。她直接冲进了盒子里。
Roxy shot toward Mr. Presto like a rocket.
"Presto!" said Mr. Presto.
A big black box appeared in front of him. Roxy was flying too fast to stop. She slammed right into the box.
普雷斯托迅速把盒子关上。“一，二，三……变！” 
玛拉，杰克，还有特勒尔盯着电视屏幕，他们都倒吸了一口凉气。
“不好！” 特勒尔喊道。
Mr. Presto quickly closed it shut. "One, two, three . . . Presto!"
Mara, Jack, and Terrell stared at the TV screen. They all gasped.
"Uh-oh!" cried Terrell.
普雷斯托站在黑盒子的旁边，然后把手伸到帽子里面。他从帽子里抽出了几把剑，然后对着摄像机微笑。
“跟火箭女孩儿说再见吧。” 他说。
Mr. Presto stood near the black box and reached into his hat. He pulled out several swords. He looked into the camera and smiled.
"Say good-bye to Rocket Girl," he said.
普雷斯托慢慢地把剑插进盒子里。
嗖！
“啊！” 玛拉叫道。
普雷斯托又往盒子里面插了另一把剑。
嗖！
“哦，不要！” 史密斯侦探叫道。
Mr. Presto slowly pushed a sword through the box. Shlink!
"Aah!" Mara cried.
Mr. Presto stuck another sword through the box. Shlink!
"Oh no!" cried Detective Smith.
一个接着一个，普雷斯托把所有的剑都插进了盒子里面。做完这些后，他打开了盒子。盒子里什么都没有。盒子后面有一个被烧焦的大洞。
One by one, Mr. Presto stuck all the swords through the box. When he was done, he opened the box. It was empty. A hole was burned through the back.
“啊！” 普雷斯托叫道，“火箭女孩儿逃跑了！” 
普雷斯托看着摄像机。
“算了。现在是把美罗城银行所有的钱变消失的时刻了！” 
“不好！” 史密斯侦探叫道，“火箭女孩儿在哪儿？” 
"Aargh!" cried Mr. Presto. "Rocket Girl escaped!"
Mr. Presto looked at the camera. "Never mind. It's time to make all the money in Metro City Bank disappear!"
"Oh no!" cried Detective Smith. "Where's Rocket Girl?"
普雷斯托走进了美罗城银行。有一些人在排队。他挥舞了一下他的魔杖。“一，二，三……变！” 
砰！所有人都消失了。他们出现在银行外面的大街上。
Mr. Presto walked into Metro City Bank. There was a line of people.
He waved his wand. "One, two, three, presto!"
Poof! All the people disappeared. A second later they appeared outside the bank.
“发生了什么事情？” 一个男人说。
银行里面，银行职员看着普雷斯托。
“你好，先生。” 她说，“请问你要办理……” 
砰！她消失不见了。
"What just happened?" said a man.
Inside, the bank teller looked at Mr. Presto.
"Hello, sir," she said. "How can I help—"
Poof! She disappeared.
普雷斯托走到了柜台的后面。他站在一扇门前。这扇门又大又圆，是用固体金属制成的。
普雷斯托看着摄像机。
“期待已久的时刻即将到来。
Mr. Presto went behind the counter. He stood in front of a door. It was big and round. It was made of solid metal.
Mr. Presto looked at the camera. "And now, the moment we've all been waiting for.
这扇门后面成山的钱，马上就要归我所有了！” 
普雷斯托举起了他的魔杖。“一，二，三……变！” 门弹开了。
普雷斯托向里面看去，他看到了——火箭女孩儿！
Behind this door is a huge pile of money. And it's all going to be mine!"
Mr. Presto raised his wand. "One, two, three . . . Presto!" The door swung open.
Mr. Presto looked inside and saw—Rocket Girl!
特勒尔，玛拉和杰克大声欢呼。
罗西从普雷斯托的手上把魔杖抢了下来。
普雷斯托还没有反应过来。“你是怎么......？” 
Terrell, Mara, and Jack cheered.
Roxy ripped the wand from Mr. Presto's hand.
Mr. Presto was confused. "How did you—?"
“你再也不能表演魔术了，普雷斯托！” 罗西说。她用双手举起魔杖，把它掰成了两段。咔嚓！
“不要！” 普雷斯托叫道。
"There will be no more magic for you, Mr. Presto!" said Roxy. She held the wand up with both hands. And she snapped it in half. Crack!
"No!" cried Mr. Presto.
史密斯侦探松了一口气。
“太好了！” 扮演大力士的演员叫道。
“耶！” 玛拉叫道。
玛拉，杰克和特勒尔高兴地跳了起来。
Detective Smith breathed a sigh of relief.
"Hurray!" shouted the Mighty Man actor.
"Yay!" shouted Mara.
Mara, Jack, and Terrell happily jumped up and down.
“这真是有史以来最棒的节目了！” 特勒尔说。
“是的。” 杰克说，“我喜欢大力士，不过火箭女孩儿才是真正的超级英雄！” 
"That was the best show ever!" said Terrell.
"Yeah," said Jack. "I like Mighty Man, but Rocket Girl is the real superhero!"
几分钟之后，罗西走了进来。
“朋友们好！” 她说，“我回来了！” 
特勒尔看了看电视，又看了看罗西。他怀疑地看着罗西。
罗西只是微微一笑。“嗯……我错过了什么吗？” 
Several minutes later Roxy walked in.
"Hey, guys!" she said. "I'm back!"
Terrell looked at the TV and then at Roxy. He gave her a suspicious look.
Roxy just smiled. "So . . . did I miss anything?"
美罗城美术馆里挤满了人。大家都为能看到新画感到非常兴奋。
“这些画真美。” 一个女人说。
The Metro City Art Gallery was very crowded. People were excited to see the new paintings.
"These paintings are beautiful," said a woman.
她的丈夫点了点头。“是的，它们非常……啊！发生什么事了？” 
浓雾渐渐弥漫了整个房间。
Her husband nodded. "Yes, they are very—Hey! What's going on here?"
Thick fog slowly filled the room.
“我什么都看不到了！” 一个声音喊道。
浓雾消散时，一个女人吓了一跳。“天啊！那些画不见了！” 
"I can't see anything!" shouted a voice.
When the fog cleared, a woman gasped. "Oh no! The paintings are gone!"
“快看我！” 杰克喊道。他以最快的速度跑过特勒尔家的后院。他猛地一跳——扑通！——落在了一堆叶子上。叶子飞得到处都是。
“哈哈！” 罗西大笑。
"Watch this!" shouted Jack. He ran across Terrell's backyard as fast as he could. He jumped—ka-boosh!—and landed in the big pile of leaves. They flew everywhere.
"Ha-ha!" Roxy laughed.
“轮到我了！” 玛拉说。
大家都拿起耙子。他们开始用耙子重新把树叶堆成一堆。
"It's my turn!" said Mara.
Everyone grabbed a rake. They all started raking leaves back into a huge pile.
很快轮到玛拉跳了。她走到后院的尽头，然后跑向树叶堆并往上一跳。
“哇喔！” 玛拉喊道。
Soon it was ready for Mara to jump in. She walked to the other end of the backyard. Then she ran toward the leaves and jumped!
"Woo-hoo!" yelled Mara.
“太有意思了。” 特勒尔拿起耙子说。
“是啊。” 罗西说。“秋天是我最喜欢的季节。我喜欢凉爽的天气。我喜欢在树叶堆里玩儿。” 
"This is so much fun," said Terrell as he picked up his rake.
"Yeah," said Roxy. "Fall is my favorite season. I love the cool air. And I love playing in the leaves."
“我最喜欢的季节是冬天。” 特勒尔说，“我喜欢在雪里玩儿。” 
“我期待着下雪天赶快到来。” 杰克说，“我希望现在就下雪！” 
"My favorite season is winter," said Terrell. "I love playing in the snow."
"I can't wait for it to start snowing," said Jack. "I wish it would snow now!"
“现在天气还太暖和。” 罗西说，“我觉得最近几个月都不会下雪。” 
“你说得对。” 杰克叹了一口气。
"It's still too warm for snow," said Roxy. "I don't think it will snow in a few more months."
"You're probably right," said Jack with a sigh.
大家又用耙子把树叶堆成了一堆。这次轮到罗西跳了。
“啊！” 罗西大喊着跳进了树叶堆里。
The friends finished raking the leaves back into a pile. Then it was Roxy's turn.
"Whee!" Roxy shouted as she jumped into the pile.
大家再次把树叶堆成一堆的时候，特勒尔想到了一个主意。
“我们应该请求火箭女孩儿去让老天下雪！” 他说。
“这个想法太可笑了。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿无法控制天气。” 
As the friends raked the leaves again, Terrell had an idea.
"We should ask Rocket Girl to make it snow!" he said.
"That's a ridiculous idea," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl has no control over the weather."
“但是她有超能力！” 特勒尔说。
没等罗西回答，她的手表响了。‘不好了。’她想。罗西看了朋友们一眼。
"But she has super powers!" said Terrell.
Before Roxy could respond, her watch beeped. "Uh-oh," she thought. She looked at her friends.
“对不起，朋友们。” 她说，“但是我想起来我告诉过妈妈中午回家吃饭。我待会儿再回来。” 
罗西一走到特勒尔家门前就马上接通了电话。
“布洛姆市长。” 她说，“发生什么事了？” 
"Sorry, guys," she said. "But I just remembered I told my mom I'd be home for lunch. I'll be back later."
As soon as Roxy was in front of Terrell's house, she answered the call.
"Mayor Bloom," she said. "What's going on?"
“我们有麻烦了，火箭女孩儿。” 布洛姆市长说，“发生了一起盗窃案。所有美罗城美术馆里的新画都被偷了！” 
“别担心，市长。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿出发了！” 
"We have a problem, Rocket Girl," said Mayor Bloom. "There's been a robbery. All the new paintings at the Metro City Art Gallery have been stolen!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl is on her way!"
刹那间罗西变身成为火箭女孩儿。
“是时候找出那个偷画的小偷了！” 罗西说着，冲向了天空。
In an instant Roxy changed into Rocket Girl.
"It's time to find that art thief!" said Roxy. She blasted up into the sky.
罗西到达美罗城美术馆后，她大笑了起来。史密斯侦探正在地上爬着。
“侦探先生。” 罗西笑着问，“这么老了还在地上玩儿？” 
When Roxy arrived at the Metro City Art Gallery, she laughed. Detective Smith was crawling around on the floor.
"Uh, Detective," Roxy asked with a grin. "Aren't you a little too old to be playing on the floor?"
史密斯侦探皱着眉头站起身来。“我没在地上玩儿。” 他说，“我在找这个。” 
史密斯侦探拿起一个棒球般大小的球。球的一面有一个小的闪电图案，另一面写着 “雾” 的字样。
Detective Smith frowned as he stood up. "I wasn't playing on the floor," he said. "I was looking at this."
Detective Smith held up a ball about the size of a baseball. It had a small lightning bolt on one side. On the other side was the word "雾(fog)"
“啊哈！” 罗西说。“这是气象员的球！” 
“你说得对！” 史密斯侦探说，“他用这个气象球制造坏天气。我跟一位目击者聊过，她说盗窃案发生时美术馆布满了浓雾。” 
"Aha!" said Roxy. "That ball belongs to Weatherman!"
"You're right!" said Detective Smith. "He uses Weather Balls to create bad weather. I talked to a witness. She said the art gallery was filled with fog during the robbery."
“嗯。” 罗西说，“所以没人看见是谁偷的画。” 
“没错！” 史密斯侦探说。就在这时他的电话响了。
"Hmm," said Roxy. "So no one could see who was stealing the paintings."
"Exactly!" said Detective Smith. Just then his phone rang.
“喂？” 他说，“很好！别让他跑了！” 史密斯侦探挂了电话后，看着罗西。“警察发现气象员正驾车行驶在西街上。他们正在追赶他。” 
"Hello?" he said. "Good! Don't lose him!" Detective Smith hung up his phone and looked at Roxy. "Police found Weatherman driving down West Street. They're chasing him now."
一听这话，罗西马上飞出了美术馆。西街上，三辆警车正在追赶一辆黑色货车。货车两边印有闪电的图案。
Without saying a word, Roxy flew out of the gallery. On West Street three police cars were chasing a black van. Two lightning bolts were painted on the van's sides.
突然街道上布满了浓雾，警察看不到货车了。货车趁机转入一个小巷里。
“又是浓雾？” 罗西说，“这对于火箭女孩儿来说不是问题！” 
Suddenly a thick fog filled the street. The police lost sight of the van, and it darted down an alley.
"More fog, huh?" said Roxy. "That's not a problem for Rocket Girl!"
罗西深呼吸之后，用力吹了一口气。浓雾立刻消失了。罗西现在可以看见隔着几条街的气象员的车了。她朝着车飞去。
Roxy took a deep breath and blew as hard as she could. The fog cleared instantly. Now Roxy could see Weatherman's van a few blocks away. She flew after it.
嗞轰！罗西用眼睛发射了激光，在货车后面烧了个洞。货车马上停了，气象员跳了出来。
“你毁了我的气象货车！” 他大叫。
Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laserbeams, burning a hole in the back of the van. The van skidded to a stop, and Weatherman jumped out.
"You ruined the Weather Van!" he yelled.
“你会付出代价的，火箭女孩儿！” 
气象员从货车后面拿出一个气象球。他把它抛向空中。
“气象球，激活！” 
"You're going to pay for that, Rocket Girl!"
Weatherman grabbed a Weather Ball from the back of the van. He threw it into the air.
"Weather Ball, activate!"
整个天空变黑了，乌云飘了过来。然后——咔嚓！天空中划过一道巨大的闪电。它正向罗西逼近过来！
The whole sky grew dark. Dark clouds moved in. And then—crack! A giant lightning bolt shot down from the sky. And it was headed straight toward Roxy!
咔嚓！
闪电朝罗西击了过来，罗西迅速躲开，闪电击中了邮箱。
Crack!
Roxy dove out of the way just as the lightning bolt struck a mailbox.
“咻！” 罗西深呼了一口气，“差一点就——” 
咔嚓！又一道闪电击了过来。罗西再次躲开了。
"Whew!" Roxy took a deep breath. "That was so close—"
Crack! Another bolt of lightning struck. Roxy jumped out of the way again.
“你以为你的速度很快吗，火箭女孩儿？” 气象员喊道，“我倒想看看你能不能躲开这个！” 
气象员把另一个气象球抛向空中。
“气象球，激活！” 他喊道。
"You think you're so quick, Rocket Girl," shouted Weatherman. "I'd like to see you try to jump away from this!"
Weatherman threw another Weather Ball into the air.
"Weather Ball, activate!" he shouted.
大风刮了起来，把罗西吹倒了。天空中下起了大雨。咔嚓！轰隆！许多道闪电划过，罗西一跃而起躲开了闪电。
A strong wind blew, throwing Roxy off her feet. Rain began to pour down. Crack! Boom! More lightning struck. Roxy jumped to her feet, dodging bolts of lightning.
“听着，气象员。” 罗西喊道，“你那愚蠢的雷雨无法阻挡我！” 
“也许吧。” 气象员得意地笑了，“但是我有可以阻挡你的东西。” 
"Listen, Weatherman," shouted Roxy. "Your dumb little thunderstorm isn't going to stop me!"
"Maybe not," said Weatherman with a smirk. "But I have something that will."
他把另一个气象球抛向空中。“气象球，激活！” 
罗西感觉到天气的变化。随着一阵轰隆隆的声音，大风刮得更猛烈了。
He threw another Weather Ball into the air. "Weather Ball, activate!"
Roxy felt a change in the air. There was a rumbling sound, and the wind grew stronger.
‘啊，发生什么事了？’罗西心想。
然后她转头看见一个巨大的龙卷风正在向西街席卷而来。
"Uh-oh. What's happening now?" Roxy wondered.
And then she saw it—a huge tornado was whipping down West Street.
“哇！” 罗西大叫着被狂风卷起。她在风里转来转去。
“我有点头晕了！” 她大叫。
"Whoa!" Roxy screamed as she was swept upward. She spun around and around.
"I'm getting dizzy!" she yelled.
罗西听到了一个声音。
“救命！” 一个女人大喊。
“火箭女孩儿！救我！” 一个男人大喊。
Roxy heard voices.
"Help!" a woman shouted.
"Rocket Girl! Save me!" shouted a man.
龙卷风把一辆公交车，一辆出租车和罗西一起卷上了天空。所有的乘客都很害怕。
‘不好了！’罗西心想。‘我必须救这些人！’
The tornado had picked up a bus and a taxi along with Roxy. All the passengers were terrified.
"Oh no!" Roxy thought. "I have to save those people!"
罗西用尽全力在龙卷风里飞行。她用一只手抓住了出租车。
“呃！” 她大喊着飞向公交车。
Roxy used all her strength to fly around the tornado. She grabbed the taxi with one hand.
"Grr!" Roxy grunted as she flew toward the bus.
“抓到了！” 她紧紧抓住了公交车。她双手都抓着车，飞出了龙卷风，想找一个安全的地方把车放下。
"Got it!" she shouted, grabbing hold of the bus.
With her hands full, Roxy flew away from the tornado. She looked for a safe place to put the vehicles.
龙卷风平息了，警察来到了小巷。
“气象员在这儿！” 一名警察喊道。
“我需要暴风雪！” 气象员大喊，并把另一个气象球抛向空中。
As the tornado died down, the police came around the corner.
"There's Weatherman!" shouted one police officer.
"I need a blizzard!" Weatherman cried, throwing another Weather Ball into the air.
天气突然变冷了。天空飘起了雪花。街道上也刮起了强风。雪越下越大，很快路面都被雪覆盖住了。警车在厚厚的积雪上滑行着。车子从车道滑到了人行道。
The air grew colder. A few snowflakes began to fall down. Then a strong wind whipped along the street. The snow fell faster, and soon the street was covered with snow. The police cars skidded through the deep snow. They slid off the street and onto the sidewalk.
气象员回到他的货车里并按下一个键。货车收起了普通车轮，换成了雪地履带式车轮。
“哈哈！” 气象员大笑着离开了。
Weatherman got back into his van and pressed a button. The van's wheels folded in and were replaced with snow treads.
"Ha-ha!" Weatherman cackled and drove away.
罗西飞过天空，手里抓着沉重的车辆。
“哇！” 地上的一个人大叫，“火箭女孩儿的手拿着一辆公交车！” 
“还有一辆出租车！” 另一个人说。
Roxy flew through the air, carrying the heavy vehicles.
"Wow!" yelled someone on the ground. "Rocket Girl is holding a bus!"
"And a taxi too!" said someone else.
罗西找到了一个安全而寂静的街道。她把车放了下来。
“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿！” 公交车上的一个女人说。
“你是我的英雄，火箭女孩儿！” 出租车司机说。
“我很乐意为大家服务！” 罗西说。
Roxy found a safe, quiet street. She put down the vehicles.
"Thank you, Rocket Girl!" said a woman on the bus.
"You're my hero, Rocket Girl!" said the taxi driver.
"Serving you is my pleasure!" said Roxy.
罗西重新飞向天空，又回到了西街。那里依然大雪纷飞。风刮得很大，雪积得越来越厚。
Roxy blasted off and headed back to West Street. Snow was still swirling everywhere. The wind was blowing strong, and deep snowdrifts were forming.
‘我从来没见过这么大的暴风雪！’罗西心想。她看到两辆警车几乎都要被埋在雪里了。警察们正试图把车挖出来。
"I've never seen a blizzard this bad!" thought Roxy. She saw two police cars half buried under the snow. Some police officers were trying to dig them out.
“气象员朝哪个方向走了？” 罗西问那些警察。
“他往那边去了，朝那个山的方向。” 一个警察喊道。
罗西跟随着货车的轮胎印追了过去。
"Which way did Weatherman go?" Roxy called to the police officers.
"He went that way, toward the mountains," yelled one officer.
Roxy zoomed after the villain, following the van's tracks in the snow.
寒风呼啸。雪花飘来飘去，几乎把货车的车轮轨迹都覆盖住了。罗西使用了她的超级视觉。隔着密集的雪花，她看到远处有一束微弱的灯光。
The wind was howling. Snow blew everywhere, covering the van's tracks. Roxy used her super vision. Far ahead she could see faint lights through the thick falling snow.
“他在那儿！” 她说，“现在是时候阻止这个坏蛋了！” 
罗西很快就追赶上了货车。她深深地吸了一口气。然后……
"There he is!" she said. "Now it's time to put a stop to this villain!"
Roxy soon caught up to the van. She took a deep, deep breath. Then . . .
呼——！罗西使尽全力吐出一口气。她吹起了一阵强风。气象员的货车前形成了一个巨大的雪堆。哐！货车撞进了雪堆里。
Whoo-ooo-oosh! Roxy blew as hard as she could. She let out a powerful gust of wind. A huge snowdrift formed in front of Weatherman's van. Boomph! The van slammed into the snowdrift.
“我要报仇，火箭女孩儿！” 气象员大喊。他从货车里跳出来，手里拿着一个气象球。就在他要扔球的时候——嗞轰！罗西用眼里发射出的激光把球炸成了碎片。
"I'll get you for that, Rocket Girl!" shouted Weatherman. He jumped out of the van and held up a Weather Ball. He was just about to throw it when—whiz-hoo! Roxy blasted the ball to pieces with her eye laserbeams.
“你今天再也不能制造坏天气了！” 罗西说，“你会坐牢的，气象员！” 
“啊！” 气象员说。
"You won't be creating any more bad weather today!" said Roxy. "You're going to jail, Weatherman!"
"Agh!" said Weatherman.
“太有意思了！” 杰克说，“我不敢相信真的下雪了！” 
杰克，玛拉和特勒尔正在特勒尔家的后院堆雪人。
"This is so much fun!" said Jack. "I can't believe it snowed!"
Jack, Mara, and Terrell were making a snowman in Terrell's backyard.
“我想知道罗西什么时候回来。” 特勒尔说，“她已经离开很久了。” 
“是啊。” 玛拉说，“她错过了所有有趣的事情！” 
“我回来了！” 罗西叫着跑到院子里。
"I wonder when Roxy will be back," said Terrell. "She's been gone a long time."
"Yeah," said Mara. "She's missing all the fun!"
"I am back!" called Roxy as she ran into the yard.
“竟然下雪了。” 
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着罗西。“我不知道火箭女孩儿是不是跟这件事情有关系。” 他说。
“谁知道呢？” 罗西笑着说。
"I'm so surprised that it snowed."
Terrell looked at Roxy suspiciously. "I wonder if Rocket Girl had something to do with it," he said.
"Who knows?" said Roxy with a smile.
某一个深夜，在美罗城公园里的湖里，青蛙呱呱叫着。
突然一个发光体从天上掉下来，扑通一声掉进湖里。湖面上冒起很多泡泡，湖水变成了紫色。
呱呱！呱呱！
It was late at night in Metro City Park. In the lake the frogs croaked softly.
Suddenly a bright object fell from the sky. It splashed into the lake. The water bubbled up and turned purple.
Ribbit! Ribbit!
第二天，罗西和朋友们在美罗城公园的小树林里玩儿。
“你们瞧！” 特勒尔站在大石头上喊道，“我比你们都高！” 
The next day Roxy and her friends were in the woods in Metro City Park.
"Look at me!" called Terrell from the top of a giant boulder. "I'm taller than everyone!"
“我也要上去！” 玛拉说。
“我也要！” 罗西说。
两个女孩儿开始往上爬。
"I'm coming up there!" said Mara.
"Me too!" said Roxy.
The two girls started climbing up.
“我不要！” 杰克说，“我不喜欢高的地方。” 
“你是害怕高的地方吗？” 玛拉问道。
“我不是害怕。” 杰克说，“我只是不喜欢待在高的地方。” 
"Not me," said Jack. "I don't like high places."
"You're scared of high places?" asked Mara.
"I'm not scared," said Jack. "I just don't like being high up."
特勒尔耸耸肩。“那也没什么。” 他说，“我就不喜欢黑的地方。” 
“我害怕怪物。” 玛拉说，“尤其是有尖牙的怪物。” 
Terrell shrugged. "That's okay," he said. "I don't like the dark."
"I'm scared of monsters," said Mara. "Especially ones with fangs!"
“没什么好怕的” 。特勒尔说，
“火箭女孩儿会保护我们的。” 他看着罗西问：“罗西，你害怕什么呢？” 
这时，玛拉大喊道：“你们看！树叶下面有一只青蛙！” 
"That's not a problem," said Terrell. "Rocket Girl can protect us from monsters." He looked at Roxy. "What are you afraid of, Roxy?"
Just then Mara called out. "Oh look! I see a frog under those leaves!"
玛拉从石头上跳下来，捡起小青蛙。特勒尔和杰克走过来。
“呃！呃！” 罗西叫道。
“你怎么了？” 玛拉问。
Mara jumped down and picked up the small frog. Terrell and Jack walked over.
"Eww! Eww!" said Roxy.
"What's wrong?" asked Mara.
“别让那只青蛙靠近我。” 罗西说，“好恶心！” 
“你是害怕青蛙吧？” 杰克说。
“我不是害怕。” 罗西说，“我只是觉得它们......很恶心。” 
"Keep that frog away from me," said Roxy. "Gross!"
"So you're scared of frogs?" said Jack.
"I'm not scared," said Roxy. "I just think they're . . . gross."
“说不定火箭女孩儿能帮你。” 特勒尔说。
“帮我？” 罗西问。
“是的。” 特勒尔说，“让你不再害怕青蛙。” 
"Maybe Rocket Girl can help you," said Terrell.
"Help me?" asked Roxy.
"Yeah," said Terrell. "Help you not to be scared of frogs."
罗西皱着眉头说：“我说了我不是——” 
呱呱！呱呱！
“那是什么声音？” 杰克边问，边看四周。
Roxy frowned. "I just said I'm not—"
Ribbit! Ribbit!
"What was that?" asked Jack, looking around.
“听起来像是青蛙。” 特勒尔说，“不过声音太大了。” 
旁边一棵树倒了。哐！又一棵树倒了。哐！孩子们吓得大气不敢出，他们看到一只巨大的动物，正在慢慢靠近。
"It sounded like a frog," said Terrell. "But it was really loud."
Nearby a tree fell over. Crack! Another tree crashed down. Smash! The friends held their breath as a huge creature moved closer.
“那......那是一只青蛙！” 特勒尔大叫！
“一只巨型青蛙！” 玛拉说。
“比车还大！” 杰克说。
"It . . . It's a frog!" cried Terrell.
"It's a huge frog!" said Mara.
"It's bigger than a car!" said Jack.
呱呱！那只巨型青蛙跃向天空，消失不见了。
罗西的脸变得苍白。很快她的手表响了。罗西避开朋友们，按下按钮，布洛姆市长出现了。
Croak! The giant frog hopped into the air and was gone.
Roxy's face turned pale. A moment later her watch beeped. Roxy moved away from her friends. She pressed a button and Mayor Bloom's face appeared.
“让我猜猜看，市长先生。” 罗西低声说，“您是因为那只巨型青蛙来找我的吧？” 
“不只是一只，火箭女孩儿！” 市长喊道，“到处都是巨型青蛙！它们正在入侵美罗城！请你想想办法！” 
"Let me guess, Mayor," whispered Roxy. "You're calling about the giant frog."
"It's not just one, Rocket Girl!" cried the mayor. "Giant frogs are everywhere! They're invading Metro City! Please do something!"
“那只青蛙好大啊！” 特勒尔说。
“哪儿来的呢？” 玛拉问。
“我不知道。” 杰克说。
"That frog was huge!" said Terrell.
"Where did it come from?" asked Mara.
"I don't know," said Jack.
罗西没有说话。她必须变身为火箭女孩儿去市区。但是她不能让朋友们看到。
罗西想了一会儿，有了主意。
Roxy didn't say anything. She had to turn into Rocket Girl and go downtown. But she couldn't let her friends see her. Roxy thought for a moment. Then she had an idea.
“啊！” 罗西假装看到另外一只青蛙，尖叫道，“巨型青蛙来了！赶快逃跑啊。” 然后她就跑进树林不见了。
“嗯。” 特勒尔看看四周，“奇怪，我没看到任何青蛙啊。” 
"Aah!" Roxy screamed as she pretended to spot another frog. "A giant frog! Run for your lives." Then she disappeared into the woods.
"Hmm," thought Terrell, looking around. "That's odd. I don't see any other giant frogs."
罗西抵达市区后，她看见到处都是巨大的，黏糊糊的青蛙。其中有三只正向西街方向跳跃，留下了一个个湿湿的脚印。其他青蛙贴在建筑物外面，呱呱叫得十分吓人。
When Roxy landed downtown, she saw giant, slimy frogs everywhere. Three of them hopped down West Street. They left a trail of wet footprints. Other frogs clung to the sides of buildings, making horrible croaking sounds.
罗西觉得太恶心了。“呃。” 她呻吟道，“要是被巨型松鼠侵略就好了，松鼠多可爱啊。” 
“火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探大喊道，“幸亏你在这里！” 
“哦，您好！侦探先生！” 她小声咕哝着。  
Roxy felt sick. "Ugh." She groaned. "It would have been nice if giant squirrels invaded. Squirrels are so cute."
"Rocket Girl!" shouted Detective Smith. "I'm glad you're here!"
"Uh, hi, Detective," she mumbled.
史密斯侦探看起来有些惊讶。
“你还好吧？你怎么不开玩笑了？” 
一只青蛙掉在旁边的车上。哐当！
“我实在没有心情开玩笑。” 罗西无力地说。
Detective Smith looked surprised. "Are you okay? Aren't you going to make a joke?"
A frog landed on a nearby car. Skrunch!
"I'm not really in a joking mood," said Roxy weakly.
另一只青蛙撞倒了一个路灯。呱呱！呱呱！
“太恐怖了。” 史密斯侦探说，“我们必须查明为什么青蛙变得这么——” 
“火箭女孩儿！救命啊！” 一个声音喊道。
Another frog knocked over a streetlamp. Ribbit! Ribbit!
"This is terrible," said Detective Smith. "We need to find out how these frogs got so—"
"Rocket Girl! Save me!" a voice screamed.
罗西抬头一看，一只青蛙爬到大楼中部，嘴里叼着一辆车。司机仍困在车里。
“不好！” 罗西大叫！
对罗西来说，害怕青蛙已经不重要了。
Roxy looked up. Halfway up a building was a frog with a car in its mouth. The driver was still inside.
"Oh no!" cried Roxy.
It didn't matter that Roxy was scared of frogs.
她是火箭女孩儿，美罗城需要她的帮助！她以最快的速度飞过去。
呱呱！一只青蛙跳到罗西面前。她躲过去了。
“到处都是青蛙！” 罗西说。
She was Rocket Girl, and Metro City needed her help! She flew as fast as she could.
Ribbit! A frog leaped in front of Roxy. She swooped over it.
"These frogs are everywhere!" said Roxy.
在街道的另一头，有人尖叫：“小心！” 
一只肥大的青蛙撞到了高大的熊雕像，差点砸到人群 。罗西飞过去接住了它。罗西把雕像重新摆回台座。
Down on the street, someone screamed. "Look out!"
A fat frog had knocked over the big bear statue. The statue was about to fall on a group of people. Roxy flew down and caught it. She placed the statue back on its platform.
罗西向叼着车的青蛙冲过去。青蛙看到罗西向她伸出了舌头。呱呱！车从青蛙嘴里掉了下来。
“啊！” 罗西大叫。
她迅速飞过去。嗖! 罗西在车子撞到地面之前接住了它。
Roxy shot toward the frog with the car. When the frog saw Roxy, it flicked its tongue at her. Rabbit! The car fell out of the frog's mouth.
"Whoa!" cried Roxy.
Roxy dived fast. Zoom! She caught the car just before it hit the street.
“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿！” 司机说。
“不客气。” 罗西说，“我很高兴能——” 
啪！
“啊！” 罗西尖叫。
"Thank you, Rocket Girl!" said the driver.
"No problem," said Roxy. "I'm glad I could—"
Thwap!
"Agh!" Roxy screamed.
“呃！青蛙的舌头！” 罗西尖叫道。
罗西在青蛙闭上嘴巴之前摆脱了它的舌头。啪嗒！
“呃！呃！呃！” 罗西叫喊着跳回街道上。“这太恶心了！我不能——” 
"Eww! Frog tongue!" Roxy cried.
Roxy pulled herself from the tongue just as the frog's mouth closed. Snap!
"Eww! Eww! Eww!" cried Roxy, jumping back down to the street. "This is so gross! I don't think I can—"
另外一只青蛙向罗西伸出了舌头。
 啪！
“啊！” 她大叫，跳到另一边躲开。
 啪！
“啊！” 罗西大声喊叫，看了看四周，到处都是巨型青蛙。
Another frog tongue flicked toward Roxy. Thwap!
"Whoa!" she cried, jumping out of the way.
Thwap!
"Aah!" Roxy yelled, looking around. Giant frogs crept everywhere.
“怎样才能除掉这些青蛙呢？” 罗西心想，“如果它们是别的东西，比如松鼠、花栗鼠、乌龟，那就没问题，我会直接把它们抓起来。可是我不想碰青蛙！” 
"How am I going to get rid of all these frogs?" Roxy wondered. "If they were anything else—squirrels, chipmunks, turtles—no problem. I would just pick them up. But I do not want to touch any frogs!"
呱呱！呱呱！
一只肥胖的，带斑点的大青蛙瞪着罗西看, 罗西向后退了一步。
但是她发现背后也有一只青蛙。
Ribbit! Ribbit!
A fat green frog with brown spots stared at Roxy. Roxy took a step back. But then she realized another frog was behind her.
她向右侧的巷子看去，一只青蛙夹在两栋楼之间。她向左看去，另一只青蛙在呱呱叫。
罗西被包围了。到处都是青蛙,到处都是青蛙鼓出来的眼睛。它们全都盯着她看。
She looked in the alley to her right. A frog was squeezed between the two buildings. To Roxy's left, another frog croaked.
Roxy was surrounded. Everywhere she looked, she saw the bulging eyes of frogs. They all stared at her.
“啊！” 罗西说,"这是我接到的最恶心的任务。"
史密斯侦探叫住了罗西。“火箭女孩儿！你还好吗？” 
“我当然不好了！” 罗西喊道，“我快变成青蛙的食物了！” 
"Ugh!" said Roxy. "This is the grossest mission I've ever been on!"
Detective Smith called to her. "Rocket Girl! Are you okay?"
"Of course I'm not okay!" yelled Roxy. "I'm about to be frog food!"
几只青蛙的舌头突然同时伸出来。啪！
罗西向上飞起，及时躲开了，下面的四只青蛙黏在了一起。
All at once the frogs' sticky tongues shot out. Thwap!
Roxy blasted straight up, getting out of the way just in time. Below her the four frogs were stuck together.
“哈哈！” 罗西大笑。
 呱呱! 一只黏糊糊的青蛙跳起来，跟在罗西后面。罗西赶紧飞起来。那只黏糊糊的青蛙在楼顶追赶罗西。罗西飞到哪里，它就跳到哪里。
"Ha-ha!" Roxy laughed.
Croak! A very slimy frog jumped into the air after Roxy. Roxy flew fast. The slimy frog hopped along the tops of buildings. Wherever Roxy flew, the frog hopped.
罗西在空中作“之” 形飞行，青蛙紧跟着。
不一会儿，罗西飞到了美罗城公园的湖的上空。
“湖水怎么回事？” 罗西很怀疑，“怎么变成紫色了！” 
Roxy zigzagged through the air with the frog right behind her.
Soon Roxy flew over the lake in Metro City Park.
"What happened to the lake?" Roxy wondered. "The water is purple!"
就在这时，另外一只青蛙从树后面跳出来，把罗西撞落进了湖里。
罗西在水下看到了一个奇怪的东西。一块神秘的石头躺在湖底，发着紫色的光。
Just then another frog leaped from behind a tree. It smashed into Roxy and sent her crashing down into the lake.
While Roxy was underwater, she saw something odd. A mysterious rock sat on the lake floor. The rock glowed bright purple.
“这块石头看起来像是陨石。” 罗西想。她正要研究这块石头的时候，她开始不太舒服。
“发生什么事了？” 罗西觉得奇怪，开始感到头晕。她觉得自己好像在飞速移动，但实际上她并没有动。
“哇！” 罗西想，“我好像在变大！” 
"That looks like a meteor," thought Roxy. As she studied the meteor, she began to feel strange.
"What's going on?" Roxy wondered, becoming dizzy. She felt as if she was moving really fast. But she wasn't moving at all.
"Uh-oh!" thought Roxy. "I think I'm growing!"
湖面开始冒泡，湖水翻滚着，
波浪拍打着湖岸。一个巨人冒出水面。
“哇！” 罗西向下看去， “我变大了！” 
The lake began to bubble and churn. Waves splashed onto the shore. A giant figure rose out of the water.
"Whoa!" said Roxy, looking down. "I'm huge!"
罗西小心走在市区的大楼之间。
“小心点。” 她告诉自己，“你不想踩到任何人。” 
Downtown, Roxy slowly walked between the buildings.
"Be careful," she told herself. "You don't want to step on anybody!"
罗西看到一只青蛙黏在美罗城银行的大楼上。那只青蛙黏糊恶心。但是现在罗西比它大多了。
罗西深深吸了一口气。“好吧，我可以的。我能拿青蛙。” 
Roxy saw a frog clinging to Metro City Bank. The frog was slimy and gross. But now Roxy was much bigger than it.
Roxy took a deep breath. "Okay. I can do this. I can pick up a frog."
她闭着眼睛向青蛙伸出手去。罗西感觉它黏黏的。“呃!” 她喊道，手赶紧缩回来。
罗西重新伸出手去，这次她小心地从大楼上捡起那个黏糊糊的东西。
She closed her eyes and reached for the frog. Roxy felt it squish. "Eww!" she cried, quickly pulling her hand back.
Roxy reached out again. This time she gently picked the slimy creature off the building.
罗西手里拿着青蛙，飞回公园。
她把青蛙扔进紫色的湖水里。
扑通！
“也不是很难。” 罗西心想。
Holding the frog in her hand, Roxy zoomed back to the park. She dropped the frog into the purple lake.
Splash!
"That wasn't so bad," thought Roxy.
罗西飞回美罗城。她一只接一只找出了所有的青蛙，并把它们都丢进湖里。
“咻！” 罗西说，“真高兴都干完了。不过这些青蛙还是太大了，我也是。到底是什么东西把我们变大的？”  
Roxy flew back to downtown Metro City. One by one, she found all the frogs. She put all of them in the lake.
"Whew!" said Roxy. "I'm glad that's done. But the frogs are still too big. And so am I. What made us grow in the first place?"
罗西想了想，低头看向紫色的湖。
“啊！” 她说，“是那块陨石。” 
罗西走进湖里，用双手在水下东摸西摸。很快就找到了陨石。罗西把它从水里拿出来以后，湖水马上退去了紫色。
Roxy thought for a moment. She looked down at the purple lake. "Aha!" she said. "The meteor!"
Roxy stepped into the lake and fished around under the water. A moment later she felt the meteor. Roxy pulled it out of the lake. Right away the water lost its purple color.
罗西把陨石抛向天空，那块紫色的石头划过天空，在远离地球的太空消失了。
罗西又开始觉得怪怪的。
“我在缩小！” 罗西想，“青蛙也在缩小。” 
Roxy flung the meteor into the sky. The purple rock disappeared as it soared through space, far from Earth. Roxy started to feel strange again.
"I'm shrinking!" Roxy thought. "And so are the frogs!"
罗西的朋友们从树林里走出来。他们站在湖边。
“我很想知道罗西去哪儿了。” 特勒尔说。
Roxy's friends were coming out of the woods. They stood near the lake.
"I wonder where Roxy went," said Terrell.
“她可能回家了吧。” 杰克说，“她真的很害怕巨型青蛙。” 
玛拉看到一只青蛙跳出水面，她伸出手。“看！” 她说，“这里还有一只青蛙，一只正常大小的青蛙。” 
"Maybe she went home," said Jack. "She was really scared of the giant frog."
Mara saw a frog hop out of the lake. She reached down. "Look!" she said. "Here's another frog—a normal-sized one."
就在这时，罗西出现了。
“大家好！” 她说，“我回来了。巨型青蛙很吓人，对吧？” 
她看着玛拉。“哇！我能抓一下那只青蛙吗？” 
Just then Roxy appeared.
"Hi everyone," she said. "I'm back. That giant frog sure was scary, right?"
She looked at Mara. "Ooh! Can I hold that frog?"
“我以为你害怕青蛙呢。” 玛拉说。她把青蛙递给罗西。
“现在不怕了。” 罗西说。
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着罗西，但是他什么也没说。
"I thought you were scared of frogs," said Mara. She handed the frog to Roxy.
"Not anymore," said Roxy.
Terrell gave Roxy a suspicious look. But he didn't say anything.
周六早上，美罗城阳光灿烂。史密斯侦探正在上班的路上。当他快要到达警察总局的时候，看到一道黑影遮住了整个广场。
It was a bright Saturday morning in downtown Metro City. Detective Smith was on his way to work. He had almost reached Police Headquarters when a dark shadow spilled over the plaza.
 史密斯侦探抬头一看。“那是什么？” 他叫道。
  一个高大的银色机器人向天空喷了一道奇怪的雾气。雾气形成了一个蓝色泡泡，把警察总局包围了起来。
Detective Smith looked up. "What is that?" he cried.
A tall, silver robot sprayed a strange blue mist into the air. A blue bubble formed and slowly began to surround Police Headquarters.
“车来了！” 玛拉向朋友们叫道。车开进了停车场。玛拉向司机挥手，指向一个牌子，上面写着“洗车” 。
"Here comes a car!" Mara called to her friends. The car pulled into the parking lot. She waved to the car's driver. Then she pointed to a sign. The sign said "Car Wash."
“你好。” 司机问，“洗车多少钱？” 
“十美元。” 玛拉说，“我们足球队正在筹钱买新队服。” 
"Hi," said the driver. "How much for a car wash?"
"Ten dollars," said Mara. "Our soccer team is raising money for new uniforms."
特勒尔和杰克提着一桶肥皂水跑来。罗西拿来了一些海绵。大家开始擦车。
“我们今天才洗了第三辆车。” 特勒尔皱着眉头说。
Terrell and Jack ran over with a bucket of soapy water. Roxy carried some big sponges. Everyone started scrubbing the car.
"This is only the third car we've washed today," said Terrell, frowning.
“我知道。” 杰克说，“我希望能来更多的车。要不然我们买队服的钱不够。” 
“我们的旧队服太丑了。” 玛拉说。
"I know," said Jack. "I hope more cars come. Otherwise we won't make enough money for new uniforms."
"And our old ones are so ugly," said Mara.
罗西把海绵泡进水里，在车盖上涂上泡沫。很快车盖就在阳光下闪闪发光。
特勒尔似乎在思考什么。
“也许火箭女孩儿能帮我们弄到新队服。” 他说。
Roxy plunked her sponge into the water. She spread bubbles on the hood of the car. Soon the hood sparkled in the sunlight.
Terrell looked thoughtful.
"Maybe Rocket Girl can help us get new uniforms," he said.
“我们应该问问她。” 杰克说。
“这太可笑了。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿不能帮我们弄到新队服。” 
"We should ask her!" said Jack.
"That's ridiculous," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl can't help us get new soccer uniforms."
“为什么不能？” 特勒尔问。
“因为......” 罗西想了想说，“火箭女孩儿不会做衣服，再说她还有更重要的事情去做。” 
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。
"Why not?" asked Terrell.
"Because," said Roxy, thinking. "She doesn't know how to sew. Besides, Rocket Girl has more important things to do."
Just then Roxy's watch beeped.
“我马上就回来。” 罗西对朋友们说。她走到停车场的另一边，按下手表上的按钮。
“什么事？布洛姆市长？” 她问。
"I'll be back in a second," she told her friends. Roxy walked to the other side of the parking lot. She pressed a button on her watch.
"What's up, Mayor Bloom?" she asked.
布洛姆市长看起来很着急。“我们有大麻烦了，火箭女孩儿。” 他说，“我觉得有人偷走了警察总局。” 
“什么？” 罗西问。她以为自己听错了。
Mayor Bloom looked worried. "We have a big problem, Rocket Girl," he said. "I think somebody stole Police Headquarters."
"What?" asked Roxy. She thought she had heard the mayor wrong.
“您认为有人从警察总局偷走了东西？” 
“不是！” 布洛姆市长大叫，“是有人偷走了警察总局！整栋大楼不见了。等一下......那......那是机器人吗？噢，不！火箭女孩儿，我......” 
"You think somebody stole something from Police Headquarters?"
"No!" cried Mayor Bloom. "I think somebody stole Police Headquarters! The whole building is gone! Wait a minute . . . Is . . . is that a robot? Oh no! Rocket Girl, I—"
罗西的手表关闭了，画面也随着消失。
“布洛姆市长？” 罗西说，“布洛姆市长，您还在吗？” 
没有回答。
“不好了！” 罗西咽了咽口水。 
The screen faded as Roxy's watch clicked off.
"Mayor Bloom?" Roxy said. "Mayor Bloom, are you there?"
There was no answer.
"Oh no!" Roxy gulped.
布洛姆市长遇到麻烦了。
“嗨，” 罗西对朋友们说，“我要......嗯......在周边放更多的洗车牌子。我们需要更多的客人！” 
Mayor Bloom was in trouble.
"Hey, guys," Roxy called to her friends. "I'm going to . . . um . . . put more Car Wash signs up around town. We need more customers!"
罗西向街道上跑去。
“奇怪。” 特勒尔看着罗西离开时想。“她没带牌子。” 
Roxy ran down the street.
"That's strange," thought Terrell, watching her go. "Roxy isn't carrying any signs."
罗西来到警察总局所在的广场。警察总局只剩下一大块空地。
“火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探在地面上挥着手叫。
罗西飞了下来。
Roxy flew over to Police Headquarters Plaza. There was a big empty spot where the police station had been.
"Rocket Girl!" called Detective Smith, waving from the ground.
Roxy flew down.
“布洛姆市长遇到麻烦了。” 她说。
“天啊！” 史密斯侦探说，“警察总局也不见了！” 他开始在口袋里翻找。
"Mayor Bloom is in trouble," she said.
"Oh no!" said Detective Smith. "And Police Headquarters is gone!" He started searching his pockets.
罗西笑了。“我想警察总局不会在您的口袋里吧，侦探先生。” 
“好笑吧。” 史密斯侦探皱着眉头，“我在找我的手机。啊，找到了。看看我拍的照片。” 
Roxy smiled. "I don't think Police Headquarters is in your pocket, Detective."
"Very funny," said Detective Smith with a frown. "I'm looking for my cell phone. Ah, here it is. Look at this picture I took."
史密斯侦探把手机递给罗西。她看到照片里有一个高大的银色机器人。
"当时我正在向警察总局走去。"史密斯侦探说，
Detective Smith handed the phone to Roxy. She saw a picture of a tall, silver robot.
"I was walking to Police Headquarters," said Detective Smith.
“那个机器人突然就出现了。他喷出一个蓝色泡泡，遮住了警察总局，然后整个大楼就随着泡泡一起飞走了！” 
“哇！” 罗西说，“看起来像是怪人博士干的。” 
"Suddenly that robot appeared. It sprayed a blue bubble around Police Headquarters. Then the bubble floated away with the whole building in it!"
"Whoa," said Roxy. "This looks like the work of Dr. Odd."
“你说得对。” 侦探说，“能够发明这种机器人的坏人，只有怪人博士这样聪明的人了。可是，他为什么要带走警察总局和布洛姆市长呢？” 
"You're right," said the detective. "Dr. Odd is the only villain smart enough to invent a robot like this one. But why did he take Police Headquarters and Mayor Bloom?"
“我知道为什么。” 罗西说，“怪人博士想偷别的东西。比如说银行，整个城市就没有人能阻止他。” 
一道阴影飘过街道。罗西抬头看去。她的头顶上飘着很多蓝色泡泡。
"I know why," said Roxy. "If there was something Dr. Odd wanted to steal—like a bank—no one in the city would be able to stop him."
A shadow moved across the street. Roxy looked up. Floating overhead were more blue bubbles!
罗西快速飞上天空。她用超级视力向离她最近的泡泡看过去。
“那是布洛姆市长的房子！” 罗西说。
Roxy shot into the sky. Using her super vision, Roxy peered into the nearest bubble.
"That's Mayor Bloom's mansion!" said Roxy.
她拼命敲打蓝色泡泡。砰！ 罗西被反弹回来，掉进了远处的一个街区里。
“哎呦。” 罗西叫道。然后她看到了蓝色雾气，于是马上站起来。
She struck the bubble as hard as she could. Boing! Roxy bounced and landed far away, in another neighborhood.
"Ow," said Roxy. Then she saw blue mist and jumped to her feet.
一辆车从拐角开过来。突然，噗通！车被泡泡吸进去飞走了。更多的泡泡出现了。噗通！噗通！它们把汽车、公交车、人，还有别的东西都带走了。
A car skidded around the corner and then bloop! It was caught in a bubble and floated away. More bubbles formed. Bloop! Bloop!
They carried away cars, buses, people, and all sorts of other things.
“啊。” 罗西心想，“我敢肯定怪人博士的机器人是......” 
哐当！轰隆！
罗西向上看去。机器人跺着脚从罗西身边经过。它把一辆车踩碎了。
"Uh-oh," thought Roxy. "I bet Dr. Odd's robot is—"
Crash! Boom!
Roxy looked up. The robot stomped past her. It stepped on a car and crushed it.
罗西迅速飞向机器人。但是，还没等她靠近，机器人突然转身。
噗通！
罗西被泡泡困住了。
Roxy shot toward the robot. But before she could reach it, the robot spun around.
Bloop!
Roxy was trapped in a bubble!
“啊！” 罗西大喊，“我被困在泡泡里了！” 
泡泡漂浮在高空中。罗西往下看去，发现机器人踩在一辆公交车上，正在往美罗城银行走去！
"Aah!" shouted Roxy. "I'm trapped in a bubble!"
The bubble drifted high in the sky. Looking down, Roxy could see the robot stomping on a bus. The robot was on its way to Metro City Bank!
“不好！” 罗西心想，“在它偷美罗城银行之前必须阻止它!” 罗西使劲儿去敲打泡泡。
砰！砰！砰！
罗西在泡泡里面蹦来蹦去。她继续敲打泡泡。
砰！砰！砰！
"Oh no!" thought Roxy. "I have to stop that robot before it steals Metro City Bank!" She hit the bubble's wall as hard as she could.
Boing! Boing! Boing!
Roxy bounced around inside the bubble for a few moments. She hit the bubble again.
Boing! Boing! Boing!
嗞! 罗西眼睛发射出激光。
砰！砰！砰！
“啊！” 罗西沮丧地喊道。她在泡泡里跳着躲闪那些反弹回来的激光。
Whiz-hoo! Roxy shot lasers from her eyes.
Boing! Boing! Boing!
"Aah!" shouted Roxy in frustration. She ducked and jumped as the laser bounced around the bubble.
“咻！” 罗西喊道。“这个主意不好。也许我的热感视力能有用。”
