罗西的眼里射出桔色的激光，激光没有反弹。但是，现在泡泡里充满了浓烟！
"Whew!" cried Roxy. "That was a terrible idea. Maybe my heat vision will work."
An orange beam radiated from Roxy's eyes. The beam didn't bounce. But now the bubble was filled with smoke!
罗西停止了发射热感视力。她看着烧过的地方，一点事儿都没有。
她现在高高地漂浮在美罗城上空。她看到机器人正站在美罗城银行前面。
Roxy stopped her heat vision. She looked at the spot she had tried to burn. There was no damage at all.
By now she was far above Metro City. She saw the robot standing in front of Metro City Bank.
罗西想都没想，迅速向机器人飞去。泡泡也跟着飞过去了。
“太棒了！” 
罗西飞到机器人面前。
Without thinking, Roxy shot toward the robot. And the bubble went with her.
"This is perfect!"
She flew in front of the robot.
她用她的透视眼向机器人看去。一个矮小的男人坐在机器人的脑袋里。那个男人秃头，带着深色的护目镜，身穿蓝色太空服。  
Using her x-ray vision, she looked into the robot. A small man sat inside its head. The man had a bald head and dark goggles. He wore a blue space suit.
“怪人博士！” 罗西喊道，“这次你跑不掉了。” 
大坏蛋听到她说话很惊讶。“火箭女孩儿？啊！” 
"Dr. Odd!" Roxy shouted. "You're not going to get away with this!"
The evil villain was surprised to hear her. "Rocket Girl? Aargh!"
罗西在泡泡里向机器人的脸撞去。砰！
“你无法阻止我，火箭女孩儿！” 怪人博士喊道，“你困在泡泡里如何能阻止我！” 
Roxy bounced her bubble into the robot's face. Boing!
"You can't stop me, Rocket Girl!" Dr. Odd yelled. "Not if you're trapped in that bubble! Ha-ha!"
怪人博士拉动操纵杆，机器人把泡泡击到一边。它抬起手臂对准银行。罗西又把泡泡撞向机器人。砰！
“我不会让你偷银行的！” 罗西喊道。
Dr. Odd pulled a lever. The robot knocked the bubble away. It raised its arm toward the bank. Roxy bounced the bubble off the robot again. Boing!
"I won't let you steal that bank!" Roxy yelled.
机器人挥动手臂，又把罗西的泡泡击到一边。
罗西不断把她的泡泡挡在机器人面前。她可以看到怪人博士变得越来越生气了。
The robot waved its arm, knocking Roxy's bubble away again.
Roxy kept moving her bubble in front of the robot. She could see Dr. Odd getting angry.
“让开！” 怪人博士大喊。
“不！” 罗西大声说。
“哼！” 怪人博士喊道，“这个泡泡挡在前面，我根本偷不了银行！” 
"Get out of my way!" shouted Dr. Odd.
"No!" Roxy shouted.
"Aargh!" cried Dr. Odd. "I'll never steal the bank with this bubble in my way!"
怪人博士按下一个按钮。机器人扎破了罗西的泡泡。砰！
“现在我要干掉你！” 怪人博士喊道。
机器人向罗西走去。
Dr. Odd pressed a button. The robot poked Roxy's bubble. Pop!
"Now I'll finish you!" yelled Dr. Odd.
The robot moved toward Roxy.
怪人博士指挥着机器人冲向罗西。罗西躲过了。机器人扎破了一个靠近它的泡泡。
砰！一辆车掉了出来。
“啊！” 司机大叫着落向地面。
“哈哈！” 怪人博士大笑。
Dr. Odd's robot charged toward Roxy. She dodged it. The robot popped a nearby bubble.
Pop! A car fell out.
"Aah!" the driver cried as the car fell toward the street.
"Ha-ha!" Dr. Odd laughed.
嗖！罗西迅速向车飞过去，抓住了它。
接着，砰！砰！砰！
“救命啊！火箭女孩儿！” 好几个声音一起喊道。
Zoom! Roxy shot toward the car and caught it.
Then—pop, pop, pop!
"Help! Rocket Girl!" shouted several voices.
罗西向上看去。机器人扎破了更多的泡泡。更多的车在掉落。
“现在你忙着救人，再也阻止不了我了！” 怪人博士大笑。  
Roxy looked up. The robot was popping more bubbles, and more cars were falling.
"Now you'll be too busy to stop me!" Dr. Odd laughed.
罗西快速飞去，在每辆车掉落之前，成功地抓住了它们。很快所有的车都安全落地。车身上都粘着蓝色的泡泡黏液。
Roxy flew fast, catching each car before it hit the street. Soon all the cars were safe on the ground. They were all covered with blue sticky goo from the bubbles.
与此同时，机器人抬起胳膊瞄向美罗城银行。罗西迅速飞过去，使劲儿拉住它的胳膊。机器人再次喷雾气的时候，罗西把它转向天空。
“你拦不住我的，火箭女孩儿！” 怪人博士说。
Meanwhile the robot aimed its arm at Metro City Bank. Roxy flew fast and yanked its arm. She pointed it at the sky just as it sprayed more mist.
"You won't stop me, Rocket Girl!" Dr. Odd shouted.
怪人博士继续喊叫的时候，罗西飞了下来。“我让警察总局消失了！我让布洛姆市长消失了！我还要让......啊！” 
Roxy flew down as Dr. Odd continued to yell. "I got rid of Police Headquarters! I got rid of Mayor Bloom! And now I will get rid of—Aah!"
罗西朝机器人踢去。一声巨响以后，机器人倒下了。
哐！罗西双脚重重踩在机器人上面。金属外壳被踩变形了，火花到处飞。机器人的胳膊里喷出最后一点蓝色雾气，在空中漂浮着。
With one kick Roxy knocked the robot over. It fell down with a loud crash. Skrunch! Roxy stomped the robot with both feet. The metal bent and twisted. Sparks flew everywhere. One last puff of blue mist rose from the robot's arm. The small cloud hung in the air.
罗西听到了开门的声音。怪人博士爬了出来准备逃跑。
“喂，怪人博士！” 罗西喊道，“你掉东西了！” 
Roxy heard a hatch open. Dr. Odd crawled out and started to run.
"Hey, Dr. Odd!" Roxy yelled. "You forgot something!"
罗西深吸一口气，用力吐出来。呼！呼！呼！
那一小块蓝色雾气追着怪人博士。噗通！
“啊！” 怪人博士在泡泡里大喊。
Roxy took a deep breath. She blew with all her power. Whoo-ooo-oosh!
The cloud of blue mist raced after Dr. Odd until—bloop!
"Argh!" Dr. Odd yelled from inside the bubble.
罗西拆下机器人的手臂，脸上浮出微笑。
“你在这里等着，怪人博士。” 她说，“我要去扎泡泡了。” 
Roxy ripped off the robot's hand and smiled.
"You wait here, Dr. Odd," she said. "I'm going to pop some bubbles."
杰克，特勒尔和玛拉坐在空空的停车场里。
“有客人来就好了。” 杰克说。 
“不知道罗西这么长时间都干什么去了。” 特勒尔说。
Jack, Terrell, and Mara were sitting in the empty parking lot.
"I wish we had some customers," said Jack.
"I wonder what's taking Roxy so long," said Terrell.
这时，玛拉听到了什么声音。“你们看！” 
车子排着长队开进了停车场。车身上粘满蓝色黏液。
Mara heard something. "Look!"
A long line of cars pulled into the parking lot. They were all covered in blue sticky goo.
“我们要洗车！” 一个司机说。
孩子们马上干起活来。
不一会儿，罗西回来了。
"We need our cars washed!" said one driver.
The kids got right to work.
A moment later Roxy returned.
“谢谢你放了那么多牌子，罗西！” 杰克说。
“是啊。” 特勒尔说，“对了，你从哪里弄了那么多牌子？” 
罗西没有回答。她只是挤挤海绵，动手洗起车来。
"Thanks for putting up more signs, Roxy!" said Jack.
"Yeah," said Terrell. "Where did you get the signs anyway?"
Roxy didn't answer. She just squeezed out a sponge and started washing cars.
布洛姆市长坐在市政府的办公室里。电话响了。
“是时候了！” 电话里的声音说。
“好的，老板。” 布洛姆市长说。他挂断了电话。
Mayor Bloom sat in his office at City Hall. His phone rang.
"It's time," said a voice on the phone.
"Yes, boss," said Mayor Bloom. He hung up the phone.
市长走进另外一个房间，打开保险箱，从里面拿出一大笔钱。
“布洛姆市长。” 秘书说，
The mayor went into another room and opened a safe. He pulled out a bunch of money.
"Mayor Bloom," said the mayor's assistant.
“您在干什么？这笔钱是用来修建美罗城游乐场的。” 
布洛姆市长一句话不说，把钱塞进一个公文包里走掉了。
"What are you doing? That's the money for the new playground in Metro City Park."
Mayor Bloom didn't say anything. He stuffed the money into a briefcase and ran.
“我希望新的游乐场能有一个大堡垒。” 杰克说，“有桥、梯子、滑梯和隧道！” 
罗西和朋友们正在美罗城公园里玩儿。
"I hope the new playground has a really big fort," said Jack. "With bridges, ladders, slides, and tunnels!"
Roxy and her friends were playing at Metro City Park.
他们站在满是杂草的空地上。新的游乐场将在这里建成。
“我希望游乐场里有一座塔！” 特勒尔说。
They were standing in an open area filled with weeds. It was where the new playground would be soon.
"I hope the playground has a tower!" said Terrell.
“我想要一个秋千。” 罗西说，“荡秋千让我觉得好像在飞。” 
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着她。
"I want a swing set," said Roxy. "Swinging makes me feel like I am flying."
Terrell gave her a suspicious look.
“我希望游乐场早点建好。” 玛拉说，“我等得不耐烦了。” 
“我们早应该让火箭女孩儿帮忙来建的。” 特勒尔说，“她很快就会建好的。” 
"I hope they build the playground soon," said Mara. "I'm tired of waiting for it."
"We should get Rocket Girl to build the playground," said Terrell. "She could build it really fast."
罗西转了转眼睛。“我觉得火箭女孩儿有更重要的事情去做。” 
特勒尔叹了一口气。“你说得对。” 突然，他眼睛一亮，“你们知道怎样才最酷吗？” 
Roxy rolled her eyes. "I think Rocket Girl has more important things to do."
Terrell sighed. "You're right," he said. Suddenly his eyes lit up. "You know what would be really cool?" he asked.
“怎样？” 杰克问。
“如果有两个火箭女孩儿就最好了！” 特勒尔说，“一个跟坏人斗争，另一个帮我们修建游乐场！” 
大家都笑了。
"What?" asked Jack.
"If there were two Rocket Girls!" said Terrell. "One could fight super villains, and the other could build our playground!"
Everyone laughed.
罗西摇了摇头。“特勒尔，这是我听过的最可笑的想法了。” 
特勒尔耸耸肩。"我只是说说而已。那会很酷。"
Roxy shook her head. "Terrell, that is the silliest thing I ever heard in my entire life."
Terrell shrugged. "I'm just saying . . . It would be cool."
 就在这时，罗西的手表轻轻地响了。罗西避开朋友，按下了手表上的按钮。史密斯先生的脸出现在屏幕上。
Just then Roxy's wristwatch beeped quietly. Roxy walked away from her friends. She pressed a button on her watch. Detective Smith's face appeared on the screen.
“啊-哈！” 罗西想，“史密斯侦探不知道我的真实身份！” 罗西迅速戴上她的面具。
“史密斯侦探。” 她小声问，“有什么事吗？布洛姆市长在哪里？” 
"Uh-oh!" thought Roxy. "Detective Smith doesn't know who I really am!" Roxy quickly put on her mask.
"Detective Smith," she whispered. "What's going on? Where's Mayor Bloom?"
史密斯清了清嗓子。“我们有麻烦了，火箭女孩儿。布洛姆市长好像偷走了修建美罗城游乐场的钱。” 
罗西愣住了。“不可能。” 她说，“布洛姆市长不可能干那样的事。” 
Detective Smith cleared his throat. "We have a problem, Rocket Girl. It looks like Mayor Bloom stole the money for the new playground at Metro City Park."
Roxy was shocked. "No way," she said. "Mayor Bloom would never do that."
“我知道很难让人相信。” 史密斯说，“但是他的秘书亲眼看到的。我希望你马上来市政府。” 
罗西眼咽了咽口水。“好吧，侦探先生。我马上就到。” 
"I know it's hard to believe," said Detective Smith. "But his assistant saw him do it. I need you to come down to City Hall right away."
Roxy gulped. "Okay, Detective. I'll be right there."
"我得去市政府一趟。"罗西想。
她跑向朋友们。“嗨，朋友们，我刚想起一件事。我必须......嗯......写一篇读书报告。一会儿见！” 
"I have to get to City Hall," thought Roxy.
She rushed back to her friends. "Hey, guys, I just remembered something. I have to . . . uh . . . do a book report. See you later!"
特勒尔看着罗西跑远了。“真奇怪。” 他心想，“老师没让写读书报告啊。” 
罗西到了市政府。史密斯侦探正在跟布洛姆市长的秘书谈话。
Terrell watched Roxy run away. "That's weird," he thought. "Our teacher didn't assign a book report."
Roxy arrived at City Hall. Detective Smith was talking to Mayor Bloom's assistant.
“......在那之后，” 秘书说，“布洛姆市长就从市政府走掉了。” 
“不知道他为什么要偷走那笔钱。” 史密斯侦探说。
“也许布洛姆市长想请一个新秘书。” 罗西说。
". . . and after that," the assistant was saying. "Mayor Bloom ran out of City Hall."
"I wonder why he stole the money," said Detective Smith.
"Maybe Mayor Bloom was going to buy a new assistant," said Roxy.
她盯着秘书。“我觉得你在撒谎。布洛姆市长才不是小偷。” 
秘书皱起眉头。“我没撒谎。” 她说，“这件事，我跟你一样吃惊。” 
She glared at the assistant. "I think you're lying. Mayor Bloom is not a thief."
The assistant frowned. "I am not lying," she said. "I'm as surprised as you are by this."
“嗯哼。” 史密斯侦探看着罗西说，“吵架是没有用的，火箭女孩儿。” 
罗西叹了一口气。“你说得对。你知道布洛姆市长去哪儿了吗？他留下什么线索了吗？” 
"Ahem," said Detective Smith, looking at Roxy. "Arguing won't help, Rocket Girl."
Roxy sighed. "You're right. Do you know where the mayor went? Did he leave any clues?"
“没有。” 秘书说，“但是，在把钱拿走之前，他接到了一个可疑的电话。” 
“谁打来的？” 史密斯侦探问。
"No," said the assistant. "But he got a mysterious phone call before he took the money."
"Who called him?" asked Detective Smith.
秘书查看了一下市长的电话记录。“电话是从美罗城大学的实验室打来的。” 
“好的，火箭女孩儿。” 史密斯侦探说，“我们要去......火箭女孩儿？” 
The assistant checked the mayor's phone. "The call came from the lab at Metro City University."
"Okay, Rocket Girl," said Detective Smith. "We need to go to the—Rocket Girl?"
罗西来到美罗城大学的实验室。两个巨大的实验箱立在墙边。电线和线圈把实验箱和一个大电脑连在一起。一个黑发男人坐在电脑前，戴着厚厚的眼镜。
Roxy arrived at the Metro City University lab. Two large booths stood along one wall. Wires and coils connected the booths to a big computer. A man sat in front of the computer. He had black hair and thick glasses.
“我一直在等你，火箭女孩儿。” 那个男人说，“你一定在找布洛姆市长吧。” 
“你是谁？” 罗西问。
男人微笑着。“我是迪托教授。” 
"I was expecting you, Rocket Girl," said the man. "You must be looking for Mayor Bloom."
"Who are you?" asked Roxy.
The man smiled. "I'm Professor Ditto."
罗西听到身后有脚步声。她转过身去，看到另外一个男人，长得跟迪托教授一模一样。
“我也是迪托教授。” 那个男人说。
又一个男人走进实验室。“我也是。” 
Roxy heard a footstep behind her. She spun around and saw another man. He looked just like the first one.
"I'm Professor Ditto too," said the new man.
Another man entered the lab. "And so am I."
罗西惊讶得直眨眼睛 。更多的男人出现在他身后。每一个都长得一模一样。
“他们都是迪托教授！” 罗西想。
Roxy blinked in surprise. That man was followed by more men. Every one of them looked the same.
"They're all Professor Ditto!" thought Roxy.
男人们向罗西靠近。罗西向后后退了几步。突然，他们把罗西推进一个实验箱里。
实验箱的门关上了。罗西大声喊叫。
The men moved toward Roxy. She took a few steps back. Suddenly the professors pushed her into one of the booths.
Roxy yelled as the door slammed shut.
电流嗡嗡接通了。灯光闪烁，火花四溅。接着，实验室安静了下来。罗西被拉出了实验箱。
罗西看到另外一个实验箱里，有人从里面走出来。罗西吓得倒吸一口气。另一个火箭女孩儿出现了！
Electricity hummed. Bright lights flashed. Sparks flew. Then the lab was quiet. Roxy was taken out of her booth.
She looked at the other booth. Someone stepped out of it. Roxy gasped. It was another Rocket Girl!
"放开我！"罗西喊道。
四个迪托教授拖着罗西在走廊走，罗西又踢又踹。教授们把她推进了一间黑屋。罗西听到身后传来重重的关门声。
"Let go of me!" yelled Roxy.
Four Professor Dittos dragged her down a hallway. Roxy kicked and squirmed. The professors pushed her into a dark room. Roxy heard a heavy door slam behind her.
“啊！” 罗西气得直跺脚。墙壁都晃动了。
“火箭女孩儿！” 一个熟悉的声音说，“你在这里干什么？” 
罗西向暗处看过去。
“布洛姆市长？” 她说，
"Aargh!" Roxy stamped her foot. The walls shook.
"Rocket Girl!" said a familiar voice. "What are you doing here?"
Roxy peered into the darkness. "Mayor Bloom?" she said.
“我来这儿找您。您的秘书说今天早上您偷了修建游乐场的钱。” 
布洛姆市长皱起眉头。“我没偷钱。我今天早上根本就没去过市政府。我被绑架到这里。” 
"I came here to find you. Your assistant said you stole the playground money this morning."
Mayor Bloom frowned. "I didn't steal any money. I never even got to City Hall this morning. I was kidnapped and brought here."
罗西糊涂了。“可是，你的秘书亲眼看见你......” 
市长叹了一口气。“她看到的只是跟我长得很像的人而已。” 他说，“迪托教授做了一个我的克隆机器人。现在我知道为什么了。他想让那个克隆人去偷那笔钱。” 
Roxy was confused. "But your assistant saw you . . ."
The mayor sighed. "She saw something that looked like me," he said. "Professor Ditto made a robot clone of me. And now I know why. He wanted my clone to steal that money!"
罗西咽了咽口水。“我觉得我们遇到了比偷钱更严重的问题，市长先生。” 
“什么意思？” 布洛姆市长问道。
“迪托教授做了一个我的克隆机器人！” 罗西说道，
Roxy gulped. "I think we have a bigger problem than stolen money, Mayor."
"What do you mean?" asked Mayor Bloom.
"Professor Ditto made a robot clone of me!" said Roxy.
“谁知道它会做什么坏事呢？” 
“天啊！” 布洛姆市长说，“它将拥有你所有的超能力！你必须阻止它！” 
罗西点点头。“请向后退一下，市长先生。我要炸了这里，我们才好出去。” 
"Who knows what it will do?"
"Oh no!" said Mayor Bloom. "It will have all of your super powers! You have to stop it!"
Roxy nodded. "Step back, Mayor. I'm going to blast us out of here."
史密斯侦探正高速向美罗城大学行驶，有人呼叫了他的对讲机。
“侦探先生！” 警察调度员说，“有人抢劫美罗城博物馆！” 
Detective Smith was speeding toward Metro City University. A call came in on his radio.
"Detective," said the police dispatcher. "The Metro City Museum is being robbed!"
“我会尽快到那儿。” 史密斯侦探说，“我得先追上火箭女孩儿。她去美罗城大学找布洛姆市长了。” 
"I'll be there as soon as I can," said Detective Smith. "First I have to catch up with Rocket Girl. She went to Metro City University to find Mayor Bloom."
“不，她没去。” 调度员说，“火箭女孩儿在博物馆里。” 
“是吗？” 史密斯侦探问，“她在那儿干什么？” 
"No, she didn't," said the dispatcher. "Rocket Girl is at the museum."
"She is?" asked Detective Smith. "What is she doing there?"
“你很难相信。” 调度员说，“火箭女孩儿竟然就是那个盗贼！” 
史密斯侦探挠挠头。“今天怎么回事？” 
"You're not going to believe this," said the dispatcher. "Surprisingly Rocket Girl is the thief!"
Detective Smith scratched his head. "What is going on today?"
一分钟后，史密斯侦探抵达了博物馆。火箭女孩儿的克隆机器人正在搬运一个贵重花瓶。
史密斯侦探惊呆了。“火箭女孩儿！” 他叫道，“你在干什么？” 
A minute later Detective Smith arrived at the museum. The Rocket Girl robot clone was carrying a priceless vase.
Detective Smith was stunned. "Rocket Girl!" he cried. "What are you doing?"
嗞！克隆机器人的眼里发射出激光。史密斯侦探躲开了。刚好真正的火箭女孩儿降落在侦探的面前，激光击中她的胸部又弹开了。
史密斯侦探看看罗西，又看看火箭女孩儿的克隆机器人。史密斯侦探擦了擦眼睛。“两个火箭女孩儿！” 
Whiz-hoo! Lasers shot from the clone's eyes. Detective Smith dodged them. Just then the real Roxy landed in front of the detective. The lasers bounced off her chest.
Detective Smith looked at Roxy. He looked at the Rocket Girl robot clone. Detective Smith rubbed his eyes. "Two Rocket Girls?"
嗖！火箭女孩儿的克隆人冲向罗西。罗西跳着躲开。然后，她用眼睛向克隆人发射出激光。嗞！
Zoom! The Rocket Girl clone shot toward Roxy.
Roxy leaped out of the way. She fired her eye laser beams at the clone. Whiz-hoo!
克隆人跳起来想要躲开，但是已经太晚了。它的脚被激光射中，开始冒烟了。
克隆人盯着脚看了看，然后飞走了。
罗西紧跟上去。
The clone jumped, but it was too slow. Its foot smoked where the laser had hit it.
The clone glanced at its foot and then flew away.
Roxy shot after it.
罗西的朋友们正在美罗城公园的湖边玩儿。玛拉和杰克看着一只乌龟，特勒尔抬着头。
嗖！火箭女孩儿的克隆机器人飞过去了！嗖！罗西也飞过去了，并向克隆人发射激光。
Roxy's friends were at the lake in Metro City Park. Mara and Jack were looking at a turtle. Terrell looked up.
Zoom! The Rocket Girl clone flew past. Zoom! Roxy flew past, shooting lasers at the clone.
“哇！两个火箭女孩儿！” 特勒尔喊道。
玛拉和杰克抬头看去。“在哪里？” 玛拉问。
“她们飞走了。” 特勒尔说。
杰克和玛拉奇怪地看着特勒尔。
"Whoa! Two Rocket Girls!" cried Terrell.
Mara and Jack looked up. "Where?" asked Mara.
"They're gone now," said Terrell.
Jack and Mara both gave Terrell a funny look.
迪托教授的克隆机器人们正在实验室里大声争吵。
“火箭女孩儿跑掉不是我的错！” 其中一个说。
“把她锁在那间房里是你的主意！” 另一个说。
The Professor Ditto clones were arguing and yelling in the lab.
"It's not my fault Rocket Girl escaped!" said one.
"It was your idea to lock her in that room!" said another.
“我想把她锁在......” 
哐当！墙壁炸飞了。火箭女孩儿的克隆人倒在地板上。
罗西也紧跟着飞进来了。 
"I wanted to lock her in the—"
Ka-boom! The wall blew apart. The Rocket Girl clone crashed onto the floor.
Roxy flew in after it.
迪托教授的克隆人们看看破损的火箭女孩儿克隆人，然后又看了看罗西。
“抓住她！” 其中一个喊道。
The Professor Dittos looked at the broken Rocket Girl clone. They looked at Roxy.
"Get her!" yelled one.
教授的克隆人们冲向罗西。嗞！罗西的激光射中了一个机器人。它的耳朵冒起烟来。
“哪位是真正的迪托教授？” 罗西喊道。教授们异口同声地回答：“我是。” 
The professors rushed toward Roxy. Whiz-hoo! Roxy's lasers hit one professor. Smoke came from his ears.
"Which one of you is the real Professor Ditto?" yelled Roxy.
The professors all answered. "I am."
嗞！罗西再次发射。机器人们跳起来躲开了。罗西的激光射中了电脑。轰隆！
嗞！嗞！
所有的克隆人都溅起火花，冒起了烟。
Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired again. The professors jumped out of the way. Roxy's lasers hit the computer. Boom!
Fzzt! Fzzt!
All the clones sparked and smoked.
“哦......” 罗西说，“电脑坏了的话，克隆人也会坏掉！我马上就能找出真正的迪托教授。” 
机器人一个接一个倒下了，直到所有的克隆人都倒下了。
罗西非常惊讶。“真正的迪托教授在哪里呢？” 
"Oh . . .," said Roxy. "Without the computer, the clones are breaking down! Soon I'll find out which one is the real Professor Ditto."
One by one, the clones fell over until none were standing.
Roxy was shocked. "Where's the real Professor Ditto?"
一个月以后，新的游乐场建成了。开幕式上，罗西看着人群倒吸一口气。
“布洛姆市长。” 罗西小声说，“那是？” 
“真正的迪托教授。” 市长说，
A month later the new playground was finished. At the opening ceremony, Roxy looked at the crowd and gasped.
"Mayor Bloom," Roxy whispered. "That's—"
"The real Professor Ditto," said the mayor.
“他十年前就从美罗城大学退休了。他感到很难过。他发明的克隆人带来了很多麻烦。所以，捐钱建了这个游乐场。” 
“这个游乐场太棒了！” 杰克说。
"He retired from Metro City University ten years ago. He felt bad that the clones he invented were causing trouble. So he donated money to help build the new playground."
"This playground is awesome!" said Jack.
“我很想知道修建游乐场的时候，两个火箭女孩儿是不是帮了忙。” 特勒尔说。
玛拉笑了。“只有一个火箭女孩儿。” 
“我看见了两个！” 特勒尔说，看起来有些生气。
罗西笑着说：“我相信你，特勒尔。”

Mara laughed. "There's only one Rocket Girl."

Roxy smiled. "I believe you, Terrell."
玛拉从一家糖果店里走出来，嘴里嚼着泡泡糖。

Mara came out of Candy Store. She was chewing bubble gum.

玛拉吹了个泡泡。
泡泡变得越来越大。

Mara blew a bubble.

泡泡变得越来越大，很快比汽车还大！
玛拉尖叫起来：“啊！” 
The bubble grew bigger and bigger. Soon it was bigger than a car!
Mara screamed. "Ahh!"

罗西，特勒尔和杰克正向美罗城公园走去。杰克拿着他的新皮球。
"I can't wait to play kickball," said Jack.
Roxy, Terrell, and Jack were walking to Metro City Park. Jack was carrying his brand-new rubber ball.
“玛拉跟我们约好两点在公园见。” 罗西说，“她说她得先写完读书报告。” 
三个朋友在公园里踢了一会儿球。
"Mara is meeting us at the park at two o'clock," said Roxy. "She said she had to finish her book report first."
At the park the three friends played kickball for a while.
踢完球，他们在饮水器台上喝了点水。可是，玛拉还没到。

特勒尔看了看手表。“已经过了两点了。” 他说，“玛拉该到了啊。” 
When they finished kickball, they got a drink from the water fountain. Mara still wasn't there.
"What time is it?" asked Jack.
Terrell looked at his watch. "It's after two o'clock," he said. "Mara should be here."
“她肯定很快就会到的。” 罗西说，“杰克，把球踢给我！” 
罗西跑到草地的另一边。杰克把球踢了过去，球划过天空。
"I'm sure she'll be here soon," said Roxy. "Jack, kick the ball to me!"
Roxy ran back across the field. Jack kicked the ball. It sailed through the air.
“接到了！” 罗西喊道。
她把球踢向特勒尔，球飞过他的头顶。

She kicked the ball to Terrell. It went over his head.
"You kicked it too hard!" Terrell called. He chased after the ball. The three friends kicked the ball back and forth for a while longer.
但是，三十分钟过去了，玛拉还是没来。

But after thirty more minutes, Mara was still not there.
"Where's Mara?" said Terrell.
"Maybe she was kidnapped by aliens!" said Jack.
Terrell laughed. "Maybe an enormous monster attacked her!"

罗西摇了摇头。“我不认为玛拉是被外星人、怪物或者巨型章鱼袭击了。她可能在写读书报告。” 
"Ha-ha! Or a lava monster!" said Jack. "Or a giant octopus!"
Roxy shook her head. "I doubt Mara was attacked by aliens or a monster or a giant octopus. She's probably still working on her book report."

市长看起来很着急。“火箭女孩儿！一个巨大的粉色胶体正在入侵美罗城市中心！ 我们需要你的帮助！”

"Whoa," said Roxy. "A pink blob! Don't worry, Mayor. Rocket Girl is on her way!"
罗西必须赶到美罗城市区，去阻止那个粉色胶体！

Roxy had to get to downtown Metro City. She had to stop that giant pink blob!

罗西说完跑走了。
杰克挠挠头。“我觉得罗西应该不知道玛拉在哪儿。” 
Roxy ran off.
Jack scratched his head. "I thought Roxy didn't know where Mara is."
特勒尔皱着眉头。

一分钟以后，罗西赶到了美罗城市区。
Terrell frowned. "I hope she comes back soon. We can't play kickball with just two people."
A minute later Roxy zoomed into downtown Metro City.
胶体是粉色的，而且非常非常大。罗西看到它正慢慢沿着高层大楼往上移动。
“那个看起来像是泡泡糖。” 罗西想。她闻了闻空气中的味道。“闻起来也像是泡泡糖！” 
The blob was pink and really, really big. Roxy watched it move slowly up the side of a skyscraper.
"That looks like bubble gum," thought Roxy. She sniffed the air. "It smells like bubble gum too!"
“火箭女孩儿！” 一个声音叫道。
是史密斯侦探。罗西向他飞去。

"Rocket Girl!" called a voice. It was Detective Smith.
Roxy flew to him.
"You know, Detective," she said. "You're supposed to throw your gum in the trash."
“哈哈！” 史密斯侦探假装大笑，“那不是我的口香糖。”

史密斯侦探摇了摇头。
"Ha-ha." Detective Smith pretended to laugh. "That's not my gum."

Detective Smith shook his head.
“谁都不知道。它在这儿已经一个多小时了，并且一直在变大。如果我们不赶快想办法的话，它会覆盖整个城市！” 
一辆公交车从拐角开过来。

A bus came around the corner.

他猛踩刹车。嘎吱！公交车打滑了。
胶体向公交车靠近。咕噜！粉色黏液粘满了整个公交车。胶体把公交车拉得更近，车里所有人都开始尖叫！
“火箭女孩儿，救救我们！” 
He slammed on the brakes. Screech!
The bus skidded.
The blob approached the bus. Shlurp! Pink slime oozed all over the bus. The blob pulled the bus closer. Everyone inside began to scream.
"Rocket Girl, save us!"
“救命！救命啊！” 
“这太可怕了！” 一个男人喊道，“我上班要迟到了！” 
罗西快速飞向公交车。她抓住车的保险杠，拼命把车往后拖。 
"Help! Help!"

Roxy shot toward the bus and grabbed its bumper. She pulled as hard as she could.
“嗯！” 罗西大声哼着。
咕噜！公交车摆脱了胶体。
“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿。” 司机说。
胶体哼叫着。咕噜！
"Grr!" Roxy grunted.
Shloop! The bus came free of the blob.
"Thank you, Rocket Girl," said the driver.
The blob groaned. Grarg!
“它要干什么？” 罗西心想。
咕噜！胶体变得更大了。它占满了整个街道，并且粘住了另外一栋大楼。 
“不好了。” 罗西说，“胶体变得更大了！” 
"What's it doing?" Roxy wondered.
Grarg! The blob was growing some more. It soon filled the street and attached to another building.
"Uh-oh," said Roxy. "The blob is getting bigger!"
罗西转向公交车司机。“快开车离开这里！马上！” 
公交车立刻开走了，而胶体粘住了第三栋大楼。

Roxy turned to the bus driver. "Drive away from here! Now!"
The bus sped away as the blob moved to a third building.
Suddenly Roxy heard a muffled sound.
"What's that sound?" Roxy wondered.
她用超级听力去听。
“救命！救命！” 
罗西转向胶体的另一边，发现有人困在里面。
罗西用她的超强力把那个人拉了出来。
She listened with her super hearing.
"Help! Help!"
Roxy shot around to the other side of the blob. Someone was stuck in it. Roxy used her super strength to pull the person out.
是玛拉！

It was Mara!

那个胶体又发出了轰隆声。咕噜！

Grarg!
罗西抓起玛拉，想带她飞到一个安全的地方。她们停在一个高楼的楼顶。

罗西和玛拉看到胶体变得越来越大。
咕噜！胶体很快就覆盖了整个城市的街区！

Grarg! It soon covered a whole city block!

玛拉从口袋里掏出那盒泡泡糖。“这是一个新产品。” 她说，“它叫‘威格尔斯夫人口香糖’。”

Mara pulled the pack out of her pocket. "It's a new kind," she said. "It's called 'Mrs. Wiggles Gum.'"
"Mrs. Wiggles?" said Roxy. "She owns the new candy factory just outside Metro City.
也许我应该去跟......”

Maybe I should go talk to—"

"I am Mrs. Wiggles," said the woman. "Soon my bubble gum blob will cover the entire city! The blob will stay unless Mayor Bloom pays me one million dollars!"
罗西怒视着她。“那只是你的想法，威格尔斯夫人！” 罗西向坏人靠近了一步。
就在这时，罗西听到了叫喊声。

罗西往下看去，发现有几个人困在胶体里！

Mrs. Wiggles laughed. "See you later, Rocket Girl!" She pulled a long rope from her coat.
她把绳子抛向楼底，然后顺着绳子滑下去。一辆长得像果冻豆的卡车在楼下等着她。威格尔斯夫人跳上车开走了。
She threw it over the side of the building and zipped down. A truck shaped like a jelly bean was waiting for her. Mrs. Wiggles hopped in and sped off.
罗西看向玛拉。“你在这儿等着！” 
罗西迅速飞向胶体。她抓住一个男人的胳膊。

胶体不断延伸着，黏住了更多的大楼，很快就覆盖了整个美罗城。

嗞！她的眼睛发射出激光。轰隆！泡泡糖胶体被炸成了上百个碎片！
罗西笑了。“太好了。再也没有......” 
咕噜！咕噜！

Suddenly the earth shook, and loud rumbles filled the air. All of the tiny blobs were now moving. And they were all growing!
Roxy gulped. "I think I just made things a whole lot worse!"
罗西看到到处都是胶体。它们有的黏在大楼外部，有的覆盖住了汽车。

一架直升飞机从玛拉的头顶飞过。一个小胶体向它跳去。

A helicopter flew over Mara. One small blob jumped toward it.
但是，胶体被冻住了，掉在了屋顶上。

玛拉看着罗西。

"Wow!" said Mara. "I think the cold breeze from the helicopter froze that blob!"
Mara looked at Roxy.
“火箭女孩儿！” 她叫道，“用你的超级呼吸！它能冻住胶体。”

"Rocket Girl!" she called. "Use your super breath! It will freeze the blobs!"
"I'll try it!" Roxy called back.
Roxy took a deep breath.
Whoosh!
黏在广告牌上的三块胶体被冻住后掉在了地面上。

呼——呼！更多的胶体被冻住了。很快所有的胶体都被冻住了。
Three blobs on a billboard froze and fell to the street.
"Yes!" Roxy cheered. She took a deeper breath and blew again.
Whoo-ooo-oosh!More blobs froze. Soon every blob was frozen solid.
威格尔斯夫人正在她的糖果工厂里。
“我一会儿给布洛姆市长打电话。” 她说，“我要他给我一百万美元！” 
威格尔斯夫人通过望远镜注视着美罗城市区。 
Mrs. Wiggles was in her candy factory.
"Soon I'll call Mayor Bloom," she said. "I'll tell him to pay me one million dollars!"
Mrs. Wiggles peered through a telescope at downtown Metro City.
“啊！” 她大叫，“我的泡泡糖胶体去哪里了？” 
就在这时，罗西闯进了糖果工厂。
“火箭女孩儿！” 威格尔斯夫人说。
“是我阻止了你的泡泡糖胶体。” 罗西说，
"Oh no!" she cried. "Where did my bubble gum blob go?"
Just then Roxy crashed into the candy factory.
"Rocket Girl!" said Mrs. Wiggles.
"I stopped your bubble gum blob!" said Roxy.
“你会进监狱的！” 
威格尔斯夫人打了个响指。几个高大的姜饼人跑进了房间。
威格尔斯夫人大笑。“我是不会进监狱的！” 
"And now you're going to jail!"
Mrs. Wiggles snapped her fingers. Several large gingerbread men ran into the room.
Mrs. Wiggles laughed. "Ha-ha-ha! You'll never take me to jail!"
罗西看着那些姜饼人。他们很高大，看起来很凶。
“我马上就回来。” 罗西说，“我忘了拿东西。” 
罗西从大楼飞了出去。
Roxy looked at the gingerbread men. They were big and mean looking.
"I'll be right back," said Roxy. "I forgot something."
Roxy flew out of the building.
威格尔斯夫人大笑。“火箭女孩儿害怕......” 
啪！一快小胶体击中了一个姜饼人。姜饼人立刻变成碎片。
“怎么回事？” 威格尔斯夫人喊道。
Mrs. Wiggles laughed. "Rocket Girl is scared of—"
Splat! A small blob hit a gingerbread man. The gingerbread man smashed into pieces.
"What's going on?" Mrs. Wiggles cried.
啪！啪！啪！罗西把胶体扔向所有姜饼人。很快，所有姜饼人都变成碎片。
“不要！” 威格尔斯夫人大叫。
罗西把威格尔斯夫人送进监狱，然后飞向玛拉。  
Splat! Splat! Splat! Roxy threw blobs at every gingerbread man. Soon all the gingerbread men were smashed.
"No!" cried Mrs. Wiggles.
Roxy took Mrs. Wiggles to jail. Then she flew back to Mara.
“谢谢你的帮助。” 罗西说。
“我的朋友们在美罗城公园。” 玛拉说，“你能带我去那里吗？” 
罗西笑了。“当然。火箭女孩儿可以做到！”  
"Thanks for your help," said Roxy.
"My friends are at Metro City Park," said Mara. "Can you take me there?"
Roxy smiled. "Sure. Rocket Girl can do that!"
一会儿，罗西脱下了火箭女孩儿的衣服，回到公园找到朋友们。
“嗨，罗西！” 特勒尔说，“玛拉在这里！猜猜是谁找到她的？” 
A little while later, Roxy was out of her Rocket Girl costume. She found her friends at the park.
"Hey, Roxy!" called Terrell. "Mara is here! Guess who found her."
“谁？” 罗西问。
“是火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉说，“是她把我从大泡泡胶体里救出来的。” 
"Who?" asked Roxy.
"Rocket Girl!" said Mara. "She saved me from a giant bubble gum blob!"
“哇！” 罗西说，“我不敢相信我又错过了火箭女孩儿。” 
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着罗西。
“我们来踢球吧！” 杰克说。
罗西和朋友们跑向球场。
"Wow," said Roxy. "I can't believe I missed Rocket Girl."
Terrell gave Roxy a suspicious look.
"Let's play kickball!" said Jack.
Roxy and her friends ran onto the field.
凌晨，天还没亮。西街上开来一辆垃圾车。突然，几道电光照亮了天空。
喀嚓！喀嚓！
It was early in the morning and still dark outside. A garbage truck drove along West Street. Suddenly bolts of electricity lit up the sky.
Za-wap! Za-wap!
很快，天空又变黑了。
“太奇怪了。” 一个清洁工说。
“是啊。” 另一个清洁工说，“不知道是什么……噢！” 
嗷！
A second later the sky was dark again.
"That was strange," said one garbageman.
"Yeah," said the other man. "I wonder what . . . Oh no!"
Roar!
“今天星期五，我太高兴了。” 杰克说，“明天不用上学。” 
罗西和朋友们正在向学校走。就要到来的周末让每个人都很兴奋。
"I'm so glad it's Friday," said Jack. "No school tomorrow!"
Roxy and her friends were walking to school. Everyone was excited about the weekend.
“我们明天去公园吧。” 特勒尔说。
“好主意。” 罗西说，“我们去那儿骑自行车吧。” 
“我带飞盘。” 杰克说，“我们可以抓飞盘玩儿。” 
"We should go to the park tomorrow," said Terrell.
"Great idea," said Roxy. "Let's ride our bikes there."
"I'll bring a Frisbee," said Jack. "We can play Frisbee tag."
玛拉叹了一口气。“我倒是希望能跟你们一起去。” 她说，“但是，爸妈已经计划好了。他们要带我去美罗城自然历史博物馆。” 
Mara sighed. "I wish I could go with you," she said. "But my parents made plans already. They're taking me to the Metro City Natural History Museum."
“我喜欢那个博物馆。” 特勒尔说，“那里有上古化石和洞穴壁画，还有恐龙骨头！” 
“恐龙最酷了。” 杰克说，“我最喜欢霸王龙了。” 
"I love that museum," said Terrell. "It has ancient fossils and cave paintings. And lots of dinosaur bones!"
"Dinosaurs are awesome," said Jack. "My favorite is T. rex."
玛拉眼睛一亮。“对了！你们跟我一起去吧。” 
“可以吗？” 罗西说。
“当然。” 玛拉说，“我爸妈不会介意的。” 
Mara's eyes lit up. "Hey! Why don't you all come with me?"
"Really?" said Roxy.
"Sure," said Mara. "My parents won't mind."
罗西和朋友们都高兴地笑了。
“我等不及了！” 杰克说，“我们说不定能看到霸王龙的骨架！” 
“我希望我们能看到活的恐龙。” 特勒尔说，“可惜它们都灭绝了。” 
Roxy and her friends grinned.
"I can't wait!" said Jack. "Maybe we'll see a T. rex skeleton!"
"I wish we could see real live dinosaurs," said Terrell. "It's too bad they're extinct."
“你肯定能看到活的恐龙，特勒尔。” 罗西说，“你只要发明一台时光机。” 
“哈哈。” 特勒尔假装大笑起来。
"You can see live dinosaurs, Terrell," said Roxy. "You just need to invent a time machine."
"Ha-ha." Terrell pretended to laugh.
然后，他变得很兴奋。“对了，火箭女孩儿说不定能帮我们做一台时光机！” 
罗西大笑着摇了摇头。
“特勒尔，这不可能！我猜火箭女孩儿不会造时光机。” 
But then he looked excited. "Hey! Maybe Rocket Girl could help us build a time machine!"
Roxy laughed and shook her head. "Terrell, that's impossible. I doubt Rocket Girl knows how to build a time machine."
特勒尔叹了一口气。“也许你是对的。” 
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。
“噢！” 她看着朋友们说，“我突然想起……嗯……我忘记带铅笔盒了。我们学校见！”  
Terrell sighed. "You're probably right."
Just then Roxy's watch beeped.
"Oh!" she said, looking at her friends. "I just realized I . . . um . . . forgot my pencil box. I'll see you at school!"
“等一下！” 特勒尔喊的时候，罗西已经离开了。“你可以借我的铅笔用！” 
但是，罗西已经走远了。她走到一个角落，确认了周围没有人。
"Wait!" called Terrell as Roxy hurried away. "You can borrow one of my pencils!"
But Roxy was already gone. She went around the corner and made sure nobody was nearby.
然后，她按下手表上的按钮。布洛姆市长的脸出现在屏幕上。他看起来很着急。
“布洛姆市长，怎么了？” 罗西问道。
“美罗城需要你的帮助，火箭女孩儿。” 市长说，
She pressed a button on her watch. Mayor Bloom's face appeared on the screen. He looked nervous.
"Mayor Bloom, what's wrong?" asked Roxy.
"Metro City needs your help, Rocket Girl," said the mayor.
“恐龙在美罗城里到处走动！” 
“恐龙不是已经灭绝了吗？” 罗西不解地说。
“这些恐龙没有！” 市长说，“现在，请你帮帮忙！” 
“别担心，市长先生。” 罗西说，“我马上就到！” 
"Dinosaurs are roaming all over downtown Metro City!"
"But dinosaurs are extinct," said Roxy, confused.
"These dinosaurs aren't!" said the mayor. "Now please, help!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "I'm on my way!"
罗西躲在栅栏后。不一会儿，她就变身为火箭女孩儿！
“对！” 罗西说，“是时候把美罗城从恐龙那里救出来了！” 
她飞向天空。
Roxy ducked behind a fence. A moment later she was Rocket Girl!
"Okay," said Roxy. "It's time to save Metro City from those dinosaurs!"
She blasted into the air.
“你们看！” 玛拉叫，“是火箭女孩儿！” 
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着正在飞的超级英雄。
当罗西到达美罗城的时候，发现到处都是恐龙。
"Look!" cried Mara. "It's Rocket Girl!"
Terrell stared suspiciously at the flying superhero.
When Roxy arrived in downtown Metro City, dinosaurs were everywhere.
“不好！恐龙！” 一个老爷爷喊道。
“火箭女孩儿，快来帮帮我们！” 一个女人抱着孩子喊。
咚！咚！两只巨型长颈恐龙踏着沉重的步子在西街上走着。
"Oh no! Dinosaurs!" yelled an old man.
"Rocket Girl, do something!" cried a woman with a baby.
Boom! Boom! Two large dinosaurs with long necks stomped along West Street.
一辆车要避开它们，却撞在商店橱窗上。
司机跳下车逃走了。“啊！” 罗西说，“真糟糕！” 
A car tried to race away from them. It crashed into a store window.
The driver got out and ran. "Whoa!" said Roxy. "This is bad!"
她听到一个熟悉的声音。
“火箭女孩儿！” 是史密斯侦探。
他与另外两名警察正躲在一条小巷里。
罗西跑向他们。“啊！” 罗西装成很害怕的样子。
She heard a familiar voice.
"Rocket Girl!" It was Detective Smith.
He and two other police officers were hiding in an alley.
Roxy ran to them. "Ahh!" Roxy pretended to be scared.
“这里还有一只恐龙，装成侦探的样子！” 
史密斯侦探皱了皱眉头。
“现在不是开玩笑的时候，火箭女孩儿。” 
“我明白。” 罗西说，“那些恐龙从哪里来的？” 
“我不知道。” 侦探说。
"It's another dinosaur—dressed as a detective!"
Detective Smith frowned.
"This is no time for jokes, Rocket Girl."
"I know," said Roxy. "So where did the dinosaurs come from?"
"I have no idea," said the detective.
“今天早上几道电光照亮天空以后，恐龙就出现了。” 
哐当！几只小恐龙撞倒了一辆热狗车。
"Early this morning electricity lit up the sky for a moment. After that the dinosaurs appeared."
Crash! Several small dinosaurs knocked over a hot dog cart.
“我的热狗全完了！” 卖热狗的男人喊道。
嗷！一只恐龙冲那个男人咆哮。
“啊！” 那个男人尖叫着逃走了。
"My hot dogs are ruined!" cried the hot dog man.
Grr! One dinosaur growled at the man.
"Aah!" T he man screamed and ran away.
恐龙们吞下了所有的热狗。
一只飞着的恐龙俯冲下来，吃掉了一个老奶奶的帽子。
“啊！” 老奶奶边叫，边向恐龙挥动着拐杖。
The dinosaurs gobbled up all the hot dogs.
A flying dinosaur swooped down and ate an old woman's hat.
"Gah!" the old woman cried. She waved her cane at the dinosaur.
就在这时，一个巨大的黑影罩住了老奶奶。
是一只霸王龙！老奶奶停止了挥动拐杖。
“火箭女孩儿！救命啊！” 她大叫。 
Just then a large shadow fell over the old woman.
It was a T. rex! The old woman stopped waving her cane.
"Rocket Girl! Help me!" she cried.
嗖！罗西迅速飞向老奶奶。
恐龙张开了嘴。嗖！罗西及时带走了老奶奶。
嗷！巨大的恐龙踩在一辆车上。
Zoom! Roxy shot toward the old woman.
The dinosaur opened its jaws. Swoosh! Roxy took the old woman away just in time.
Roar! The huge dinosaur stomped on a car.
“我的新车！” 穿西服的男人喊道，“那辆车花了我不少钱！” 
霸王龙转过身，向空中嗅了嗅，跑向一辆校车。
"My new car!" cried a man in a suit. "That car cost a lot of money!"
The T. rex spun around. It sniffed the air. Then it ran toward a school bus.
“哎呦！” 罗西说。她以最快的速度向校车飞去，把车提起来，移到远离霸王龙的地方。
嗷！最后，霸王龙转身沿着街道跑了。
"Uh-oh!" said Roxy. She flew as fast as she could. She picked up the bus and moved it far from the T. rex.
Roar! Finally, the T. rex turned and ran down the street.
“咻！” 罗西说，“霸王龙逃走了，太棒了！” 
但是，她马上咽了咽口水。
“不好！恐龙正沿着山脉街在跑。那条街是通向美罗城小学的！” 
"Whew!" said Roxy. "I'm glad that T. rex is running away."
But then she gulped.
"Oh no! The dinosaur is running down Mountain Street. That street leads to Metro City Elementary School!"
霸王龙踏着沉重的脚步走向美罗城小学。
嗷！整个学校都震动了。
霸王龙透过窗户仔细往里看。
The T. rex stomped toward Metro City Elementary School.
Roar! The entire school shook.
The T. rex peered into a window.
特勒尔咽了咽口水。
“我以为看见真正的恐龙会很好玩儿。现在，我不那么想了！” 
“你看那些牙！” 杰克大叫。
“我希望火箭女孩儿马上过来！” 玛拉说。 
Terrell gulped.
"I thought it would be cool to see real live dinosaurs. I don't think so anymore!"
"Look at those teeth!" Jack cried.
"I hope Rocket Girl comes soon!" said Mara.
突然——嗖！罗西飞过霸王龙的头顶。
“火箭女孩儿！” 特勒尔喊道。
罗西降落在球场上。“喂，霸王龙！来抓我啊！” 
Suddenly—zoom! Roxy flew past the T. rex's head.
"Rocket Girl!" cried Terrell.
Roxy landed in the kickball field. "Hey, T. rex! Try to get me!"
霸王龙咆哮着踏着沉重的步伐走向罗西。
嗞！罗西眼睛发射的激光击中了地面，炸出了一个大洞。
霸王龙掉进了洞里。嗷！
The T. rex roared and stomped toward Roxy.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy's eye laser beams blasted a big hole in the ground.
The T. rex tumbled into it. Roar!
恐龙在洞里转来转去。它被困住了。
罗西正要飞走时，看到附近有一辆吉普车。
车里的男人头上戴着一顶探险帽，手里拿着一副望远镜。
The dinosaur stomped around in the hole, trapped.
Roxy was about to fly away when she noticed a jeep nearby.
The man inside the jeep was wearing a safari hat and had a pair of binoculars in his hands.
他正在看两只大恐龙吃树叶。
“嗯。” 罗西心想，“那个男人是谁呢。” 
就在这时，那个男人看到了罗西，然后倒吸一口气。
He was watching two tall dinosaurs eat leaves.
"Hmm," thought Roxy. "I wonder who that man is."
Just then the man looked at Roxy and gasped.
他扔掉望远镜，飞快地开车离开了。
“这很奇怪！” 罗西说。她飞向天空紧跟那辆吉普车。
罗西跟着吉普车来到了山里。
He dropped the binoculars and drove off fast.
"Now that is suspicious!" said Roxy. She blasted into the air and flew after the jeep.
Roxy followed the jeep into the mountains.
很快就到了一栋大别墅前。
那个男人跳下吉普车，跑进了屋。
轰！罗西炸毁了别墅大门，走了进去。
但是，到处都不见那个男人。
It soon arrived at a large mansion.
The man jumped out of the jeep and ran inside.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy blasted open the mansion's doors and went in.
But she didn't see the man anywhere.
罗西用她的超级听力，听到了一些声音。
嘀嗒！嘀嗒！嘀嗒！
罗西听到了很多钟表的声音，并且走动一致。
Using her super hearing, she listened.
Tick-tock, tick-tock, tick-tock.
Roxy could hear many clocks, all ticking at once.
罗西顺着声音来到了地下室。
在那里，她发现了一个实验室。里面摆满了钟表，手表和日历。
戴着探险帽的男人正站在一个巨大的钟表前。
钟表上刻的不是时针和分针，而是年份和世纪。
Roxy followed the sounds to the basement.
There she found a laboratory full of clocks, watches, and calendars.
The man with the safari hat stood before a giant clock.
Instead of hours and minutes, years and centuries marked the clock.
“你是怎么进来的？” 那个男人问。
罗西没有回答。“你是谁？” 她问道。
男人双臂交叉。
“我是闪回教授。” 他说，“我正在做时间旅行。” 
"How did you get in here?" asked the man.
Roxy didn't answer. "Who are you?" she asked.
The man folded his arms.
"I'm Professor Flashback," he said. "And I'm time traveling."
“时间旅行？” 罗西问。
“对。” 闪回教授说，“我想研究真正的活恐龙。
所以，我让美罗城回到了几百万年前。” 
"Time traveling?" asked Roxy.
"Yes," said Professor Flashback. "I wanted to study real live dinosaurs.
So I made Metro City travel millions of years into the past."
“你必须让城市回到现在。” 罗西说，“恐龙正在破坏一切！” 
“嗯。” 闪回教授说，“现在实在是太无聊了。
我们不如回到石器时代吧！” 
"Well, you have to return the city to the present," said Roxy. "Dinosaurs are destroying everything!"
"Hmm," said Professor Flashback. "The present is so boring.
Let's go to the Stone Age instead!"
他把手伸向指针。
“不！” 罗西说，“你不能……” 
哐！实验室的门猛地被撞开了。
一群恐龙冲了进来！
He reached for the clock's hand.
"No!" said Roxy. "You can't ……"
Smash! The laboratory door burst open.
Dinosaurs swarmed inside!
“把这些恐龙赶走！” 闪回教授大叫。
几只恐龙跳上桌子，打翻了设备。
一个小钟表掉到地上摔坏了。
"Get these dinosaurs out of here!" cried Professor Flashback.
Several dinosaurs jumped onto a table and knocked over equipment.
A small clock fell down and broke.
另一只恐龙吃掉了书架上的书。
“它们正在毁掉我的实验室！” 闪回教授抓着自己头发。
罗西看到一只大恐龙撞上了那个大钟表。
Another dinosaur ate books from the bookshelf.
"They're destroying my laboratory!" Professor Flashback pulled at his hair.
Roxy saw a big dinosaur bump into the big clock.
钟表晃动起来。罗西咽了咽口水。
“如果钟表坏了，美罗城就会被困在过去！” 
The clock rocked. Roxy gulped.
"If that clock breaks, Metro City will be trapped in the past!"
她冲向那个钟表抓住了它。
钟表的大指针指着公元前6500万年。
“走开！” 闪回教授叫道。
他用扫帚赶着三只小恐龙。
She darted to the clock and grabbed it.
The clock's big hand was pointing to the year 65 million BC.
"Shoo!" said Professor Flashback.
He was pushing three small dinosaurs away with a broom.
他突然注意到罗西正在钟表旁边。“你在干什么？” 
罗西怒视着他。“我要把美罗城带回到现在！” 
罗西抓住了钟表指针。
He suddenly spotted Roxy near the clock. "What are you doing?"
Roxy glared at him. "I'm bringing Metro City back to the present!"
She grabbed the clock's hand.
 “不！” 闪回教授大叫，“不要！哦！” 
一只肥胖的恐龙把教授撞倒了。
罗西抓住了钟表指针。她把指针转到现代。
"No!" cried Professor Flashback. "Do not—oof!"
A fat dinosaur knocked the professor down.
She grabbed the clock's hand. She turned it to the present.
实验室里电光闪烁。
不久之后，电光消失了。恐龙也消失了。
罗西深深地呼了一口气。“咻！” 
闪回教授笑了。
Electricity shot through the lab.
In a moment the electricity was gone. And so were the dinosaurs.
Roxy took a deep breath. "Whew!"
Professor Flashback grinned.
“谢谢你救了我的钟表。” 他说。
罗西回头看着那个钟表。
嗞！她用眼睛发射出激光，把钟表炸成了碎片。
“不！” 教授大叫。
"Thanks for saving my clock," he said.
Roxy turned back to the clock.
Whiz-hoo! Her eye laser beams blew the clock into a million pieces.
"No!" the professor cried.
“钟表很危险。” 罗西说，“还有你，闪回教授。你惹大麻烦了。” 
教授眯着眼睛看着罗西。
他把袖子卷起来，露出腕上的一只小金表。
"That clock is dangerous," said Roxy. "And you, Professor Flashback, are in big trouble."
The professor narrowed his eyes at Roxy.
He pulled his sleeve up. A small golden watch was on his wrist.
“再见！ 火箭女孩儿。” 闪回教授说。
他按下手表上的按钮。
嗞！电光闪烁，闪回教授不见了！
罗西挠挠头。“他去哪儿了？” 
"Good-bye, Rocket Girl," said Professor Flashback.
He pressed a button on his watch.
Za-wap! Electricity flashed and the professor disappeared!
Roxy scratched her head. "I wonder where he went."
第二天，罗西和朋友们去了自然历史博物馆。
那里展示着很多化石和恐龙骨头。
“哇！” 杰克说，“霸王龙的骨架！” 
The next day Roxy and her friends were at the Natural History Museum.
Lots of fossils and dinosaur bones were on display.
"Wow!" said Jack. "A T. rex skeleton!"
玛拉笑了。“活的霸王龙比它要吓人多了。” 
罗西假装叹了一口气。
“我没想到自己错过了那些恐龙。” 
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着她。
Mara smiled. "It's a lot less scary than a live T. rex."
Roxy pretended to sigh.
“I can't believe I missed those dinosaurs.”
Terrell gave her a suspicious look.
朋友们来到了一个石器时代的洞穴壁画前。
画中原始人正在打猎。
其中一个原始人看起来跟其他人很不一样。
“那个男人戴的是帽子吗？” 特勒尔问。
The friends saw a cave painting from the Stone Age.
It showed cavemen hunting animals.
One caveman looked different from the others.
"Is that guy wearing a hat?" asked Terrell.
“我觉得是的。” 杰克说，“他好像还带着望远镜。” 
“真奇怪。” 玛拉说，“那个时代哪有望远镜。” 
罗西看着那个男人笑了。但是，她什么都没说。
"I think so," said Jack. "It looks like he has binoculars too."
"That's weird," said Mara. "Binoculars didn't exist back then!"
Roxy looked at the man and smiled. But she didn't say a word to her friends.
一辆运钞车行驶在西街上，车里坐着两名警卫。
“不堵车真好。” 司机说。
“是啊。” 另一名警卫说。
An armored truck drove along West Street. Two guards sat in the front.
"I'm glad there's no traffic," said the driver.
"Yep," said the other guard.
突然......嗖！
运钞车被什么东西抓住了。
“啊！” 司机大叫。
运钞车撞上一个邮筒。
有人叫道：“咦哈！” 
Suddenly—shwoosh!
Something grabbed the truck.
"Whoa!" cried the driver.
The truck crashed into a mailbox.
A voice called out, "Yee-ha!"
轰隆！轰隆！
“这些怪兽卡车太有意思了！” 玛拉喊道。
罗西和朋友们正在美罗城赛车场里，观看怪兽卡车比赛。
Brumm! Brumm!
"Those monster trucks are awesome!" cried Mara.
Roxy and her friends were at Metro City Arena. They were watching monster truck competition.
卡车的声音很大。它们看起来都不一样。有一辆像大猩猩，另一辆像鲨鱼。
轰隆！轰隆！
一辆红蓝相间的怪兽卡车开进了竞技场。
The trucks were really loud. They all looked like different things. One truck looked like a gorilla. Another one looked like a shark.
Brumm! Brumm!
A red and blue monster truck drove into the arena.
人群欢呼着。
“那是火箭女孩儿卡车！” 杰克喊道。
罗西笑了。
卡车上有一件披风和两束头发。
The crowd cheered.
"It's the Rocket Girl monster truck!" Jack cried.
Roxy smiled.
The truck had a cape and two bunches of hair.
前轮上方伸出了两只手。
“太酷了！” 特勒尔说，“火箭女孩儿看起来好像在飞！” 
轰隆！轰隆！火箭女孩儿卡车在泥里行驶。
Two arms stuck out over its front wheels.
"Cool!" said Terrell. "It looks like Rocket Girl flying!"
Brumm! Brumm!
The Rocket Girl monster truck tore through the mud.
所有人都在欢呼。
“我想快点儿看到那辆卡车压碎那些车！” 杰克指着赛车场里的一堆废车说。
卡车开上了一道土坡，然后向空中飞去。
Everyone cheered.
"I can't wait to see the truck crush those cars!" said Jack. He pointed to a row of junky cars in the arena.
The truck went up a dirt ramp and flew through the air.
所有人再次欢呼。
哐当！火箭女孩儿卡车落在了废车上。金属变了形，玻璃也碎了。
人群大声欢呼。“去吧，火箭女孩儿卡车！” 
Everyone cheered again.
Crunch! The Rocket Girl monster truck landed on the junky cars. Metal twisted. Glass shattered.
The crowd cheered loudly. "Go, Rocket Girl monster truck!"
“呜呼！” 
“火箭女孩儿卡车是最棒的！” 
轰隆，轰隆，轰隆，轰隆！
火箭女孩儿卡车原地打转，泥土溅得到处都是！
"Woo-hoo!"
"The Rocket Girl monster truck is the best!"
Brumm, brumm, brumm, brumm! The Rocket Girl monster truck spun around in circles. Mud went everywhere!
罗西和朋友们欢呼着。
“我很想知道是不是火箭女孩儿在开那辆卡车。” 杰克说。
“应该不是。” 特勒尔说。
罗西很惊讶。“是吗？” 
Roxy and her friends cheered.
"I wonder if Rocket Girl is driving that truck," said Jack.
"I doubt it," said Terrell.
Roxy was surprised. "Really?"
特勒尔耸耸肩。“嗯。火箭女孩儿肯定有更重要的事情去做。” 
罗西笑了。“你说得没错，特勒尔。” 
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。她看着朋友们。
Terrell shrugged. "Yeah. I'm sure Rocket Girl has more important things to do."
Roxy smiled. "You're probably right, Terrell."
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. She looked at her friends.
“我要去......嗯......拿些零食来。” 她说完，站起来开始往外走。
“好啊！” 玛拉说，“你能帮我拿些爆米花吗？” 
“还要一瓶汽水！” 杰克说。
"I'm going to, um, get some snacks," she said. She stood up and started to walk away.
"Ok!" cried Mara. "Can you get some popcorn for me?"
"And another soda for me!" said Jack.
“我要一个椒盐脆饼！” 特勒尔说。
罗西转了转眼睛。“哦，嗯，好的。” 
罗西跑上阶梯，找到一个安静的地方，然后按下手表上的按钮。
"I'll have a pretzel!" said Terrell.
Roxy rolled her eyes. "Oh, uh, sure."
Roxy ran up the stairs and found a quiet area. She pressed a button on her watch.
“布洛姆市长。” 罗西说，“有什么事吗？” 
“我们遇到麻烦了，火箭女孩儿。” 市长说，“有人在西街抢劫了一辆运钞车！” 
“别担心。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿很快就到！” 
"Mayor Bloom," said Roxy. "What's going on?"
"We have a problem, Rocket Girl," said the mayor. "Someone robbed an armored truck on West Street!"
"Don't worry," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl is on her way!"
“我得去市区。” 罗西想，“我得找出是谁抢劫了运钞车。” 
罗西看了一眼零食店。“我还要给朋友们买零食。回来的时候再买吧。” 
"I have to get downtown," thought Roxy. "I need to figure out who robbed that armored truck."
Roxy looked at the snack bar. "I also need to buy my friends' snacks. I'll do that when I get back."
就在这时，她看见一个男人买走了最后一个椒盐脆饼。
“哎呀！” 罗西说，“特勒尔想要椒盐脆饼呢。算了，现在我有更重要的事情要做！” 
Just then she saw a man buy the last pretzel.
"Oh no!" said Roxy. "Terrell wanted a pretzel. Oh well. I have more important things to do right now!"
很快罗西到了美罗城市区。一辆运钞车停在路边上，侧倒着。
史密斯侦探正一边跟两名警卫交谈，一边在小本子上写着什么。
Soon Roxy was in downtown Metro City. An armored truck was on the sidewalk. It was lying on its side.
Detective Smith was talking to two guards. He was writing in his small notebook.
“您好！侦探先生！” 罗西落到地面后喊道，“您要给这些人开罚单吗？” 
“你真有意思。” 侦探说，“我不是开罚单，我在记笔记。” 
"Hi, Detective!" called Roxy as she landed. "Are you giving these guys a parking ticket?"
"Very funny," said the detective. "I'm not writing a parking ticket. I'm taking notes."
他看着两名警卫。“接下来发生了什么？” 
“嗯。” 司机说，“我们当时正在去银行的路上。” 
“是的。” 另一名警卫说。
He looked at the two guards. "What happened next?"
"Well," said the driver. "We were on our way to the bank."
"Yep," said the other guard.
“突然有东西抓住了卡车。” 司机说，“然后卡车就翻了。我们下车以后，所有的钱都不见了！” 
罗西仔细地看了看那辆卡车。“奇怪。” 她说。
"Suddenly something grabbed the truck," said the driver. "Then the truck turned over. By the time we got out, all the money was gone!"
Roxy looked closely at the truck. "That's weird," she said.
她指着车身的一圈印记说。“好象是绳子之类的东西缠住了卡车。” 
司机眼睛一亮。“很有可能是绳子！我们翻倒以后，听到有人喊 ‘咦哈’！” 
She pointed to a dent that went around the whole truck and said, "It looks like something was wrapped around the truck, like a lasso."
The driver's eyes lit up. "Maybe it was a lasso! After we crashed, we heard someone yell 'Yee-ha'!"
他看向另外一名警卫。“记得吗？” 
“记得。” 另一名警卫说。
“咦哈？” 史密斯说，“那是牛仔经常说的话。” 
He looked at the other guard. "Remember?"
"Yep," said the other guard.
"Yee-ha?" said Detective Smith. "That's what cowboys say."
“应该是的。” 司机说，“我们还听到马的声音。” 
“是的。” 另一位警卫说。
罗西交叉着双臂。“我知道是谁抢劫了那辆运钞车。” 
"It sure is," said the driver. "We heard a horse too."
"Yep," said the other guard.
Roxy folded her arms. "I just figured out who robbed this armored truck."
史密斯显得很惊讶。“你真的知道了吗？” 
“是的。” 罗西说，“是臭巴特！” 
“臭巴特？那个不守法的牛仔？” 侦探说。
Detective Smith looked surprised. "You did?"
"Yes," said Roxy. "It was Stinky Bart!"
"Stinky Bart, the outlaw cowboy?" said the detective.
“是的！” 罗西说，“他是美罗城唯一一个不守法的牛仔。” 
史密斯侦探摸着下巴。“你是对的，火箭女孩儿。小偷一定是臭巴特。” 
"That's right!" said Roxy. "He's the only outlaw cowboy in Metro City."
Detective Smith rubbed his chin. "You're right, Rocket Girl. Stinky Bart must be the thief."
“我敢肯定他会抢更多的运钞车。” 罗西说，“我们得阻止他。” 
“我们首先要找到他。” 侦探说。
"And I'm sure he'll try to rob more armored trucks," said Roxy. "We need to stop him."
"First we need to find him," said the detective.
罗西点点头，看向繁忙的街头。有很多车经过。有大型公交车，还有一辆运钞车。
“我去跟着那辆运钞车。” 罗西说，“臭巴特肯定会来抢，我已经准备好了！” 
Roxy nodded and stared at the busy street. Lots of cars went by. Big city buses went by. And then an armored truck went by.
"I'll follow that armored truck," said Roxy. "Stinky Bart will surely try to rob it. I am already ready!"
罗西飞向天空。她想到了一个主意。
“我跟着那辆运钞车。” 她想，“臭巴特一定会来抢劫它的。” 
Roxy flew into the air. She already had an idea.
"I'll follow that armored truck," she thought. "Stinky Bart will definitely try to rob it."
罗西跟着运钞车。
运钞车离开了西街，停在一家杂货店前。警卫把一些钱装进了卡车。卡车继续开。在两家商店和一家银行前停过。
Roxy followed the armored truck.
The truck turned off West Street. It stopped at a grocery store. The guards put some money into the truck. The truck drove some more. It stopped at two more stores and one bank.
然后，它遇上了塞车。在拐了两个弯之后，卡车重新回到了西街。罗西一直没有看到臭巴特。
罗西叹了一口气。“这是个笨主意。我应该......” 
Then it got stuck in a traffic jam. After two more turns, the truck was back on West Street. Roxy didn't see Stinky Bart anywhere.
Roxy sighed. "This was a dumb idea. I should—"
“咦哈！” 一个声音传来。
“臭巴特！” 罗西心想。
一个男人正骑着马追赶运钞车。他穿着牛仔靴，戴着宽大的牛仔帽。
"Yee-ha!" shouted a voice.
"Stinky Bart!" thought Roxy.
A man on a horse was chasing the armored truck. He wore cowboy boots and a floppy cowboy hat.
他在头顶挥动着绳子。
“我要那笔钱！” 臭巴特喊道。
他把绳子抛向运钞车。
“哎呀！” 罗西喊道。
He was swinging a lasso over his head.
"I want that money!" shouted Stinky Bart.
He threw the lasso toward the armored truck.
"Uh-oh!" cried Roxy.
她用眼睛发射出激光。嗞！砰！
激光击中了绳子，绳子弹开了，没有套中卡车。
“哇！” 罗西说，“我眼睛发射的激光对绳子一点都不管用！不过至少救了那辆车。” 
She fired her eye laser beams. Whiz-hoo! Ping!
The laser beams hit the lasso. The lasso bounced off and missed the truck.
"Wow," said Roxy. "My eye laser beams didn't harm that lasso at all! But at least I saved the truck."
臭巴特跳下马狠狠地看着罗西。“你这么做我很生气，火箭女孩儿。” 牛仔说。他开始挥动绳子。“对！我现在非常生气！” 
Stinky Bart jumped off the horse and glared at Roxy. "That sure made me angry, Rocket Girl." said the cowboy. He started swinging the lasso. "Yep! I'm mighty angry right now!"
嗖！绳子飞向罗西，她迅速避开了。
“没抓到我！” 罗西大笑。
Shwoosh!The lasso sailed toward Roxy. She darted out of the way.
"Missed me!" Roxy laughed.
“哼！你！” 臭巴特说，“气死我了！” 他接着挥动绳子。
罗西笑着躲开了。“你别想抓住我，臭巴特！” 
"Errr, how dare you!" said Stinky Bart. "I am furious!" He threw the lasso again.
Roxy laughed as she moved out of the way again. "Don't try to catch me, Stinky Bart!"
臭巴特停止挥绳子。
“就算是吧。” 他说，“不过我似乎没必要。” 
牛仔看了看周围。一群人围在高大的熊雕像前。
Stinky Bart stopped swinging the lasso. "Maybe not," he said. "But maybe I don't need to." The cowboy looked around.
A crowd of people stood near the big bear statue.
他们在椒盐脆饼摊前买椒盐脆饼。
臭巴特挥出绳子。“咦哈！” 
绳子套住了熊雕像的头部后，臭巴特用力一拉。
They were buying pretzels at a pretzel stand.
Stinky Bart tossed the lasso. "Yee-ha!"
The lasso looped around the bear statue's head. Stinky Bart pulled.
熊雕像眼看就要砸向人群。
每个人都吓得尖叫。
“救救我们，火箭女孩儿！” 卖椒盐脆饼的男人大叫。
The bear was going to hit the crowd.
Everyone screamed.
"Save us, Rocket Girl!" cried the pretzel man.
罗西赶紧飞过去。她在熊雕像砸到人群之前抓住了它。她没发现绳子已经滑脱了。
罗西把雕像摆正之后，大家欢呼起来。
“谢谢你！” 卖椒盐脆饼的男人说。
Roxy flew fast. She caught the bear statue just before it hit the crowd. She didn't notice the lasso slip off.
Roxy stood the statue back up, and everyone cheered.
"Thank you!" said the pretzel man.
罗西笑了。“不客气。我......啊！” 罗西觉得自己被绳子套住了。
“咦哈！” 臭巴特喊道，“现在我抓到你了！” 
Roxy smiled. "No problem, folks. I—aah!" Roxy felt the lasso loop around her.
"Yee-ha!" cried Stinky Bart. "I got you now!"
“呃！” 罗西试图挣脱绳子，但是绳子变得更紧了。
臭巴特大笑起来。“你休想摆脱我的绳子！它可结实呢！” 
"Grr!" Roxy tried to break free. But the lasso got tighter.
Stinky Bart laughed. "Don't even think about getting out of my lasso! It's super strong!"
嗞！罗西用眼睛向绳子发射激光，激光马上弹开了。
“啊！” 罗西说。
臭巴特又笑了。
Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams at the rope. The laser beams bounced right off.
"Ugh!" said Roxy.
Stinky Bart laughed again.
“我要试试热感视力！” 罗西想。她盯着绳子，眼中发出桔色光线。但是，绳子一点事儿都没有。
"I'll try my heat vision!" thought Roxy. She stared at the lasso. An orange beam radiated from her eyes. But the rope didn't burn at all.
臭巴特又笑了。“死心吧，火箭女孩儿！” 
卖椒盐脆饼的男人大喊道：“飞起来，火箭女孩儿！绳子可能比你的力气大，但是臭巴特不是。” 
Stinky Bart laughed again. "Just give up, Rocket Girl!"
The pretzel man called out, "Fly, Rocket Girl! The lasso might be stronger than you. But Stinky Bart isn't!"
罗西眼睛一亮。她冲向天空。臭巴特试图抓紧绳子，但是绳子从他手中挣脱了。
“不！” 牛仔大喊道。
Roxy's eyes lit up. She shot into the air. Stinky Bart tried to hold on to the lasso. But it was ripped from his hands.
"No!" cried the cowboy.
罗西看到高楼上的天线。
“太好了！” 罗西说。
她飞到天线上方，然后向下飞。天线穿过绳子上的结。
Roxy spotted an antenna on top of a skyscraper.
"Great!" said Roxy.
She flew over the antenna and then dropped down. The antenna poked through the knot in the lasso.
罗西一拉，结松开了。
“太棒了！” 罗西欢呼起来。
她拿起绳子飞回街道。
Roxy pulled, and the knot came loose.
"Yes!" Roxy cheered.
She took the lasso and flew back down to the street.
臭巴特想要到他的马那里，但是人们挡住了他的路。
“你逃不掉的，你这个臭牛仔！” 卖椒盐脆饼的男人喊道。
Stinky Bart was trying to reach his horse. But people were blocking his way.
"You're not going to escape, you smelly cowboy!" shouted the pretzel man.
“不，我能走！” 臭巴特喊道。
“你站住，臭巴特！” 罗西喊道，“你该进监狱！” 
罗西在头顶挥动着绳子。嗖！她把绳子抛向牛仔。
"Yes, I am!" shouted Stinky Bart.
"Stop right there, Stinky Bart!" cried Roxy. "You're going to jail!"
Roxy swung the lasso over her head. Shwoosh! She threw it at the cowboy.
臭巴特迅速跳起来。砰！他跳到旁边的公交车上。
“我有弹力牛仔靴！” 臭巴特大笑。
罗西又在头顶挥舞绳子。
Stinky Bart quickly jumped. Boing! He bounced on top of a nearby bus.
"I've got bouncy cowboy boots!" Stinky Bart laughed.
Roxy started swinging the lasso over her head again.
砰！臭巴特从公交车上跳到一辆大货车上。
罗西把绳子抛了出去。嗖！它套住了臭巴特的腿。
“不！” 他喊道。
臭巴特掉到地上以后，罗西迅速把他绑了起来。
Boing! Stinky Bart bounced off the bus and toward a big truck.
Roxy threw the lasso. Shwoosh! It snagged Stinky Bart's leg.
"No!" he cried.
Stinky Bart fell to the street. Roxy quickly tied him up.
史密斯侦探跑了过来。“做得好，火箭女孩儿！” 
“谢谢，侦探先生。” 罗西说，“你可以把他送进监狱了。一定要让他洗澡。他太臭了！” 
罗西赶快回到卖椒盐脆饼的摊位。“请给我一包椒盐脆饼。” 
Detective Smith ran over. "Well done, Rocket Girl!"
"Thanks, Detective," said Roxy. "You can take him to jail now. And make sure he gets a shower—he stinks!"
Roxy hurried over to the pretzel stand. "One pretzel, please."
罗西回到赛车场找到朋友们。
“不好意思花了这么长时间。” 罗西说。
她拿出了零食。
Roxy got back to the arena and found her friends.
"Sorry that took so long," she said.
Roxy took out the snacks.
“谢谢你的椒盐脆饼，罗西。” 特勒尔说。
“不用谢。” 罗西说，“是火箭女孩儿帮了我。” 
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着她。“你在开玩笑吧？” 
“对。” 罗西说。
"Thanks for the pretzel, Roxy," said Terrell.
"No problem," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl helped me get it."
Terrell eyed her suspiciously. "You're kidding, right?"
"Yep," said Roxy.
早上，威格先生散步后回到家里。他走进厨房给自己倒了杯橙汁。突然，他听到卧室里有什么声音。咔嚓！咔嚓！咔嚓！嗡嗡！嗡嗡！
“怎么回事儿？” 威格先生疑惑地说。
Mr. Wig came home from his morning walk. He went into his kitchen and poured some orange juice. Suddenly he heard sounds in his bedroom. Click, click, click. Buzz, buzz.
"What is going on in there?" Mr. Wig wondered.
他走进卧室，大吃一惊。房间里到处都是蜘蛛网，保险箱的门被打开了，里面是空的。
“天啊！” 威格先生喊道，“我的钱全不见了！” 
He went into his bedroom and gasped. Spider webs were everywhere in the room. The door to his safe was open, and the safe was empty.
"Oh no!" cried Mr. Wig. "All my money is gone!"
“不用了，谢谢。” 一个女人说，“我不想买巧克力棒。” 她说完就把门关上了。罗西和朋友们正在卖巧克力棒。
“好吧。” 玛拉说，“我们去下一家试试吧。” 
"No, thank you," said a woman. "I don't want to buy any chocolate bars," the woman said. She shut the door. Roxy and her friends were selling chocolate bars.
"Oh well," said Mara. "Let's try the next house."
他们正在为美罗城的贫困家庭筹钱。
四个孩子来到了下一家。罗西敲了敲门。
一位老爷爷打开了门。“什么事儿？” 他问。
They were raising money to help poor families in Metro City.
The four friends arrived at the next house. Roxy knocked on the door.
An old man answered. "Yes?" he said.
“您好，爷爷！” 罗西说， “你想买好吃的巧克力棒吗？我们有三种口味。所有的钱会......” 
“吃巧克力棒会长蛀牙的。” 老爷爷说，“我从来不吃巧克力棒。” 
"Hello, sir!" said Roxy. "Would you like to buy a delicious chocolate bar? We have three kinds. All of the money will go to—"
"Chocolatebars rot your teeth," the man said. "I never eat them."
“我们在为贫困家庭筹钱。” 玛拉说。
老爷爷摇摇头。“我不感兴趣，而且我很忙。再见。” 他关上了门。
"But we're raising money to help poor families," said Mara.
The man shook his head. "I'm not interested. And I'm very busy. Good-bye." He closed the door.
“真是太糟了！” 大家离开房子时，杰克说，“没人买巧克力棒。” 
“别着急。” 玛拉说，“我们还得继续努力。” 
"This stinks!" said Jack as they walked away from the house. "Nobody wants to buy any chocolate bars."
"Don't worry," said Mara. "We just have to keep trying."
“也许我们该去别的小区。” 杰克说。
“这里是富人区。” 罗西说，“肯定有人会买巧克力棒。” 
"Maybe we should go to a different neighborhood," said Jack.
"This is a rich neighborhood," said Roxy. "I'm sure someone here will buy some chocolate bars."
特勒尔的脸上露出笑容。“我有一个好主意。” 他说，“我们请火箭女孩儿帮我们卖巧克力棒吧。” 
罗西笑了。“火箭女孩儿有什么办法？她不能强迫人家买东西啊。” 
A smile appeared on Terrell's face. "I have an idea," he said. "Let's ask Rocket Girl to help us sell the chocolate bars."
Roxy laughed. "What can Rocket Girl do? She can't make people buy anything."
“你也许是对的。” 特勒尔叹了一口气。“我们去下一家吧。” 
四个朋友又走了一会儿。
"You're probably right." Terrell sighed. "Let's go to the next house."
The four friends walked some more.
当他们走到下一家时，罗西的手表响了。朋友们往门口走时，罗西停在人行道上。
“布洛姆市长！” 罗西问，“有什么事吗？” 
When they reached the next house, Roxy's watch beeped. She stayed on the sidewalk as her friends went to the door.
"Mayor Bloom," said Roxy. "Is there a problem?"
“火箭女孩儿！” 市长说，“你知道威格先生是谁吗？” 
“当然知道。” 罗西说，“他是美罗城最有钱的人之一。我刚好在他家附近。” 
"Rocket Girl," said the mayor. "Do you know who Mr. Wig is?"
"Of course," said Roxy. "He's one of the richest people in Metro City. I'm right near his house now, actually."
“很好！” 布洛姆市长说，“有人闯进他家，偷走了钱。” 
“别担心，市长先生。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿会找到那个小偷的。” 
"Good," said Mayor Bloom. "Someone just broke into his house and stole his money."
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl will find the thief!"
“有人偷了威格先生的钱。” 罗西想，“我得马上去他家！” 
罗西的朋友们向她走过来。
"Somebody stole Mr. Wig's money," thought Roxy. "I need to get to his house right away!"
Roxy's friends were coming back toward her.
他们看起来很不高兴。
“那个人也不想要巧克力棒。” 杰克说。
“你们知道吗？” 罗西说。
They didn't look happy.
"That guy didn't want any chocolate bars either," said Jack.
"You know what?" said Roxy.
“我觉得我们漏掉了几家，我回去再问问他们。” 罗西跑掉了。
特勒尔挠挠头。“我们没有漏掉哪家啊。” 
玛拉指着天空。“你们看！火箭女孩儿！” 
"I think we skipped some houses. I'll go back to them." Roxy ran off.
Terrell scratched his head. "We didn't skip any houses."
Mara pointed to the sky. "Look! It's Rocket Girl!"
罗西很快就到了威格先生的家。史密斯侦探正往保险箱里钻。
罗西笑了。“我不认为小偷还在里面，侦探先生。” 
A moment later Roxy arrived at Mr. Wig's house. Detective Smith was climbing into the safe.
Roxy laughed. "I doubt the robber is still in there, Detective."
“很有意思。” 史密斯假装大笑，“我知道小偷不在里面，我正在找线索。” 
威格先生对罗西皱了皱眉头。“我不敢相信你还能开玩笑！我的钱被偷走了！” 
"Very funny." Detective Smith pretended to laugh. "I know the robber isn't in here. I'm looking for clues."
Mr. Wig frowned at Roxy. "I can't believe you're making jokes! My money was stolen!"
“别担心，威格先生。” 史密斯侦探说。他站了起来。“我们会抓到小偷，拿回你的钱的。火箭女孩儿有很多超能力。” 
"Don't worry, Mr. Wig," said Detective Smith. He stood back up. "We'll find the thief and get your money back. Rocket Girl has lots of super powers."
“是，我知道火箭女孩儿的超能力。” 威格先生说。他看着罗西。“你会飞，对吗？” 
“是！” 罗西说。
“我也能飞！” 威格先生说，“我有自己的私人飞机。” 
"Yes, I know about Rocket Girl's super powers," said Mr. Wig. He looked at Roxy. "You can fly, right?"
"Yep!" said Roxy.
"Well, so can I," said Mr. Wig. "Because I have my very own jet."
“那有什么了不起。” 罗西说，“我的眼睛可以发射激光，还能透视墙壁。” 
“哼！” 威格先生双臂交叉，“我是美罗城最有钱的人之一。” 
"Big deal," said Roxy. "I can shoot lasers from my eyes. And I can see through walls."
"Hmph!" Mr. Wig folded his arms. "I'm one of the richest people in Metro City."
罗西也双臂交叉。“我能举起卡车。” 
威格先生耸耸肩。“找到我的钱就行，拜托了。” 
罗西和史密斯走到外面。
Roxy folded her arms. "I can lift a truck."
Mr. Wig shrugged. "Just find my money, please."
Roxy and Detective Smith went outside.
“我不喜欢那个人。” 罗西说。
“我们只管破案。” 史密斯侦探说，“威格先生说他听到了嗡嗡的声音。卧室里到处都是蜘蛛网。” 
"I do not like that man," said Roxy.
"Let's just try to solve this case," said Detective Smith. "Mr. Wig said he heard a buzzing sound. And there were spider webs in his bedroom."
罗西想了想。“也许是昆虫抢劫了威格先生。” 
“哈哈！” 史密斯侦探假装大笑。
“不，我是认真的。” 罗西说，“您还记得那个坏蛋冯·巴兹吗？他训练昆虫去偷东西。” 
Roxy thought about it. "Maybe bugs robbed Mr. Wig."
"Ha-ha," said Detective Smith, pretending to laugh.
"No, I'm serious," said Roxy. "Remember the villain Von Buzz? He trained bugs to steal things."
史密斯侦探摇摇头。“不可能是冯·巴兹，他还在监狱里。” 
“他以前在监狱里。” 罗西说，“不过两周前，已经出狱了。” 
Detective Smith shook his head. "It can't be Von Buzz. He's in jail."
"He was in jail," said Roxy. "But he got out two weeks ago."
“没错！” 史密斯侦探说，“我忘记了。” 
“说不定冯·巴兹又开始偷东西了。” 罗西说。
就在这时，史密斯侦探的电话响了。
"You're right!" said Detective Smith. "I forgot about that."
"Maybe Von Buzz started robbing people again," said Roxy.
Just then Detective Smith's phone rang.
“什么？” 侦探说，“真的吗？我们马上就到！” 
他挂断电话。“有人闯进了布恩太太的家。她也住这条街。” 他说着，回头看罗西。“我们......火箭女孩儿？” 
"Yes?" said the detective. "Really? We'll be right there!"
He hung up the phone. "Someone just broke into Mrs. Bun's house. She lives on this street too.” He turned back to Roxy. “Let's . . . Rocket Girl?"
罗西飞快赶往布恩太太家。布恩太太正躲在桌子下面，她偷偷看了一眼罗西。
“它们在楼上。” 布恩太太小声说。
“小偷吗？” 罗西问。
Roxy rushed into Mrs. Bun's house. Mrs. Bun was hiding under a table. She peeked out at Roxy.
"They're upstairs," Mrs. Bun whispered.
"The robbers?" asked Roxy.
“不是小偷。” 布恩太太看起来非常害怕，“它们是......昆虫！” 
罗西飞到楼上后，吓了一跳。
到处都是蜘蛛网。
"They're not robbers." Mrs. Bun looked really scared. "They're . . . bugs!"
Roxy flew upstairs and gasped.
Webs were everywhere.
一只大蜈蚣在走廊上飞快地爬行，撞倒了家具。一只大蜜蜂在蜈蚣后面飞，提着一袋钱。一只大蜘蛛在天花板上爬着。
A giant centipede charged down the hallway. It knocked over furniture as it went by. A large bee flew behind the centipede. The bee was carrying a sack of money. A big spider ran along the ceiling.
昆虫们从开着的窗口跑掉了。罗西跑到窗口往下一看。
一个男人站在院子里。他戴着一副大大的护目镜，还有一顶带两个天线的头盔。
The bugs went out through an open window. Roxy ran to the window and looked down.
A man stood in the yard. He wore big goggles and a helmet with two antennae.
“冯·巴兹！” 罗西想。
“干得好，小家伙们。” 那个坏蛋对昆虫们说，“我们该走了！我们还要抢很多家呢。” 
"Von Buzz!" thought Roxy.
"Well done, pets," the villain told the bugs. "Now let's go! We have lots of houses to rob today!"
“站住！” 罗西喊道。她跳到地上。
冯·巴兹转过身，惊讶地睁大眼睛。“火箭女孩儿！” 
"Stop right there!" yelled Roxy. She jumped down to the ground.
Von Buzz spun around. His eyes went wide with surprise. "Rocket Girl!"
“我不会让你偷走那笔钱的。” 罗西说。
“哈哈！” 冯·巴兹大笑，“你阻止不了我！我找到了一种方法，让昆虫变大。再也没有人能阻止我偷东西了。” 
"I'm not letting you steal that money," said Roxy.
"Ha-ha!" Von Buzz laughed. "You can't stop me! I discovered a way to grow big bugs. Nobody will ever stop me from stealing again!"
“我会阻止你。” 罗西说，“再把你送回监狱。” 
冯·巴兹咧嘴笑了。“哦，我再也不想回到监狱了，那地方太可怕了。” 
"I will stop you," said Roxy. "And then I'll take you back to jail."
Von Buzz grinned. "Oh, I'm never going back to jail. It was an awful place."
他按下头盔侧面的按钮。“攻击火箭女孩儿！” 
大蜈蚣冲向罗西。它锋利的前爪一张一合。
咔嗒！咔嗒！
He pressed the button on the side of his helmet. "Attack Rocket Girl!"
The big centipede charged toward Roxy. Its sharp claws snapped open and shut. Click! Click!
嗞！罗西用她的眼睛发射出激光，把地面烧出了一个洞。大蜈蚣跳着向后躲开。
大蜈蚣紧张地看着罗西。
“攻击她！” 冯·巴兹又说。
Whiz-hoo! Roxy shot her eye laser beams. They blasted a small hole in the ground. The big centipede jumped back.
The centipede looked nervously at Roxy.
"Attack her!" Von Buzz said again.
大蜈蚣向罗西爬了一小步。
嗞！罗西再次用眼睛发射激光。大蜈蚣又向后退了一步。它把身体缩成了一个球。
The centipede took a tiny step toward Roxy.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams again. The centipede jumped back once more. Then it curled up into a ball.
冯·巴兹跺着脚。“啊！” 
“哈！” 罗西大笑，“你的大蜈蚣害怕我，冯·巴兹！” 
冯·巴兹不理罗西。
Von Buzz stamped his foot. "Aargh!"
"Ha!" Roxy laughed. "Your big centipede is afraid of me, Von Buzz!"
Von Buzz ignored Roxy.
他又按了下头盔侧面的按钮。“攻击火箭女孩儿。” 
大蜘蛛跑向罗西，罗西转过身一看，它已经飞快地织了一只巨大的网。
那只大蜜蜂突然撞向她。砰！
He pressed the botton on the side of his helmet again. "Attack Rocket Girl."
The spider ran past Roxy. Roxy turned around and watched as it quickly spun a large web.
Suddenly the bee crashed into her. Pow!
“啊！” 罗西大叫，她被撞飞到蜘蛛网上。罗西想要挣脱，不过蜘蛛网实在是太黏了。
“不好！” 她大叫道，“我动不了了。” 
"Oof!" cried Roxy. She was hit and flew onto the web. Roxy tried to move, but the web was too sticky.
"Oh no!" she cried. "I'm stuck!"
冯·巴兹按了下头盔上的按钮。“飞起来。” 他说。
蜜蜂抓起冯·巴兹飞走了，蜈蚣和蜘蛛跟在后面。
Von Buzz pressed the button on his helmet. "Fly away," he said.
The bee grabbed Von Buzz and flew off. The centipede and spider followed.
“呃！” 罗西想用力挣脱蜘蛛网，“这个蜘蛛网太黏了！” 
她停下来，不动了。“我来试试热感视力。” 
罗西把头转向蜘蛛网。
"Grr!" Roxy struggled to free herself from the web. "This spider web is too sticky!"
She stopped moving. "I'll try my heat vision."
Roxy turned her head toward the web.
她的眼睛里发射出一道桔色光线，蜘蛛网化掉了，罗西自由了！
“咻！” 罗西说，“现在我得找到冯·巴兹，砸了他的头盔。他就是用头盔来控制昆虫的。” 
An orange beam radiated from her eyes. The spider web melted, and Roxy was free!
"Whew!" said Roxy. "Now I have to find Von Buzz and destroy his helmet. He uses it to control those big bugs."
罗西在两个街区外找到了冯·巴兹。他的昆虫正准备闯进另一栋房子。
那个坏蛋看到了罗西。“你怎么逃出来的？” 他叫道。
Roxy found Von Buzz two blocks away. His bugs were breaking into another house.
The villain saw Roxy. "How did you escape?" he cried.
冯·巴兹按了下头盔上的按钮，看着蜜蜂。“攻击火箭女孩儿！” 
蜜蜂冲向罗西，用巨大的蜂针对着罗西。
Von Buzz pressed the button on his helmet and looked at the bee. "Attack Rocket Girl!"
The bee shot toward Roxy. Its giant stinger was pointed right at her.
“啊！” 罗西飞快地躲开了。
蜜蜂撞上了一棵树，蜂针刺进了树干里。嗡嗡！蜜蜂想要拔出蜂针，但是插得太深了。
"Yikes!" Roxy quickly moved out of the way.
The bee crashed into a tree. Its stinger stuck into the tree's trunk. Buzz! The bee tried to pull its stinger out. But the stinger was in too deep.
“啊！” 冯·巴兹看着蜘蛛，“攻击火箭女孩儿！” 
嘶！嘶！蜘蛛向罗西吐丝。罗西深吸一口气。呼！她用力吹气。
"Aargh!" Von Buzz looked next at the spider. "Attack Rocket Girl!"
Fwit! Fwit! Spider webs shot toward Roxy. She took a deep breath. Whoosh! She blew as hard as she could.
蜘蛛丝向蜘蛛飞回去，缠住了它的脚。蜘蛛跌倒了。
“攻击火箭女孩儿！” 冯·巴兹边喊，边看着蜈蚣。
The webs flew back at the spider and stuck to its legs. The spider fell over.
"Attack Rocket Girl!" cried Von Buzz. He looked at the centipede.
蜈蚣又把身体缩成了一个球。
罗西狠狠看着冯·巴兹。嗞！她用眼睛发射出激光。冯·巴兹的头盔被击碎了。
“不！” 冯·巴兹喊道。
The centipede just curled up into a ball again.
Roxy glared at Von Buzz. Whiz-hoo! She fired her eye laser beams. Von Buzz's helmet blew apart.
"No!" cried Von Buzz.
罗西拖着冯·巴兹走在街上，找到了史密斯侦探，他和威格先生在一起。
“给你！侦探先生。” 她说。
Roxy dragged Von Buzz down the street. She found Detective Smith. Mr. Wig was with him.
"Here you go, Detective," she said.
 “干得好！小姑娘。” 威格先生说，“你比我想象中更厉害。我该怎么报答你呢？” 
罗西看到朋友们正走过来。
"Well done, young lady," said Mr. Wig. "You're more super than I'd realized. How do I repay you?"
Roxy saw her friends coming.
“谢谢您，威格先生。” 罗西说，“不过，我有一个更好的主意。您可以帮那些孩子。” 
“火箭女孩儿！” 特勒尔喊道。
“有人想买巧克力棒吗？” 玛拉问。
"Thanks, Mr. Wig," said Roxy. "But I have a better idea. You can help out those kids."
"Rocket Girl!" cried Terrell.
"Does anyone want to buy some chocolate bars?" asked Mara.
罗西笑了。“威格先生想买一点。” 
“嗯，是的。” 威格先生说，“我愿意买下所有的巧克力棒！” 
几分钟以后，罗西再次见到朋友们。
Roxy smiled. "Mr. Wig would like to buy some."
"Um, yes,﻿" said Mr. Wig. "I'll buy all the chocolate bars!"
Roxy found her friends again a few minutes later.
“我们把巧克力棒都卖光了！” 杰克说，“你知道吗？是火箭女孩儿帮了我们！” 
“我就知道她会帮我们卖巧克力棒的。” 特勒尔说。
罗西笑了。
"We sold all our chocolate bars!" said Jack. "And guess what! Rocket Girl helped us!"
"I knew she could help us sell chocolate bars," said Terrell.
Roxy just smiled.
美罗城的某一个早晨。一辆车开进工地，三名建筑工人从车里走下来。他们正在建一座新的高楼。
“我们今天有很多活儿要干。” 一个男人说。
It was early morning in Metro City. A pickup truck drove onto a construction site. Three workers got out of the truck. They were building a new skyscraper.
"We have a lot of work to do today," said one man.
突然，工人们听到什么声音。嗡！
“那是什么声音？” 一个女人问。
嗡！
“你们看！” 另一位男人大叫道，“新大楼正在变小！” 
Suddenly the workers heard something. Whirr!
"What's that sound?" asked a woman.
Whirr!
"Look!" cried the other man. "The new skyscraper is shrinking!"
罗西和朋友们走在上学的路上。他们路过了落基山面包店。
“嗯......” 玛拉说，“面包闻起来真香！” 
Roxy and her friends were walking to school. They walked past Rocky Mountain Bakery.
"Mmm," said Mara. "The bread smells good!"
“我们放学后买些饼干吧。” 特勒尔说。
“好主意。” 杰克说。
“看！” 玛拉说，“那里就是美罗城电影院。” 
"We should buy cookies after school," said Terrell.
"Good idea," said Jack.
"Look," said Mara. "It's the Metro City Movie Theater."
玛拉指向一栋旧大楼，大楼的窗户都被木板盖住了，墙壁上都是裂纹，楼前长满了杂草。
“我听说旧电影院关门了。” 杰克说，“我在这里看过很多电影。” 
Mara pointed to a very old building. Boards covered its windows. Cracks ran along the walls. Weeds grew in front of it.
"I heard that the old theater went out of business," said Jack. "I saw lots of movies there."
“我也是。” 特勒尔说，“不过现在，市内有了一个新电影院。里面有十二个厅！还有3D电影！” 
“我也在旧电影院看过很多电影。” 玛拉说，“但是现在，我父母希望拆了它。” 
"I did too," said Terrell. "But now there's a new theater downtown. It has 12 screens! It even has movies in 3-D!"
"I saw lots of movies in the old theater too," said Mara. "But now my parents hope it gets knocked down."
“为什么？” 杰克问。
“因为大家想在那里建一个社区花园。” 玛拉说，“他们想种水果和蔬菜。” 
"Why?" asked Jack.
"People want to plant a community garden on the lot," said Mara. "They want to grow fruits and vegetables there."
“那一定很漂亮。” 罗西说，“花园一定比旧楼好看。” 
玛拉点头。“不过，工人得先把它拆了。” 
"That would be cool," said Roxy. "A garden would look much nicer than that old building."
Mara nodded. "But first workers need to knock it down."
特勒尔眼睛一亮。“他们应该叫火箭女孩儿来帮忙！她能拆掉那个旧电影院！” 
罗西转了转眼睛。“火箭女孩儿肯定有更重要的事情去做。” 
Terrell's eyes lit up. "They should get Rocket Girl to help! She could knock down the old theater!"
Roxy rolled her eyes. "I'm sure Rocket Girl has more important things to do."
特勒尔皱了皱眉头。“也许，你是对的。不过，我相信她能做到。” 
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。她看着朋友们。
“啊！” 罗西说，“我带午饭钱了吗？” 
Terrell frowned. "You're probably right. But I'm sure she could do it."
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. She looked at her friends.
"Oh," said Roxy. "Did I bring my lunch money?"
罗西停下脚步，假装翻背包。然后，按下手表上的按钮。
“布洛姆市长。” 她小声问，“有什么事吗？” 
Roxy stopped walking and pretended to look in her backpack. She pressed a button on her watch.
"Mayor Bloom," she asked quietly. "What's up?"
“火箭女孩儿！” 市长说，“美罗城的新摩天大楼不见了！” 
“不见了？” 罗西不解地问，“怎么回事？” 
“它变小后不见了。” 市长说。
"Rocket Girl!" said the mayor. "Metro City's new skyscraper is gone!"
"It's gone?" Roxy was confused. "What happened to it?"
"It shrank and then disappeared." said the mayor.
“工人看到......不好了！” 
“布洛姆市长！” 罗西说，“发生什么事了？” 
“救救我们，火箭女孩儿！” 布洛姆市长声音突然低下来，“救救我们！” 
"Workers saw a . . . Oh no!"
"Mayor Bloom!" said Roxy. "What's wrong?"
"Help us, Rocket Girl!" Mayor Bloom's voice suddenly sounded tiny. "Help us!"
“布洛姆市长？布洛姆市长？” 罗西叫道。
市长没有回答。
“怎么了？” 罗西说。
"Mayor Bloom? Mayor Bloom?" cried Roxy.
The mayor didn't answer.
"What happened?" said Roxy.
“我得查出布洛姆市长发生了什么事！” 罗西想。她看着朋友们。
“嗨，朋友们。” 罗西说，“我忘记带午饭钱了。我们学校见吧。” 
"I have to find out what happened to Mayor Bloom!" thought Roxy.
She looked at her friends.
"Hey, guys," said Roxy. "I forgot my lunch money. I'll meet you at school."
 “我能借给你。” 特勒尔说。
但是，罗西已经不见了。
罗西很快到了市政府。但是，那栋大楼已经不见了！
"I can lend you some money," said Terrell.
But Roxy was already gone.
A moment later Roxy arrived at City Hall. But the building had disappeared!
“真是奇怪。” 罗西想。“我最好先找到史密斯侦探！他也许知道美罗城发生了什么事。” 
罗西飞到警察总局。
“不好！” 罗西喊道。那栋楼也不见了。
"This is really weird," thought Roxy. "I'd better find Detective Smith! Maybe he knows what's going on in Metro City."
Roxy flew to Police Headquarters.
"Oh no!" Roxy cried. That building was gone too.
“火箭女孩儿！” 一个微弱的声音喊道。
“嗯？” 罗西看了看四周，什么也没看到。
“奇怪。” 她想，“我是听到有人叫我的名字。” 
"Rocket Girl!" a tiny voice called.
"Huh?" Roxy looked around but didn't see anything.
"That's strange," she thought. "I thought I heard someone say my name."
那个声音又叫了。“火箭女孩儿！我在下面！” 
罗西往下看去。“噢！” 
史密斯侦探站在地上，旁边有一棵蒲公英。他看起来只有一厘米高。他看上去很不高兴。
The voice called out again, "Rocket Girl! I'm down here!"
Roxy looked down. "Oh!"
Detective Smith stood in the grass, next to a dandelion. He was about a centimeter tall. He didn't look happy.
罗西笑了。“看起来您有一个‘小’问题，史密斯侦探。” 
史密斯侦探皱起眉头。“这不好玩儿，火箭女孩儿。” 
“你说得对。” 罗西说，“你能告诉我发生什么事了吗？” 
Roxy smiled. "It looks like you have a little problem, Detective Smith."
Detective Smith frowned. "This isn't funny, Rocket Girl."
"You're right," said Roxy. "Can you tell me what happened?"
“我们听到了一个奇怪的声音。” 侦探说，“然后，警察总局开始变小。里面的人也开始变小。我从窗户里跳了出来。然后，一个巨人把大楼捡起来带走了！” 
"We heard a strange sound," said the detective. "Police Headquarters began to shrink, and so did everyone inside. I jumped out a window. Then an enormous figure picked up the building and walked away!"
罗西挠挠头。“美罗城的新大楼也变小了。但是，没有道理啊。为什么会有人把大楼变小了呢？” 
Roxy scratched her head. "Metro City's new skyscraper shrank too. But it doesn't make sense. Why would someone shrink buildings?"
“我不知道。” 侦探说，“但是，我们需要查清楚，我不能一直这样子......” 
突然，传来一阵巨响。嗡！
"I don't know," said the detective. "But we need to find out. I can't stay like this for—"
Suddenly there was a loud sound. Whirr!
罗西转过身去。另一栋大楼正在缩小！
“不好了！” 罗西说。她低下头看着史密斯侦探。“您在这儿等着，侦探先生。我去看看怎么回事儿！” 
Roxy spun around. Another tall building was shrinking!
"Uh-oh!" said Roxy. She looked down at Detective Smith. "You stay here, Detective. I'll find out what's going on!"
罗西飞到美罗城上空。她又听到那个声音。
嗡！嗡！又有两栋大楼变小后不见了！罗西落地以后看看四周。
Roxy flew over Metro City. She heard the sound again.
Whirr! Whirr! Two more buildings shrank and disappeared! Roxy landed and looked around.
她用超级听力去听。
“嘻嘻！” 
“听起来好像是一个小女孩儿在咯咯地笑。” 罗西想，“声音是从停车场的另一边儿传来的。” 
She used her super hearing to listen.
"Tee-hee!"
"That sounds like a young girl giggling," thought Roxy. "The sound is coming from the other side of that parking garage."
罗西飞到停车场上方向地面望去。她吓了一跳。
一个穿着宇航服的小女孩儿，手里拿着一个奇怪的仪器。
Roxy flew to the top of the parking garage and looked down. She gasped.
A young girl in a space suit held a strange device.
她把仪器瞄准了熊雕像。
嗡！熊雕像变小了！小女孩儿把它放进了口袋里。
“啊！” 罗西喊道，“是那个小女孩儿把东西变小带走的。” 
She pointed it at the bear statue.
Whirr! The bear statue shrank! The girl put it in her pocket.
"Whoa!" cried Roxy. "That young girl is shrinking things and taking them away."
罗西看到那个奇怪的小女孩儿，沿着西街蹦蹦跳跳走着。
“啦啦啦啦啦！” 小女孩儿唱着歌。
“是那个小女孩儿把美罗城所有的东西变小的。” 罗西想，“在整个城市都消失前，我必须阻止她！” 
Roxy watched the strange girl skip down West Street.
"La la la la la!" the girl sang.
"It's that girl who is shrinking things all over Metro City," thought Roxy. "I have to stop her before the entire city is gone!"
罗西刚飞起来就听到一个声音。
喵！一只猫正盯着路边的什么东西看。
罗西低头一看。“是那些被变小的人！” 罗西喊道。
As Roxy started to fly, she heard a sound.
Meow! A cat was looking at something on the sidewalk.
Roxy looked down."Tiny people!" Roxy cried.
受惊的小人们吓得到处逃。
“救命啊！” 有人喊道。
“猫要吃掉我们！” 另一个人喊道。
喵！猫向空中扑去。
Small, scared people were running away from the cat.
"Please help!" someone cried.
"That cat is going to eat us!" shouted another person.
Meow! The cat leaped through the air.
罗西在猫落地之前抓住了它。“坏猫！” 她说，“不可以吃人！” 
罗西把小人们带进了一家披萨店。
“待在这里。” 她说，“我马上就去阻止这件事。” 
Roxy caught the cat before it landed. "Bad kitty!" she said. "You shouldn't eat people!"
Roxy led the tiny people into a pizza shop.
"Stay here," she said. "I'm going to stop this shrinking right now."
罗西跑到外面。
“火箭女孩儿！” 一个微弱的声音喊道，“救救我！” 
“现在，还有谁需要帮助呢？” 罗西心想。
Roxy ran back outside.
"Rocket Girl!" screamed a tiny voice. "Help me!"
"Who needs help now?" Roxy wondered.
她抬头看到一只老鹰飞过。罗西用她的超级视力看着那只老鹰。
“啊哦！” 罗西喊道，“那只老鹰抓了一个小人！” 
She looked up and saw a hawk flying away. Roxy used her super vision to look at the hawk.
"Uh-oh!" Roxy cried. "That hawk caught a tiny man!"
罗西赶紧飞起来。嗖！
“把那个人还给我！” 罗西向老鹰喊道。
老鹰扔下男人，飞走了。
“天啊！” 男人大叫，“我掉下去了！” 
Roxy flew up right away. Zoom!
"Hand over that little man!" Roxy yelled at the hawk.
The hawk dropped the man and flew away.
"Oh no!" the man shouted. "I'm falling!"
嗖！罗西迅速飞过去，抓住了那个男人。
“咻！” 罗西降落的时候，松了一口气。
哐！
“那是什么？” 罗西心想。
Zoom! Roxy flew fast and caught the man.
"Whew!" said Roxy as she landed.
Crunch!
"What was that?" Roxy wondered.
“喂！” 一个小声音叫道，“那是我才买的车！” 
罗西低头一看，从她的靴子底下，掉下一辆被踩得粉碎的小车。
“对不起！” 罗西说。
"Hey!" A tiny voice yelled. "I just bought that car!"
Roxy looked down. A small smashed car fell from the bottom of her boot.
"Sorry about that!" Roxy said.
罗西再一次飞向天空。
“现在，我得找到那个奇怪的小女孩儿。” 罗西说。
罗西在美罗城上方飞着，找遍了所有的地方，都没有发现那个小女孩儿。
Again Roxy leaped into the air and flew off.
"Now I need to find that strange girl," said Roxy.
Roxy flew above Metro City. She looked everywhere, but she didn't see the girl.
“嗯！” 罗西坐在一栋大楼的楼顶上思考着。
突然，嗡！她坐着的大楼开始缩小了！而那个小女孩儿就站在下面的街道上。
罗西跳离了那栋大楼。
"Hmph!" Roxy sat on the roof of a building to think.
Suddenly . . . Whirr! The building under her started shrinking! And the girl was down on the street!
Roxy leaped off the building.
“多可爱的小楼啊！” 那个小女孩儿咯咯笑着，把大楼放进了口袋里。
“啦啦啦啦啦！” 小女孩儿唱着歌，蹦蹦跳跳走在街上。
"What a cute little building!" The girl giggled and put the building into one of her pockets.
"La la la la la!" The girl sang as she skipped down the street.
“喂！” 罗西喊道，“你给我站住！” 
那个奇怪的小女孩儿抬头一看，罗西正向自己飞过来。小女孩儿看起来很害怕。
"Hey!" yelled Roxy. "Stop right there!"
The strange girl looked up and saw Roxy zooming down at her. The girl looked scared.
“啊！” 小女孩儿喊道，“不要啊！” 
小女孩儿用仪器瞄准罗西。嗡！
“啊！” 罗西尖叫道，“我在变小！” 
"Oh!" the girl cried. "Oh no!"
The little girl pointed the device at Roxy. Whirr!
"Ahh!" Roxy screamed. "I'm shrinking!"
罗西跺着小脚。“谁敢把火箭女孩儿变小！” 
小女孩儿现在看起来像个巨人。罗西看着小女孩儿蹦蹦跳跳走了。
“啦啦啦啦啦！” 小女孩儿唱着歌。
Roxy stomped her tiny foot. "Nobody shrinks Rocket Girl!"
The little girl now looked like a giant. Roxy watched the girl skip away.
"La la la la la!" the girl sang.
罗西跟着小女孩儿飞，并用眼睛发射激光。
嗞！小小的激光打中了小女孩儿的脖子。但是，都被弹开了。
罗西发射了一次又一次。嗞！嗞！
“这是什么？” 小女孩儿摸着脖子说，
Roxy flew after the girl and fired her eye laser beams.
Whiz-hoo! The tiny laser beams bounced off the girl's neck. Roxy fired again and again. Whiz-hoo! Whiz-hoo!
"What was that?" the girl said, feeling her neck.
“感觉有蚊子在叮我。” 
小女孩儿蹦蹦跳跳又走了一会儿。她抬头看到了美罗城大酒店。
“这栋楼真可爱！” 小女孩儿说。
"It feels like mosquitoes are biting me."
The girl skipped some more. Then she looked up at Metro City Grand Hotel.
"That's a cute building!" said the girl.
她用仪器瞄准大楼。
“我必须阻止这个小女孩儿。” 罗西心想，“但要怎么做呢？我太小了！” 
罗西想了一会儿，有了主意。
She aimed the device at the building.
"I have to stop this girl," thought Roxy. "But how? I'm too small."
Roxy thought for a moment. Then she had an idea.
嗖！罗西飞进仪器里。在里面，她看到了各种电线和齿轮。
罗西的眼睛再一次发射出激光。嗞！
哐当！
Zoom! Roxy flew inside the device. She could see all sorts of wires and gears.
Roxy fired her eye laser beams again. Whiz-hoo!
Ka-boom!
小女孩儿手里的仪器爆炸了。罗西飞了出来。
小女孩儿低头看着坏掉的仪器，吸了吸鼻子，嘴唇发抖，眼里含着泪水。
“哇！哇！” 小女孩儿哭着说，“我的收缩射线坏了！” 
Roxy flew back out as the device exploded in the girl's hand.
The girl looked down at the broken device. She sniffed. Her lip shook. Tears filled her eyes.
"Waa-aa! Waa-aa!" the girl cried. "My shrink ray is broken!"
突然，一个男人和一个女人跑向小女孩儿。他们都穿着宇航服。
“艾巴！” 男人说，“你妈妈和我一直在找你。” 
Suddenly a man and woman ran toward her. They were both wearing space suits.
"Abba!" said the man. "Your mom and I were looking for you."
“收缩射线坏掉了！” 艾巴哭着说。
“你不该玩儿那个！” 小女孩儿的妈妈说。
她的爸爸看看四周，皱起了眉头。
"The shrink ray is broken!" Abba cried.
"You're not supposed to play with that!" said the girl's mom.
Her dad looked around and frowned.
“你为了你的收藏品，把很多东西都变小了吧？” 
艾巴点点头。
“你不应该那么做。” 她妈妈说。
“对不起。” 艾巴说。
"You shrank a bunch of things for your collection, didn't you?"
Abba nodded.
"You shouldn't do that," said her mom.
"I'm sorry," said Abba.
“不让你外出了。” 她爸爸说。
艾巴的妈妈摸着下巴。“我去把放大射线拿过来。” 
罗西飞到艾巴妈妈面前。“您好！” 罗西说，“您能把‘人’重新变大吗？” 
"You're grounded," said her dad.
Abba's mom rubbed her chin. "I'll get the un-shrink ray."
Roxy flew up to Abba's mom. "Hi!" said Roxy. "Can you un-shrink people?"
“当然。” 艾巴的妈妈说，“所有的建筑和别的东西，我都会还原。” 
“太好了！” 罗西说。她想了一会儿又说：“但是，有一栋大楼可以不用还原。” 
"Of course," said Abba's mom. "I will unshrink all the buildings and everything else too."
"Great!" said Roxy. She thought for a second. "There's one building that can stay small though."
美罗城很快恢复了正常。所有的东西和人都恢复到正常大小。
艾巴和她的父母回到了太空。
Metro City was soon back to normal. Everything and everyone was the right size.
Abba and her parents returned to space.
罗西和朋友们走在回家的路上。
“看！” 玛拉喊道，“旧电影院不见了！” 
“哇。” 杰克说，“也许大家现在就可以建社区花园了。” 
Roxy and her friends walked home from school.
"Look!" cried Mara. "The old theater is gone!"
"Wow," said Jack. "Maybe people can plant that community garden now."
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着空地。“我很想知道，火箭女孩儿跟这件事有没有关系。” 
罗西笑了。“谁知道呢？这里有面包店。我们去买饼干吧！” 
Terrell looked at the empty lot suspiciously. "I wonder if Rocket Girl had something to do with this."
Roxy smiled. "Who knows? But there's the bakery. Let's buy some cookies!"
嗖！罗西飞过西街。
“火箭女孩儿在干什么？” 一个男人喊道，“她在追赶谁吗？” 
“我什么也没看见。” 另一个人说。
Zoom! Roxy flew over West Street.
"What's Rocket Girl doing?" cried a man. "Is she chasing someone?"
"I don't see anyone," said another person.
罗西用眼睛发射出激光。砰！一个邮箱被炸毁了。信件飞得到处都是。嗞！她再一次用眼睛发射激光。这次一个垃圾箱被炸毁了。
Roxy fired her eye laser beams. Ka-boom! A mailbox blew up. Letters went everywhere. Whiz-hoo! She fired her eye laser beams again. This time a garbage can blew up.
“火箭女孩儿在毁灭美罗城！” 一个女人喊道。
“她看起来很生气！” 一个孩子说。
罗西落地以后看看四周，然后用力跺了一下脚。
“啊！” 罗西大叫。
"Rocket Girl is destroying Metro City!" cried a woman.
"She looks really angry!" said a kid.
Roxy landed and looked around. She stamped her foot.
"Aargh!" Roxy cried.
“这是最精彩的一集！” 杰克说。
罗西和朋友们正在杰克家看《大力士》。
“我希望大力士能阻止那只蜥蜴怪兽！” 玛拉说。
"This is the best episode ever!" said Jack.
Roxy and her friends were watching Mighty Man at Jack's house.
"I hope Mighty Man can stop the monster lizard!" said Mara.
罗西笑了。“大力士肯定能阻止怪兽。他是超级英雄嘛！” 
就在这时，一则新闻报道出现在电视屏幕上。
Roxy laughed. "Mighty Man surely can stop the monster. He's a superhero!"
Just then news appeared on the TV screen.
“这里有一条重大新闻。” 记者说，“今天早上，有人看到火箭女孩儿正在毁灭美罗城。” 
“什么？” 特勒尔说，“火箭女孩儿绝对不会那样做！” 
"We have some important news," said the reporter. "Earlier today witnesses saw Rocket Girl trying to destroy Metro City."
"What?" cried Terrell. "Rocket Girl would never do that!"
记者继续报道。“一名目击者录下了整个过程。录像显示，火箭女孩儿正在毁灭东西。正如大家看到的，她看起来非常生气。没有人知道她为什么那么做。MBS新闻将会持续报道这一事件！现在，我们回到《大力士》。” 
The reporter was still talking. "One witness recorded the whole process. It shows Rocket Girl blowing things up. As you can see, she looks pretty angry. Nobody knows why she did this. But MBS News will be following the story! We now return to Mighty Man."
画面回到《大力士》，但是罗西和朋友们已经不想看了。
“火箭女孩儿不可能毁灭美罗城。” 特勒尔说，“我不相信！” 
Mighty Man came back on. But Roxy and her friends didn't want to watch anymore.
"There's no way Rocket Girl would destroy Metro City," said Terrell. "I don't believe it!"
杰克耸耸肩。“新闻都播出来了。” 
特勒尔想了一下。“也许她正在追赶一个坏人。” 他说。
Jack shrugged. "It was on the news."
Terrell thought for a second. "Maybe she was chasing a bad guy," he said.
玛拉摇摇头。“录像里没有别人啊。” 
特勒尔摸着下巴。“嗯，也许那个坏人速度太快了，我们看不见。” 
Mara shook her head. "Nobody else was in the video."
Terrell rubbed his chin. "Well, maybe the bad guy was really fast and got away."
 “一个比火箭女孩儿还快的坏人？” 玛拉说，“不可能！” 
特勒尔看着罗西。她看起来非常不高兴。
“你没事儿吧，罗西？” 特勒尔问。
"A villain faster than Rocket Girl?" asked Mara. "No way!"
Terrell looked at Roxy. She seemed upset.
"Are you okay, Roxy?" asked Terrell.
罗西跳了起来。“呃......啊？我？哦，我还好。怎么了？” 
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着她。“你怎么看待火箭女孩儿的行为呢？你不会觉得她是一个坏人吧？” 
Roxy jumped. "Me? Yeah, I'm fine. Why?"
Terrell looked at her suspiciously. "What do you think of Rocket Girl's behavior? You don't think she's a bad guy now, do you?"
就在这时，火箭女孩儿的手表响了。
“我去去就回来。” 罗西说，“我要喝点水。” 
罗西走进杰克家的厨房后，按下了手表上的按钮。
Just then Roxy's watch beeped.
"I'll be right back," said Roxy. "I need some water."
Roxy went into Jack's kitchen and pressed the button on her watch.
“火箭女孩儿。” 布洛姆市长说，“我们差点儿就抓到了幽灵强盗。他刚才打算抢劫美罗城造币厂。警察已经把大楼包围了，但是他们到处都找不到他。” 
“别担心，市长。” 罗西说，“我马上就到！” 
"Rocket Girl," said Mayor Bloom. "We're close to catching the Ghost Bandit. He just tried to rob the Metro City Mint. Police have the building surrounded, but they can't find him anywhere."
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "I'm on my way!"
罗西必须赶到美罗城造币厂。幽灵强盗在那里。她必须抓住他。
“嗨！” 罗西对朋友们说，
Roxy had to get to the Metro City Mint. The Ghost Bandit was there, and she needed to catch him.
"Hey, everybody," said Roxy to her friends.
“我想我得回家了。我......嗯......有点不舒服。” 
“嗯。” 罗西离开后，特勒尔说，“难怪她看起来有些不高兴。” 
"I think I should go home. I, um, don't feel well."
"Hmm," said Terrell after Roxy left. "No wonder she seemed upset."
罗西很快就到了美罗城造币厂。警察包围了整栋大楼。史密斯侦探向罗西招手。她飞了下去。
“这是为幽灵强盗准备的惊喜派对吗？” 罗西问。
史密斯侦探皱了皱眉。“不，这不是一个派对。” 
Roxy soon arrived at the Metro City Mint. Police surrounded the entire building. Detective Smith waved to her. Roxy flew down.
