"Is this a surprise party for the Ghost Bandit?" asked Roxy.
Detective Smith frowned. "No, it's not a surprise party."
“我只是开个玩笑。” 罗西说，“那他现在在哪里？” 
“幽灵强盗还在造币厂里。” 侦探说，“但是，我们不知道他在哪儿。因为他是隐形的。” 
"I'm just kidding," said Roxy. "So where is he?"
"The Ghost Bandit is still in the mint," said the detective. "But we don't know where, since he's invisible."
罗西点点头。“他很难抓到。今天早上，我差点儿就抓到他了，但是他逃走了。大家都以为我在毁灭美罗城呢。” 
“我明白。” 史密斯侦探说，“我们需要尽快抓到他。” 
Roxy nodded. "He's not an easy villain to catch. I almost caught him earlier today. But he got away. Everyone thinks I was trying to destroy Metro City."
"I know," said Detective Smith. "We need to catch him soon."
“是的，尽快。” 罗西说，“大家开始把我当坏人看了。” 
“要是我们能知道他是怎么隐形的就好了。” 史密斯侦探说。
"Yes, very soon," said Roxy. "People are starting to think I'm a villain!"
"I wish we knew how he makes himself invisible," said Detective Smith.
罗西想了想。“他一定有一件特殊的衣服。我不相信他是真正的幽灵。” 
“你不相信？” 史密斯侦探怀疑地问。
Roxy thought for a moment. "He must have a special suit. I don't think he's a real ghost."
"You don't?" asked Detective Smith. He looked doubtful.
“是的。” 罗西说，“真正的幽灵能穿透墙壁。但是，这个坏人是从门进去的。” 
“你说得对。” 史密斯侦探说。
"No," said Roxy. "A real ghost would be able to move through walls. But this villain uses doors."
"You're right," said Detective Smith.
罗西向大楼走了几步。“我用我的超级听力试试。” 她说，“也许我能听到幽灵强盗在哪里。” 
罗西闭上眼睛，仔细听。
Roxy stepped toward the building. "I'll use my super hearing," she said. "Maybe I can hear where the Ghost Bandit is."
Roxy closed her eyes and listened carefully.
她听到了办公室风扇转动的声音，小虫子在走廊飞舞的声音，还有脚步声。
罗西猛地睁开眼睛。“我听到了。他在走路！” 
She heard a fan humming in an office. She heard a tiny bug flying down a hallway. And then she heard footsteps.
Roxy's eyes popped open. "I heard him! He's walking!"
罗西迅速飞进造币厂，跟着脚步声来到一个堆满钱的大房间。钱币整齐地排成几行。
Roxy shot into the mint and followed the sound of the footsteps. She arrived in a huge room filled with tall stacks of money. The stacks were in long, neat rows.
看上去少了一部分钱。
罗西走到钱堆中间。“幽灵强盗在哪里呢？” 她想。
It looked like some of the money was missing.
Roxy walked between the rows of money. "I wonder where the Ghost Bandit is," she thought.
罗西再一次仔细地听。她听到了呼吸声。
“喂，幽灵强盗！” 罗西大叫，“我知道你在这里！” 
“呜！” 一个声音喊道，并大笑起来。
Roxy listened carefully again. She heard breathing.
"Hey, Ghost Bandit!" Roxy cried. "I know you're in here!"
"Boo!" A voice called out and then laughed.
罗西飞到钱堆上面。她看了看四周，但是没有看到任何人。
“我穿着隐形衣。” 那个声音说，“你绝对找不到我！” 
Roxy leaped onto a stack of money. She looked around but didn't see anyone.
"I'm wearing an invisible suit," said the voice. "You'll never find me!"
“你在哪里？” 罗西大声叫。
幽灵强盗就在这个房间里，但是罗西不知道他到底在哪儿。
"Where are you?" Roxy cried.
The Ghost Bandit was somewhere in the room. But Roxy didn't know where.
罗西突然听到跑步的声音。她转身看到一扇门很快地打开，又很快关上了。
“他在那儿！” 罗西从钱堆上跳了下来。她打开门，冲进长长的走廊。
Suddenly she heard someone running. She spun around and saw a door quickly open and close.
"There he is!" Roxy leaped from the stack of money. She burst through the door and into a long hallway.
那个坏人的脚步声拐了一个弯儿。罗西跟过去。
当她在拐弯的时候，她看到另一扇门打开了。
嗞！罗西用眼睛发射激光。
砰！门被炸开了。
The villain's footsteps went around a corner. Roxy followed.
As she turned the corner, she saw another door open.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams.
Boom! The door exploded.
“哈哈！你看不见我！” 幽灵强盗笑着继续跑。
罗西站住，仔细听。
"Ha-ha! You can't see me!" The Ghost Bandit laughed and kept running.
Roxy stood still and listened.
“我能听见他的脚步声。” 她想，“他正在另一个走廊上跑。” 
罗西跟在后面，边听边走。
"I can hear his footsteps," she thought. "He's running down another hallway."
Roxy followed, listening as she went.
脚步声到了另一个大房间。这间房墙边有一台巨大的机器。机器上有大型滚轮和传送带。纸币铺满了传送带。旁边还有几桶墨水。
The footsteps led into another big room. This room had a huge machine along one wall. The machine had big rollers and a conveyor belt. Money covered the belt. Buckets of ink sat nearby.
“这一定是工人印钞票的地方。” 罗西想。
哐！突然，一个垃圾桶砸在罗西旁边的墙壁上。
“啊！” 幽灵强盗喊道，“没打中！” 
"This must be where workers print the money," thought Roxy.
Crash! A garbage can suddenly hit the wall near Roxy.
"Aargh!" cried the Ghost Bandit. "I missed!"
罗西看到另一个垃圾桶飞在空中，然后砸向自己。
在垃圾桶砸到自己之前，罗西躲开了。
Roxy saw another garbage can float into the air. Then it shot toward her.
Roxy ducked just before the garbage can hit her.
垃圾箱砸在机器上。
罗西赶紧飞过去，想要抓住强盗。
“哈！你永远抓不到我！” 强盗说完，就安静了下来。
It smashed against the big machine.
Roxy flew as fast as she could and tried to grab the bandit.
"Oh, you'll never catch me!" said the bandit. Then he was quiet.
用自己的超级听力，罗西听到那个坏蛋的心跳声就在附近。她向声音飞过去，想要抓住幽灵强盗。
Using her super hearing, Roxy heard the villain's heartbeat nearby. She flew toward the sound and tried to grab the Ghost Bandit again.
但是，她再次错过了。幽灵强盗大笑着。每次罗西听到声音，都会飞过去。但是，每次幽灵强盗都躲开了。
"啊！” 罗西跺着脚，墙壁摇晃起来。
But again she missed. The Ghost Bandit laughed. Each time Roxy heard him, she flew to the sound. But every time, the Ghost Bandit moved away.
"Grr!" Roxy stamped the floor. The walls shook.
“如果他是隐形的，我永远都阻止不了这个大坏蛋！我真是受够了！啊！” 
一个箱子击中罗西，把她撞倒了。她碰到了一桶墨水。墨水溅到她的靴子上。
"I'm never going to stop this dumb villain if he's invisible! I'm getting really tired of—oof!"
A box hit Roxy, knocking her over. She bumped into one of the buckets of ink. Some ink spilled on her boot.
罗西看着墨水。“嗯。” 她想，“我有办法了！” 
罗西跳起来，举起一桶墨水，洒向空中。呼！罗西把墨水吹得满屋都是。
Roxy looked at the ink. "Hmm," she thought. "I have an idea!"
Roxy jumped to her feet and lifted up a bucket. She tossed the ink into the air. Then . . . Whoosh! Roxy blew the ink across the room.
墨水洒到墙壁上，机器上，还有幽灵强盗的身上！
“啊哈！” 罗西喊道，“我现在能看见你了！” 
The ink sprayed across the walls. It sprayed across the machine. And it sprayed across the Ghost Bandit!
"Aha!" cried Roxy. "I can see you now!"
“哎呀！” 幽灵强盗大喊。他身上洒满了墨水。
现在，罗西能看见那个坏蛋了。他又高又瘦，手里拿着一个大袋子。
"Oh no!" cried the Ghost Bandit. He was covered in ink.
Now Roxy could see the villain. He was tall and thin. He carried a large bag.
他的背上有一个圆圆的东西。
“那可能是隐形衣用的电池。” 罗西想，“他就是用它来隐形的。” 
A round object was on his back.
"That's probably a battery for his suit," Roxy thought. "He uses it to stay invisible."
“你还是抓不到我！” 幽灵强盗喊道。他举起一个小仪器。叮！一个钢爪飞了出来。它连着一根绳子。钢爪勾住了高高的窗台。
"You still won't catch me!" yelled the Ghost Bandit. He held up a small device. Shling! A claw shot out. It was attached to a cable. The claw hooked onto a windowsill high up.
幽灵强盗按下仪器上的按钮。绳子很快把他拉到窗台边。
罗西笑了。“你逃不掉的。” 她说，“警察已经包围了整栋大楼。” 
The Ghost Bandit pressed a button on the device. The cable quickly pulled the villain up to the windowsill.
Roxy laughed. "You can't escape," she said. "Police have the entire building surrounded."
幽灵强盗低头一看。楼下站满了警察。新闻记者也到了。
“啊！” 幽灵强盗喊道，“那里有一个喷泉！” 他再一次发射钢爪，从窗户跳了出去。
The Ghost Bandit looked down. Below the building many police were standing. Some news reporters had arrived too.
"Ha!" cried the Ghost Bandit. "There's a fountain!" He fired the device again. Then he shot out the window.
“不好！” 罗西说。她赶快飞过去。在外面，她看到幽灵强盗从警察头顶飞过去了。
一位警察抬头一看。“幽灵强盗在那里！” 他喊道。
"Uh-oh!" said Roxy. She flew as fast as she could. Outside, she saw the Ghost Bandit zipping above the police.
A police officer looked up. "There's the Ghost Bandit!" he cried.
幽灵强盗眼看就要到喷泉了。
罗西看着那个坏蛋。“如果他跳进水里，就会再次隐形的。” 她心想。
The Ghost Bandit was soon above the fountain.
Roxy watched the villain. "If he lands in that water, he'll be invisible again!" she thought.
幽灵强盗跳下去。罗西用她的眼睛发射出激光。嗞！电池爆炸了。
哗啦！幽灵强盗从水池跳了出来。
The Ghost Bandit dropped down. Roxy fired her eye laser beams. Whiz-hoo! The battery exploded.
Splash! The Ghost Bandit leaped out of the fountain.
“哈哈！” 他大笑，“你再也抓不到我了！我要......啊！” 幽灵强盗从商店橱窗里看到自己的映像，“我的衣服。它坏了！” 
"Ha-ha!" He laughed. "Now you'll never catch me! I'll—ah!" The Ghost Bandit saw his reflection in a store window. "My suit—it's ruined!"
罗西的朋友们还在杰克家看电视。电视上新闻记者正在采访罗西。幽灵强盗戴着手铐。警察们从大袋子里拿出钱。
Roxy's friends were still watching TV in Jack's house. The news reporter was talking to Roxy. The Ghost Bandit was in handcuffs. Police officers were taking money out of the bag.
  “火箭女孩儿 。” 记者说，“他就是你早上追赶的坏人吗？” 
罗西笑了。“他就是幽灵强盗。那时候，他是隐形的。不过，我还是抓到了他！” 
"Rocket Girl," said the reporter. "Is that the villain you were chasing earlier today?"
Roxy smiled. "That's the Ghost Bandit. He was invisible. But I finally caught him!"
“所以说火箭女孩儿是一个好人，观众朋友们。” 记者说，“因为她，美罗城又安全了。现在，回到《大力士》。” 
"So Rocket Girl is a good guy, folks," said the reporter. "And thanks to her, Metro City is safe once again! Now back to Mighty Man."
“我就知道火箭女孩儿是清白的。” 特勒尔说。
杰克和玛拉笑了。
“我真高兴，火箭女孩儿不是坏人。” 杰克说。
罗西走进了房间，脸上挂着大大的笑容。
"I knew Rocket Girl was innocent," said Terrell.
Jack and Mara smiled.
"I'm glad Rocket Girl isn't a bad guy," said Jack.
Roxy walked into the room. She had a big smile.
“朋友们！我回来了！” 
特勒尔看看电视，又看看罗西。“你好点儿了吗？” 
罗西重重坐在沙发上。“我觉得好极了！” 
"Hey, everybody! I'm back!"
Terrell looked at the TV and then at Roxy. "Are you feeling better?"
Roxy flopped onto the sofa. "I feel great!"
美罗城大酒店正在举办一场盛大的舞会。城里最富有的人都在这里。
“多好的舞会啊！” 一个戴着钻石项链的女人说。
Metro City Grand Hotel was hosting a fancy party. All of Metro City's richest people were there.
"What a lovely party!" said a woman with a diamond necklace.
“是啊。” 另一个女人说。她的礼服上有一颗巨大的红宝石。
突然，一声巨响。轰隆隆！轰隆隆！
“我听到了摩托车的声音。” 一个男人说。
"Yes, it is," said another woman. She had a large ruby pinned to her dress.
Suddenly there was a loud noise. Rumble! Rumble!
"I hear motorcycles," said a man.
一道电光闪过！嗞！灯熄灭了！
当灯光再次亮起时，大家都开始尖叫起来。
“我们的珠宝！” 一个女人大喊，“被人偷走了！” 
A bolt of electricity flashed! Zap! The lights went out!
When they came back on, everyone screamed.
"Our jewelry!" a woman cried. "Someone stole it!"
“哇！” 杰克说，“火星，看得好清楚啊！” 
罗西和朋友们在杰克家的后院里。他们在玩儿杰克的新望远镜。
“能让我看一下吗？” 玛拉问。
"Wow!" said Jack. "I can see Mars perfectly!"
Roxy and her friends were in Jack's backyard. They were using Jack's new telescope.
"Can I have a turn now?" asked Mara.
“当然。” 杰克说。他把望远镜让给了玛拉。
“我看见火星了！” 她说，“它是红色的，有很多石头！” 
"Sure," said Jack. He gave the telescope to Mara.
"I see Mars!" she said. "It's red and rocky!"
“你看到火星人了吗？” 特勒尔笑了。
“哈哈！” 玛拉也笑了，“我没看到火星人！” 
杰克翻开了一本关于宇宙的书。“接下来，我们找这个星系吧！” 他指着一张色彩丰富的图片。
"Do you see any Martians?" Terrell laughed.
"Ha-ha!" Mara laughed too. "I don't see any Martians!"
Jack opened a book about space. "Let's try to find this galaxy next!" He pointed to a colorful picture.
“好酷！” 特勒尔说，“我们先要在星图上找到它。” 特勒尔打开星图。
罗西靠过去看。
"Cool!" said Terrell. "First we have to find it on your star chart." Terrell unfolded the star chart.
Roxy leaned in to look.
“我们要在这两颗星星之间找。” 她指着星图上两颗明亮的星星说。
“好的。” 杰克说。他在天空上找到了那两颗星星。
"We need to look between those two stars," she said. Roxy pointed to two bright stars on the chart.
"Okay," said Jack. He spotted the two stars in the sky.
玛拉把望远镜转到有星星的方向。“当宇航员一定很酷。” 她说，“我想坐火箭上太空！” 
Mara turned the telescope toward the stars. "It would be so cool to be an astronaut," she said. "I would love to go into space in a rocket!"
“宇航员是很酷。” 特勒尔说，“但是，你知道谁比宇航员更酷吗？” 
“让我猜猜。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿！” 
"Astronauts are cool," said Terrell. "But you know who's even cooler than an astronaut?"
"Let me guess," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl!"
“对！” 特勒尔咧嘴笑了。“宇航员需要火箭才能进入太空，但是火箭女孩儿不用。” 
“好吧，不过我还是觉得宇航员非常酷。” 罗西说。
"Yeah!" Terrell grinned. "An astronaut needs a rocket to fly in space. But Rocket Girl can fly in space without one."
"Well, I think astronauts are pretty cool anyway," said Roxy.
特勒尔眼睛一亮。“火箭女孩儿也许现在正在太空飞行呢！我们应该用望远镜去找找她！” 
罗西笑了。“我觉得火箭女孩儿现在不在天上。” 
这时，她的手表响了。
Terrell's eyes lit up. "Maybe Rocket Girl is flying through space right now! We should try to find her with the telescope!"
Roxy laughed. "I don't think Rocket Girl is up there right now."
Just then her watch beeped.
她悄悄离开朋友们。
“布洛姆市长。” 罗西小声说，“有什么事吗？” 
“是的，火箭女孩儿。” 市长说，
She quietly stepped away from her friends.
"Mayor Bloom," Roxy whispered. "Is there a problem?"
"Yes, Rocket Girl," said the mayor.
“出大事儿了！有人偷了珠宝展！所有的珠宝——钻石，红宝石，珍珠，都被偷走了！” 
“别担心，市长先生。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿会找到小偷的！” 
"There's a terrible problem! Someone has robbed the jewelry convention! All the jewels—diamonds, rubies, pearls—they were all stolen!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl will find the thief!"
“我得赶到美罗城会展中心。” 罗西想，“我要找出谁偷了珠宝！” 
罗西看了看朋友们。
"I have to get to the Metro City Convention Center," thought Roxy. "I need to find out who stole the jewels!"
Roxy looked at her friends.
“我马上就回来。” 她说，“我刚想起来，我忘了遛狗了！” 
“好吧。” 特勒尔说，“一会儿......” 
罗西跑远了。
"I'll be back soon," she said. "I just remembered something. I forgot to walk my dog!"
"Okay," said Terrell. "See you in a little—"
Roxy ran off.
罗西到了美罗城会展中心。她看到一群人站在那里。他们看起来很难过。所有的珠宝展示柜都是空的。
“火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探看到罗西后叫道，“你来了，我很高兴。” 
Roxy arrived at the Convention Center. She saw a crowd of people. They looked upset. All of the jewelry cases were empty.
"Rocket Girl!" Detective Smith called when he saw Roxy. "I'm glad you're here."
罗西笑了。“您在这里干什么，侦探先生？要买钻石戒指吗？” 
“哈哈！” 史密斯侦探假装笑道，“这次很严重，火箭女孩儿。有人偷了很多名贵的珠宝。” 
Roxy smiled. "What are you doing here, Detective? Shopping for a diamond ring?"
"Ha-ha." Detective Smith pretended to laugh. "This is serious, Rocket Girl. Someone stole a lot of valuable jewels."
“我知道。” 罗西说，“您找到什么线索了吗？” 
“没有。” 史密斯侦探说，“不过，这不是今晚唯一的抢劫案。美罗城大酒店舞会上的珠宝也被偷了。” 
"I know," said Roxy. "Have you found any clues?"
"No," said Detective Smith. "But this wasn't the only robbery tonight. Jewels were also stolen from the party at the Metro City Grand Hotel."
“嗯。” 罗西说，“也许是同一个小偷干的。两次偷的都是珠宝。” 
“是的！” 一个男人说，“非常名贵的珠宝。那些可怕的小偷，偷走了我所有珍贵的绿宝石！” 
"Hmm," said Roxy. "Maybe it's the same thieves. Jewels were stolen both times."
"Yes!" said a man. "Very valuable jewels. Those horrible thieves stole my entire collection of rare emeralds!"
“他们偷走了我的红宝石耳环！” 一个高个子女人说。
“还有我的钻石太阳镜！” 一个老太太说。她吸了吸鼻子。“那是我最喜欢的太阳镜。” 
"They took my ruby earrings!" said a tall woman.
"And my diamond sunglasses!" said an old woman. She sniffed. "They were my favorite sunglasses."
“有人能告诉我刚才发生了什么事吗？” 史密斯侦探问。他从口袋拿出一个小本子。“有人看到什么了吗？” 
"Can anyone tell us what happened?" asked Detective Smith. He took a small notebook out of his pocket. "Did any of you see anything?"
高个子女人走上前。“我什么都没看见。” 她说，“不过，我听到了声音，很大的轰鸣声。听起来像是几辆摩托车的声音。” 
The tall woman stepped forward. "I didn't see anything," she said. "But I heard something—a loud rumble. It sounded like a bunch of motorcycles."
“我也听到了轰鸣声。” 男人说，“然后，是嗞嗞的声音。” 
“一道闪电出现了。” 他的妻子补充说，“接着，灯光都熄灭了。当灯光再亮时，所有的珠宝都不见了！” 
"I heard the rumble too," said the man. "Then I heard a zapping sound."
"There was a bolt of electricity," his wife added. "Next the lights went out. When the lights came back on, all the jewels were gone!"
“这些小偷还偷走了我的新钻石头冠。” 另一个女人说，“我本来想戴它参加明天的展会。” 
“什么展会？” 罗西问。
"The thieves even took my brand-new diamond tiara," said another woman. "I was going to wear it to the exhibit tomorrow!"
"What exhibit?" asked Roxy.
“你不知道吗？” 老太太惊讶地说，“王冠珠宝将在美罗城博物馆展出。” 
“王冠珠宝非常华丽。” 男人说。
"You don't know?" said the old woman. She looked surprised. "The crown jewels will be on display at the Metro City Museum."
"The crown jewels are magnificent," said the man.
“它们今天才到美罗城，明天将对外展示。这是世界上最大，最名贵的珠宝。” 
"They just arrived in Metro City today. And tomorrow the exhibit will be open to the public. It's the biggest, most valuable collection of jewels in the world."
罗西倒吸一口气。“我知道小偷接下来要偷什么了——王冠珠宝！” 
Roxy gasped. "I know what the jewel thieves are going to steal next—the crown jewels!"
“你说得对。” 史密斯侦探说，“小偷接下来会偷王冠珠宝。我们......火箭女孩儿？” 
  很快，罗西就到了美罗城博物馆。
"You're right," said Detective Smith. "The jewel thieves will try to steal the crown jewels next. We should . . . Rocket Girl?"
A moment later Roxy was in the Metro City Museum.
整个大楼很静，很空。
王冠珠宝都放在一间大房子里。玻璃柜里放着数百颗闪闪发亮的钻石、绿宝石和红宝石。
The whole building was quiet and empty.
The crown jewels were in a large room. Hundreds of diamonds, emeralds, and rubies sparkled in glass cases.
房子中央展示柜里放着一顶大王冠。王冠上镶满钻石。
“嗯......” 罗西想，“也许我错了......” 
A large crown sat in a case in the center of the room. Diamonds covered the crown.
"Hmm," thought Roxy. "Maybe I was wrong about . . ."
突然，她听到了一个声音。
轰隆隆！轰隆隆！
“摩托车！” 罗西想，“珠宝大盗来了！” 罗西躲到了一个展示柜后面。
Suddenly she heard a sound.
Rumble! Rumble!
"Motorcycles!" thought Roxy. "The jewel thieves are here!" Roxy hid behind a display case.
一道电光照亮了房间，接着灯灭了。
“有超级视力真好。” 罗西想，“我在黑暗中也看得见东西。” 
A flash of electricity shot through the room. The lights went out.
"It's a good thing I have my super vision," thought Roxy. "I can see in the dark."
一群小矮人跑进房间。他们穿着长靴子和黑马甲。
“电力精灵！” 罗西想，“他们是美罗城里最坏的飞车党！” 
A group of small figures rushed into the room. They wore big boots and black vests.
"The Electric Elves!" Roxy thought. "They're the worst motorcycle gang in Metro City!"
“快！” 精灵的队长说，“把王冠放进去！” 他把袋子给另一个精灵。
另一个精灵打碎玻璃柜，抓起一些红宝石。
"Quick!" said the elf leader. "Put the crown in here!" He handed a sack to another elf.
Another elf smashed a glass case. He grabbed some rubies.
“珠宝真漂亮！” 他说。
“这些都是我们的！” 另一个精灵说。
“不，是我的。” 队长说，“如果你们不住口，我就不分给你们。赶紧干活！” 
"Pretty jewelry!" he said.
"And it's all ours!" said another elf.
"No, it's mine," said the leader. "And if you don't stop talking, I won't share it with you. Now get to work!"
罗西从展示柜后面走出来。
“住手！你们这些可恶的精灵！” 她说。
“火箭女孩儿！” 队长喊道。
Roxy stepped out from behind the case.
"Stop right there, you nasty elves!" she said.
"Rocket Girl!" cried the elf leader.
“把珠宝赶紧放回去！” 罗西说。
“没人能命令电力精灵！” 队长说。他举起手，电光在他手中闪烁。
"Put back those jewels right now," said Roxy.
"Nobody tells the Electric Elves what to do!" said the leader. He raised his hand. Sparks sparkled on his hand.
罗西笑了。“你以为我会害怕吗？我是火箭......” 
嗞！一道电光从队长的手里发射出来。
“啊！” 罗西突然感到被电击了。电流穿过罗西，她倒下了。
Roxy smiled. "You think I'm scared? I'm Rocket—"
Zap! A bolt of electricity shot from the elf's hand.
"Aah!" Roxy felt a sudden shock. Electricity buzzed through her. She fell over.
精灵们大笑着拿剩下的宝石。
“干得好，老大！” 
“火箭女孩儿再也不会烦我们了！” 
“我们回俱乐部去吧！” 队长说。
The elves laughed and grabbed the rest of the jewels.
"Good job, boss!"
"Rocket Girl won't bother us anymore!"
"Let's go back to our clubhouse!" said the elf leader.
罗西站起来时，精灵们已经跑出了房间。
“我必须阻止那些精灵们！” 罗西想。她飞向空中，但却掉在地上。
The elves ran out of the room as Roxy stood up.
"I have to stop those elves!" thought Roxy. She leaped into the air but fell back to the floor.
“哎哟！” 罗西说。她挠挠头。“我为什么飞不起来了？” 
罗西试着用眼睛发射激光，但是什么都没发生。她接着试超级呼吸。
“不好！” 罗西喊道，“我失去了我的超能力！” 
"Ouch!" said Roxy. She scratched her head. "Why can't I fly?"
Roxy tried to fire her eye laser beams. Nothing happened. Next she tried to use her super breath.
"Oh no!" Roxy cried. "I lost my super powers!"
罗西向外看去。电力精灵们正向他们的摩托车跑去。
嗞！队长的手里发射出电光。所有的摩托车都发动了。
轰隆隆！轰隆隆！
Roxy looked outside. The Electric Elves ran to their motorcycles.
Zap! Electricity shot from the elf leader's hand. All the motorcycles started up.
Rumble! Rumble!
电力精灵们跳上摩托车逃走了。
“啊！” 罗西跺着脚，“精灵俱乐部离这里很远。我又飞不了！” 
The Electric Elves hopped onto the motorcycles and rode away.
"Grr!" Roxy stamped her foot. "The elves' clubhouse is really far from here. And I can't fly!"
罗西叹了口气。“虽然我失去了我的超能力，但我还是火箭女孩儿。火箭女孩儿可以阻止那些精灵！” 
罗西走到外面，沿着街道走。一些人盯着她看。
Roxy sighed. "I've lost my super powers. But I'm still Rocket Girl. And Rocket Girl can still stop those elves!"
Roxy went outside and stomped down the street. A few people stared at her.
“奇怪！” 一个带着狗的男人说，“火箭女孩儿在走路！” 
“你为什么不飞呢，火箭女孩儿？” 一个小女孩儿问。
罗西叹了一口气，继续走。
"That's strange," said a man with a dog. "Rocket Girl is taking a walk!"
"Why aren't you flying, Rocket Girl?" asked a little girl.
Roxy sighed and kept walking.
终于，罗西走到了电力精灵的俱乐部。她很累，很生气！
精灵们的摩托车停在俱乐部前面。摩托车周围有嗡嗡的电流声音。罗西用力踢向一辆摩托车。
Finally she got to the Electric Elves' clubhouse. She was tired and she was mad!
The elves' motorcycles were parked in front of the clubhouse. Electricity buzzed all around them. Roxy kicked a motorcycle hard.
嗞！嗞！
“啊！” 罗西再一次感到被电击。电流再一次穿过她的身体。
然后，突然......
嗞！她的眼睛发射出了激光！
Zap! Zap!
"Whoa!" Roxy felt another shock. Electricity buzzed through her again. And then suddenly . . .
Whiz-hoo! Her eye laser beams fired!
精灵们的摩托车被炸成碎片。
“耶！” 罗西欢呼，“火箭女孩儿回来了！” 
罗西用她的X射线往俱乐部里面看去。精灵们正坐在桌子旁玩儿牌。
The elves' motorcycles exploded into little pieces.
"Yes!" Roxy cheered. "Rocket Girl is back!"
Roxy used her X-ray vision and looked into the clubhouse. The elves were sitting at a table and playing cards.
罗西用她的超级听力一听。
“哈哈！” 精灵的队长大笑道，“火箭女孩儿是世界上最差劲儿的超级英雄！” 
“是的！” 另一个精灵说，“我们让她失去了超能力！” 
Roxy listened with her super hearing.
"Ha-ha!" The elf leader laughed. "Rocket Girl is the worst superhero in the world!"
"Yeah!" said another elf. "We took away her super powers!"
“你是说‘我’让她失去超能力吧！” 队长说。
“当然，老大。” 精灵说，“是‘您’让她失去了超能力。” 
“我们明天去抢银行吧！” 第三个精灵说。
"You mean took away her super powers!" said the elf leader.
"Of course, boss," said the elf. "You took away her super powers."
"Let's rob some banks tomorrow!" said a third elf.
精灵们都笑了。
“这些精灵会后悔的！” 罗西想。
她冲向天空。
特勒尔正在用望远镜看星星。
All the elves laughed.
"Those elves are going to be sorry!" thought Roxy.
She blasted off into the air.
Terrell was looking through the telescope.
他倒吸一口气。“火箭女孩儿！” 
嗖！罗西快速飞向地球，撞向俱乐部。
砰！碎片飞得到处都是。
He gasped. "Rocket Girl!"
Zoom! Roxy shot back down to Earth and smashed into the clubhouse.
Ka-boom! Pieces went everywhere.
 “我们的俱乐部！” 精灵队长喊道。
他抬起手。嗞！电光射向罗西。
罗西挡回了电光。嗞！砰！电光向队长射了回去。
"Our clubhouse!" cried the elf leader. He held up his hand. Zap! Electricity shot toward Roxy.
Roxy blocked the electricity. Zap-pow! The sparks flew back at the elf leader.
电流穿过他的全身。他倒下了。
罗西笑了。“你们这些精灵进监狱吧。” 
“我回来了！” 罗西说着，走进了杰克家的后院。
特勒尔还在用望远镜看。
Electricity buzzed through him, and he fell to the floor.
Roxy smiled. "You elves are going to jail."
"I'm back!" said Roxy, walking into Jack's backyard.
Terrell was still looking through the telescope.
“特勒尔说他看到火箭女孩儿在太空飞。” 玛拉说。
特勒尔皱起眉头。“我是看到了！” 
“我相信你。” 罗西说，“现在，能让我用一下望远镜吗？” 
"Terrell thinks he saw Rocket Girl in space," said Mara.
Terrell frowned. "I did!"
"I believe you," said Roxy. "Can I have a turn with the telescope now?"
那是美罗城繁忙的一天。人们在路上匆匆行走。西街上挤满了汽车和公交车。
轰隆！轰隆！大地突然震动起来。
It was a busy day in downtown Metro City. People hurried along the sidewalk. Cars and buses filled West Street.
Rumble! Rumble! Suddenly the ground shook.
“地震了！” 一个女人喊道。
一道巨大的影子遮住了街道。所有人都抬头看。
一个男人咽了一口口水。“那......那是什么？” 
"Earthquake!" a woman shouted.
A large shadow fell over the street. Everyone looked up.
A man gulped. "W-what is that?"
杰克有一只新飞盘。罗西和她的朋友们正在玛拉家的后院里玩儿飞盘。
“嗨，玛拉，接着！” 杰克大声叫道，把飞盘扔了出去。
Jack had a new Frisbee. Roxy and her friends were playing with it in Mara's backyard.
"Hey, Mara, catch!" yelled Jack. He threw the Frisbee.
玛拉快速地跑过去接它。“接住了！” 
“把它扔过来！” 特勒尔叫道。
特勒尔接住飞盘后，扔向罗西。罗西接住后又扔给杰克。
Mara ran fast to catch it. "Got it!"
"Throw it over here!" called Terrell.
Terrell caught the Frisbee and then threw it to Roxy. She caught it and then threw it to Jack.
杰克拿着飞盘扇风。
“今天太热了。” 他说，“我们要是能去游泳就好了。” 
“我让妈妈带我们去市区游泳馆了。” 玛拉说，
Jack fanned himself with the Frisbee.
"It's so hot today," he said. "I wish we could go swimming."
"I asked my mom to take us to the city pool," said Mara.
“不过，她今天事儿太多了。” 
“今天不能去新开的水上乐园，真是太可惜了。” 特勒尔说，“那里有水滑梯，还有很棒的人工造浪机。比游泳馆好多了！” 
"But she has too much work to do today."
"It's too bad we can't go to the new water park," said Terrell. "It's got water slides and a really cool wave machine. That's even better than a pool!"
玛拉耸耸肩。“热，我们也没办法。” 她说，“我们还是接着玩儿飞盘吧。这里，罗西，接着！” 
罗西接住了飞盘，然后又把它扔向了特勒尔。 
Mara shrugged. "We can't do anything about the heat," she said. "So let's just keep playing Frisbee. Here, Roxy, catch!"
Roxy caught the Frisbee. Then she flung it toward Terrell.
“哎呀！对不起，特勒尔！” 她叫道，“刚才我扔得不好。” 
特勒尔去追飞盘。不过，飞盘在他抓住之前，已经飞过栅栏了。
"Oops! Sorry about that, Terrell!" she called. "That was a bad throw."
Terrell chased after the Frisbee. But he couldn't grab it before it sailed over the fence.
飞盘掉进了邻居家的后院里。
“我的新飞盘！” 杰克说。
“我去捡。” 特勒尔说。他翻过栅栏。几分钟以后，特勒尔带着飞盘回来了。
It dropped into a neighbor's backyard.
"My new Frisbee!" said Jack.
"I'll get it," said Terrell. He climbed over the fence. He was back a few minutes later, carrying the Frisbee.
汗从他的额头上流下来。
“我现在好热啊。” 他抱怨道，“要是火箭女孩儿在这里就好了。她也许可以改变天气——下雨或者下雪，让我们凉快凉快。” 
Sweat dripped down his forehead.
"Now I'm really hot," he complained. "I wish Rocket Girl was here. She could probably change the weather—make it rain or even snow, to cool us off."
罗西大笑起来。“对，火箭女孩儿肯定能做到。” 
“你也这么认为吗？” 特勒尔充满希望地看着她。
“不。” 罗西说，
Roxy grinned. "Yeah, Rocket Girl could definitely do that."
"You think so?" Terrell looked at her hopefully.
"Nope," said Roxy.
“火箭女孩儿是很强大，但是她不能改变天气。再说，火箭女孩儿有更重要的事情要做。” 
“你说得对，罗西。” 特勒尔皱着眉头，把飞盘扔给杰克。
"Rocket Girl is powerful, but she can't change the weather. Besides, she has more important things to do."
"You're right, Roxy." Terrell frowned and tossed the Frisbee to Jack.
就在这时，罗西的手表响了起来。“我很快就回来。” 罗西说。
罗西很快地跑进玛拉家里。她马上打开手表。布洛姆市长的脸出现了。他看上去很担心。
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. "I'll be right back," she said.
Roxy hurried into Mara's house. She flipped open her watch. Mayor Bloom's face appeared. He looked very worried.
“布洛姆市长。” 罗西说，“您有什么事吗？” 
“我们需要你的帮助，火箭女孩儿。” 市长说，“一只巨大的怪物正在毁灭美罗城。” 
“别担心，市长！” 罗西说，“我很快就到！” 
"Mayor Bloom," said Roxy. "What's wrong?"
"We need your help, Rocket Girl," said the mayor. "A giant monster is destroying Metro City!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "I'm on my way!"
罗西很快跑出玛拉家。
“听着，朋友们。” 她说，“我得……” 
“练习扔飞盘？” 特勒尔说。他再一次把飞盘扔向了罗西。
Roxy hurried out of Mara's house.
"Listen, guys," she said. "I have to—"
"Practice throwing a Frisbee?" said Terrell. He tossed the Frisbee to Roxy again.
“哈哈！” 飞盘掉在草地上，罗西假笑了一下。“我得先回家了。” 她说，“我忘了……嗯……喂我的金鱼！” 
"Ha-ha!" Roxy pretended to laugh as the Frisbee dropped onto the grass. "First I have to go home," she said. "I forgot to, um, feed my goldfish!"
罗西很快就飞到了美罗城的上空。西街上到处都是毁坏的汽车和公交车。罗西看到街上到处都有巨大的脚印。
A minute later Roxy was soaring over downtown Metro City. West Street was filled with smashed cars and buses. Roxy saw enormous footprints everywhere on the street.
“看上去像是一只大蜥蜴留下的脚印。” 罗西想。
史密斯侦探站在一堆砖头旁边。砖头上面有一个坏了的牌子，上面写着“快捷超市” 。
"It looks like a giant lizard made those footprints," thought Roxy.
Detective Smith stood near a huge pile of bricks. There was a broken sign in the pile. The sign read "Quick Mart."
罗西微笑着说：“您为什么把‘快捷超市’推倒了，侦探先生？是他们把咖啡都卖完了吗？” 
“很有意思，火箭女孩儿。” 史密斯侦探皱着眉头，“不是我推倒的‘快捷超市’。是一个巨大的怪物踩了它。” 
Roxy smiled. "Why did you knock down Quick Mart, Detective? Were they out of coffee?"
"Very funny, Rocket Girl." Detective Smith frowned. "I didn't knock down Quick Mart. A huge monster stepped on it."
罗西看了看四周。“我看到了怪物的脚印。不过，它现在在哪儿呢？” 
侦探耸耸肩。“我刚到这里。我来的时候，怪物已经不见了。” 
Roxy looked around. "I see the monster's footprints. But where is the monster now?"
The detective shrugged. "I just got here. The monster was already gone when I arrived."
一个女人跑过来。“那个怪物往南走了。” 她指着街道。她看了一下对面的街道，叹了口气。“我是一个园丁，来这个公共花园除草，但是现在全毁了。” 
A woman ran over. "The monster went south." She pointed down the street. Then she looked across the street and sighed. "I'm a gardener. I was here to weed the public garden. But it's ruined."
“我的车也毁了！” 一个男人生气地说。他走向史密斯侦探和罗西。“怪物踩坏了我的车！” 
“怪物踩坏了我的公交车！” 公交车司机说。
"And so is my car!" said an angry man. He was walking over to Detective Smith and Roxy. "The monster stepped on it!"
"The monster stepped on my bus!" said a bus driver.
又一个男人跑过来。“真是太气人了！那个怪物把我花店的屋顶掀开了，吃光了我所有的花！” 
“那个怪物吃花？” 史密斯侦探问道。
Another man ran over. "This is infuriating! That monster tore the roof off my flower store. Then it ate all my flowers!"
"The monster ate the flowers?" asked Detective Smith.
他拿出笔记本，开始写。
园丁眨了眨眼。“我也看到了，那怪物吃光了花园里所有的花。” 
开花店的男人仍然很生气。
He took out his notepad and started writing.
The gardener blinked. "I saw the monster eat all the flowers in the garden too."
The man from the flower store was still angry.
他看向罗西。“你打算怎么办，火箭女孩儿？” 
罗西举起双手。“放心。我会找到那个怪物，阻止它的。” 她看着园丁，
He looked at Roxy. "What are you going to do about this, Rocket Girl?"
Roxy held up her hands. "Relax. I will find the monster and stop it." She looked at the gardener.
“你说那个怪物往南走了，对吧？” 
“是的。” 园丁说，“就是美罗城会展中心那边。本来我是打算要去那儿……” 她咽了一口口水。
"You said the monster went south, right?"
"Yes," said the gardener. "That's where the Metro City Convention Center is. I was actually going to go there later today because—" She gulped.
“怎么了？” 罗西问道。
“我知道那只怪物为什么去会展中心了。” 园丁说，“今天那里有个很大的花展！” 
"What's wrong?" asked Roxy.
"I know why the monster went toward the convention center," said the gardener. "There's a huge flower show today!"
“不好了！” 史密斯侦探说，“那只怪物会毁了美罗城的会展中心。我们必须……火箭女孩儿？” 
"Oh no!" said Detective Smith. "That monster will destroy the Metro City Convention Center! We must . . . Rocket Girl?"
罗西落在了美罗城会展中心门前。大楼的屋顶不见了。到处都是破碎的玻璃和砖头。
人们正往大楼外面跑。
Roxy landed in front of the Metro City Convention Center. The building's roof was gone. Broken glass and bricks were everywhere.
People ran out of the building.
“怪物吃了我的花！” 一个男人喊道。
“快逃命啊！” 一个抱着空花盆的女人大喊道。
嗷！
"A monster ate my flowers!" cried a man.
"Run for your lives!" shouted a woman carrying an empty flowerpot.
Rooaarr!
大地震动起来。一道影子遮住了会展中心。一只巨大的怪物站在大楼后面。怪物有一条长尾巴，身上还有绿色的鳞片。看起来像一只巨型爬行动物。
The ground shook. A shadow fell over the convention center. A huge monster stood up from behind the building. The monster had green scales and a long tail. It looked like a giant reptile.
罗西咽了一口口水。“怪物比我想象中的更大。” 
嗷！
怪物把爪子伸向会展中心，掏出一把玫瑰，吃掉了。
Roxy gulped. "The monster is bigger than I thought!"
Rooaarr!
The monster reached into the convention center. It pulled out a bunch of roses and ate them.
怪物打了一个大饱嗝，然后转身离开了会展中心。
怪物用鼻子闻了闻花园里的花，然后把它们都拔掉了。它继续往前走。
The monster burped loudly. Then it turned and walked away from the convention center.
The monster sniffed and pulled all the flowers out of a garden. Then it walked some more.
“我得阻止它！” 罗西说，“它正往玛拉家所在的小区走呢！” 
罗西快速追向怪物。嗞！罗西的眼睛里发射出激光，但是激光又被怪物反弹了回来。
"I have to stop that monster!" said Roxy. "It's headed for Mara's neighborhood!"
Roxy shot after the monster. Whiz-hoo! She fired her eye laser beams. The laser beams bounced off the monster.
怪物转过身来。嗷！怪物把罗西拍进了屋顶。
怪物继续往前走。一边闻，一边吃花。
The monster spun around. Rooaarr! It batted Roxy, knocking her onto a roof.
The monster walked some more, sniffing and eating flowers.
在玛拉家的后院里，杰克、特勒尔和玛拉抬头向上看。
“哇！” 杰克叫道。 
“好大一只怪物！” 特勒尔叫道。
Jack, Terrell, and Mara looked up from Mara's backyard.
"Whoa!" cried Jack.
"It's a huge monster!" cried Terrell.
罗西飞在怪物后面。“我眼睛激光不管用。” 她想，“我要想个别的办法。” 她发现了一个大水箱，举起来快速飞向怪物。
Roxy flew after the monster. "My eye laser beams didn't work," she thought. "I need to think of another way." She spotted a big water tank. She lifted it and shot toward the monster.
“你们看！” 玛拉叫道，“火箭女孩儿！” 
罗西把水箱砸向怪物。水箱破了。水泼在玛拉、杰克和特勒尔身上。
嗷！
"Look!" shouted Mara. "Rocket Girl!"
Roxy threw the water tank at the monster. The tank broke. Water dumped onto Mara, Jack, and Terrell.
Rooaarr!
“坏了！” 罗西想，“怪物现在生气了！” 
怪物跑向罗西，想要再一次打她。
罗西躲开了。“哈！” 罗西说，“你打不到我……啊！” 
"Uh-oh!" thought Roxy. "The monster is angry now!"
The monster ran toward Roxy and batted her again.
Roxy ducked out of the way. "Ha!" she said. "You can't . . . Whoa!"
怪物扬起了大尾巴，把罗西打出了很远。罗西砰的一声掉到了城市另一边。
罗西快速飞回玛拉的小区。怪物正在往山那边走。
The monster whipped its tail, knocking Roxy far away. She landed with a crash on the other side of the city.
Roxy quickly flew back to Mara's neighborhood. Now the monster was heading up into the mountains.
咚！咚！咚！山在晃动。一块巨大的石头掉下来，向山下滚去。又一块石头掉下来了。接着，另一块也掉下来了。很快，很多石头都快速地向山下滚去。山下有很多大楼。
“坏了！” 罗西叫道，“这些石头会毁了美罗城的！” 
Boom, boom, boom! A mountain shook. A boulder broke loose and started to roll. Then another boulder broke loose, and another. Soon lots of boulders were rolling fast down the mountain. There were many buildings at the bottom of the mountain.
"Uh-oh!" cried Roxy. "Those boulders will ruin Metro City!"
“我得拦住这些石头！” 罗西喊道。
巨大的石头飞快地滚向美罗城。罗西用眼睛向山脚下发射激光。
轰隆！地上出现了一个大坑。
"I have to stop those boulders!" cried Roxy.
The giant boulders rolled fast toward Metro City. Roxy fired her eye laser beams at the bottom of the mountain.
Ka-boom! A huge hole appeared in the ground.
石头滚到了山脚，掉进坑里。
“好了！” 罗西欢呼道，“那怪物去哪里了呢？” 
罗西飞过了一座山。
The boulders rolled to the bottom of the mountain, right into the hole.
"Yes!" cheered Roxy. "Now where is that monster?"
Roxy flew over the mountains.
罗西终于发现了巨大的脚印。她跟着脚印穿过山谷，绕过了一座高山。
突然，罗西停住了。她听到了低低的隆隆声。“好像有人在打呼噜。” 
She finally spotted enormous footprints. She followed the footprints through a valley and around a tall mountain.
Then Roxy stopped. She heard a deep rumbling sound. "That sounds like someone snoring!"
她飞过另一座山，看到满地的野花。怪物正趴在草地中央，睡在一栋大房子旁边。
一个男人正站在阳台上。
She flew over another mountain and saw a field of wildflowers. The monster lay in the middle of the field, sleeping next to a mansion.
A man stood on the balcony.
他对着罗西眨了眨眼睛。“你是火箭女孩儿吧？” 
罗西点点头。“你是谁？” 
“我是纽特教授。” 男人说，“我是研究爬行动物的。你为什么来这里？” 
He blinked at Roxy. "You're Rocket Girl, right?"
Roxy nodded. "Who are you?"
"Professor Newt," said the man. "I study reptiles. Why are you here?"
罗西很疑惑。“你认识这只怪物？” 
“它不是怪物。” 纽特教授说，“它是我的爬行宠物，它叫贝西。” 
“贝西？” 罗西重复道。
Roxy was confused. "Do you know this monster?"
"She's not a monster," said Professor Newt. "She's my pet reptile. Her name is Bessie."
"Bessie?" Roxy repeated.
纽特教授点点头。“我生日的时候，朋友给了我一个神秘爬行动物的蛋。当这只蛋孵化以后，贝西出来了。” 他笑了。“我没想到它会长这么大！” 
Professor Newt nodded. "My friend gave me a mysterious reptile egg for my birthday. When the egg hatched, out came Bessie." He laughed. "I had no idea she would grow this big!"
罗西皱着眉头。“嗯，纽特教授，贝西差点儿毁了整个美罗城！” 
“天啊！” 纽特教授说，“它一定是闻到花展的花香了。” 他看着那只巨大的爬行动物。
Roxy frowned. "Well, Professor Newt, Bessie almost destroyed Metro City!"
"Oh dear!" said Professor Newt. "She must have smelled the flower show." He looked at the large reptile.
“贝西非常喜欢花。它一般只吃这儿的野花。我觉得它是想吃一些没吃过的花。它做了哪些破坏？” 
罗西把贝西所做的事情告诉了纽特教授。
"Bessie loves flowers. She usually just eats the wildflowers here. But I guess she wanted to try some flowers she had never eaten before. How much damage did she do?"
Roxy told Professor Newt what Bessie had done.
教授惊呆了。“天啊！我得向布洛姆市长道歉。从现在起，我让贝西只呆在这儿的山里。贝西很可爱，不过它会惹大麻烦。” 
The professor gasped. "Oh no! I must apologize to Mayor Bloom. And from now on, I will keep Bessie up here in the mountains. Bessie is sweet, but she can cause a lot of trouble!"
“你们还在玩儿飞盘吗？” 罗西大声问。她走到玛拉家的后院。到处都是水坑。玛拉和杰克全淋湿了。
“没有。” 杰克说。
"Are you still playing Frisbee?" Roxy called. She walked into Mara's backyard. Puddles were everywhere. Mara and Jack were soaked.
"Nope," said Jack.
“刚才有一只巨大的怪物！” 玛拉说，“ 还有，火箭女孩儿把水泼在了我们身上！” 
罗西笑了。“特勒尔不是说想去水上乐园吗？特勒尔呢？” 
"There was a huge monster!" said Mara. "And Rocket Girl dumped water on us!"
Roxy grinned. "Didn't Terrell say that he wanted to go to the water park? Terrell?"
特勒尔从灌木丛里跳了出来。他拿着用来浇花园的水管。
“抓到了！” 他叫道，把水浇到罗西身上。
Terrell jumped out from behind a bush. He was holding a garden hose.
"Gotcha!" he yelled, blasting Roxy with the hose.
“喂！” 罗西惊讶地叫起来。但是，很快她就和朋友们一起笑了起来。
这么热的天，水凉凉的感觉好极了！
"Hey!" Roxy yelped in surprise. But then she laughed along with her friends.
On such a hot day, the cool water felt great!
深夜，一个哨兵在一个旧军事基地里巡逻。
“晚上真安静啊。” 哨兵自言自语，“我还是去办公室睡一会儿吧。” 
Late at night, a guard was patrolling an old army base.
"It's a quiet night," the guard said to himself. "I'd better go to the office and sleep for a while."
哨兵走到一栋楼房的拐角，大吃一惊。
“坏了！” 他叫道，“一辆坦克被偷了！” 
The guard went around the corner of a building and gasped.
"Oh no!" he cried. "One of the army tanks was stolen!"
“太好了！” 特勒尔说，“不用在教室里上课！” 
学校的花园里，罗西和朋友们正在帮格林老师的忙。
"This is great!" said Terrell. "No need to have classes in the classroom."
Roxy and her friends were in the school garden. They were helping Mr. Green.
“早上好！同学们！” 格林老师说，“今天会特别好玩儿。每个人都得有手套和铲子。” 
罗西和朋友们拿到了他们的园艺工具。
"Good morning, everybody!" said Mr. Green. "We're going to have lots of fun today. Everybody needs gardening gloves and a trowel."
Roxy and her friends got their gardening equipment.
杰克笑了。“我等不及把自己弄脏了！” 
“我这里有很多花种和菜种。” 格林老师说，“你们可以选自己想种的。只要付出时间和爱心，这些植物就会长大！” 
Jack grinned. "I can't wait to get dirty!"
"I have lots of seeds for flowers and vegetables," said Mr. Green. "Each of you can choose what you want to plant. With time and care, all the plants will grow!"
玛拉选了向日葵种子。“我喜欢向日葵。” 她说，“它们又大又阳光。” 
“我喜欢午餐的时候，吃新鲜的蔬菜。” 罗西说，“我要种胡萝卜和生菜。” 
Mara picked out some sunflower seeds. "I love sunflowers," she said. "They're so big and bright."
"I want fresh vegetables for lunch," said Roxy. "I'm going to plant carrots and lettuce."
杰克一脸不在乎。“谁要关心蔬菜！我只是喜欢挖土！” 
他把铲子插进土里，挖出一些土。他捡起一条蠕动的小蚯蚓。
Jack looked unconcerned. "Who cares about vegetables? I just like digging in the dirt!"
He stuck his trowel into the ground. He scooped out some soil. Then he picked up a wiggling, little worm.
“真酷！” 杰克拿起蚯蚓给朋友们看。
“呃……” 特勒尔说，“把它拿开！” 
“真恶心，杰克。” 玛拉说。
"Cool!" Jack held the worm out to his friends.
"Eww," said Terrell. "Keep that thing away from me!"
"That's gross, Jack," said Mara.
“蚯蚓很可爱。” 罗西说，“而且，它可以让土壤变得更肥沃。” 
玛拉和罗西挖土。“我等不及看向日葵开花了。” 玛拉说。
"Worms are cute," said Roxy. "Plus, they help the soil to stay healthy."
Mara and Roxy dug in the soil. "I can't wait until my sunflowers bloom," said Mara.
“你得先把它们种上！” 罗西笑着说。
“你们知道这个花园少了什么吗？” 杰克说，“一个水池！” 
“我希望是个有青蛙的水池。” 玛拉说，“还有几只乌龟。” 
"You have to plant them first!" Roxy laughed.
"You know what this garden needs?" said Jack. "A pond!"
"I want a pond with frogs in it," said Mara. "And maybe some turtles."
“也许火箭女孩儿能帮我们挖一个大水池！” 特勒尔说。
罗西转了转眼睛。“火箭女孩儿太忙了，特勒尔。她没时间挖水池。” 
特勒尔耸了耸肩。
"Maybe Rocket Girl can dig a big pond for us!" said Terrell.
Roxy rolled her eyes. "Rocket Girl is pretty busy, Terrell. She doesn't have time to dig a pond."
Terrell shrugged.
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。
罗西离开了朋友们。她按了一下手表上的按钮。
“布洛姆市长。” 罗西说，“有什么事吗？” 
Just then Roxy's watch beeped.
Roxy stepped away from her friends. She pressed a button on her watch.
"Mayor Bloom," said Roxy. "What's wrong?"
“火箭女孩儿！” 布洛姆市长说，“有人抢劫了美罗城中央银行！” 
“别担心，市长！” 罗西说，“我很快就到！” 
"Rocket Girl!" said Mayor Bloom. "Somebody is robbing Metro City Central Bank!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "I'm on my way!"
“我得去美罗城中央银行。” 罗西想，“有人在那抢劫。” 
她跑向格林老师。
"I have to get to Metro City Central Bank," thought Roxy. "Somebody is robbing it!"
She ran over to Mr. Green.
“格林老师。” 罗西说，“我刚想起来了，潘校长说……嗯……想要和我谈谈。” 
“你去吧，罗西。” 格林老师说。
罗西很快就飞上了天空。
"Mr. Green," said Roxy. "I just remembered something. Principal Penn wanted to, um, talk to me."
"Go ahead, Roxy," said Mr. Green.
A moment later Roxy shot through the air.
“你们看！” 玛拉叫道，“火箭女孩儿！” 
特勒尔挠挠头。“罗西去哪里了？” 
罗西到了美罗城中央银行。警车包围了大楼。
"Look!" cried Mara. "Rocket Girl!"
Terrell scratched his head. "Where did Roxy go?"
Roxy arrived at Metro City Central Bank. Police cars surrounded the building.
银行的大门被砸破了，有浓烟从里面冒出来。街对面站着一堆人。
“火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探叫道。
罗西飞向侦探。
The bank's front doors were smashed. Smoke poured out of them. A crowd of people stood across the street.
"Rocket Girl!" called Detective Smith.
Roxy flew over to the detective.
“您是要存支票吗，侦探先生？” 罗西笑着问。
史密斯皱着眉头。“这不好笑，火箭女孩儿。这儿发生了抢劫！” 
“我知道。” 罗西说，“抢劫犯还在银行里吗？” 
"Are you trying to deposit a check, Detective?" Roxy grinned.
Detective Smith frowned. "This isn't funny, Rocket Girl. A robbery is taking place!"
"I know," said Roxy. "Is the bank robber still in the bank?"
史密斯侦探点点头。“我觉得是。” 
“您知道是谁吗？” 罗西问。
人群中一个女人站了出来。“你是想问他是‘什么’吧？” 
Detective Smith nodded. "I think so."
"Do you know who he is?" asked Roxy.
A woman in the crowd stepped forward. "Do you mean 'what' he is?"
罗西不明白。
“我看见那个抢劫犯了。” 那个女人说，“他看起来像一台巨型机器！” 
“的确是。” 一个穿西装的男人说。
Roxy was confused.
"I saw the robber," said the woman. "He looks like a giant machine!"
"It's true," said a man in a suit.
“他穿着又大又重的盔甲。看起来像是军队里的坦克！” 
“嗯……” 史密斯侦探说，“这肯定跟美罗城军事基地的案件有关。” 
“军事基地发生了什么事？” 罗西问。
"He is wearing big, heavy armor. He looks like an army tank!"
"Hmm," said Detective Smith. "This must be connected to the crime at Metro City army base."
"What happened at the army base?" asked Roxy.
“有人偷走了坦克。” 侦探说，“发生在几天前的晚上。” 
“我要出去了！” 一个很粗的声音在银行里吼道，“你们最好都给我让开！” 
"Somebody stole a tank," said the detective. "It happened a few days ago at night."
"I'm coming out!" shouted a deep voice from inside the bank. "Everybody better stay out of my way!"
史密斯侦探举起喊话器。“银行被包围了。举着手出来吧！” 
“哈哈！” 那个声音笑着。
Detective Smith picked up a megaphone. "The bank is surrounded. Come out with your hands up!"
"Ha-ha!" The deep voice laughed.
“我叫汉克坦克，我是美罗城最厉害的犯人。谁都别想阻止我。我现在要带着所有的钱出去了！” 
罗西听到银行里面传来沉重的脚步声。
"My name is Hank Tank, and I'm the toughest criminal in Metro City. Nobody can stop me. I'm coming out now with all the money I stole!"
Roxy heard heavy footsteps inside the bank.
哐！哐！哐！大楼和街道都在震动。
人们四处逃散。
“抢劫犯出来了！” 女人尖叫道。
“快逃命啊！” 男人叫道。
Stomp, stomp, stomp! The building and street shook.
People ran in all different directions.
"The robber is coming out!" shouted a woman.
"Run for your lives!" cried a man.
史密斯侦探咽了一口口水。“汉克坦克听上去很大。” 
“是啊。” 罗西点头。
脚步声停住了。一时间一切变得很安静。
然后……哗啦！
Detective Smith gulped. "Hank Tank sounds pretty big."
"Yeah." Roxy nodded.
The footsteps stopped. For a moment everything was quiet.
Then—ka-boom!
有什么东西砸破了银行的墙壁。 
罗西挡在史密斯侦探前面。砖头和瓦片碰到罗西，又弹了回去。
Something smashed through the wall of the bank.
Roxy stood in front of Detective Smith. Bricks and rubble bounced off her.
烟尘散去后，罗西看到人行道上有一个巨大的男人。他全身都是盔甲，背上的盔甲又大又圆，像乌龟的壳。
When the dust cleared, Roxy saw a huge man on the sidewalk. His body was covered in armor. The armor on his back was huge and round, like a turtle shell.
男人手上拿着一个大袋子。罗西用她的X射线，看到袋子里面有钱。
汉克坦克认出罗西。“火箭女孩儿！” 他叫道，“你阻止不了我！” 
The man held a large bag. Using her x-ray vision, Roxy saw money inside the bag.
Hank Tank had spotted Roxy. "Rocket Girl!" he shouted. "You'll never stop me!"
罗西盯着坏蛋。“不，我能，汉克坦克！” 
“绝对不能！” 汉克坦克转身要跑。这时，他看到警车挡住了他的路。
他按了按胸前的按钮。“坦克模式！” 他叫道。
Roxy glared at the villain. "Yes, I will, Hank Tank!"
"Never!" Hank Tank turned to run. Then he saw all the police cars in his way.
He pressed a button on his chest. "Tank mode!" he shouted.
他的盔甲开始轰鸣。各个部件开始组装移动。橡胶轮胎伸了出来。汉克变成了一辆行进的军用坦克！
“坏了！” 史密斯侦探叫道。
His armor rumbled. Each part started to shift and move together. Rubber tank treads popped out. Hank was now a rolling army tank!
"Uh-oh!" cried Detective Smith.
“我猜这就是他偷军用坦克的原因了。” 罗西说，“用它来让自己变成坦克！” 
轰隆！轰隆！轰隆！嚓！嚓！嚓！汉克坦克从警车上开过去。咔擦！金属弯了，玻璃碎了。
"I guess this is why he stole that army tank," said Roxy. "He used it to turn himself into a tank!"
Brumm, brumm, brumm! Chug, chug, chug! Hank Tank rolled over the police cars. Crunch! Metal twisted. Windows shattered.
“哈哈！” 坏蛋在道路上边走边笑。他从邮箱上开过去。咔擦！他从热狗摊上开过去。哐！
“我的热狗全完了！” 卖热狗的人尖叫道。
"Ha-ha!" The villain laughed as he rolled down the street. He rolled over a mailbox. Crunch! He rolled over a hot dog stand. Smash!
"My hot dogs are all ruined" cried the hot dog man.
“我得阻止汉克坦克！” 罗西想。
她的眼睛发射出激光。嗞！
激光射在汉克坦克的外壳上，但是被反射回来，射中了广告牌子。广告牌子被炸开了。
"I have to stop Hank Tank!" thought Roxy.
She fired her eye laser beams. Whiz-hoo!
The beams hit Hank Tank's shell. But they bounced off and hit a billboard. The billboard exploded.
“哎呀！” 罗西说。
“你的激光对我的盔甲根本不管用，火箭女孩儿！” 汉克叫道。
哐！咔擦！汉克从更多的汽车和一辆出租车上开过去。
"Oops!" said Roxy.
"Your laser beams don't work on my armor, Rocket Girl! " shouted Hank.
Bash! Crunch! Hank drove over more cars and then a taxi.
罗西朝着汉克快速地飞过去。罗西伸出拳头。砰！汉克滑出路面，撞倒了一个红绿灯。
“你使劲儿打我啊，火箭女孩儿。” 汉克坦克说，“你绝对打不坏我的盔甲！” 
Roxy flew toward Hank fast. She held out her fist. Bam! Hank slid across the street and knocked over a traffic light.
"Hit me as hard as you want, Rocket Girl," said Hank Tank. "You'll never break my armor!"
“哼！” 罗西跺脚。她一次又一次飞向汉克坦克。哐！哐！
但是，汉克坦克继续向前移动。
“汉克的盔甲真是很坚固！” 罗西想，“要怎么阻止他呢？” 
"Grr!" Roxy stomped her foot. Then she flew at Hank again and again. Bam! Bam!
But Hank Tank kept rolling along.
"Hank's armor is really strong!" thought Roxy. "How will I stop him?"
汉克转身向罗西发射了一枚火箭。罗西抓住它并把它掰成了两半。
“哈！” 罗西说，“你的盔甲也许很坚固，但我是火箭女孩儿啊！没有什么能伤害我！哎呀！” 
Hank spun around and fired a rocket at Roxy. Roxy caught it and broke it in half.
"Ha!" said Roxy. "You armor might be very strong, but I am Rocket Girl! Nothing can hurt—oof!"
第二枚火箭射中了罗西。她砰的一声从空中掉了下来。
汉克坦克向罗西飞快地开过去。“我要从你身上开过去，火箭女孩儿！” 
A second rocket hit Roxy. She fell down with a thud.
Hank Tank sped toward her. "I'm going to run right over you, Rocket Girl!"
汉克坦克向罗西开过去。嗞！罗西向他的一个橡胶轮胎发射激光。
砰！轮胎爆炸了。
Hank Tank rolled toward Roxy. Whiz-hoo! She fired her eye laser beams at one of his rubber treads.
Boom! The tread exploded.
罗西站起来。
汉克想要移动，但是轮胎坏了，他动不了。他的身下冒出浓烟。
“人类模式！” 汉克叫道。
Roxy jumped to her feet.
Hank tried to move. But the tread was broken, and he couldn't move. Smoke poured out from under him.
"Human mode!" shouted Hank.
身体各部件组装移动。汉克重新站了起来。
他盯着罗西。“你会后悔弄坏了我的坦克的，火箭女孩儿！” 
汉克坦克扑上去，撞向罗西。哐！他们撞倒了一辆公交车。
All the parts on his body shifted and moved together. Hank stood up again.
He glared at Roxy. "You'll regret breaking my tank, Rocket Girl!"
Hank Tank charged. He slammed into Roxy. Bam! They knocked over a bus.
“啊！” 公交车司机大叫道。
“对不起！” 罗西说。她赶紧把公交车扶正。
汉克又撞向罗西。哐！公交车再次被撞倒。
"Ahh!" cried the bus driver.
"Sorry!" said Roxy. She quickly put the bus back on its wheels.
Hank slammed into Roxy again. Bam! The bus fell over again.
“啊!” 公交车司机再次大叫道。
罗西跳起来打了一拳。哐！汉克坦克被打中了。
“啊！” 汉克叫道。他掉进了一家商店的橱窗里，玻璃碎了。
"Ahh!" cried the bus driver again.
Roxy jumped to her feet and punched. Crack! Hank Tank was hit.
"Oof!" cried Hank. He crashed through a store window, and the glass broke.
罗西重新把公交车扶正。她看到汉克再一次向她扑过来。
罗西握紧了拳头。当汉克撞过来的时候，她打了过去。罗西和汉克同时往后退。罗西再一次撞在公交车上。
Roxy set the bus back up. Then she saw Hank charging toward her again.
Roxy made a fist. As Hank slammed into her, she punched. Roxy and Hank both flew backward. Again Roxy slammed into the bus.
“啊！” 公交车司机叫起来。
“呃！” 罗西想。“我该怎么阻止汉克坦克呢？” 
罗西刚要站起来的时候，汉克的大脚踩下来。 
“我要把你踩碎了，火箭女孩儿！” 汉克笑道。
"Ahh!" cried the bus driver.
"Ugh!" thought Roxy. "How am I going to stop Hank Tank?"
As Roxy tried to get up, Hank's big foot came down.
"I'm going to squash you, Rocket Girl!" Hank laughed.
罗西滚着躲开了。哐！汉克的脚踩碎了人行道。
罗西注意到汉克巨大的圆形外壳。“我有主意了。” 她想。
Roxy rolled out of the way. Stomp! Hank's foot cracked the pavement.
Roxy noticed Hank's large round shell. "I have an idea," she thought.
汉克的脚再次踩下来。罗西抓住这只脚并把它扔了出去。汉克向后倒下，圆形外壳着地。
汉克挥动着他的手和脚，但是他像一只四脚朝天的乌龟，起不来。
Hank's foot came down again. Roxy grabbed the foot and flung it up. Hank fell backward, landing on his round shell.
Hank waved his arms and legs. But he was stuck lying on his back, like a turtle.
“帮帮我！” 坏蛋叫道，“我起不来了！” 
史密斯侦探跟其他警官过来了。
罗西笑了。“你可以把汉克送进监狱了，侦探先生！” 
"Help!" cried the villain. "I can't get up!"
Detective Smith arrived with some other police officers.
Roxy smiled. "You can take Hank to jail, Detective!"
第二天，罗西再一次跟她的朋友们在学校花园里见面。
格林老师在分发手套。
“喂，你们看！” 玛拉说。她指着花园的对面说。“那里有个水池！” 
The next day Roxy and her friends were in the school garden again.
Mr. Green handed out gloves.
"Hey, look!" said Mara. She pointed at the opposite side of the garden. "It's a pond!"
“真棒！” 杰克说，“看起来像个大乌龟壳！” 
格林老师笑起来。“那个壳是一个坏蛋的盔甲。他昨天抢劫了银行。幸好火箭女孩儿抓住了他，并把这个壳送给学校。” 
"Cool!" said Jack. "It looks like a big turtle shell."
Mr. Green chuckled. "That shell was part of a bad guy's armor. He robbed a bank yesterday. Luckily, Rocket Girl caught him. She gave the shell to the school."
特勒尔笑了。“看见了吧，罗西？我就知道火箭女孩儿会给我们一个水池的！” 
罗西什么也没说，只是戴上手套准备挖土。
Terrell grinned. "See, Roxy? I knew Rocket Girl could get us a pond!"
Roxy didn't say anything. She just put on her gloves and started to dig.
一列火车在美罗城城外的轨道上疾驰。火车上运载着一些美罗城动物园的动物。
A train sped along the tracks outside Metro City. The train was carrying several animals from Metro City Zoo.
“这将是一次激动人心的动物园巡游。” 火车司机说。
“是的。” 乘务员说，“人们将会看到一些特别的动物。” 
"This will be an exciting zoo tour," said the train's engineer.
"That's right," said the conductor. "Lots of people will get to see the special animals from the zoo."
“大家一定会很喜欢蓝狒狒。” 司机说，“他是所有人的最爱……天啊！另一列火车开过来了。” 
 砰！ 
"People will really love Blue Baboon," said the engineer. "He's everybody's favorite—Oh no! Another train is coming!"
Crash!
罗西和朋友们在美罗城动物园。他们站在狒狒馆前面。罗西看到一座小山和许多树，但是没有看到狒狒。
Roxy and her friends were at Metro City Zoo. They were standing in front of the baboon exhibit. Roxy saw a small hill and lots of trees. But there was no baboon.
“蓝狒狒今天离开动物园去巡游了。” 玛拉说，“我已经开始想念它了！” 
“我也是。” 特勒尔说，“我希望它能早点回来。动物园没有它很没意思。” 
"Blue Baboon left for the zoo tour today," said Mara. "I miss him already!"
"Me too," said Terrell. "I hope he comes back soon. The zoo isn't much fun without him."
四个朋友参观飞禽馆。
“动物园里还有很多很棒的动物。” 罗西说。她指着一只颜色亮丽的鹦鹉。“我很喜欢鹦鹉皮特。” 
“你好！” 鹦鹉皮特说。
The four friends were watching the bird exhibit.
"The zoo still has lots of cool animals," said Roxy. She pointed at a brightly colored parrot. "I really like Parrot Pete."
"Hello," said Parrot Pete.
罗西咯咯笑。“你好！” 
“真棒！” 杰克说，“我看到秃鹫了！” 
玛拉叹了一口气。“这些鸟都很棒。不过，我最喜欢的动物还是蓝狒狒！” 
Roxy giggled. "Hello!"
"Cool!" said Jack. "I see vultures!"
Mara sighed. "All these birds are great. But Blue Baboon is my favorite animal."
“我也是。” 特勒尔说。
杰克耸耸肩。“几个月以后，他就会回来的。” 
特勒尔眼睛突然亮了起来。“我有一个好主意！” 他说。“我们可以让火箭女孩儿把蓝狒狒带回来！” 
"Mine too," said Terrell.
Jack shrugged. "He'll be back in a few months."
Terrell's eyes suddenly lit up. "I have a great idea!" he said. "We can ask Rocket Girl to bring Blue Baboon here!"
“那真是太好了！” 玛拉的拳头不停地伸向空中。“那样我们就不用想蓝狒狒了！” 
罗西转了一下眼睛。“我怀疑火箭女孩儿能不能做到，特勒尔。” 
"That would be great!" Mara pumped her fist in the air. "Then we wouldn't have to miss Blue Baboon at all!"
Roxy rolled her eyes. "I doubt Rocket Girl can do that, Terrell."
“为什么做不到？” 特勒尔问，“她飞得那么快！” 
“那是事实。” 罗西说，“不过火箭女孩儿不是出租车司机。她有更重要的事情要做。” 
特勒尔点点头。“是，你说得对。” 
"Why not?" asked Terrell. "She can fly really fast!"
"That's true," said Roxy. "But Rocket Girl isn't a taxi driver. She has more important things to do."
Terrell nodded. "Yeah, you're right."
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。罗西离开朋友们。确信他们都没有看到以后，她按了一下手表上的按钮。布洛姆市长的脸出现了。他看上去像是受到了惊吓。
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. She stepped away from her friends. She made sure they weren't looking and then pressed a button on the watch. Mayor Bloom's face appeared. He looked shocked.
“火箭女孩儿！” 布洛姆市长说，“刚刚发生了严重的火车相撞事故！” 
“天啊！” 罗西说，“在哪儿发生的？” 
“就在美罗城城外。” 布洛姆市长说。
"Rocket Girl!" said the mayor. "There's been a terrible train crash!"
"Oh no!" said Roxy. "Where did it happen?"
"Just outside Metro City," said Mayor Bloom.
“运载动物园动物的火车跟另一列火车相撞了。另一列火车上装满了危险的化学物质。我想我们需要你的帮助！” 
罗西咽了咽口水。“别担心，市长。我马上就到！” 
"The train carrying the zoo animals crashed into another train. The second train was loaded with dangerous chemicals. I think we need your help!"
Roxy gulped. "Don't worry, Mayor. I'm on my way!"
“那里发生了严重的火车相撞事故。” 罗西想。“我得去帮忙！” 
罗西跑回朋友们那里。“朋友们，我很快就回来。 我想……嗯……再去看一次鳄鱼！” 
"There was a big train crash," Roxy thought. "I have to help!"
Roxy ran back to her friends. "I'll be right back, guys. I want to go see the, um, crocodiles one more time!"
“等等！” 杰克对着已经跑掉的罗西叫道。“我们也去。我喜欢鳄鱼！” 
但是，罗西已经不见了。玛拉指着天空。“你们看！ 那是火箭女孩儿！” 
"Wait!" called Jack as Roxy ran off. "We'll come too. I love crocodiles!"
But Roxy was already gone. Mara pointed at the sky. "Look! It's Rocket Girl!"
罗西沿着火车轨道，一直飞到撞车现场。这里一片混乱。两列火车的车厢扭在一起。有的车厢里冒出奇怪的烟雾，在空中弥漫。
Roxy flew over the train tracks until she reached the scene of the crash. It was a huge mess. Cars from the two trains were jumbled together. Strange smoke poured from some cars and filled the air.
动物园的动物们到处乱跑。警察和饲养员正在抓它们。 
火箭女孩儿落到史密斯侦探身旁。
Zoo animals were running in every direction. Police officers and a zookeeper were trying to catch them.
Rocket Girl landed next to Detective Smith.
“您的玩具火车出了什么问题吗？侦探先生。” 她问。
“哈哈。” 史密斯侦探假笑道，“现在不是开玩笑的时候，火箭女孩儿！” 
“我知道。” 罗西说，“有人受伤吗？” 
"Is there trouble with your train set, Detective?" she asked.
"Ha-ha." Detective Smith pretended to laugh. "This is no time for jokes, Rocket Girl."
"I know," said Roxy. "Was anybody hurt?"
史密斯侦探摇摇头。“庆幸的是没有人或者动物受伤。不过动物们都跑掉了。” 他咳嗽起来。“这个烟雾很可怕。消防员也无法消除。” 
Detective Smith shook his head. "Luckily no people or animals were hurt. But now the animals are escaping." He coughed. "And this smoke is terrible. The firefighters can't get rid of it."
罗西看看四周。两名消防员正拿着水管向火车喷水。但是，烟雾还是很浓。
罗西深吸了一口气，然后尽最大力气吹出去。呼！她的超级呼吸把烟雾吹散了。
Roxy looked around. Two firefighters were spraying the train cars with a hose. But the smoke was still thick.
Roxy took a deep breath. Then she blew as hard as she could. Whoosh! Her super breath blew away the smoke.
“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿。” 饲养员说，“现在我们能看见动物，去抓它们了！” 
当饲养员和警察追赶动物的时候，罗西拎起火车车厢。她把它们一一放回轨道。
"Thank you, Rocket Girl," said the zookeeper. "Now we can see the animals and catch them!"
As the zookeeper and police officers chased animals, Roxy picked up train cars. She put them back on the tracks, one by one.
史密斯侦探带着一只巨嘴鸟回来了。“我想我们已经抓回了所有的动物。” 他说。
“让我们数一数来确认一下。” 饲养员说。
Detective Smith came over with a toucan. "I think we caught all the animals," he said.
"Let's count them to make sure," said the zookeeper.
饲养员一边数，一边在板夹的纸上做记录。当他数完以后，挠了挠头。“还有一只动物没找到。” 
然后他大吃一惊。“蓝狒狒去哪里了？” 
The zookeeper counted the animals. He made notes on a clipboard. When he was done, he scratched his head. "One animal is still missing."
Then he gasped. "Where's Blue Baboon?"
突然，一声吼叫震动了大地。“哇呜！哇呜！” 
饲养员皱起眉头。“听起来好像是蓝狒狒的声音。” 他说，“不过吵多了。” 
罗西点点头。“也大多了！” 
Suddenly a loud sound shook the ground. "Wah-hu! Wah-hu!"
The zookeeper frowned. "That sounds like Blue Baboon," he said. "But louder."
Roxy nodded. "And bigger!"
哐，哐，哐！大地再次震动起来。所有人都往声音发出的方向看过去。一团巨大的化学烟雾正在穿越农场。哐，哐，哐！
Stomp, stomp, stomp! The ground shook again. Everyone turned to look toward the sound. A huge cloud of chemical smoke moved across a farm field. Stomp, stomp, stomp!
“化学烟雾里面好像有什么东西。” 史密斯侦探说，“你认为是……?” 
饲养员的板夹掉在地上。“蓝狒狒！” 
"There's something inside that chemical cloud," said Detective Smith. "Do you think it's . . . ?"
The zookeeper dropped his clipboard. "Blue Baboon!"
罗西看到化学烟雾穿过更多的农场土地。沉重的脚步声震动着大地。
“我不知道蓝狒狒是不是就在那团烟雾里。” 罗西说，“但是，它正往美罗城的方向走。我得阻止它！” 
Roxy watched the chemical smoke move across more farm fields. The sound of heavy footsteps shook the ground.
"I don't know if Blue Baboon is in that smoke," said Roxy. "But it's heading straight toward Metro City. I have to stop it!"
罗西快速地飞向那团化学烟雾。它现在正在曼先生的玉米地里。她深吸了一口气，然后吐出。呼！
Roxy flew fast toward the chemical cloud. It was now in Mr. Mann's cornfield. She took a deep breath and then blew. Whoosh!
一只巨大的手从烟雾中伸出来，打了罗西一下。砰！她在空中翻滚。当罗西落地的时候，那团烟雾不见了。
A huge hand popped out of the cloud and smacked Roxy. Whack! She tumbled through the air. By the time she landed, the cloud was gone.
一只巨大的狒狒站在地里， 身上都是亮晶晶的化学物质。狒狒在挠痒。它看上去很生气。
“天啊！” 罗西说。“那肯定是蓝狒狒。不过它有大楼那么高！肯定是化学物质让它长高的！” 
An enormous baboon, covered in glowing chemicals, stood in the field. The baboon was scratching himself. He looked angry.
"Oh boy," said Roxy. "That's definitely Blue Baboon. But he's as tall as a building! The chemicals must have made him grow!"
“哇呜！哇呜！” 蓝狒狒吼叫。大狒狒挠了挠它的身子，然后走向罗西。狒狒的嘴张得大大的，露出又大又尖的牙。
"Wah-hu! Wah-hu!" Blue Baboon barked. The giant baboon scratched his body and then stomped toward Roxy. He opened his mouth wide, showing his huge and sharp fangs.
“天啊！” 罗西叫道。
蓝狒狒狠狠打向罗西，罗西快速躲开了。狒狒再一次吼叫起来。他挠着痒， 一脚踩向曼先生的仓库。
"Uh-oh!" Roxy cried.
Blue Baboon swatted at Roxy, who quickly dodged the blow. The baboon barked again. Then he scratched and stomped on Mr. Mann's barn.
哗啦！仓库变得粉碎。
曼先生从屋里跑了出来。“出什么事了，我的……？” 他抬头看到蓝狒狒。
Smash! The barn shattered into tiny pieces.
Mr. Mann ran out of his house. "What happened to my—?" He looked up and saw Blue Baboon.
“啊！” 曼先生跑进屋子，躲在床下面。
“哇呜！哇呜！” 蓝狒狒生气地吼叫着。它跺着脚，挠着痒。“哇呜！哇呜！” 
罗西看到蓝狒狒在挠肩膀。
"Aah!" Mr. Mann ran back into his house and hid under his bed.
"Wah-hu! Wah-hu!" Blue Baboon barked angrily. He stomped. He scratched. "Wah-hu! Wah-hu!"
Roxy watched Blue Baboon scratch his shoulder.
然后，它转过身，跺着脚，穿过地里。它正往美罗城方向走去。
“我不能让蓝狒狒到美罗城去！” 罗西想，“它会毁了美罗城所有的大楼的！” 
Then he turned around and stomped across the field. He was heading toward Metro City again.
"I can't let Blue Baboon reach Metro City!" Roxy thought. "He'll destroy every building in the city!"
罗西飞向大狒狒。她双手抱住狒狒的脚。她的身上沾满了亮晶晶的化学物质。
“哇呜！” 蓝狒狒猛地抬起脚。它挣脱了罗西，又使劲儿踢了她一脚。
Roxy flew after the giant baboon. She wrapped her arms around his foot. Glowing chemicals got all over her.
"Wah-hu!" Blue Baboon jerked his foot. He shook Roxy off. Then he kicked her hard.
罗西从空中掉了下来，撞在一辆拖拉机上。“哎呦！” 
罗西站起来，满身都是亮晶晶的化学物质。她挠了一下痒。接着又挠了几下。
Roxy sailed through the air and crashed into a tractor. "Oof!"
She stood up, still covered in the glowing chemicals. She scratched. Then she scratched some more.
“呃！” 罗西的脸变红了。“我为什么这么痒呢？” 她跺着脚，不停地挠。
罗西咬着牙。“啊！太可怕了！我痒死了。我变得越来越生气了！” 
"Grr!" Roxy's face turned red. "Why am I so itchy?" She stomped her foot and scratched some more.
Roxy gritted her teeth. "Ack! This is awful! It's too itchy. I'm getting really, really angry!"
罗西全身都是亮晶晶的化学物质。
“我得洗掉这些化学物质！” 罗西想，“它们让我变得又痒又生气！” 
Roxy was covered in glowing chemicals.
"I have to wash these chemicals off!" thought Roxy. "They're making me itchy—and angry!"
罗西想起火车事故现场的消防车。“消防员可以用水管往我身上喷水。” 罗西想。
哐，哐，哐！
“哇呜！哇呜！” 蓝狒狒继续往美罗城方向走。
She remembered the fire trucks back at the train crash. "The firefighters can spray me with the hose," thought Roxy.
Stomp, stomp, stomp!
"Wah-hu! Wah-hu!" Blue Baboon was still walking toward Metro City.
“我得快点行动！” 罗西自言自语地说。她在空中飞的时候，化学物质进到了她的眼睛里。罗西差点儿碰到了电线，又差点儿撞在火车车厢上。最后，罗西落在史密斯侦探身旁。
"I need to move fast!" Roxy said to herself. As Roxy flew through the sky, chemicals got into her her eyes. She almost crashed into some power lines. Then she almost plowed into a train car. Finally she landed near Detective Smith.
“帮帮我！” 罗西叫道，“这些化学物质太可怕了！真的好痒啊！” 
“天啊！” 史密斯侦探说，“我怎么帮你？” 
“告诉消防员让他们向我喷水！” 罗西说。
"Help!" Roxy cried. "These chemicals are awful! They're really, really itchy!"
"Oh no!" said the detective. "How can I help?"
"Tell the firefighters to blast me with the hose!" said Roxy.
“知道了！” 侦探说。
消防员用水管对着罗西喷水。很快，所有的化学物质都洗掉了。
“咻！” 罗西叹了口气。“现在好多了。” 
"Right!" said the detective.
The firefighters shot water at Roxy with the hose. A moment later all the chemicals were gone.
"Whew!" Roxy sighed. "That's better."
突然，她意识到了什么。“我知道蓝狒狒为什么那么生气了！化学物质让它发痒！” 
罗西举起消防车。“我要借一下这个。” 罗西对消防员说。
Then she realized something. "I know why Blue Baboon is so angry! He's itchy from all the chemicals!"
Roxy picked up the fire truck. "I need to borrow this," she told the firefighters.
她向蓝狒狒飞去。现在，蓝狒狒已经到了市内。“哇呜！哇呜！” 
人们边跑边喊。
“一只大狒狒！” 
She flew after Blue Baboon. By now he had reached the city. "Wah-hu! Wah-hu!"
People ran and screamed.
"It's a big baboon!"
“快逃命啊！” 
“救救我们，火箭女孩儿！” 
哗！罗西把消防车里的水倒在蓝狒狒身上。所有的化学物质都被洗掉了。
"Run for your lives!"
"Save us, Rocket Girl!"
Splash! Roxy dumped the fire truck's water on Blue Baboon. All the chemicals washed off.
蓝狒狒不再发光。它不再跺脚。它也不再挠痒。蓝狒狒坐下来，闭上了眼睛。它看起来心情好多了。
Blue Baboon stopped glowing. He stopped stomping. And he stopped scratching. The big baboon sat down and closed his eyes. He looked much happier.
“耶！” 罗西叫道，“蓝狒狒不再生气了，但是它还是很大。它没办法继续巡游了。它也不能回动物园了。“嗯……” 罗西敲着下巴开始思考。
"Yay!" Roxy cried. "Blue Baboon isn't angry anymore. But he's still a giant. There's no way he can go on the tour now. And he can't return to the zoo either. Hmm . . ." Roxy tapped her chin and thought.
一个月以后，罗西和她的朋友们在杰克家看电视。
玛拉笑了。“当我发现蓝狒狒没有回到动物园的时候很难过。但是，现在我一点都不难过了。” 
A month later Roxy and her friends were watching TV at Jack's house.
Mara grinned. "I was sad when we found out Blue Baboon wasn't returning to the zoo. But I'm not sad anymore."
“我也不难过了。” 杰克说，“这样更好！” 
“电影开始了。” 特勒尔说。
电影名字出现在屏幕上：蓝狒狒拯救地球！
"Me neither," said Jack. "This is much better!"
"The movie is starting," said Terrell.
A movie title appeared on the screen: Blue Baboon Saves the World!
“真棒！” 杰克说，“我很高兴火箭女孩儿把蓝狒狒送到了好莱坞。现在，它变成大明星了！” 
"Awesome," said Jack. "I'm glad Rocket Girl brought Blue Baboon to Hollywood. Now he's a famous movie star!"
“火箭女孩儿真了不起。” 罗西说。
特勒尔怀疑地看着罗西。罗西只是笑笑，伸手去拿碗里的爆米花。
"Rocket Girl sure is amazing," said Roxy.
Terrell gave her a suspicious look. Roxy just smiled, and then reached into the bowl for more popcorn.
一个春天的早晨。一个女人开车去上班。
“希望我不要迟到。” 她说，“我可不想被解雇！” 
It was a spring morning. A woman was driving to work.
"I hope I'm not late," she said. "I don't want to be fired!"
女人把车停在了工地外面。她向大门跑去。
“糟糕！” 女人说，“我把午餐忘在车里了。” 
The woman parked her car outside a construction site. She ran toward the gate.
"Oh no!" said the woman. "I left my lunch in the car!"
突然，地面震动起来。一个大洞出现了，车开始下沉！
女人大吃一惊。“我的车！” 
Suddenly the ground rumbled! A hole appeared, and the car began to sink!
The woman gasped. "My car!"
罗西和朋友们正在去足球训练的路上。
“我喜欢春天。” 杰克说。
“那是因为你喜欢足球。” 玛拉说。
杰克笑了。“我就是喜欢在外面玩儿。” 
Roxy and her friends were walking to soccer practice.
"I love spring," said Jack.
"That's because you love soccer," said Mara.
Jack grinned. "I just like playing outside."
“有谁不喜欢在外面玩儿吗？” 特勒尔说。
“我敢肯定火箭女孩儿是个很棒的足球运动员。” 杰克说。
“没人踢得过她。” 特勒尔说。
玛拉笑了。“她守门的同时还能进球！” 
"Who doesn't like playing outside?" Terrell asked.
"I bet Rocket Girl is an awesome soccer player," said Jack.
"Nobody could beat her," said Terrell.
Mara smiled. "She could score even while playing goalie!"
特勒尔做出踢球的样子。“她能一脚把球踢过所有的防守。” 
“穿过整个球场！” 杰克说。
“跟火箭女孩儿踢球不公平。” 罗西说。
Terrell pretended to kick a ball. "She could kick the ball past everyone at one shot."
"Down the whole field!" said Jack.
"It wouldn't be fair for Rocket Girl to play," said Roxy.
“她有很多超能力。你们想跟她比赛吗？” 
“火箭女孩儿一定要跟我们一个队！” 特勒尔说。
四个朋友来到了学校足球场。
"She has super powers. Would you want to play against her?"
"Rocket Girl would be on our team!" said Terrell.
The four friends arrived at the school's soccer field.
“对不起，同学们。” 尼科尔教练大声说。她看起来很不高兴。“今天不训练。” 
杰克皱着眉头。“为什么不训练？” 
“真奇怪。” 尼科尔教练指着身后说，“器材室不见了。我们所有的足球都在里面。” 
“嗯？” 特勒尔说。
"Sorry, kids," Coach Nicole called out. She looked upset. "No practice today."
Jack frowned. "Why not?"
"It's so strange," Coach Nicole said, pointing behind her. "The equipment shed is missing. And all our soccer balls were inside."
"Huh?" said Terrell.
罗西和朋友们往教练指的地方看过去。
“哇！” 杰克说，“地上有一个大洞！” 
Roxy and her friends looked at the spot where the coach was pointing.
"Whoa!" said Jack. "There's a big hole in the ground!"
“这是一个陷坑。” 教练说，“我猜器材室掉进那个坑里了。” 
玛拉叹了口气。“有办法把器材室取出来吗？” 
“火箭女孩儿可以。” 特勒尔说。
"It's a sinkhole," said the coach. "I guess the shed fell into it."
Mara sighed. "Is there any way to get the shed back out?"
"Rocket Girl could do it," said Terrell.
“我觉得火箭女孩儿有更重要的事情要做。” 罗西说。“她不能整天去找掉下去的器材室。” 
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。她离开了朋友们，按了一下按钮。
"I think Rocket Girl has more important things to do," said Roxy. "She can't look for the sunken equipment shed all day long."
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. She moved away from her friends and pressed a button.
“我们有麻烦了，火箭女孩儿。” 布洛姆市长说，“美罗城到处都是陷坑！” 
“学校的足球场也出现了一个陷坑。” 罗西说，“器材室掉进里面去了。” 
"We have a problem, Rocket Girl," said Mayor Bloom. "Sinkholes are appearing all over Metro City!"
"A sinkhole appeared at the school's soccer field too," said Roxy. "The equipment shed sank into it."
“你得做点什么。” 市长说，“所有新工地上的车辆都不见了！” 
“别担心，市长。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿很快就到!” 
"You must do something," said the mayor. "All the vehicles at the new construction site are gone!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl is on her way!"
“我得赶到工地。” 罗西想。“我得查出是什么引起陷坑出现的！” 
"I have to rush to the construction site," Roxy thought. "I have to find out what's causing the sinkholes!"
罗西对着朋友们大声喊。“嗨，朋友们！我很快就回来。我……嗯……忘了带护膝！” 她飞快地从足球场跑开了。
She called over to her friends. "Hey, guys! I'll be back. I, um, forgot my shin guards!" She hurried away from the soccer field.
“你不需要护膝！” 特勒尔在她身后喊。“我们没有足球训练！” 
罗西已经不见了。很快，火箭女孩儿像闪电一样划过天空。
"But you don't need them!" Terrell called after her. "We're not having soccer practice!"
Roxy was already gone. A second later Rocket Girl flashed through the sky.
“你们看！” 玛拉说，“是火箭女孩儿！” 
罗西飞过美罗城。她看到到处都是大洞。它们看起来像是巨型鼹鼠洞。
"Look!" cried Mara. "It's Rocket Girl!"
Roxy flew over Metro City. She saw large holes everywhere. They looked like giant gopher holes.
她看到史密斯侦探在工地上。他正跟两个工人说话。在他旁边有一栋还没有完工的大楼。整个工地到处都是大洞。
She spotted Detective Smith at the construction site. He was talking to two workers. Nearby stood a building that wasn't yet finished. The entire site was filled with large holes.
罗西落在史密斯侦探身旁。“这里有什么事吗，侦探先生？” 她笑着问，“您是在挖宝藏吗？” 
Roxy landed next to the detective. "What's going on here, Detective?" she asked with a grin. "Are you digging for treasure?"
史密斯皱着眉头。“这不好笑，火箭女孩儿。美罗城里正在发生一些奇怪的事情。” 
“我知道。” 罗西说，“到处都是大陷坑。有人知道是什么引起的吗？” 
Detective Smith frowned. "That's not funny, Rocket Girl. Something very strange is happening in Metro City."
"I know," said Roxy. "Big sinkholes are everywhere. Does anyone know what caused them?"
“完全不知道。” 史密斯侦探说，“但是，我们得马上查出来。东西掉进坑里不见了！” 
“所有工地上的车辆都不见了，对吧？” 罗西说。
"We have no idea," said the detective. "But we need to find out right away. Things are disappearing into the holes!"
"All the vehicles from this construction site are missing, right?" said Roxy.
“对！” 一个工人说。“所有的卡车，吊车和推土机都不见了！” 
“我的车也不见了。” 另一个工人说。她看上去很震惊。
"Yep," said one of the workers. "Every dump truck, crane, and bulldozer!"
"My car is gone too," said the other worker. She looked frightened.
“它掉进地底下了！” 她指着附近一个大洞说。
“你亲眼看到的吗？” 史密斯侦探问。
那个工人点点头。“先是听到很大的轰鸣声。地面震动起来。感觉像一场小地震，然后这个洞就出现了。我的车刚好掉进去了！” 
"It just sank into the ground!" She pointed to a big hole nearby.
"Did you see it happen?" asked Detective Smith.
The worker nodded. "First there was a loud rumble. The ground shook. It felt like a small earthquake. Then the hole appeared. My car just sank right into it!"
突然，轰隆！轰隆！地面剧烈地震动起来。
“天啊！” 史密斯侦探叫道，“地震了！” 
大楼晃动起来。一块大钢板掉下来。
Suddenly—rumble, rumble! The ground shook violently.
"Oh no!" cried Detective Smith. "It's an earthquake!"
The building wobbled. A big piece of steel fell from it.
“小心！” 罗西叫道。
史密斯侦探和工人们跑开了。罗西飞起来接住了钢板。
“咻！” 罗西把钢板安全地放在地上以后松了口气。
"Look out!" Roxy cried.
Detective Smith and the workers ran out of the way. Roxy flew up and caught the piece of steel.
"Whew!" After Roxy laid it safely on the ground, she breathed a sigh of relief.
“火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探在吵闹的轰鸣中喊道，“你认为是什么引起地震的？” 
“我不知道！” 罗西大声回答，“但是，我们得查出来……” 
"Rocket Girl!" Detective Smith called over the loud rumble. "What do you think is causing this earthquake?"
"I don't know!" Roxy called back. "But we need to find out . . ."
罗西突然不说话了。她用超级听力听到一个新的声音。吵闹的轰鸣声中，她听到意想不到的……说话的声音！
Roxy stopped talking. She heard a new sound with her super hearing. Through the loud rumble, she heard something very unexpected—voices!
罗西继续听地下传来的声音。“我听到地在动的声音。” 她想，“地下好像有一台大机器。又听到那些说话的声音了。它们是从哪里来的呢？” 
Roxy kept listening to the underground sounds. "I hear the ground shaking," she thought. "There seems to be a big machine underground. Plus those voices again. Where are they coming from?"
罗西看着史密斯侦探和建筑工人。“所有人，都往后退！” 她说。
罗西像一只陀螺一样开始旋转。她的脚下出现一个洞。沥青块飞得到处都是。
Roxy looked at Detective Smith and the construction workers. "Everyone, stand back!" she said.
Roxy started to spin like a top. A hole formed under her feet. Pieces of blacktop flew everywhere.
她越转越快，以极快的速度钻进地下。
“火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探叫道，“你在干什么？” 
She went faster and faster, drilling into the ground at super speed.
"Rocket Girl!" called Detective Smith. "What are you doing?"
但是，罗西没有回答。她已经到了很深的地下了。
罗西来到一个巨大的黑洞里。
“你们看！有一个人类！” 轰鸣声中一个声音大叫道。
But Roxy didn't answer. She was already deep underground.
Roxy arrived in a huge dark cave.
"Look! A human!" shouted a voice over the loud rumble.
黑暗中，罗西用她的超级视力，看到几个小矮人。他们长着鼹鼠的脸，穿着棕色的工作服。
Using her super vision to see in the dark, Roxy spotted several tiny men. They had mole-like faces and wore brown jumpsuits.
那些人站在一台大机器旁边。机器看上去像是用卡车零件和其他建筑设备组装的。
“你们是谁？” 罗西生气地问。
The men stood next to a big machine. It looked like it was built out of truck parts and other construction equipment.
"Who are you?" Roxy asked angrily.
其中一个男人拉了一下操作杆，机器停止了运作。“我们是鼹鼠人！” 他说，“我们打算毁了美罗城！” 
罗西咽了一口口水。“你们为什么要那么做？” 
One of the men pulled a lever, and the machine stopped running. "We're the mole men!" he said. "And we're going to destroy Metro City!"
Roxy gulped. "Why do you want to do that?"
鼹鼠人生气地看着罗西。“我们讨厌人类在这里挖下水道和地铁。地下只能是我们鼹鼠人的！” 他看着其他鼹鼠人，“抓住她！” 
The mole man glared at Roxy angrily. "We're sick of humans digging sewers and subways down here. The underground is for mole men only!" He looked at the other mole men. "Grab her!"
两个鼹鼠人跑向罗西，向她挥动着铁管。
罗西跳着躲开了。鼹鼠人撞到洞穴的墙壁上。
“哎呦！” 其中一个喊道。
Two mole men ran toward Roxy, swinging iron pipes at her.
Roxy jumped out of the way. The mole men crashed into the cave wall.
"Ouch!" one cried.
嗖！另一个鼹鼠人挥动着铁管。
“哎哟！” 第一个鼹鼠人又叫起来。
“哎呀！” 另一个鼹鼠人说。
Whap! The other one swung his pipe.
"Ouch!" the first one cried again.
"Oops!" said the other.
两个鼹鼠人看了看四周。“她去哪里了？” 他们问。
“这些鼹鼠人看不太清楚。” 罗西想，“就像真正的鼹鼠一样！” 
The two mole men looked around. "Where did she go?" they asked.
"These mole men don't see very well," Roxy thought. "Just like real moles!"
“她在那里！” 一个鼹鼠人指着罗西说，“抓住她！” 
更多的鼹鼠人向罗西跑去。
“地下不能有人类！” 一个鼹鼠人大声说。
"There she is!" One mole man pointed at Roxy. "Get her!"
More mole men ran toward Roxy.
"No humans underground!" shouted one mole man.
“地下只能是鼹鼠人的！” 第二个鼹鼠人说。
罗西再一次跳着躲开了。所有的鼹鼠人撞在一起。他们被绊倒，撞在了墙上。
"The underground is for mole men only!" shouted a second mole man.
Again Roxy jumped out of the way. All the mole men bumped into one another. They tripped and crashed into the wall.
一个鼹鼠人仍然站在地震机器前面。他拉下操作杆，机器发出吵闹的轰鸣声。
嗞！机器发射出一道强烈的光线。光线炸毁了洞穴的顶部，一块块大石头向罗西砸下来。
One mole man was still near the earthquake machine. He pulled the lever, and the machine rumbled loudly.
Zap! A ray shot from the machine. It blasted the ceiling of the cave, and big rocks crashed down onto Roxy!
罗西被埋在一大堆石头下面。
“幸好我是火箭女孩儿。” 罗西想，“我一点儿都没受伤。不过我要怎么去阻止鼹鼠人破坏美罗城呢？” 
Roxy was buried under a huge pile of rocks.
"It's a good thing I'm Rocket Girl," thought Roxy. "I didn't get hurt at all. But how will I stop the mole men from destroying Metro City?"
罗西想了一会儿。“我有办法了！” 
罗西再一次快速旋转。她钻到洞穴下面。罗西仔细听。她听到了上面鼹鼠人的声音。
She thought for a moment. "I have an idea!"
Again Roxy spun fast. She drilled into the ground below the cave. Roxy listened carefully. She heard the mole men above her.
“那个人类去哪里了？” 一个鼹鼠人问。
“我把她困在那堆石头下面了！” 机器旁边的鼹鼠人说。
罗西用她的X射线往上看。
"Where did the human go?" one asked.
"I trapped her under that pile of rocks!" said the mole man near the machine.
Roxy looked up, using her x-ray vision.
她看到鼹鼠人开始在石堆里翻找。罗西还看到了地震机器的底部。
“我得毁了那台机器。” 罗西想。
罗西朝机器冲上去。
She saw the mole men start searching through the pile of rocks. She could also see the bottom of the earthquake machine.
"I need to destroy that machine," thought Roxy.
She blasted up toward the machine.
哐！
罗西冲破洞穴地面， 毁了机器。
“她毁了我们的地震机器！” 一个鼹鼠人叫道。
Boom!
Roxy burst through the cave's floor and smashed the machine to pieces.
"She destroyed our earthquake machine!" cried a mole man.
“抓住她！” 另一个鼹鼠人喊道。
鼹鼠人冲向罗西。罗西飞上天空。鼹鼠人挥动着铁管，互相撞在了一起。哐！
"Get her!" shouted another one.
The mole men rushed toward Roxy. Roxy flew up into the air. The mole men ran straight into one another, swinging their pipes. Crash!
“哎呦！你打到我了！” 一个鼹鼠人大叫。
“对不起！我没有……啊！谁打了我的头？” 另一个鼹鼠人说。
“哎呀！” 第三个鼹鼠人说。“我以为是你……哎呦！” 
鼹鼠人打架的时候，罗西看了看洞穴四周。
"Ouch! You hit me!" cried one.
"Sorry! I didn't—oof! Who hit my head?" said another.
"Oops!" said a third. "I thought you were—ouch!"
As the mole men fought, Roxy glanced around the cave.
她看到了轮胎，铁管和别的东西。她还看到了一些电线。她拿着电线迅速把鼹鼠人捆起来。
“放了我们！” 一个鼹鼠人大叫道。
She saw tires, pipes, and other items. She then saw some electrical wire. She grabbed the wire and quickly tied up the mole men.
"Let us go!" shouted one mole man.
“你不能这样对我们。” 另一个鼹鼠人叫道。“地下是鼹鼠人的！” 
“你们最好习惯在地上生活。” 罗西说，“因为我要把你们送进监狱！” 
"You can't do this to us," cried another. "The underground belongs to the mole men!"
"You'd better get used to living above ground," said Roxy. "Because I'm taking you to jail!"
特勒尔、杰克，还有玛拉正要离开足球场。他们听到了轰鸣声，转过头去。器材室突然从地下冒出来，紧跟着……
“火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉大叫道。
Terrell, Jack, and Mara were walking away from the soccer field. They heard a rumble and looked back. The equipment shed popped out of the ground, followed by . . .
"Rocket Girl!" cried Mara.
过了一会儿，罗西回到了足球场。玛拉，特勒尔和杰克正在练球。尼科尔教练看着罗西，向她挥挥手。
“哇！” 罗西说，“器材室找回来了！” 
Later Roxy returned to the soccer field. Mara, Terrell, and Jack were practicing soccer. Coach Nicole spotted Roxy and waved.
"Wow!" said Roxy. "The equipment shed is back!"
“你猜是谁找回来的？” 特勒尔说，“是火箭女孩儿！” 
“真的？” 罗西假装不知道，“我想我错了，特勒尔。火箭女孩儿是可以从地下取出器材室的。” 
"Guess who got it back?" said Terrell. "Rocket Girl!"
"Really?" Roxy pretended she didn't know. "I guess I was wrong, Terrell. Rocket Girl was able to get the shed out of the ground!"
特勒尔怀疑地看着罗西。
罗西笑了。她拿起一个足球，准备往球场上运球。
Terrell gave her a suspicious look.
Roxy smiled. She grabbed a soccer ball and started to dribble it down the field.
“这些车真不错！” 布洛姆市长说。
  布洛姆市长在美罗城车展上。会展中心到处都是车。
一个穿实验服的男人走上台阶。
"These cars are very fancy!" said Mayor Bloom.
Mayor Bloom was at the Metro City Car Show. The convention center was filled with cars.
A man in a lab coat went up the steps.
在他身边有一辆盖着白色盖布的车。
“大家将会看到我的最新发明。” 男人说，“这是有史以来最了不起的车！” 
他走向那辆车。
Nearby a car was covered by a white sheet.
"You're about to see my latest invention," said the man. "It's the most amazing car ever!"
He walked toward the car.
大家都身体前倾，想仔细看看。男人抓起了盖布。
“请看……” 男人猛地掀开盖布。“全能车！” 
所有人都大吃一惊。这辆车有羽翼，火箭，以及很多高级装置。
Everyone leaned closer to see. The man grabbed the sheet.
"Behold . . ." The man yanked off the sheet. "The Ultra Car!"
Everybody gasped. The car had wings, rockets, and lots of fancy gadgets.
突然，发动机响了。车轮发出刺耳的声音，大家跳着让出一条路。
呜！全能车撞破玻璃门，开出去了。
Suddenly the car's engine roared. Tires screeched, and everyone jumped out of the way.
Vroom! The Ultra Car smashed through the glass doors and drove away.
罗西和朋友们在公交车站。他们去了图书馆。现在，他们打算回家。
杰克看着一张海报。“我们要是能去美罗城车展就好了。” 
Roxy and her friends were at a city bus stop. They'd been at the library. Now they were going home.
Jack looked at a poster. "I wish we could go to the Metro City Car Show."
“我们该回家了。” 罗西说。
杰克转了转眼珠。“我不是说马上。我是说近期。一定会很棒的！” 
"We have to go home," said Roxy.
Jack rolled his eyes. "I didn't mean right now. I meant soon. It would be cool."
“我希望是这个周末。” 特勒尔说，“说不定爸爸妈妈会带我们去。” 
“我今天晚上就去问爸爸妈妈！” 玛拉说。
"We should go this weekend," said Terrell. "Maybe our parents will take us."
"I'll ask my parents tonight!" said Mara.
“我很想知道车展上有没有会飞的车。” 杰克说，“呜！” 他双手举起，跑了一圈。
“一辆会飞的车一定很酷。” 特勒尔说。
"I wonder if there are cars that fly at the show," said Jack. "Zoom!" He held out his arms and ran in circles.
"A flying car would be awesome," said Terrell.
“我希望我能飞。” 玛拉说，“那会很有趣儿!” 
罗西点点头。“听起来是很有意思。” 
“我们可以飞着去图书馆。” 特勒尔说。“或者去动物园。” 
"I wish I could fly," said Mara. "It would be so much fun!"
Roxy nodded. "It does sound like fun."
"We could fly to the library," said Terrell. "Or to the zoo."
“或者去车展！” 杰克说。
玛拉看到一只鸽子飞过。“我们可以飞到任何想去的地方。” 她说，“像鸟一样。” 
"Or to the car show!" said Jack.
Mara watched a pigeon fly by. "We could fly anywhere we wanted," she said. "Just like birds."
“我有一个主意。” 特勒尔说，“我们可以请火箭女孩儿帮我们飞起来！” 
罗西笑了。“火箭女孩儿太忙了，肯定帮不了我们。” 
特勒尔皱起眉头。“你说得对。” 
"I have an idea," said Terrell. "We can ask Rocket Girl to help us fly!"
Roxy laughed. "I'm sure Rocket Girl is too busy for that."
Terrell frowned. "I guess you're right."
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。她离开朋友们以后，按了一下手表上的按钮。布洛姆市长的脸出现了。
“布洛姆市长。” 罗西轻声说，“有什么事吗？” 
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. She stepped away from her friends and pressed a button on the watch. Mayor Bloom's face appeared.
"Mayor Bloom," Roxy whispered. "What's wrong?"
“车展上发生了盗车事件！” 布洛姆市长说，“有人偷了全能车！这是有史以来最了不起的发明。但是，现在到了小偷手里！” 
“不要担心，市长。” 罗西说，“火箭女孩儿很快就到！” 
"A car theft happened at the car show!" said the mayor. "Someone has stolen the Ultra Car! It's the most amazing car ever invented. But now a thief has it!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," said Roxy. "Rocket Girl is on her way!"
罗西看了朋友们一眼。
“糟糕！” 她说。
“怎么了？” 玛拉问。
Roxy glanced at her friends.
"Oh no!" she said.
"What's wrong?" asked Mara.
“我把一本书落在图书馆了。” 罗西说，“你们先回家。我坐下一趟公交车。” 
罗西沿着拥挤的人行道跑着。
“等等！” 特勒尔大声喊，“我们可以帮你找那本书。” 
"I forgot a book at the library," said Roxy. "You all go home. I'll take the next bus."
Roxy ran down the crowded sidewalk.
"Wait!" called Terrell. "We can help find the book!"
但是，罗西已经不见了。
“你们看！那是火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉叫道。
嗖！罗西飞过天空。她直接飞向车展。
But Roxy was already gone.
"Look! It's Rocket Girl!" cried Mara.
Swoosh! Roxy zoomed across the sky. She flew right to the car show.
会展中心的前门被撞得粉碎。地上到处都是碎玻璃。停车场的几辆车也被撞坏了。
史密斯侦探站在粉碎的门附近。
The front doors of the convention center were shattered. Bits of glass lay everywhere. Several cars in the parking lot were smashed.
Detective Smith stood near the shattered doors.
他正在跟布洛姆市长和几个人谈话。一个男人穿着实验服。
罗西落在侦探身边，笑了。“您在买新车吗，侦探先生？” 
He was talking to Mayor Bloom and some other people. One man wore a lab coat.
Roxy landed next to the detective and grinned. "Shopping for a new car, Detective?"
“现在不是开玩笑的时候。” 侦探说，“偷车是很严重的犯罪行为。” 
“它不是普通的车。” 穿实验服的男人说，“它是全能车！” 
"This is no time for jokes," said the detective. "Car theft is a serious crime."
"It isn't just any car," said the man in the lab coat. "It's the Ultra Car!"
“为什么叫它全能车呢？” 罗西问。
“这是有史以来最了不起的车！” 男人说，“它跟军用坦克一样坚固。它能发射激光。它可以在水中游，甚至可以在天上飞！” 
"Why is it called the Ultra Car?" Roxy asked.
"It's the most amazing car ever invented!" said the man. "It's as tough as an army tank. It has lasers. It can go under water and even fly!"
罗西咽了一口口水。这辆车无所不能。它现在到了一个小偷手里。真是一个坏消息。
“有人看到是谁偷的吗？” 罗西问。
发明者摇摇头。布洛姆市长也摇摇头。
Roxy gulped. The car could do all of those things. And now a thief had it . . . This was bad news.
"Did anyone see who stole it?" Roxy asked.
The inventor shook his head. Mayor Bloom did too.
一个女人跑过来。她身上戴满钻石。“我知道是谁开走了那辆车。” 她说。
罗西认出了她。她是维多利亚·卡什——美罗城最富有的女人。
A woman rushed over. She wore lots of diamonds. "I know who took the car," she said.
Roxy recognized her. She was Victoria Cash, the richest woman in Metro City.
“你知道小偷是谁？” 罗西说，“是谁呢？” 
卡什夫人用手绢擦了擦眼睛。“那不是小偷。” 她说，“是我的女儿，鲁比。” 
"You know who the thief is?" said Roxy. "Who is it?"
Mrs. Cash dabbed her eyes with a handkerchief. "It wasn't a thief," she said. "It was my daughter, Ruby."
“鲁比为什么要偷车？” 史密斯侦探问。
“她不是有意的。” 卡什夫人说，“鲁比本来想坐那辆全能车，我说不行。” 她叹了口气。“鲁比讨厌听到‘不行’这个词。” 
"Why would Ruby steal a car?" asked Detective Smith.
"She didn't mean to," said Mrs. Cash. "She wanted to ride in the Ultra Car, but I told her no." She sighed. "Ruby doesn't like to hear the word 'no.'"
“鲁比好像是有点被宠坏了。” 罗西想。
“我只是转过去一会儿。” 卡什夫人继续说，“鲁比肯定是坐上了那辆车。很快，那辆车就发动了！” 
"Ruby sounds a little spoiled," thought Roxy.
"I just turned my back for a moment," Mrs. Cash went on. "Ruby must have gotten into the car. A moment later the car started!"
史密斯侦探的电话响了。“我是史密斯。” 侦探说，“真的吗？太糟糕了！” 
他收起电话，看着罗西。“全能车正在破坏美罗城市中心！” 
Detective Smith's phone rang. "Smith here," the detective said. "Really? Oh no!"
He put his phone away and looked at Roxy. "The Ultra Car is destroying downtown Metro City!"
“真是太可怕了！” 布洛姆市长说，“全能车在破坏美罗城！” 
“我可怜的鲁比！” 卡什夫人喊道。
“我可怜的车！” 车发明者喊道。
"This is terrible!" said Mayor Bloom. "The Ultra Car is destroying the city!"
"My poor Ruby!" cried Mrs. Cash.
"My poor car!" cried the inventor.
“我可怜的城市！” 布洛姆市长喊道。
“火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探说，“你必须……火箭女孩儿？” 
嗖！罗西迅速飞上天空。
"My poor city!" cried Mayor Bloom.
"Rocket Girl!" said Detective Smith. "You must . . . Rocket Girl?"
Zoom! Roxy shot through the air.
她以最快的速度飞向市中心。远远地，她看到黑色的浓烟弥漫整个天空。
“什么东西着火了！” 罗西想。
罗西用她的超级视力透过浓烟看过去。
She flew toward downtown as fast as she could. Up ahead, she saw black smoke fill the sky.
"Something's burning!" thought Roxy.
She used her super vision to see through the smoke.
街上的车在燃烧。一栋大楼也在燃烧。一个水果摊倒在地上。几家商店的玻璃碎了。
一辆很酷的车在西街上飞奔。
Cars were burning in the street. A building was on fire too. A fruit cart lay on its side. Several store windows had been smashed.
A cool car was going down West Street very fast.
车上有羽翼和火箭。 
“那肯定是全能车！” 罗西想。
嗖！罗西飞向那辆车。
哐！全能车撞倒了甜甜圈摊。
It had wings and rockets.
"That must be the Ultra Car!" thought Roxy.
Whoosh! She flew toward it.
Crash! The car smashed a donut stand.
甜甜圈飞得到处都是。
“啊！” 甜甜圈主人大声喊道，“我花了整整一个上午才做好的甜甜圈！” 
罗西再一次使用了她的超级视力。
Donuts flew everywhere.
"Ugh!" cried the donut maker. "It took me all morning to make those donuts!"
Roxy used her super vision again.
她盯着全能车看，看到里面有一个女孩儿。女孩儿戴着钻石太阳镜。
“那是鲁比·卡什。” 罗西想。
车在西街上到处乱跑。鲁比大声笑着。
She peered into the Ultra Car and saw a young girl. The girl wore diamond sunglasses.
"That's Ruby Cash," thought Roxy.
The car swerved all over the street. Ruby laughed.
罗西和车并排飞着。“鲁比，停车！” 她大声喊道。
“不可能！” 鲁比喊道。“太好玩儿了！” 
哐！
Roxy flew alongside the car. "Ruby, stop the car!" she cried.
"No way!" cried Ruby. "This is fun!"
Smash!
全能车撞在喷泉上。吓得鸽子们四处飞。
“耶！” 车快速地跑起来的时候鲁比欢呼着。
嘎！全能车重新滑回道路上。 
The Ultra Car crashed through a fountain. Startled pigeons flew everywhere.
"Woo-hoo!" shouted Ruby as the car zoomed forward.
Screech! The Ultra Car skidded back onto the street.
它差点儿撞倒了一个抱着猫的女人。
“不要命的司机！” 女人喊道，“看好你的路！” 
“喵！” 猫尖叫。
It almost hit a woman carrying a cat.
"Crazy driver!" the woman shouted. "Watch where you're going!"
"Meow!" yelped the cat.
“别冲我叫！” 鲁比大声喊道。
“在有人受伤之前，必须让这辆车停下来！” 罗西说。
她飞到车前面站在路中央。
"Don't yell at me!" Ruby shouted.
"I have to stop that car before someone gets hurt!" said Roxy.
She flew ahead of the Ultra Car and landed in the street.
当车开过来的时候，罗西伸出双手。
嗞！嗞！车头发射出的激光打中了罗西。罗西向后翻滚，撞在了邮筒上。
She held up her hands as the car raced toward her.
Zap! Zap! Laser beams shot from the car's headlights and blasted Roxy. She tumbled backward and crashed into a mailbox.
“这辆车真是太棒了。” 鲁比说，“我要让妈妈给我买。我不管要多少钱。哦，不！” 
罗西跳起来。全能车正朝公交车开过去。
"This car is totally fabulous," said Ruby. "I'll tell Mother to buy it for me. I don't care how much it costs—oh no!"
Roxy jumped to her feet. The Ultra Car was racing straight toward a bus.
罗西可以看到特勒尔，杰克和玛拉在公交车上。
“火箭女孩儿，帮帮我！” 鲁比大喊道，“我停不了这辆车！” 
罗西咽了一口口水。“鲁比要撞上我的朋友们了！” 
Roxy could see Terrell, Jack, and Mara on the bus.
"Rocket Girl, help!" cried Ruby. "I can't stop this car!"
Roxy gulped. "Ruby's going to crash into my friends!"
嗖！罗西快速飞向公交车。
“是火箭女孩儿！” 杰克喊道。
“我不敢相信罗西竟然错过了！” 特勒尔说。
“大家抓好了！” 罗西对着吓坏了的乘客们说。
Zoom! Roxy shot toward the bus.
"It's Rocket Girl!" cried Jack.
"I can't believe Roxy is missing this!" said Terrell.
"Hang on, everyone!" Roxy called to the scared passengers.
罗西举起公交车，飞到空中。全能车从她下方飞快地开了过去。
“咻！” 罗西松了口气。
公交车上所有的人都欢呼起来。
Gripping the bus, Roxy flew up into the air. The Ultra Car zoomed by below her.
"Whew!" Roxy let out of a sigh of relief.
Everyone on the bus cheered.
罗西把公交车带到下一站，放下它。
“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿！” 公交车司机说。
“不客气！” 罗西说。她重新飞回天空。“我得让全能车停下来。” 她想，“鲁比控制不了它！” 
Roxy carried the bus to its next stop. She set it down.
"Thanks, Rocket Girl!" said the bus driver.
"You're welcome!" called Roxy. She flew into the air again. "I have to stop the Ultra Car," she thought. "Ruby can't control it!"
突然，嗖！全能车飞过罗西。
“天啊！” 罗西喊道，“我忘了这辆车会飞！” 
罗西飞在飞行的车后面。
Suddenly—whoosh! The Ultra Car flew past Roxy.
"Uh-oh!" cried Roxy. "I forgot that car could fly!"
Roxy flew after the flying car.
鲁比尖叫着。“救救我，火箭女孩儿！” 鲁比按下按钮，打开开关。但是，车仍然在飞。
嗞！嗞！激光在发射。
罗西躲开它们。
Ruby screamed. "Save me, Rocket Girl!" Ruby pressed buttons and flipped switches. But the car kept going.
Zap! Zap! Lasers fired.
