Roxy dodged them.
全能车向下飞。哗啦！它掉进了河里。
车很快浮了上来。现在，它变成了一艘船，在水面上飞快地滑行。
罗西也飞得很快。她抓住了车篷。
The Ultra Car dived down. Splash! It plunged into the river.
Then the car popped out of the water. Now it was a boat! It glided fast over the water.
Roxy flew fast too. She grabbed the car's roof.
罗西用她的超级力量掀开了车篷。嘶啦！
“太好了！” 鲁比欢呼着。
罗西把鲁比从车里拉出来。接着，罗西使用了她的热感视力。
Roxy used her super strength to pull off the roof. Rip!
"Great!" Ruby cheered.
Roxy pulled Ruby from the car. Next Roxy used her heat vision.
桔色的激光烧毁了车的控制系统。全能车速度降下来，然后在水里摇摆。
鲁比笑了。“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿。” 
罗西皱起眉头。“你惹了不少麻烦，鲁比。” 
Orange beams melted the car's control panel. The Ultra Car slowed down and then bobbed in the water.
Ruby grinned. "Thank you, Rocket Girl."
Roxy frowned. "You caused a lot of damage, Ruby."
“是吗？” 鲁比看着四周，“没关系。妈妈会花钱请人修好的。” 
罗西一只手拎起车。另外一只手抱着鲁比。她飞回车展。
"Did I?" Ruby glanced around. "Oh well. Mother will pay someone to fix everything."
Roxy picked up the car with one hand. She carried Ruby with the other. She flew back to the car show.
“嗨，妈妈。” 鲁比说，“你最喜欢的女儿安全回来了。是善良的火箭女孩儿救了我。” 
卡什夫人再一次用手绢擦了擦眼睛。“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿！谢谢你救了我的女儿！” 
"Hello, Mother," said Ruby. "Your favorite daughter is safe. Rocket Girl was kind enough to save me."
Mrs. Cash dabbed her eyes with the handkerchief again. "Thank you, Rocket Girl! Thank you for saving my daughter!"
不久，罗西和朋友们在玛拉家里。他们在打电游。
“今天有意思的你都错过了，罗西。” 杰克说。
“我们坐在车里在天上飞！” 玛拉说。
Later Roxy and her friends were at Mara's house. They were playing video games.
"You missed all the fun today, Roxy," said Jack.
"We flew through the air in a bus!" said Mara.
罗西假装很吃惊。“哇！那是怎么回事儿啊？” 
特勒尔笑了。“是火箭女孩儿举着公交车飞的。我告诉过你她能帮我们飞起来！” 
Roxy pretended to be surprised. "Wow! How did that happen?"
Terrell grinned. "Rocket Girl carried the bus through the air. I told you she could help us fly!"
“真的好棒哦！” 杰克举起双手，遥控器掉了下来。“哎呦！” 
所有人都大笑起来。
“幸好火箭女孩儿没把你们坐的公交车掉下来！” 罗西说。
"It was awesome!" Jack threw up his hands and dropped his controller. "Oops!"
Everyone laughed.
"Good thing Rocket Girl didn't drop your bus!" said Roxy.
苏西在厨房里玩儿拼图。
“喵！” 她的猫用爪子挠后门。
“你现在不能出去，雪球。” 苏西说。
Susie worked on a jigsaw puzzle in her kitchen.
"Meow!" Her cat pawed at the back door.
"You can't go outside right now, Snowball," said Susie.
“喵！” 雪球又挠了几下门。
“现在不行，雪球。” 苏西说，“你刚剃了毛……” 
“喵！” 突然，雪球长出了锋利的牙齿和尖尖的毛。
"Meow!" Snowball pawed some more.
"Not right now, Snowball," said Susie. "You just had a haircut and—"
"MEOW!" Suddenly Snowball grew sharp fangs and spiky hair.
噗！雪球吐出一个燃烧的毛球。厨房里到处都是烟雾。当烟雾散去时，门不见了。雪球也不见了。
Phwoof! She spit out a flaming hairball. Smoke filled the kitchen. When the smoke cleared, the door was gone. And so was Snowball.
“坐下，麦克斯！” 玛拉说，“坐下！” 
罗西和她的朋友们在美罗城公园里。他们在训练玛拉家的新狗，麦克斯，但是麦克斯不听话。
“麦克斯，你给我坐下。” 玛拉说。
“汪！” 麦克斯叫了一声，然后它趴下，打了个呵欠。
"Sit, Max!" said Mara. "Sit!"
Roxy and her friends were at Metro City Park. They were trying to train Mara's new dog, Max. But Max wasn't listening.
"Max, you need to sit," said Mara.
"Woof!" Max barked. Then he lay down and yawned.
“坐着对麦克斯来讲也许太无聊了。” 杰克说，“我们得教它一些有意思的技能。” 
杰克跑到一棵树那儿。“麦克斯！” 他叫道，“过来！” 
麦克斯翻了个身，侧躺着。
"Maybe sitting is too boring for Max," said Jack. "We should teach him some exciting tricks."
Jack ran to a tree. "Max!" he called. "Come!"
Max rolled onto his side.
特勒尔伸出他的手。“把你的爪子给我，麦克斯。” 
麦克斯站起来。
“它喜欢这个技能！” 特勒尔说。
但是，麦克斯只是挠了挠耳朵后面，又趴下了。
Terrell held out his hand. "Give me your paw, Max."
Max sat up.
"He likes this trick!" said Terrell.
But Max just scratched behind his ear and then lay back down.
玛拉叹了口气。“真是没希望了。麦克斯什么技能也学不会。” 
杰克在麦克斯旁边坐下，摸了摸它的头。“我相信麦克斯能学会技能。它只是需要时间。” 
Mara sighed. "This is hopeless. Max can't learn any tricks."
Jack sat down next to Max and patted his head. "I'm sure Max can learn tricks. He just needs more time."
罗西挠了挠麦克斯耳朵后面。“麦克斯是一只很棒的宠物，玛拉。” 罗西说，“它只是有点儿……” 
“无聊。” 玛拉说。
“无聊也没什么不对。” 杰克说。
Roxy scratched Max behind the ear. "Max is a good pet, Mara," she said. "He's just a bit—"
"Boring," said Mara.
"There's nothing wrong with being boring," said Jack.
玛拉皱起眉头。“我希望麦克斯是最棒的。” 
“是啊！有一只最棒的狗很酷！” 特勒尔说，“我们也许可以让火箭女孩儿来训练麦克斯。她可以让麦克斯变成真正‘最棒的’！” 
Mara frowned. "I want Max to be super."
"Yeah! A super dog would be cool!" said Terrell. "Maybe we could get Rocket Girl to train Max. She could make him really super!"
罗西大笑。“我觉得火箭女孩儿不会训练宠物，特勒尔。” 
“你说的也对。” 特勒尔说。他摸了摸麦克斯。
Roxy laughed. "I don't think Rocket Girl knows how to train pets, Terrell."
"You're probably right," said Terrell. He patted Max.
罗西跳起来。“我刚刚想起来了，玛拉！麦克斯肯定会一个技能。” 
“什么技能？” 玛拉说。她的眼睛亮了。
罗西严肃地看着麦克斯。“麦克斯，别动！” 
Roxy jumped to her feet. "I just thought of something, Mara! Max definitely knows one trick."
"What?" said Mara. Her eyes lit up.
Roxy looked at Max sternly. "Max, stay!"
这个时候，麦克斯正安静地打着呼噜。它一动不动。
“看到了吧？” 罗西笑了。
特勒尔和杰克大笑起来。玛拉皱起了眉头。
就在这时，罗西听到她的手表在响。
By now Max was snoring quietly. He didn't move at all.
"See?" Roxy grinned.
Terrell and Jack laughed. Mara frowned.
Just then Roxy heard her watch beep.
罗西离开了朋友们。
“布洛姆市长。” 罗西低声说，“有什么问题吗？” 
“出现了严重的问题，火箭女孩儿！” 市长大声说，“现在，怪兽宠物在西街上到处跑！” 
She moved away from her friends.
"Mayor Bloom," Roxy whispered. "Is there a problem?"
"There is a terrible problem, Rocket Girl!" cried the mayor. "Monster pets are running all over West Street!"
罗西对朋友们大声说。“我得回家了。” 她说，“我得……嗯……准备明天的数学测验！” 
罗西跑远了。
特勒尔挠了挠头。“我们明天没有数学测验啊。” 
Roxy called to her friends. "I have to go home," she said. "I have to . . . um . . . study for tomorrow's math quiz!"
Roxy ran off.
Terrell scratched his head. "We don't have a math quiz tomorrow."
罗西飞过美罗城。她看到西街上发生了一起公交车撞车事故。人们举着手，尖叫着，往四面八方逃跑。
Roxy flew over Metro City. She saw a bus crash on West Street. People were raising their hands, screaming, and running in every direction.
“那些人一定是在躲怪兽宠物。” 罗西想。
罗西落在街道上。到处都是怪兽宠物。
“我的卷毛狗咬我！” 一个老人大喊道。
"Those people must be running from the monster pets," thought Roxy.
She flew down to the street. Monster pets were everywhere.
"My poodle is biting me!" cried an old man.
“汪！汪！呜！” 卷毛狗猛地咬住了那个人的脚。
一只猫打掉了一个老奶奶的拐杖。
“坏小猫！” 老奶奶大声说道。
"WOOF! WOOF! Grr!" The poodle snapped at the man's feet.
A cat swatted at an old lady's cane.
"Bad kitty!" cried the lady.
一个大个子男人被一只喷火的小狗追着跑。
“快逃命啊！” 男人大喊道。
“火箭女孩儿！” 有人喊道。
A large man ran from a tiny dog that was breathing fire.
"Run for your lives!" shouted the man.
"Rocket Girl!" cried a voice.
是史密斯侦探。他躲在一辆被撞的车后面。跟一个女人在一起。罗西看到一只狗长着尖尖的毛，咬下了汽车轮胎。狗的项圈闪闪发光。
罗西飞到车的上方。狗跑掉了。
It was Detective Smith. He was hiding behind a crashed car. A woman was with him. Roxy saw a dog with spiky fur bite a tire off the car. The dog's collar was glowing.
Roxy flew over to the car. The dog ran away.
“嗨，侦探先生。” 罗西说，“我觉得你需要送你的狗去训狗学校！” 
“哈哈！” 史密斯侦探假笑着，“那不是我的狗，火箭女孩儿！” 
"Hi, Detective," said Roxy. "I think you need to take your dog to dog training school!"
"Ha-ha." Detective Smith pretended to laugh. "That's not my dog, Rocket Girl."
“那是我的狗。” 一个女人说，“它叫拉尔菲。” 
“拉尔菲平时也那样吗？” 罗西问。
“当然不是。” 女人说。她笑得很自豪。“它总是得奖。今天早上还毛茸茸的很可爱，但是现在……” 
"He's my dog," said a woman. "His name is Ralphie."
"Does Ralphie always act like that?" asked Roxy.
"Of course not," said the woman. She smiled proudly. "He wins awards all the time. He was cute and furry this morning. But now . . ."
女人哭了。“它现在像个怪兽！唉，可怜的拉尔菲！” 
“为什么会变成这样呢？” 史密斯侦探问，“今天拉尔菲吃了什么特别的东西吗？” 
“没有。” 女人摇摇头。
The woman cried. "He looks like a monster! Oh! Poor Ralphie!"
"Why has it changed like this?" asked Detective Smith. "Did Ralphie eat anything special today?"
"No." The woman shook her head.
罗西看了看四周。怪兽宠物们都不见了。“我很想知道它们都去哪儿了。” 她想。
“今天拉尔菲还做了什么？” 史密斯侦探问。
Roxy glanced around. The monster pets were gone. "I wonder where they went," she thought.
"What else did Ralphie do today?" asked Detective Smith.
女人想了一会儿。“吃完东西以后，我带它去了一个非常好的新宠物沙龙—— 斯尼皮先生宠物沙龙。拉尔菲剃了毛，修了指甲。斯尼皮先生人很好。他给了拉尔菲一个发光的新项圈。” 
The woman thought for a moment. "After he ate, I took him to a wonderful new pet salon—Mr. Snippy's. Ralphie got a haircut and a manicure. Mr. Snippy is a lovely man. He gave Ralphie a new collar that glows."
一个留着胡子的男人跑过来。他戴着太阳镜，穿着白色网球服。
“怪兽宠物们跑到美罗城公园里去了！” 男人大声说，“一只狗吃了网球网，一只猫吃了我的球拍。” 
“天啊！” 罗西想，“特勒尔，玛拉和杰克在美罗城公园！” 
A man with a beard ran over. He wore sunglasses and a white tennis outfit.
"Monster pets are invading Metro City Park!" the man shouted. "A dog ate the tennis net. Then a cat ate my racket!"
"Uh-oh," thought Roxy. "Terrell, Mara, and Jack are at Metro City Park!"
罗西落在美罗城公园里。
“是火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉大喊道。
罗西看了看四周。到处都是怪兽狗和怪兽猫。还有几只怪兽宠物在网球场上。
Roxy landed in Metro City Park.
"It's Rocket Girl!" cried Mara.
Roxy looked around. Monster dogs and cats were everywhere! Several monster pets were on the tennis court.
网球场被高高的栅栏围着。
一只怪兽猫对卖气球的人发出嘶嘶声。猫跳起来伸出爪子。啪！啪！啪！猫把所有的气球都抓破了。
The court was surrounded by a tall fence.
A monster cat hissed at a man selling balloons. The cat jumped up and stuck out its claws. Pop! Pop! Pop! The cat popped all the balloons.
“我的气球全完了！” 卖气球的人哭着喊道。
罗西注意到猫的项圈。它闪着光。
“喵！” 
"My balloons are all ruined!" cried the balloon man.
Roxy noticed the cat's collar. It was glowing.
"MEOW!"
罗西飞快地转过身。另外一只怪兽猫正向她慢慢走过来。
罗西吓了一跳。“它也有一个发光的项圈！” 
噗！猫向罗西吐出一个燃烧的毛球。
Roxy spun around. Another monster cat was creeping toward her!
Roxy gasped. "It has a glowing collar too!"
Phwoof! The cat shot a flaming hairball toward Roxy.
罗西握紧拳头，然后......啪！她打掉了毛球。
“帮帮我们，火箭女孩儿！” 特勒尔大喊道。
罗西回头看了朋友们一眼。两只怪兽狗正叫着走向他们。
Roxy made a fist and—bam! She knocked the hairball away.
"Help, Rocket Girl!" cried Terrell.
Roxy glanced back at her friends. Two monster dogs were growling and moving toward them!
罗西大声吹口哨。狗转身向罗西冲去。罗西跑向网球场，在打开的门前面站住。
“呜！” 狗叫着向罗西冲过去。
Roxy whistled loudly. The dogs turned and charged toward Roxy. She ran to the tennis court and stood in front of the open gate.
"GRR!" The dogs growled and raced toward Roxy.
当狗就要碰到罗西的时候，她跳了起来。狗滚进了网球场。
“哈！” 罗西大叫着关上了门。
特勒尔，玛拉和杰克欢呼起来。
Just before they reached her, she jumped up. The dogs tumbled onto the tennis court.
"Ha!" cried Roxy as she slammed shut the gate.
Terrell, Mara, and Jack cheered.
“太棒了！火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉喊道。
罗西飞到空中。“肯定是那些发光的项圈让宠物们变成怪兽的。” 罗西想，“拉尔菲的主人说，她是从斯尼皮先生那里得到那个项圈的，但是斯尼皮先生的宠物沙龙在哪儿呢？” 
"Great! Rocket Girl!" cried Mara.
Roxy zoomed into the air. "Those glowing collars must be turning pets into monsters," she thought. "Ralphie's owner said she got the glowing collar from Mr. Snippy. But where is Mr. Snippy's Pet Salon?"
就在这时，一个男人大喊道：“坏狗，巴斯特！” 
罗西向下看去。一个男人掉了一只鞋。他正指着一只怪兽狗在骂。
Just then a man yelled, "Bad dog, Buster!"
Roxy looked down. The man was missing a shoe. He was pointing at a monster dog, scolding him.
那只狗戴着发光的项圈，正在嚼什么东西。
罗西在那个男人身边落下。“请问，这是您的狗吗？” 
“是的。” 男人说，“它太坏了！它刚刚吃了我的鞋！” 
The dog was chewing on something as his collar glowed.
Roxy flew down to the man. "Excuse me. Is this your dog?"
"Yes," said the man. "And he's very bad! He just ate my shoe!"
“你是从斯尼皮先生的宠物沙龙里得到那个项圈的吗？” 
“是的。” 男人看上去很吃惊，“你怎么知道的？” 
“你别管。” 罗西说，“你只要告诉我沙龙在哪里就行。” 
男人跟罗西说了沙龙的地址。
"Did you get that collar from Mr. Snippy's Pet Salon?"
"Yes." The man looked surprised. "How did you know?"
"Never mind," said Roxy. "Just tell me where the salon is."
The man told Roxy the salon's address.
罗西再一次迅速飞过天空。过了一会儿，她用力推开了沙龙的门。
一个瘦瘦的带着领结的男人转过身来。他戴着一副有锋利刀片的手套。
Roxy zipped through the air again. A moment later she threw open the salon's doors.
A thin man with a bowtie spun around. He wore gloves with sharp blades.
当他看到罗西时，脸上露出邪恶的微笑。“欢迎光临斯尼皮先生宠物沙龙，火箭女孩儿！” 他锋利的刀片发出很大的响声。“我想你是来这儿剪头发的吧！” 
When he saw Roxy, his lips curled into a nasty smile. "Welcome to Mr. Snippy's, Rocket Girl!" His sharp blades clacked loudly. "I suppose you're here for a cut!"
斯尼皮先生在空中挥舞着刀片。咔擦！咔擦！他慢慢靠近罗西。
罗西用眼睛向刀片发射激光。嗞！刀片变得粉碎。
Mr. Snippy was swinging blades in the air. Snip! Snip! He moved closer to Roxy.
Roxy shot her eye laser beams at the blades. Whiz-hoo! The blades exploded into little pieces.
“啊！” 斯尼皮先生大声喊道，“我不怕你的激光。你阻止不了我，火箭女孩儿！” 
斯尼皮先生向沙龙的后面跑去。一只白色的小卷毛狗被拴在桌腿上。
"Gah!" cried Mr. Snippy. "I am not afraid of your laser beams. You'll never stop me, Rocket Girl!"
Mr. Snippy ran to the back of the salon. A tiny white poodle was tied to a table leg.
“汪！汪！” 卷毛狗叫着。
“黛西刚剃了毛。” 斯皮尼先生说，“现在，我要给它戴上新项圈！” 
"Yip, yip!" The poodle barked.
"Daisy just had a haircut," said Mr. Snippy. "And now I'll put on her brand-new collar!"
斯皮尼先生给黛西戴上了项圈。罗西大吃一惊，那只小卷毛狗变成了凶恶的怪兽狗。
“我猜对了，斯尼皮！” 罗西生气地说，“是你的项圈把宠物们变成怪兽的！” 
Mr. Snippy put the collar onto Daisy. Roxy was surprised to see the little poodle turn into a fearsome monster dog!
"I was right, Snippy!" Roxy said angrily. "Your collars are turning pets into monsters!"
斯尼皮先生露出邪恶的微笑。“我的公寓不让养宠物。所以我只能抛弃我可爱的小狗。现在，在美罗城再也没有人能拥有一只可爱的小宠物了！” 
Mr. Snippy had an evil grin. "My apartment building doesn't allow pets. So I had to give away my cute little puppy. Now no one in Metro City will ever have a cute little pet again!"
“哈哈哈！” 斯尼皮先生的笑声充满了整个沙龙。那只卷毛狗扑向罗西。
“汪，汪！” 黛西叫着。
"Ha-ha-ha!" Mr. Snippy's laugh filled the salon as the poodle leaped at Roxy.
"YIP, YIP!" Daisy barked.
“啊！” 罗西跳起来，躲开了。那只小狗试着攻击罗西。
罗西在大叫的卷毛狗的上方飘着。“我得想个办法。” 她想。
"Ahh!" Roxy jumped out of the way. The little dog was trying to attack her.
Roxy floated in the air above the barking poodle. "I need to think of a plan," she thought.
就在这时，她听到了嗡嗡的响声。声音来自于一扇门的后面。
“汪，汪！” 黛西还在叫。
罗西用她的X射线向门里看去。
Just then she heard a whirring noise. It was coming from behind a door.
"YIP, YIP!" Daisy was still barking.
Roxy used her x-ray vision to look through the door.
房间里有显示屏，开关和闪烁的指示灯。
“我敢肯定是这些设备控制了所有的项圈。” 罗西想。
她握紧拳头，飞向那扇门。
There was a room with video screens, switches, and blinking lights.
"I'll bet that equipment controls all the collars," thought Roxy.
She made a fist and flew at the door.
哐！罗西把门砸得粉碎，然后……嗞！她的眼睛发射出激光，设备爆炸了。
“不！” 斯尼皮先生大声喊道，“你毁了项圈控制中心！” 
Ka-bam! She smashed the door into pieces. Then—whiz-hoo! She fired her eye laser beams, and the equipment exploded.
"No!" cried Mr. Snippy. "You destroyed Collar Control Central!"
“汪，汪！” 黛西叫着。它高兴地舔着罗西的脸。它重新变成了一只正常的狗。
罗西等到了黛西的主人。然后，她把斯尼皮先生送进了监狱。
"Yip, yip!" Daisy barked. She licked Roxy's face happily. She was a normal dog again.
Roxy waited for Daisy's owner to come. Then she took Mr. Snippy to jail.
罗西回到了美罗城公园。她看到了只穿一只鞋的男人。他正跟巴斯特在散步。
“我很高兴你重新变成了一只正常的狗，巴斯特。” 男人说。
罗西很快找到了朋友们。麦克斯仍然在睡觉。
Roxy returned to Metro City Park. She saw the man with one shoe. He was walking Buster.
"I'm glad you're a normal dog again, Buster," said the man.
Roxy soon found her friends. Max was still sleeping.
“你猜猜发生了什么事！” 特勒尔说，“火箭女孩儿把我们从怪兽宠物中救了出来！” 
玛拉点点头。“那些宠物太可怕了！” 她低头看着麦克斯，然后抱住它。“跟无聊的麦克斯不一样！” 
罗西笑了。“好狗狗，麦克斯！” 
"Guess what!" said Terrell. "Rocket Girl saved us from monster pets!"
Mara nodded. "The pets were awful!" She looked down at Max and hugged him. "Not like boring Max!"
Roxy laughed. "Good dog, Max!"
美罗城地铁站里， 人们脚步匆匆。
“让开!” 一个男人说，“我上班要迟到了！” 
一个年轻女人走进地铁站。她背着小提琴，拿着帽子。她把帽子放在地上。
People hurried through the Metro City subway station.
"Out of my way!" a man said. "I'm late for work!"
A young woman walked into the station. She carried a violin and held a hat. She placed the hat on the floor.
然后，她开始拉小提琴。奇怪的音乐在空中响起。所有人都停下脚步。他们全都看向那个年轻女人。突然，他们掏出钱包，扔到了帽子里。
Then she started to play her violin. Strange music filled the air. Everyone stopped walking. They all turned to stare at the young woman. Suddenly they pulled out their wallets and tossed them into the hat!
“我等不及音乐会开始了。” 玛拉说，“能听到真正的管弦乐真是太棒了！” 
罗西和朋友们在美罗城公园里。美罗城交响乐团将要在这里举行一场音乐会。人们在草地上铺上毯子坐着。音乐家们在舞台上调试乐器。
"I can't wait for the concert to start," Mara said. "It'll be so cool to hear a real orchestra!"
Roxy and her friends were at Metro City Park. The Metro City Symphony Orchestra was going to perform a concert. People sat on blankets on the grass. The musicians were onstage, tuning their instruments.
“今天天气真暖和。” 玛拉说，“温度会影响乐器。所以音乐家们要检查。” 
“我很喜欢现场音乐。” 特勒尔说，“说不定明年我就能进学校的爵士乐队。我一直在学单簧管。” 
"It's really warm today," Mara said. "Temperature affects musical instruments. That's why the musicians are checking them now."
"I love live music," Terrell said. "I might join the school jazz band next year. I've been taking clarinet lessons."
杰克耸耸肩。“音乐会应该不错。不过我不怎么喜欢古典音乐。我喜欢摇滚乐！” 杰克跳起来。他两手举起来好像抱着吉他。大家看到杰克装摇滚歌手跳舞，都笑了。
Jack shrugged. "I guess the concert will be okay. I don't really like classical music though. I like rock and roll!" Jack jumped to his feet. He held up his hands as if he was holding a guitar. Everyone laughed as soon as Jack pretended to be a rock star, dancing around.
“嗯…..我喜欢古典音乐。” 玛拉说，“管弦乐队今天将演奏我最喜欢的歌曲。我正在学习用大提琴演奏它，但是真的好难。” 
“只要你一直练习。” 罗西说，“你会拉得越来越好的。说不定有一天你也能在这里表演。” 
"Well, I like classical music," Mara said. "The orchestra is going to play my favorite song today. I'm trying to learn it on the cello, but it's really hard."
"Just keep practicing," Roxy said. "You'll get better and better. Maybe one day you'll perform here!"
玛拉笑了。“我好像不行。” 
“我知道一个人可能非常擅长音乐。” 特勒尔说。
罗西转了一下眼睛。“嗯......特勒尔。我怀疑火箭女孩儿会不会乐器。” 
Mara laughed. "I doubt that!"
"I know someone who's probably really good at music," Terrell said.
Roxy rolled her eyes. "Ugh, Terrell. I doubt Rocket Girl even plays an instrument."
特勒尔看起来很吃惊。“你怎么知道我说的是火箭女孩儿？” 
罗西笑了。“特勒尔，你总是提到火箭女孩儿！” 
Terrell looked surprised. "How did you know I was talking about Rocket Girl?"
Roxy laughed. "Terrell, you always talk about Rocket Girl!"
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。罗西看看周围，又看看她的朋友们。“我很快就回来。我……嗯……好像看到我家邻居了。我想去打个招呼。” 
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. She looked around and then back at her friends. "I'll be right back. I, um, think I saw my neighbor. I want to go say hi."
罗西躲在雕像后，按了一下手表的按钮。布洛姆市长的脸出现在屏幕上。
“有什么事吗，市长？” 罗西问。
Roxy ducked behind a statue and pressed a button on her watch. Mayor Bloom's face appeared on the screen.
"What's wrong, Mayor?" Roxy asked.
“我们需要你的帮助，火箭女孩儿。” 布洛姆市长说，“邦恩太太办了一个花园派对。所有客人都被抢劫了！” 
“别担心，市长！” 罗西说，“我马上到！” 
"We need your help, Rocket Girl," Mayor Bloom said. "Mrs. Bun was having a fancy garden party. All of her guests were robbed!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," Roxy said. "I'm on my way!"
“我得赶到邦恩太太家。” 罗西想，“有人抢劫了客人的东西。” 
“我很快就回来。我要给爸妈打电话。” 罗西大声对朋友们说。
"I have to get to Mrs. Bun's house," Roxy thought. "Someone robbed her guests!"
"I'll be right back! I need to call my parents." Roxy yelled to her friends.
“别去太久了。” 特勒尔说，“音乐会马上就要开始了。” 
过一会儿，罗西飞上了天空。
“哇！” 玛拉大声说，“是火箭女孩儿！” 
"Don't take too long," Terrell said. "The concert is starting soon."
A moment later Roxy shot up into the sky.
"Whoa!" Mara cried. "Rocket Girl!"
罗西到了邦恩太太家。邦恩太太看上去很难过，史密斯侦探正在玫瑰丛里爬来爬去。
罗西笑了。“ 您在做园艺工作吗， 侦探先生？” 
Roxy arrived at Mrs. Bun's house. Mrs. Bun looked upset as Detective Smith crawled around in some rosebushes.
Roxy grinned. "Doing some gardening, Detective?"
“哈哈！火箭女孩儿。” 史密斯侦探假装大笑，“哎呦！刺扎到我了。” 他站起来，举起笔记本。“我把这个掉在玫瑰丛里了。” 
史密斯侦探转向邦恩太太。“对不起。刚才您说到哪儿了？” 
"Ha-ha, Rocket Girl." Detective Smith pretended to laugh. "I—ouch! A thorn poked me." He got back to his feet and held up his notebook. "I dropped this in the rosebushes."
The detective turned to Mrs. Bun. "I'm sorry. What were you saying?"
邦恩太太叹了一口气。“说到了我的客人。如果你想跟他们谈的话，他们都还在这里。服务人员和四重奏乐团也在。” 
“四重奏乐团？” 史密斯侦探扬起一边的眉毛。
Mrs. Bun took a deep breath. "I was telling you about my guests. They are all still here if you want to talk to them. The servers and the quartet are here too."
"Quartet?" Detective Smith raised an eyebrow.
“管弦乐四重奏乐团。” 邦恩太太说，“我请了四个音乐家在派对上表演。” 
“抢劫以前发生过什么事吗？” 罗西问，“有什么可疑的地方吗？” 
"A string quartet," Mrs. Bun said. "I hired four musicians to play during the party."
"What happened before the robbery?" Roxy asked. "Did you see anything suspicious?"
邦恩太太耸耸肩。“真奇怪，我竟然什么都不记得了。前一分钟，我们还在享受美好的时光，后一分钟，每个人的钱包都不见了！还有我们的珠宝！” 
Mrs. Bun shrugged. "It's odd, but I don't remember anything. One minute we were enjoying a lovely afternoon. And the next minute, everyone's wallets were missing! Our jewelry too!"
史密斯侦探做了一些笔记。“我们要跟每个人都谈谈，邦恩太太。” 
罗西看到了音乐家。“从他们开始吧。” 
Detective Smith made some notes. "We'll need to interview everyone, Mrs. Bun."
Roxy spotted the musicians. "Let's start with them."
“有人看到可疑的事情了吗？” 罗西问音乐家们。
“没有。” 大提琴家说，“不过我希望你能找到罪犯。那个小偷偷走了我的手表。” 他看着自己的大提琴，叹了一口气。“幸好我还有它。” 
"Did anybody see anything suspicious?" Roxy asked the musicians.
"No," the cellist said. "But I hope you find the criminal. That thief stole my new watch." He looked at his cello and sighed. "I'm just glad I still have this."
“我的红宝石耳环不见了！” 一位小提琴家说。
“等一下！” 史密斯侦探说，“你们只有三个人。邦恩太太说你们是四重奏乐团。” 
“哦，天啊！” 第三个音乐家说，“瓦奥莱特去哪里了？” 
"My ruby earrings are gone!" a violinist said.
"Wait a second," Detective Smith said. "There are only three of you. Mrs. Bun said you were a quartet."
"Oh, goodness!" the third musician said. "Where's Violet?"
“谁？” 罗西问。
 “瓦奥莱特·夏普。” 大提琴家说，“她是我们另外一位小提琴家。” 
“嗯……” 罗西说，“有人偷了客人的东西。现在瓦奥莱特又不见了。的确很可疑啊。” 
"Who?" Roxy asked.
"Violet Sharp," the cellist said. "She's our other violinist."
"Hmm," Roxy said. "Someone robbed the guests, and now Violet is gone. That's pretty suspicious."
“不可能！” 小提琴家说，“瓦奥莱特才不是小偷呢。她是个很有才的音乐家。事实上，美罗城交响乐团还邀请她去面试呢。” 
"Nonsense," the violinist said. "Violet is no thief. She's a very talented musician. In fact, the Metro City Symphony Orchestra invited her to try out."
“让人印象深刻啊。” 史密斯侦探说。正在这时，他的手机响了。 “喂？天啊！我马上就过去！” 他挂了电话，看着罗西。“刚才又发生了一起抢劫案，这次是在美罗城购物中心。” 
"Impressive," Detective Smith said. Then his phone beeped. "Hello? Oh no! We'll be right there!" He hung up and looked at Roxy. "Another robbery just took place. This one was at Metro City Shopping Mall!"
“对了，火箭女孩儿。” 史密斯侦探把手机放回口袋，我们得……火箭女孩儿？” 
火箭女孩儿看到一个年轻的女人从美罗城购物中心跑了出来。女人背着小提琴盒子和一个大袋子。
"Okay, Rocket Girl." Detective Smith put his phone back in his pocket. "We have to—Rocket Girl?"
Roxy saw a young woman run out of Metro City Shopping Mall. The woman carried a violin case and a large sack.
“那个人应该就是瓦奥莱特·夏普！” 罗西想。 
罗西落在街上。“站住，瓦奥莱特！” 
瓦奥莱特看着罗西。“你想要干什么，火箭女孩儿？” 
"That must be Violet Sharp!" Roxy thought.
Roxy landed in the street. "Stop right there, Violet!"
Violet glared at Roxy. "What do you want, Rocket Girl?"
“你偷了别人的东西吗？” 罗西问。
瓦奥莱特没有回答。
 “你是很有才的音乐家。” 罗西说，“听说美罗城交响乐团还邀请你去面试呢。你为什么要偷东西呢？” 
"Are you stealing stuff from people?" Roxy asked.
Violet didn't reply.
"You're a talented musician," Roxy said. "I heard the Metro City Symphony Orchestra invited you to try out. Why are you stealing?"
“哼！” 瓦奥莱特表情很不好。“他们说我拉得不够好，进不了那个愚蠢的管弦乐队。我就是要给他们看看。我做了会催眠的小提琴。 现在，我比历史上所有的音乐家都要有钱！” 她跳上一辆等在那里的公交车。
"Hmph!" Violet's expression wasn't good. "They said my performance skills weren't good enough, so I couldn't join their silly orchestra. I'll show them. I made a violin that hypnotizes people. Now I'll be richer than any musician in history!" She jumped into a waiting bus.
公交车开走了。罗西紧跟在公交车后面。
瓦奥莱特透过车窗瞪着罗西。“你阻止不了我！” 她大声叫道。她拿出小提琴。她一拉小提琴，其他乘客都看着她，眼睛里一片茫然。
The bus drove off. Roxy shot after it.
Violet glared at Roxy through the window. "You can't stop me!" she shouted. She pulled out her violin. As soon as she played her violin, the other passengers stared at her. Their eyes looked blank.
瓦奥莱特从公交车上跳下来，跑向一个拐角。罗西正要去追她。但是，公交车失控了！汽车开进了人行道上。人们跑起来，躲在垃圾桶后面。
一个男人挥着拳头。“公交车司机发疯了！” 
Violet jumped off the bus and ran around a corner. Roxy was about to chase her. But the bus was driving out of control! Cars drove onto the sidewalk. People ran and dived behind garbage cans.
One man shook his fist. "Crazy bus driver!"
“天啊！” 罗西大叫，“瓦奥莱特给公交车司机催眠了！” 她飞快地飞向公交车，拉住它，让它停下来。
司机醒了，眨了眨眼睛。“发生了什么事儿？” 
"Oh no!" Roxy cried. "Violet hypnotized the bus driver!" She shot after the bus and pulled it to a stop.
The driver woke up and blinked. "What happened?"
罗西来不及回答。“我必须阻止瓦奥莱特！” 她飞向拐角。瓦奥莱特跑着穿过一个工地。工人们在建一栋大楼。男人和女人走在高高的钢梁上。
Roxy didn't have time to answer. "I must stop Violet!" She flew around the corner. Violet was running past a construction site. Workers were building a skyscraper. Men and women walked along metal beams high above.
“瓦奥莱特！” 罗西大声叫，“停下来！” 
瓦奥莱特转过身来，露出邪恶的微笑。她拉了几个音符。罗西隔得太远， 听得不清楚。但是，瓦奥莱特身边的人都停了下来。上面工人的工具掉了下来。
"Violet!" Roxy shouted. "Stop!"
Violet spun around with an evil grin. She played a few notes. Roxy was too far away to hear clearly. But everyone near Violet stood still. Workers above dropped their tools.
罗西飞快地飞过去。她抓住被催眠的人，把他们送到了安全的地方。工具哐哐掉在人行道上。
“火箭女孩儿，小心！” 一个女人叫道。
Roxy flew fast. She grabbed the hypnotized people and moved them to safety. Tools slammed down onto the sidewalk.
"Rocket Girl, watch out!" a woman shouted.
罗西抬头一看，一块巨大的钢梁掉了下来。罗西伸手抓住了它。
“咻！” 她松了一口气。正在这时， 罗西听到了奇怪的音乐。瓦奥莱特正在拉小提琴。在罗西做出反应之前，一切变得很模糊。
Roxy looked up and saw a huge steel beam falling. She reached up and caught it.
"Whew!" Roxy gave a sigh of relief. Then she heard strange music next to her ear. Violet was playing her violin! Before Roxy could react, everything became blurry.
“哦，不！” 罗西自言自语道，“我……变得……” 
瓦奥莱特发出邪恶的笑声。“催眠！” 
"Oh no," Roxy murmured. "I'm . . . becoming . . ."
Violet let out an evil laugh. "Hypnotized!"
瓦奥莱特笑了。“再见，火箭女孩儿！我要去公园里举行的音乐会了。那将是我现在为止最盛大的表演。” 
罗西举着钢梁站在那儿。她感觉自己像在做梦。
Violet laughed. "Good-bye, Rocket Girl! I'm going to the concert at the park. It will be my biggest performance yet."
Roxy stood there, holding the steel beam. She felt as if she was in a dream.
“火箭女孩儿！” 一个女人叫道，“你醒醒！” 
但是，罗西动不了，脑子也不清楚。她觉得手上没力气了。钢梁从她的手上掉下来，砸在地上。
"Rocket Girl!" a woman cried. "Wake up!"
But Roxy couldn't move or think clearly. Her arms felt weak. The beam fell from her hands and slammed onto the ground.
哐！罗西眨了眨眼睛，醒了。
“发......发生了什么事？” 罗西问。
“你被催眠了。” 女人说，“刚才有个小提琴家，她……” 
Bang! Roxy blinked and woke up.
"W-what's going on?" she asked.
"You were hypnotized," the woman said. "There was a violinist, and she—"
“我现在想起来了！” 罗西还想起了瓦奥莱特说过公园里的音乐会。她飞进了一家商店。很快又飞向美罗城公园。
"I remember now!" Roxy also remembered what Violet had said about the concert at the park. She flew into a store. A minute later she shot toward Metro City Park.
瓦奥莱特站在舞台上，正在拉小提琴。管弦乐队的成员一动不动。他们呆呆地看着虚空。观众走向舞台。他们拿出钱包和珠宝。
Violet stood onstage, running her bow across the violin's strings. Members of the orchestra sat still. They were all staring into space. Audience members walked toward the stage. They held out their wallets and jewelry.
瓦奥莱特大笑。“我将变得非常非常非常有钱！” 
罗西远远看着。“幸亏我买了耳塞。” 她把耳塞塞进耳朵里。
Violet laughed. "I'm going to be very, very, very rich!"
Roxy watched from far away. "I'm glad I bought these earplugs." She popped them into her ears.
“你的盛大表演结束了，瓦奥莱特！” 罗西飞快地飞向舞台。
“火箭女孩儿！” 瓦奥莱特狠狠地说道。她开始用小提琴演奏一首新的歌曲。
“你尽管拉。” 罗西说，“我戴了耳塞。” 
"Your big performance is over, Violet!" Roxy darted toward the stage.
"Rocket Girl!" Violet snapped. She started to play a new song on her violin.
"Play all you want," Roxy said. "I'm wearing earplugs!"
罗西的眼睛发射出激光。嗞！瓦奥莱特跳起来躲开了。一支圆号被激光射中，熔化了。
“啊！” 罗西大声叫道，“我要怎么阻止瓦奥莱特呢？我不能再用眼睛发射激光了。可能会有人受伤。” 
Roxy fired her eye laser beams. Whiz-hoo! Violet leaped out of the way. A French horn melted down in the laser beams.
"Yikes!" Roxy cried. "How can I stop Violet? I can't use my eye laser beams again. Someone might get hurt."
罗西想起了玛拉的话。“温度会影响乐器。” 罗西向瓦奥莱特吹了一口冷气。呼！
“呃！” 瓦奥莱特苦着脸，“我的小提琴走调了。” 
Roxy remembered what Mara had said: "Temperature affects musical instruments." Roxy blew her freeze breath at Violet. Whoosh!
"Ugh!" Violet made a face. "My violin is going out of tune!"
罗西飞快地飞过去抢过小提琴。“你的表演被取消了，瓦奥莱特！” 
观众们醒过来了。他们看着周围很惊讶。
“发生什么事了？” 一个男人大声说，“我为什么会在舞台上？” 
Roxy zoomed over and grabbed the violin. "Your performance has been canceled, Violet!"
Audience members woke up. They looked around in surprise.
"What's going on?" a man shouted. "Why am I on the stage?"
“你们看！” 特勒尔说，“火箭女孩儿在舞台上！她在拉小提琴吗？” 
罗西抓着瓦奥莱特的手腕，把她送到了警察总局。
“罗西！” 玛拉说，“你错过了音乐会的开头。” 
"Look!" Terrell cried. "Rocket Girl is onstage! Is she playing the violin?"
Roxy grabbed Violet's wrist and flew her to Police Headquarters.
"Roxy!" said Mara. "You missed the beginning of the concert."
罗西在朋友们身边坐下。舞台上，管弦乐队正在演奏。
特勒尔靠向罗西。“关于火箭女孩儿，你错了。” 他低声说，“她拉小提琴。” 
“嘘！” 罗西笑着轻声说，“好好欣赏音乐吧。” 
Roxy sat down next to her friends. Up onstage, the orchestra played.
Terrell leaned toward Roxy. "You were wrong about Rocket Girl," he whispered. "She plays the violin."
"Shh," Roxy whispered with a smile. "Let's just enjoy the music."
一个女人从一栋高档的SPA会所走出来。她伸手从包里拿出一面小镜子。
“太棒了！” 她说，“那个SPA太神奇了，我看上去......” 
A woman walked out of a fancy spa. She reached into her bag for a small mirror.
"Wonderful!" she said. "That spa is amazing. I look—"
突然，她开始发抖。她变得越来越小了。然后……
“咕…咕！嘎…嘎！” 
Suddenly she started to shake. She grew smaller and smaller. And then . . .
"Goo-goo! Ga-ga!"
“我喜欢艾普卡特老师给我们自由时间。” 杰克说。他正在画一艘宇宙飞船。
玛拉从书中抬起头。“我是高兴快放学了。我跟你们说了我的好消息了吗？” 
"I love when Teacher Apricot lets us have free time," Jack said. He was drawing a spaceship.
Mara looked up from her book. "I'm just glad the school day is almost over. Did I tell you my big news?"
特勒尔扬起一边的眉毛。“什么消息？” 
“跟我们说说！” 罗西说。
“我有工作了。” 玛拉说，“从今天放学后开始！” 
“哇！” 杰克大声说。
艾普卡特老师 抬起头。“嘘！” 
Terrell raised an eyebrow. "What news?"
"Tell us!" Roxy said.
"I have a job," Mara said. "I start today after school!"
"Whoa!" Jack said loudly.
Teacher Apricot looked up from her desk. "Shh!"
“对不起。” 杰克说。他转过头看着玛拉小声说，“哇！” 
“什么工作？” 特勒尔问，“你会在商店里工作吗？” 
杰克咧嘴笑了。“你会经营一家大公司，赚很多很多钱吗？” 
"Sorry," Jack said. Then he looked back at Mara and whispered, "Whoa."
"What's the job?" Terrell asked. "Will you be working in a store?"
Jack grinned. "Will you be running a huge company, making millions of dollars?"
“你要去做老板吗？” 特勒尔问。
杰克和特勒尔笑了。
玛拉转了一下眼睛。“我去给一个妈妈做帮手！” 
“真了不起！” 罗西说，“是去照看小孩子，对吧？” 
"Are you going to be president?" Terrell asked.
Jack and Terrell laughed.
Mara rolled her eyes. "I'm going to be a mother's helper."
"Cool!" Roxy said. "That's like babysitting, right?"
玛拉点点头。“对！我去帮邻居加森太太。她要办一个派对，需要我照看她两岁的孩子。不过，加森太太也会在那儿。跟照看小孩子不完全一样。” 
Mara nodded. "Yep! I'll be helping my neighbor Mrs. Garson. She needs me to watch her two-year-old while she plans a party. Mrs. Garson will be there though. So it's not exactly like babysitting."
“我也想工作。” 杰克说，“但是，我不喜欢照看小孩子。我想经营大公司，赚很多很多钱！” 
“照看小孩子是件很难的事情。” 特勒尔说，“我相信火箭女孩儿一定做得很好！” 
"I'd like to get a job," Jack said. "But I don't want to watch little kids. I'd rather run a huge company and make millions of dollars!"
"Watching little kids is hard," Terrell said. "I bet Rocket Girl is great at it!"
玛拉又转了一下眼睛。
罗西也转了一下眼睛。“火箭女孩儿有更重要的事情要做，特勒尔。” 
Mara rolled her eyes again.
Roxy rolled her eyes too. "Rocket Girl has more important things to do than babysit, Terrell."
突然，罗西的手表响了。她问艾普卡特老师能不能去一下洗手间。然后，她走到走廊上。“布洛姆市长！” 她说，“有什么…哇！您变得好年轻啊！” 
Suddenly her watch beeped. Roxy asked Teacher Apricot if she could go to the restroom. Then she stepped into the hallway. "Mayor Bloom," she said. "What's . . . Oh, wow! Mayor, you seem younger!"
布洛姆市长的脸红了。“哦，谢谢! 今天早上我去SPA会所做了一个特殊护理。我感觉非常好！” 
“那有什么问题吗？” 罗西问。
Mayor Bloom blushed. "Oh, thank you. I went to a spa this morning and got a special treatment. I feel wonderful!"
"So what's the problem?" Roxy asked.
布洛姆市长愣了一会儿。“哦，对了！我们遇到一个很奇怪的问题，火箭女孩儿！美罗城管道供应公司的老板，库珀先生不见了！这还不算，他的办公室出现一个婴儿。” 
罗西挠了挠头。“是很奇怪哦。不过您不用担心，市长先生！我马上就去看看。” 
Mayor Bloom looked confused for a moment. "Oh, right! Yes, we have a very odd problem, Rocket Girl. The owner of Metro City Plumbing Supply, Mr. Copper, has disappeared. And that's not all. There's a baby in his office."
Roxy scratched her head. "That is odd. But don't worry, Mayor. I'll go right away and check it out."
“我得去美罗城管道供应公司。” 罗西想，“库珀先生不见了！” 
罗西把头伸进教室。“ 艾普卡特老师，我很快就回来。嗯…… 潘校长在图书馆需要人帮忙！” 
"I have to get to Metro City Plumbing Supply," Roxy thought. "Mr. Copper has disappeared!"
Roxy popped her head into the classroom. "I'll be back soon, Teacher Apricot. Um, Principal Penn needs help in the library!"
特勒尔挠了挠头。“ 罗西总是跑到别的地方去。” 
艾普卡特老师抬起头。“嘘！” 
罗西穿过走廊，从正门跑出去。她飞向天空。嗖！
Terrell scratched his head. "Roxy is always running off somewhere."
Teacher Apricot looked up. "Shh!"
Roxy ran down the hall and out the front door. She shot into the air. Zoom!
罗西到了美罗城管道供应公司。史密斯侦探正在办公室里。他坐在桌子边上，手里抱着一个可爱的小婴儿。
“你好，侦探先生！” 罗西说，“您找了照看孩子的新工作吗？” 
Roxy arrived at Metro City Plumbing Supply. Detective Smith was in an office. He sat on the edge of the desk. A cute little baby snuggled in his arms.
"Hi, Detective," Roxy said. "Did you get a new job as a babysitter?"
“哈哈！” 史密斯侦探皱起了眉头，“我不是照看小孩子的，火箭女孩儿。有人把这个……哎呦！” 婴儿开始拉侦探的耳朵。“有人把这个婴儿留在这里了。” 
罗西靠近史密斯侦探。“您看起来有些不一样，变得更年轻了。” 
"Ha-ha." Detective Smith frowned. "I'm not babysitting, Rocket Girl. Somebody left this—ouch!" The baby was pulling on the detective's ear. "Somebody left this baby here."
Roxy went up closely to Detective Smith. "You look different. You seem younger."
史密斯侦探笑了一下。“谢谢你看出来了。我今天在万达SPA会所做了一次新护理。万达说会让我年轻几岁。” 史密斯侦探清了清嗓子。“不过，我们现在有更重要的事情要说，火箭女孩儿。” 
Detective Smith gave a laugh. "Thanks for noticing. I got a new treatment at Vanda's Day Spa Club. Vanda said it would make me look years younger." Detective Smith cleared his throat. "But we have more important things to discuss now, Rocket Girl."
罗西点点头。“这个婴儿看上去好眼熟。” 
小婴儿边笑边拍手。“哒！哒！咕！” 
罗西咯咯笑起来。“哇！他太可爱了！” 
“是，他是很可爱。” 史密斯侦探说，“不过，我们还有一个解不开的谜。” 
Roxy nodded. "This baby looks familiar."
The baby smiled and clapped. "Da-da! Goo!"
Roxy giggled. "Aww! He's so cute!"
"Yes, he's very cute," Detective Smith said. "But we still have an unsolved mystery."
“对！” 罗西看了看办公室。这个地方没什么特别。只有一张桌子，一把椅子，放文件夹的书架和一个小保险箱。“有人看到库珀先生离开了吗？” 
"Right!" Roxy looked around the office. There wasn't anything special in it. It had a desk, a chair, a shelf with binders, and a small safe. "Did anyone see Mr. Copper leave?"
“我想没有。” 史密斯侦探说，“我来的时候，一个人也没有。” 
就在这时，办公室的门突然被打开了，一个女人走了进来。“这里发生了什么事？” 
"I don't think so," Detective Smith said. "There was no one else here when I arrived."
Just then the office door flew open, and a woman stepped in. "What's going on in here?"
“库珀先生不见了。” 史密斯侦探说，“您认识他吗？” 
女人双臂交叉。“当然。他是我爸爸。他去休假了。现在，可以请你们出去吗？我有重要的工作要做。” 
"Mr. Copper disappeared," Detective Smith said. "Do you know him?"
The woman folded her arms. "Of course I do. He's my father. He went on vacation. Now can you please leave? I have important work to do."
罗西和史密斯侦探走了出来。就在这时，罗西大吃一惊。
婴儿们正沿着人行道爬行。
“我先生去哪里了？” 一个女人大声说道，“为什么那个婴儿戴着他的领带？” 
Roxy and Detective Smith went outside. Right away Roxy gasped.
Babies crawled along the sidewalk.
"Where did my husband go?" a woman shouted. "And why is that baby wearing his tie?"
“人们正在变成婴儿！” 史密斯侦探说。
“吧！吧！吧！” 他手里抱着的婴儿流着口水在唱歌。
罗西再次吃了一惊。“这个婴儿看上去跟库珀先生非常像。我觉得他应该就是库珀先生！” 
"People are turning into babies!" Detective Smith said.
"Ba-ba-ba!" The baby in his arms sang and drooled.
Roxy gasped again. "This baby looks just like Mr. Copper. I think it is him!"
“那在办公室的那个女人呢？” 史密斯侦探问，“她真的是库珀先生的女儿吗？” 
 罗西迅速返回办公室。那个女人不见了，保险箱变空了。
"What about that woman in the office?" Detective Smith asked. "Was it really Mr. Copper's daughter?"
Roxy rushed back into the office. The woman was gone, and the safe was empty!
罗西盯着空空的保险箱。“那个女人抢劫了保险箱。” 
她飞回到外面。
史密斯侦探的外套躺在人行道上。一个婴儿从外套里爬出来。“吧！吧！吧！” 
Roxy stared at the empty safe. "That woman robbed the safe!"
She flew back outside.
Detective Smith's coat lay on the sidewalk. A baby crawled out from under it. "Ba-ba-ba!"
罗西大吃一惊。“史密斯侦探！您变成了一个婴儿！” 
哐当！罗西转过身来，看到一辆汽车撞在另一辆面包车上。一个婴儿站在方向盘后面，咯咯笑着。
一个男人从商店走出来。“这些婴儿是从哪里来的？” 
Roxy was greatly surprised. "Detective Smith—you're a baby!"
Crash! Roxy spun around as a car rolled into a parked van. A baby stood behind the wheel, giggling.
A man walked out of a store. "Where did all these babies come from?"
一辆公交车飞快地开过去。差点儿撞到人了。
一个坐在公交车上的女人从窗户里大喊。“救命啊！司机是个婴儿，她不会开车！” 
嗖！罗西追上公交车。她飞进车里，拎起婴儿司机。然后，她踩了刹车。
A bus zipped by. It almost hit someone.
A woman inside the bus yelled out of a window. "Help! The driver is a baby! She can't drive!"
Zoom! Roxy shot after the bus. She flew inside and picked up the baby driver. Then she hit the brakes
罗西和女人把所有的婴儿都集中起来，让他们坐在人行道上。“咻！” 罗西叹了一口气。
“我得告诉布洛姆市长发生了什么事。” 罗西想。她打开手表。一个婴儿坐在布洛姆市长的椅子上。
Roxy and the woman gathered all the babies. They sat them on the sidewalk. "Whew!" Roxy said.
"I need to tell Mayor Bloom what's happening," Roxy thought. She opened her watch. A baby was sitting in Mayor Bloom's chair.
“哦，不！” 罗西大声叫道，“布洛姆市长也变成了婴儿！” 
罗西看到附近还有一个婴儿。他正在咬一个钱包。婴儿把钱包扔了，爬走了。
"Oh no!" Roxy cried. "Mayor Bloom is a baby too!"
Roxy saw another baby nearby. He was chewing on a wallet. The baby dropped the wallet and crawled away.
罗西捡起钱包。里面有一张名片。“万达SPA会所：我们新的护理能让您年轻几岁！” 
“这就是史密斯侦探去的那家SPA会所！” 罗西说。
不一会儿，罗西就到了万达SPA会所。两个女人笑着走了出来。
Roxy picked up the wallet. Inside was a business card: "Vanda's Spa Club. Our new beauty treatment will make you years younger!"
"That's the spa that Detective Smith went to!" Roxy said.
A moment later Roxy arrived at Vanda's Spa Club. Two women walked out smiling.
“这里的护理真是不错！” 一个女人说。
“我们看起来棒极了！” 另外一个女人说。
罗西跑到中心里面。她看到柜台后面有一个女人，看上去很眼熟。
“你刚才在美罗城管道供应公司！” 罗西大声说，“你说你是库珀先生的女儿！” 
"That treatment was wonderful," one woman said.
"We look fabulous!" the other said.
Roxy ran inside. Roxy saw a woman who looked familiar behind the counter.
"You were at Metro City Plumbing Supply!" Roxy cried. "You said you were Mr. Copper's daughter!"
女人走向罗西。“我叫万达。你来这里是为了做护理吗，火箭女孩儿？” 
“不是！” 罗西说，“我……” 
The woman walked toward Roxy. "My name is Vanda. Are you here for a treatment, Rocket Girl?"
"No," Roxy said. "I—"
突然，那个女人把罗西推到椅子上！咔嚓！罗西被困住了。一个玻璃罩从上方罩下来。 玻璃罩和大水箱之间用一根管子连着。水箱上覆盖着冰霜。
“怎么回事儿啊？” 罗西拼命挣扎。
The woman suddenly pushed Roxy into a chair. Click! Roxy was strapped in! A glass dome came down over her head. A hose connected the dome to a big tank. The tank was covered in frost.
"What's going on?" Roxy desperately struggled.
万达大笑。“我的护理能让人变成婴儿。那样我就可以偷他们的东西了！” 
“我不会让你逃掉的！” 罗西咬着牙说。
“不，你会的！我给你准备了超强度的护理！” 万达按下了水箱的按钮。
Vanda laughed. "My treatment turns people into babies. Then I ca steal their things!"
"I won't let you get away with this!" Roxy said, gritting her teeth.
"Oh, yes, you will! I have a super dose of treatment ready for you!" Vanda pressed a button on the water tank.
罩子里充满了冰凉的雾气。罗西开始变小。“ 哦，不！ 我怎么了？咕咕！ 嘎嘎！” 
A cold mist filled the dome. Roxy began to shrink. "Oh no! What's happening to me? Goo-goo! Ga-ga!"
变成婴儿的火箭女孩儿流着口水咯咯笑着。
万达跑到外面。“火箭女孩儿现在阻止不了我了。我要出去偷更多的钱！” 
变成婴儿的罗西在冰凉的雾气里冷得发抖。她哭起来。
The baby Rocket Girl giggled and drooled.
Vanda hurried outside. "Rocket Girl can't stop me now. I'll go out and steal more money!"
Baby Roxy shivered in the cold mist. She began to cry.
罗西的眼睛发出桔色的光。她的热感视力让雾气变热。突然，罗西变大了。她重新变成了八岁！
“哇！” 罗西说，“万达的护理只有在冷的时候才起作用！” 她看了一下 SPA会所的四周。“我得找出万达，阻止她偷东西。” 
Orange beams radiated from her eyes. Her heat vision warmed up the mist. Suddenly Roxy grew. She was an eight-year-old again!
"Wow!" Roxy said. "Vanda's treatment only works if it's cold!" She looked around the spa. "I have to find Vanda and stop her from stealing."
火箭女孩儿用她的热感视力把水箱加热。然后，拎着它飞走了。火箭女孩儿边飞边把热雾气喷在城市上空。街上的婴儿们慢慢变成了大人。
罗西飞到自己小区的上空时，听到了玛拉的声音。
She used her heat vision to warm up the tank. Then she picked it up and flew off. As she flew, she sprayed the warm mist over the city. Down on the streets, babies slowly turned back into adults.
Roxy was flying over her own neighborhood when she heard Mara.
“火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉大声说，“我需要帮忙！” 
罗西落到地面。她看到玛拉跟一个婴儿和一个小孩儿在一起。
 “见到你太好了。” 玛拉说，“我本来是要帮加森太太照看孩子的。但是，我现在找不到她。她两岁的孩子在这儿， 还有一个来历不明的婴儿！我该怎么办？” 
"Rocket Girl!" Mara cried. "I need help!"
Roxy landed and saw Mara with a toddler and a baby.
"I'm so glad I saw you," Mara said. "I'm supposed to be look after Mrs. Garson's kids. But I can't find her. Her two-year-old is here, and so is this unknown baby! What should I do?"
罗西对着那个婴儿喷了一下热雾气。那个婴儿变成了成人女性。
“加森太太！” 玛拉大声叫道。
加森太太看上去很困惑。“我怎么了？” 
“别担心，加森太太。” 罗西说，“您现在没事了。” 
Roxy sprayed the baby with the warm mist. The baby turned into a grown woman.
"Mrs. Garson!" Mara cried.
Mrs. Garson looked confused. "What happened to me?"
"Don't worry, Mrs. Garson," Roxy said. "You're fine now!"
罗西再次出发了。她把更多的婴儿变回了大人。她的超级耳朵听到了市内传来的警报声。罗西朝声音发出的地方飞过去。万达带着很多袋钱从银行跑了出来。
Roxy took off again. She turned more babies back into adults. Then her super ears heard an alarm going off across town. Roxy flew toward the sound. Vanda was running out of a bank with bags of money.
罗西用她的超级呼吸把水箱变冷。她飞向万达。她喷出了冷雾气。万达变小了。“咕咕，嘎嘎!” 
罗西把变成婴儿的万达抱起来飞走了。
Roxy used her super breath to cool down the tank. She swooped at Vanda. She sprayed cold mist. Vanda grew small. "Goo-goo, ga-ga!"
Roxy scooped up the baby Vanda and flew off.
特勒尔和杰克正在踢足球。
“我看到火箭女孩儿了！” 特勒尔说。
杰克大吃一惊。“她带着一个婴儿！” 
Terrell and Jack were playing soccer.
"I see Rocket Girl!" Terrell said.
Jack was greatly surprised. "She's carrying a baby!"
罗西重新回到美罗城管道供应公司，再次加热了水箱。她把热雾气喷向变成婴儿的史密斯侦探和库珀先生。他们变回了大人。
Back at Metro City Plumbing Supply, Roxy heated up the tank again. Then she sprayed the Detective Smith and Mr. Copper babies. They turned back into adults.
“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿！” 史密斯侦探说，“做一个婴儿真是太糟了！” 
罗西把变成婴儿的万达递给他。“你可以把这个婴儿送进监狱，侦探先生！” 
"Thanks, Rocket Girl!" Detective Smith said. "Being a baby was terrible!"
Roxy handed him the baby Vanda. "You can take this baby to jail, Detective!"
那天晚上，罗西跟朋友在下棋。
“你的工作怎么样，玛拉？” 罗西问。
“很不错。” 玛拉说，“ 我还见了火箭女孩儿！” 
“哇！” 罗西假装很吃惊。
That evening Roxy and her friends were playing a board game.
"How was your job, Mara?" Roxy asked.
"It was great," Mara said. "I saw Rocket Girl!"
"Wow!" Roxy pretended to be surprised.
“我也看到她了。” 特勒尔说，“她在照看孩子。” 
“是吗？” 罗西耸耸肩，“有点儿奇怪哦。” 
特勒尔怀疑地看着她。“是的，的确是很奇怪。” 
"I saw her too," Terrell said. "She was babysitting."
"Really?" Roxy shrugged. "That’s odd."
Terrell gave her a suspicious look. "Yes, it was very odd."
深夜，一辆监狱巴士等在美罗城监狱外面。
一个狱警从监狱走出来看了看四周。“很安全。把犯人带出来吧。” 
又一个狱警出来了。她的身边站着一个带手铐的小丑。突然，几个人影从黑暗中跳了出来。
“不好！” 第一个狱警大声说，“来了更多的小丑！” 
It was late at night. A prison bus waited outside Metro City Prison.
A guard came out of the prison and looked around. "It's all clear. Bring out the prisoner."
Another guard came out. A clown in handcuffs stood next to her. Suddenly several shadows of people jumped out of the darkness.
"Oh no!" the first guard cried. "More clowns came!"
“我今天真不想上学。” 杰克说，“我们一整天都会被关在教室里。” 
罗西和朋友们走在上学的路上。
"I am not looking forward to school today," Jack said. "We're going to be stuck in class all day!"
Roxy and her friends were walking to school.
玛拉挠了挠头。“ 我以为今天魔术师会来学校呢！他要给全校学生表演魔术。” 
“你昨晚没收到潘校长的邮件吗？” 特勒尔问，“魔术师感冒了。今天没有表演。” 
Mara scratched her head. "I thought a magician was coming today. He was going to do a magic show for the entire school."
"Didn't you get the email from Principal Penn last night?" Terrell asked. "The magician has the flu, so there's no show today."
玛拉皱起了眉头。“真可惜。” 
“我希望魔术师早点好起来。” 杰克说，“说不定他能让所有老师都消失。” 他和特勒尔都笑起来。
Mara frowned. "That stinks."
"I hope the magician gets better soon," Jack said. "Maybe he can make all of our teachers disappear!" He and Terrell laughed.
玛拉摇了摇头，叹了一口气。“ 也许魔术师可以让你们俩消失。” 玛拉假装向杰克和特勒尔挥动魔术棒。“阿布拉卡达布拉，变！” 
罗西笑了。“那会很有意思！” 
Mara shook her head and sighed. "Maybe we can get a magician to make you two disappear." Mara pretended to wave a magic wand at Terrell and Jack. "Abracadabra, change!"
Roxy laughed. "Now that would be funny!"
“我想看逃脱术。” 杰克说，“以前我在电视上看过一个男人逃脱。那个男人被绑在很大的玻璃箱里。他必须在玻璃箱装满水以前逃脱！” 杰克双臂交叉，假装挣扎。
"I'd like to see an escape act," Jack said. "Once I saw a guy escape on TV. He was tied up in a big glass tank. He had to escape before the glass tank filled with water!" Jack folded his arms and pretended to struggle.
特勒尔看着罗西。“说不定火箭女孩儿会来我们学校。她会给我们展示她的各种超能力。那将是最精彩的表演！” 
Terrell looked at Roxy. "Maybe Rocket Girl could come to our school. She could show off all her super powers. That would be the best show ever!"
“特勒尔为什么看我？” 罗西想。
“那会很酷！” 玛拉突然说。
“对！” 杰克说。
罗西耸耸肩。“是会很酷。” 她说，“但是，我觉得火箭女孩儿不会来学校表演。” 
"Why did Terrell look at me?" Roxy thought.
"That would be pretty cool!" Mara said suddenly.
"Yeah!" Jack said.
Roxy shrugged. "I guess it would be cool," she said. "But I don't think Rocket Girl does school shows."
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。她停下来打开背包。“嗯……我带作业了吗？” 她一直等着朋友们走远了。特勒尔一直回头看她。
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. She stopped walking and opened her backpack. "Oh, um, did I remember my homework?" She waited until her friends had walked a little more. Terrell kept looking back at her.
“布洛姆市长！” 罗西小声说，“有什么事吗？” 
“有一个坏消息，火箭女孩儿。” 市长看起来很严肃，“昨天晚上一个危险的犯人从美罗城监狱逃走了。” 
“谁逃走了？” 罗西问。
"Mayor Bloom," Roxy whispered. "What's wrong?"
"Bad news, Rocket Girl." The mayor looked very serious. "A dangerous criminal escaped from Metro City Prison late last night."
"Who?" Roxy asked.
“他是我们市里最可怕、最邪恶的犯人之一。” 布洛姆市长说。“他叫巴布斯。” 
罗西扬起一边的眉毛。“他叫巴布斯？” 
布洛姆市长点点头。
罗西耸耸肩。“我知道了，市长先生。我马上就到！” 
"He's one of the most terrible, evil criminals in the city," Mayor Bloom said. "His name is Bubbles."
Roxy raised an eyebrow. "His name is Bubbles?"
Mayor Bloom nodded.
Roxy shrugged. "Okay, Mayor. I'm on my way!"
“巴布斯从监狱逃走了。” 罗西想，“我得帮忙去抓他！” 
罗西朝着朋友们大声喊道：“嗨，朋友们！等会儿学校见。我忘了带作业！” 
"Bubbles escaped from prison," Roxy thought. "I have to help catch him!"
Roxy called to her friends. "Hey, guys! I'll meet you at school. I forgot my homework!"
特勒尔看着罗西匆匆离开。“嗯……” 他说，“真想知道……” 他又摇了摇头。“不对，她应该不是。” 
很快，罗西就飞上了天空。她落在美罗城监狱的停车场里。一辆监狱囚车翻倒在地上。 监狱的栅栏上有一个大洞。
Terrell watched Roxy hurry away. "Hmm," he said. "I wonder . . ." He shook his head. "No, she couldn't be."
A moment later Roxy was zooming through the air. She landed in the Metro City Prison parking lot. A prison bus lay on its side. There was a big hole in the fence.
史密斯侦探正在跟两个狱警谈话。他拿着笔和笔记本。狱警看上去很紧张。
罗西咧着嘴笑了。“天啊！侦探先生。我不知道你被关进监狱了呢！” 
Detective Smith was talking to two guards. He held a pen and a small notepad. The guards looked nervous.
Roxy grinned. "Oh no, Detective! I didn't know you were sent to prison!"
史密斯侦探转向火箭女孩儿的方向。“现在不是开玩笑的时候，火箭女孩儿。有一个非常危险的犯人逃走了。” 
“我已经知道了。” 罗西说。
史密斯侦探重新转向两个狱警。“跟我说说那个犯人吧。他叫巴布斯，对吧？” 
Detective Smith turned to Roxy. "This is no time for jokes, Rocket Girl. A very dangerous prisoner escaped."
"I know," Roxy said.
Detective Smith turned back to the guards. "So tell me about the prisoner. His name is Bubbles, right?"
一个狱警点点头。“他是美罗城最坏的犯人之一。他是个小丑。” 
史密斯侦探的笔掉到了地上。“你说他是个小......小丑？” 
“对的。” 那个狱警说。
史密斯侦探的脸变得苍白。
One guard nodded. "He's one of the worst criminals in Metro City. He's a clown."
Detective Smith dropped his pen. "Did you say he's a c-clown?"
"That's right," the guard said.
Detective Smith's face went pale.
罗西捅了捅侦探的肩膀。“侦探先生，您还好吗？” 
史密斯侦探什么都没说。
罗西看着狱警。“ 那么巴布斯是怎么逃走的？” 
Roxy tapped the detective's shoulder. "Detective, are you okay?"
Detective Smith didn't say anything.
Roxy looked at the guards. "So how did Bubbles escape?"
女狱警发着抖。“我带着巴布斯从监狱里出来。我们打算把他送到别的监狱。当我走出来的时候，他的同伙在黑暗中等着。他们抢了巴布斯，逃走了。” 
The female guard shuddered. "I was leading Bubbles out of the prison. We were going to take him to a different prison. But when I stepped outside, his gang was waiting in the dark. They grabbed Bubbles and ran off."
“他的同伙有谁？” 罗西问，“你们看清楚他们了吗？” 
第一个狱警点点头。“当然。他们也是小丑，跟巴布斯一样。” 
"Who is in his gang?" Roxy asked. "Did you get a good look at any of them?"
The first guard nodded. "We sure did. They were clowns too, just like Bubbles."
史密斯侦探看上去很不舒服。
“侦探先生，您今天怎么了？” 罗西问，“你的行为有点古怪。” 
就在这时，史密斯侦探的手机响了。手机在他的口袋里，他好像没听到。
"Gulp!" Detective Smith looked ill.
"Detective, what is wrong with you today?" Roxy asked. "You're acting strange."
Just then the detective's phone rang. It was in his pocket, but he didn't seem to hear it.
“史密斯侦探！” 罗西说，“你的手机在响。你不接吗？” 
“嗯？” 史密斯侦探突然看着罗西。“哦！是我的手机。” 史密斯侦探从口袋里掏出手机。
"Detective Smith," Roxy said. "Your phone is ringing. Are you not going to answer it?"
"Huh?" Detective Smith suddenly looked at Roxy. "Oh! My phone. Right." The detective pulled his phone from his pocket.
“喂？什么？哦……嗯，好吧。 我想我们会……嗯……去查看一下的。” 史密斯侦探挂了电话，看着罗西。“刚才一名警察发现一辆小丑车在西街上超速行驶。” 
"Hello? What? Oh . . . Um, okay. We'll, um, go and check it out, I guess." Detective Smith hung up the phone and looked at Roxy. "A policeman just spotted a tiny clown car speeding down West Street."
“那肯定是巴布斯！” 罗西说，“我们得赶到那儿，侦探先生。我们……侦探先生？您在哪儿？” 
"That must be Bubbles!" Roxy said. "We'd better get over there, Detective. Let's . . . Detective? Where are you?"
“史密斯侦探！” 罗西挠了挠头。“他去哪儿了呢？” 
一个狱警指了指监狱囚车。
罗西飞过去。她看到史密斯侦探躲在车后面。
罗西皱起了眉头。“您在做什么？我们得去抓巴布斯！” 
"Detective Smith!" Roxy scratched her head. "Where did he go?"
One of the guards pointed toward the bus.
Roxy flew over. She found the detective hiding behind the bus.
Roxy frowned. "What are you doing? We have to catch Bubbles!"
史密斯侦探咬了咬嘴唇。“你不要告诉任何人。我怕小丑。” 
 罗西吓了一跳。“真的吗？” 
“真的！” 史密斯侦探说，“你能自己去抓巴布斯吗？” 
Detective Smith bit his lip. "Don't tell anyone. But I'm afraid of clowns."
Roxy was shocked. "Really?"
"Yes!" Detective Smith said. "So can you catch Bubbles on your own?"
罗西双手掐腰。“我不会告诉任何人您怕小丑的，侦探先生。但是，您得面对自己的恐惧。” 
史密斯侦探叹了一口气。“你说得对。你先走。我开着巡逻车跟你在市内见！” 
“好的，侦探先生，” 罗西说，“您一定要去哦。” 
Roxy put her hands on her hips. "I won't tell anyone you're afraid of clowns, Detective. But you should really face your fear."
Detective Smith sighed. "You're right. You go ahead. I'll follow in my patrol car and meet you downtown."
"Okay, Detective," Roxy said. "You should come right away!"
罗西飞走了。她很快就发现了一辆小小的小丑车在市内开得飞快。两辆警车跟在后面。 
一个小丑从小车的窗户伸出头来。他的头发绿得发亮。“我再也不会回到那个肮脏的监狱了！你们听到了吗？绝对不会了！” 
Roxy flew off. She soon spotted a tiny clown car speeding through downtown Metro City. Two police cars chased it.
A clown leaned out of the tiny car's window. His hair was bright green. "I'm never going back to that filthy prison! Do you hear me? Never!"
罗西的眼睛发射出激光。嗞！那辆小车的一个轮胎爆了。小车打滑，停下了。
那个绿头发的小丑从车里走下来。他的夹克上别着一朵花。另外一个小丑也下车了。接着还有两个小丑也下车了。
Roxy fired her eye laser beams. Whiz-hoo! One of the tiny car's tires popped. The car skidded to a stop.
The clown with green hair stepped out. A flower was pinned to his jacket. Another clown got out of the car. Then two more clowns got out too.
“那么小的车，他们怎么坐下的？” 罗西想。
绿头发的小丑盯着罗西。“火箭女孩儿！” 
“我会把你送回监狱的，巴布斯！” 罗西大声说，“你们一伙都会跟着你进去的。” 
"How did they all fit in that tiny car?" Roxy thought.
The clown with green hair glared at Roxy. "Rocket Girl!"
"I'm taking you back to prison, Bubbles!" Roxy shouted. "And everyone in your gang will be joining you!"
巴布斯哈哈大笑。“你们怎么想？让那个小姑娘把我们送进监狱吗？” 
其他的小丑都笑了。
“绝对不行，老大！” 
“监狱听起来太可怕了！” 
Bubbles laughed loudly. "What do you think, boys? Should we let this little girl take us to prison?"
The other clowns laughed.
"No way, boss!"
"Prison sounds terrible!"
巴布斯盯着罗西看。“你听到小丑们说的了吧，我们不去！” 他从口袋里拿出一个瓶子，按了一下按钮。有液体喷出来。
罗西跳起来，液体射中了邮箱，邮箱被熔化了。
Bubbles stared at Roxy. "You heard the clowns. We're not going!" He pulled a bottle from his pocket and pressed a button. Liquid sprayed out.
Roxy jumped up, and the liquid hit a mailbox. The mailbox melted into a puddle.
“呃！” 罗西咽了一口口水。“这个小丑真是可恶！” 
“哈哈哈！” 巴布斯坏笑着，再次按下按钮。但是，再也没有液体出来了。
"Yikes!" Roxy gulped. "This clown really is evil!"
"Ha-ha-ha!" Bubbles let out an evil laugh and pressed the button again. But no more liquid came out.
“呃！用光了！” 巴布斯把瓶子扔到地上。
“别担心，老大！” 另外一个小丑跑向小车，“让火箭女孩儿领教一下这个！” 他猛地打开后备箱。罗西听到轰隆声和刺耳的摩擦声。
罗西吓得倒吸了一口气。巨大的气球动物从后备箱跑了出来。
"Ugh! It's empty!" Bubbles threw the bottle at the ground.
"Don't worry, boss!" Another clown ran back to the tiny car. "This will take care of Rocket Girl!" He popped open the trunk. Roxy heard a rumble and some loud squeaks.
Roxy gasped. Big balloon animals leaped from the trunk!
气球动物们开始砸玻璃，追赶人。小丑们笑着跑走了。
哐！气球狮子把热狗摊推倒了。
“我的热狗！” 老板大声喊道。
“火箭女孩儿，救救我！” 一个女人尖叫着。气球老虎张大了嘴巴追赶她。
The balloon animals started smashing windows and chasing people. The clowns laughed and ran off.
Crash! A balloon lion knocked over a hot dog stand.
"My hot dogs!" the owner cried.
"Rocket Girl, help!" a woman cried. A balloon tiger snapped its jaws at her.
罗西赶紧飞向气球老虎。老虎转过身，面对着罗西。罗西抓住它，把它按倒在地上。老虎挣脱了，把罗西压在了下面。
“啊！” 罗西跟老虎扭打在一起。她使劲儿掐住气球。
Roxy shot toward the balloon tiger. The tiger spun around and faced her. Roxy grabbed it and held it on the ground. The tiger wriggled free and Roxy became buried beneath it.
"Grr!" Roxy struggled with the big balloon. She squeezed as hard as she could.
嘭！气球老虎破了，边放气边在空中乱飞。很快， 泄了气的气球掉在街上。
罗西迅速把其他气球动物都打破了。然后，她去追小丑们。
Pop! The balloon tiger zipped back and forth as the air left it. The airless balloon fell onto the street.
Roxy quickly popped all the other balloon animals. Then she went after the clowns.
特勒尔，杰克和玛拉正在上科学课。
特勒尔指着窗外。“我看到小丑了！” 
玛拉挠了挠头。“他们为什么要跑呢？” 
Terrell, Jack, and Mara were in science.
Terrell pointed out the window. "I see clowns!"
Mara scratched her head. "Why are they jogging?"
巴布斯不跑了。
“我们休息一会儿！” 他说，“我要……喘......口气。” 
其他小丑都倒下了。
“我跑不动了，老大。” 一个小丑说，“腿太累了！” 
“真不该把车留下。” 另外一个小丑说。
Bubbles stopped jogging.
"Let's take a break," he said. "I need . . . to catch . . . my breath."
The other clowns fell over.
"I can't run anymore, boss," one said. "My legs are tired!"
"We shouldn't have left the car," another said.
巴布斯点点头。“这次逃跑不顺利啊。” 
“原来你们在这儿！” 罗西猛地飞向小丑们。
 “大家快点儿！” 巴布斯大喊道，“跑！” 
其他的小丑想要动，但是警察已经赶到把他们包围了。
Bubbles nodded. "This escape isn't going well."
"There you are!" Roxy swooped down toward the clowns.
"Everyone, fast!" Bubbles cried. "Run!"
The other clowns tried to move. But police officers arrived and surrounded them.
罗西没有看到史密斯侦探。“我觉得他还是怕小丑。” 
罗西抓住巴布斯的胳膊。
“你会回到监狱去的！” 她说。
巴布斯从他的口袋里拿出一个橡皮鸡。“变大！” 
Roxy didn't see Detective Smith. "I guess he's still afraid of clowns."
She grabbed Bubbles' arm.
"You're going back to prison!" she said.
Bubbles pulled a rubber chicken from his pocket. "Grow!"
橡皮鸡很快变大。
咯！咯！巨大的橡皮鸡对着罗西啄。嗞！罗西的眼睛发射出激光，把它炸成了碎片。
特勒尔看了看四周。“火箭女孩儿出现的时候，罗西总是不在。” 他想。
The rubber chicken grew fast.
Cluck, cluck! The giant rubber chicken pecked at Roxy. Whiz-hoo! Roxy's eye laser beams blasted it into little pieces.
Terrell looked around. "Roxy is never around when Rocket Girl shows up," he thought.
巴布斯捏了一下夹克上的花。一股烟雾冒了出来。罗西觉得小丑从她的手上溜走了。
“他去哪儿了？” 罗西什么也看不到。她听到咔嚓的声音。罗西用她的超级呼吸把烟雾吹散了。
Bubbles squeezed the flower on his jacket. Smoke poured out. Roxy felt the clown slip from her hand.
"Where did he go?" Roxy couldn't see anything. She heard a click. Roxy used her super breath to blow away the smoke.
史密斯侦探站在巴布斯的旁边。小丑戴着手铐。
“您来了！” 罗西说。
史密斯侦探点点头。“我决定去面对自己的恐惧，就像你说的那样。谢谢你，火箭女孩儿。” 
Detective Smith stood next to Bubbles. The clown was in handcuffs.
"You came!" Roxy said.
Detective Smith nodded. "I decided to face my fear, just like you said. Thanks, Rocket Girl."
罗西走进学校。
“你错过了小丑，罗西。” 杰克说。 
“还有一只大橡皮鸡！” 玛拉说。
“真的吗？” 罗西做出吃惊的样子。
Roxy walked into school.
"You missed the clowns, Roxy!" Jack said.
"And a giant rubber chicken!" Mara said.
"Really?" Roxy pretended to be surprised.
特勒尔怀疑地看着罗西。“你也错过了火箭女孩儿，又一次。” 
罗西只是耸耸肩。
Terrell gave Roxy a suspicious look. "You also missed Rocket Girl–again."
Roxy just shrugged
一个保安站在真实储蓄银行里面。他看了一下手表。“银行开门时间到了。” 
  他打开锁，推开了门。几个高大的人站在门口。
“啊！” 其中一个人咆哮着说，“把你们所有的钱都给我们！” 
A security guard stood inside True Savings Bank. He looked at his watch. "It's time to open the bank."
He unlocked the door and pushed it open. Several large people were standing at the entrance.
"Arr!" one of the people growled. "Give us all your loot!"
“走这边。” 杰克看着手机说，“跟着我！” 
罗西和她的朋友们在玩儿寻宝游戏。杰克用手机查找宝藏箱的位置。有人把箱子藏在了美罗城公园里。
"It's this way." Jack was looking at his phone. "Follow me!"
Roxy and her friends were on a scavenger hunt. Jack was using his phone and looking for directions to a treasure box. Someone had hidden the box in Metro City Park.
“你们觉得箱子里会有什么东西？” 玛拉问。
“我希望是一些很酷的东西。” 特勒尔说，“说不定箱子里装满了糖果。” 
“我希望是宝藏！” 杰克继续看着手机说，“现在，我们要往右转了。” 
“要是宝藏就太棒了！” 特勒尔说，“我们就都变成有钱人了！” 
"What do you think will be in the box?" Mara asked.
"I hope it's something cool," Terrell said. "Maybe the box is filled with candy!"
"I hope it's treasure!" Jack said, still looking down at his phone. "Now we need to turn right."
"Treasure would be awesome," Terrell said. "We'd all be rich!"
罗西笑了。“我怀疑我们能不能找到宝藏。也许箱子里只有一张纸条。也许是一些羽毛。” 
杰克拐进了一条小路。他走路的时候一直看手机。
Roxy laughed. "I doubt we'll find treasure. The box will probably just have a note. And maybe some bird feathers."
Jack turned onto a path. He looked closely at his phone as he walked.
玛拉担心地看着杰克。“你看着路走，杰克。你会……” 
“哎呦！” 杰克被树根绊倒了。他摔倒时，手里的手机飞了出去。他坐起来，对着玛拉咧嘴笑了。“我会……被什么东西绊倒吗？” 
Mara gave him a worried look. "Watch where you're walking, Jack. You might—"
"Oof!" Jack tripped over a tree root. The phone flew out of his hand as he fell. He sat up and grinned at Mara. "I might . . . trip over something?"
特勒尔捡起杰克的手机。“别担心。没摔坏。” 他把手机递给杰克。
他们往前走了一会儿。杰克停下来挠了挠头。“我们好像走错路了。” 他看着手机抱怨道，“这个地图有问题。” 
Terrell picked up Jack's phone. "Don't worry. It's not broken." He handed it back to Jack.
They walked a little farther. Then Jack stopped and scratched his head. "I think we went the wrong way." He groaned as he looked at his phone. "This map doesn't make any sense."
“真可惜火箭女孩儿不在这里。” 特勒尔说，“我相信她很快就能找到箱子！” 他看着罗西，“对吧，罗西？” 
罗西咽了一下口水。“呃哦！” 她想，“我觉得他知道了。” 
玛拉笑了。“特勒尔，火箭女孩儿有更重要的事情要做。” 
“是的。” 杰克说，“火箭女孩儿总是忙着打大坏蛋们。” 
"It's too bad Rocket Girl isn't here," Terrell said. "I bet she could find the box really fast!" He stared at Roxy. "Right, Roxy?"
Roxy gulped. "Uh-oh," she thought. "I think he knows!"
Mara laughed. "Rocket Girl has better things to do, Terrell."
"Yeah," Jack said. "She's always busy fighting super villains."
罗西赶紧点点头。“是的！火箭女孩儿……嗯……有别的事要做。” 
特勒尔耸耸肩。“也许吧。不过，她要是在这儿的话，一定能帮我们找到那个箱子的。她可以用 X射线力透视所有的东西。” 
Roxy quickly nodded. "Right! Rocket Girl has, um, other things to do."
Terrell shrugged. "Maybe. But if she was here, she could definitely find the box for us. She could use her x-ray vision and see right through everything."
罗西的手表响了。“哦，我把水瓶掉哪儿了。” 她说，“你们继续走。我会跟上来的。” 
罗西按了一下手表上的按钮。“布洛姆市长。您有什么事吗？” 
Roxy's watch beeped. "Oh, I dropped my water bottle somewhere," she said. "You guys go ahead. I'll catch up to you."
Roxy pressed a button on her watch. "Mayor Bloom. What's wrong?"
“火箭女孩儿！” 市长说，“真实储蓄银行刚才被抢劫了。我们需要你的帮助！” 
罗西点点头。“请您相信我，市长！” 
"Rocket Girl," the mayor said. "True Savings Bank was just robbed. We need your help!"
Roxy nodded. "You can count on me, Mayor!"
罗西向朋友们大声喊。朋友们已经走远了。“我很快就回来！我还没找到我的水壶！” 
“等等！” 特勒尔回答道，“我们可以帮忙……” 
在特勒尔说完之前，罗西已经跑不见了。她很快就飞向天空。
Roxy called to her friends. They were farther up the trail. "I'll be back in a minute! I still can't find my water bottle!"
"Wait!" Terrell called back. "We can help—"
Before Terrell could finish, Roxy ran off. A moment later she shot through the sky.
“哇！” 玛拉大喊，“是火箭女孩儿！” 
特勒尔摇了摇头。“我们看到火箭女孩儿的时候，罗西总是不在。” 
罗西到了真实储蓄银行。前面停着警车。银行里面，史密斯侦探站在柜台后面。
"Whoa!" Mara cried. "Rocket Girl!"
Terrell shook his head. "Roxy is never around when we see Rocket Girl."
Roxy arrived at True Savings Bank. Police cars were parked in front. Inside, Detective Smith was standing behind the counter.
“先生， 您好！” 罗西说，“我想开户。” 
史密斯侦探皱起了眉头。“很有意思，火箭女孩儿。不过，我们有一个案子要破。这家银行被抢劫了。” 
“我知道。” 罗西说，“您知道强盗是谁吗？” 
史密斯侦探摇了摇头。“我也是刚到的。我正在找线索。” 
"Hello, sir," Roxy said. "I'd like to open a bank account."
Detective Smith frowned. "Very funny, Rocket Girl. But we have a crime to solve. This bank was robbed."
"I know," Roxy said. "Do you know who the robber is?"
Detective Smith shook his head. "I just got here a moment ago. I'm looking for clues."
“强盗不止一个。” 一个保安跑过来说，“他们有一伙。他们真的太可怕了，又脏又丑又凶！” 
史密斯侦探从口袋里掏出一个小本子。“能描述一下他们的长相吗？” 
"It wasn't just one robber." A security guard ran over. "There was a whole group of them. They were horrible—dirty and smelly and mean!"
Detective Smith took his small notebook from his pocket. "Can you describe what they looked like?"
保安点点头。“强盗头目戴着一顶大帽子，手上有一个钩子。一只鹦鹉坐在她的肩上。鹦鹉不停地说‘哟呵呵’！” 
史密斯侦探扬起一边的眉毛。“哟呵呵？” 
“对的！” 保安说，“哟呵呵。” 
“别的强盗长什么样子呢？” 罗西问。
The security guard nodded. "The boss wore a large hat and has a hook for a hand. A parrot was sitting on her shoulder. It kept saying 'Yo-ho-ho!'"
Detective Smith raised an eyebrow. "Yo-ho-ho?"
"That's right," the security guard said. "Yo-ho-ho."
"What did the other robbers look like?" Roxy asked.
保安摸了摸下巴。“其他的三个强盗。一个留着长胡子，戴着一只眼罩；另外两人戴着头巾，一个人有一条木腿。” 
“听起来像是海盗！” 罗西说。
The security guard rubbed his chin. "There were three other robbers. One had a long beard and an eye patch. The other two wore bandannas. One guy had a wooden leg."
"It sounds like they're pirates!" Roxy said.
史密斯侦探挠了挠头。“美罗城没有海盗。他们一定是从别的地方来的。” 
“在他们抢劫另外一家银行之前，我们必须阻止他们。” 罗西说。
 就在这时，史密斯侦探的电话响了。“喂？天啊！好的，我们马上赶过去。” 
Detective Smith scratched his head. "There aren't any pirates in Metro City. They must be from out of town."
"We have to stop them before they rob another bank," Roxy said.
Just then Detective Smith's phone beeped. "Hello? Oh no! Okay, we'll hurry over there right now!"
“发生什么事了？” 罗西问，“那些海盗又抢了别的银行了吗？” 
“不是！” 史密斯侦探说，“他们正在吃午饭。” 
“嗯？” 罗西糊涂了。
"What's going on?" Roxy asked. "Are the pirates robbing another bank?"
"Nope," Detective Smith said. "They're eating lunch."
"Huh?" Roxy was confused.
“那些海盗在‘码头餐厅’。 那是城里最高档的海鲜餐厅。” 史密斯侦探说，“餐厅老板说他们惹了很多麻烦。把餐厅搞得一团糟，摔东西，威胁别的客人。” 
"The pirates are at The Wharf. That's the city's fanciest seafood restaurant," Detective Smith said. "The owner said they're causing lots of trouble. They are making a mess, breaking things, and scaring the other customers."
罗西双臂交叉。“我们得去抓他们！” 
史密斯侦探把手机放进口袋。“好的，火箭女孩儿。我们……火箭女孩儿？” 
Roxy folded her arms. "We have to catch them!"
Detective Smith put away his phone. "Okay, Rocket Girl. Let's—Rocket Girl?"
嗖！罗西快速地飞过美罗城。“我得阻止这些海盗。” 她想。
罗西看到了“码头餐厅” 。 很多人正从里面跑出来。他们看起来很害怕。一声巨响从餐厅传来。接着，罗西听到了笑声。
Whoosh! Roxy zoomed over Metro City. "I have to stop those pirates," she thought.
She saw a restaurant called The Wharf. Many people dashed out from inside. They looked scared. A loud crash came from inside the restaurant. Then Roxy heard laughter.
罗西冲进餐厅。地上到处是食物和摔破的盘子。人们躲在椅子后面和桌子下面。
“太可怕了！” 一个女人尖叫道，“我应该在家吃的！” 
Roxy rushed into the restaurant. Food and broken plates covered the floor. People were hiding behind chairs and under tables.
"This is terrible!" a woman cried. "I should have eaten at home!"
长相凶恶的海盗们围着长桌站着，又叫又笑。一个服务员站在桌子上。海盗们用剑指着他。他吓得直发抖。
“你要去走木板！” 一个海盗大声说。她的肩上坐着一只鹦鹉。
Mean-looking pirates stood around one long table, shouting and laughing. A waiter stood on the table. He shook with fear as the pirates pointed swords at him.
"You're going to walk the plank!" one pirate shouted. A parrot sat on her shoulder.
“木板！” 鹦鹉说。
服务员咬着嘴唇。“火箭女孩儿在这里就好了！” 
“谁是火箭女孩儿？” 那个海盗问。
“谁是火箭女孩儿？” 鹦鹉说。
“我就是！” 罗西说，“现在，我要阻止这件事！” 
"The plank!" the parrot said.
The waiter bit his lip. "I wish Rocket Girl was here!"
"Who's Rocket Girl?" the pirate asked.
"Who's Rocket Girl?" the parrot said.
"I am!" Roxy said. "And I'm putting a stop to this right now!"
海盗们猛地转过身来。
“咻！” 服务员说，“谢谢你，火箭女孩儿！” 
罗西盯着海盗们。“你们不可以在餐厅里这样乱来！” 
The pirates spun around.
"Whew!" the waiter said. "Thanks, Rocket Girl!"
Roxy glared at the pirates. "This is not how you behave in a restaurant!"
“我叫邦尼·博恩斯。” 带着鹦鹉的海盗说，“我们是海盗，我们想怎么来就怎么来。我们抢劫银行，制造麻烦！” 她踢倒了椅子。
“哟呵呵！” 鹦鹉说。
“你们都被捕了！” 罗西说。
"My name is Bonnie Bones," the pirate with the parrot said. "We're pirates, and we behave any way we like. We rob banks and we cause trouble!" She kicked a chair.
"Yo-ho-ho!" the parrot said.
"You're all under arrest," Roxy said.
邦尼·博恩斯用钩子指着罗西说：“ 抓住她！” 
“啊！” 海盗们挥着剑向罗西冲过去。嗞！罗西的眼睛发射出激光。一个海盗的剑被炸断了。
Bonnie Bones pointed her hook at Roxy. "Get her, men!"
"Arr!" The pirates charged toward Roxy, waving their swords. Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams. One pirate's sword exploded.
另一个海盗的剑刺过来，罗西躲开了。剑把桌子劈成了两半。
第三个海盗走上前。他的短剑尖差点儿划到了罗西的鼻子。“你现在有麻烦了。” 他笑着说，“我要……” 
Roxy ducked as another pirate swung his sword at her. The sword split a table in half.
The third pirate stepped closer. The tip of his sword brushed Roxy's nose. "Now you're in trouble!" He laughed. "I'll—"
就在这时，警察冲进餐厅。
三个海盗吓得一动不动。但是，邦尼·博恩斯 冲出了门。罗西紧跟在她后面。
“啊！” 邦尼·博恩斯大声喊道，“你绝对抓不到我，火箭女孩儿！” 她爬上了停车场里的海盗船。
Just then police officers rushed into the restaurant.
Three pirates froze. But Bonnie Bones ran for the door. Roxy shot after her.
"Arr!" Bonnie Bones shouted. "You'll never catch me, Rocket Girl!" She climbed into a big pirate ship in the parking lot.
轰隆！轰隆！海盗船离开地面，飞了起来。
“停下！” 罗西飞在船后面。
咔嚓！船侧面的舱门打开了。罗西看到里面有什么东西。那个东西亮亮的，有锋利的牙齿。它从船里飞出来，嘴巴使劲儿地一张一合。
Rumble, rumble! The ship lifted off the ground and flew away.
"Stop!" Roxy flew after the ship.
Creak! A hatch on the side of the ship opened. Roxy saw something inside. The thing was shiny, with sharp teeth. Its jaws opened and shut strongly as it flew out of the ship.
咔嚓！咔嚓！它对着罗西张开大嘴。
“是一只会飞的机器鲨鱼！” 罗西大喊道。
邦尼·博恩斯笑了。“再见，火箭女孩儿！” 
鹦鹉笑了。“再见，火箭女孩儿！” 
Chomp! Chomp! It snapped at Roxy.
"A flying robot shark!" Roxy cried.
Bonnie Bones laughed. "Good-bye, Rocket Girl!"
The parrot laughed. "Good-bye, Rocket Girl!"
咔嚓！咔嚓！咔嚓！机器鲨鱼冲向罗西。
“哇！” 罗西飞快地躲开。鲨鱼张大的大嘴差点儿咬到她。
地面街道上的人们用手指着天空。
“会飞的机器鲨鱼！” 一个男人喊道。
“逃命啊！” 一个女人大声喊。
Chomp! Chomp! Chomp! The robot shark shot toward Roxy.
"Whoa!" Roxy quickly dodged to the side. The shark's snapping jaws just missed her.
People on the street below pointed.
"A flying robot shark!" a man cried.
"Run!" a woman shouted.
鲨鱼再次向罗西飞过去。鲨鱼的嘴巴张得大大的。
呼！罗西对着鲨鱼吹冷气。鲨鱼的下巴当场被冻住了。
罗西抓住鲨鱼，使劲儿把它扔到地上。它被摔成碎片。
“现在，我要去抓邦尼·博恩斯了！” 
嗖！
The shark flew at Roxy again. Its jaws were wide open.
Whoosh! Roxy blew her freeze breath at the shark. Its jaws froze in place.
Roxy grabbed the shark and swung it toward the ground. It smashed into a million pieces.
"Now I need to catch Bonnie Bones!"
Zoom!
她看到海盗船飞过美罗城公园的上空。罗西落在船的甲板上。邦尼·博恩斯站在船舵的旁边。 她的身边有一门大炮。
“你马上降落这艘船！” 罗西大声喊道，“我要送你去监狱！” 
She spotted the pirate ship flying over Metro City Park. Roxy landed on the ship's deck. Bonnie Bones stood at the wheel. A big cannon sat near her.
"Land this ship right now!" Roxy shouted. "I'm taking you to jail!"
“监狱！” 鹦鹉大声唱到。
“啊！” 邦尼·博恩斯把大炮对准罗西，点燃了导火线。嘭！一枚炮弹发射了出去。罗西跳上前去抓住了炮弹。
"Jail!" the parrot sang.
"Arr!" Bonnie Bones pointed the cannon at Roxy and lit the fuse. Boom! A cannonball shot out. Roxy leaped forward and caught the cannonball.
邦尼·博恩斯睁大了眼睛。“你怎么可以……” 
罗西把炮弹重新扔给邦尼·博恩斯。海盗跳着躲开了。接着，她又点燃了导火线。罗西的眼睛睁得大大的。她的眼睛发射出桔色的光，把大炮熔化了。
Bonnie's eyes went wide. "How did you . . . ?"
Roxy threw the cannonball back at Bonnie. The pirate jumped out of the way. Then she lit the fuse again. Roxy opened her eyes wide. Orange beams shot from her eyes and melted the cannon.
“啊！” 邦尼想要逃走。
嗞！罗西再次用眼睛发射出激光。
邦尼用钩子挡住了激光。激光弹开，击中了船舵。哐！
"Arr!" Bonnie tried to run away.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams.
Bonnie blocked the laser beams with her hook. The beams bounced off and hit the ship's wheel. Ka-boom!
“啊！” 海盗船坠落在公园的时候，邦尼紧紧抓住栏杆。船舱裂开了。 海盗们从银行里抢来的钱都掉了出来。
杰克大吃一惊。“海盗的宝藏！” 
玛拉指着甲板说。“火箭女孩儿！” 
"Ahh!" Bonnie held onto a railing as the ship crash-landed in the park. The ship's hull broke open. Money from the pirates' bank robberies spilled out.
Jack gasped. "Pirate treasure!"
Mara pointed at the ship's deck. "Rocket Girl!"
罗西站在邦尼前面。海盗回头一看。她正站在船的木板上，离地面很高。警察们都在下面等着。
Roxy stood in front of Bonnie. The pirate looked back. She was standing on the ship's plank, the highest place from the ground. Police officers waited below.
“你有两个选择。” 罗西说，“现在去监狱，或者你走完木板以后再去！” 
“走木板！” 鹦鹉唱道。
邦尼·博恩斯低下头，“哎！我们现在去。” 
"You have two choices," Roxy said. "Go to jail now—or after you walk the plank!"
"Walk the plank!" the parrot sang.
Bonnie Bones hung her head. "Arr. We'll go now."
不久，罗西在公园里找到了朋友们。
“你去哪儿了？” 玛拉问，“你错过了所有精彩的事情。” 
“是吗？” 罗西问，“你们找到那个箱子了吗？” 
Later Roxy found her friends in the park.
"Where were you?" Mara asked. "You missed all the excitement!"
"Really?" Roxy asked. "Did you find the box?"
“我们看到了更好的。” 杰克说，“海盗的宝藏！” 
特勒尔点点头。“火箭女孩儿找到的。你大概早就知道，对吧？” 
“嗯？” 杰克说，“罗西怎么可能知道?” 
"We saw something better," Jack said. "Pirate's treasure!"
Terrell nodded. "Rocket Girl found it. But you probably knew that, right?"
"Huh?" Jack said. "How would Roxy know that?"
就在这时，罗西发现灌木丛里有什么东西。“宝藏箱！” 
他们跑过去看里面装了什么东西。 
“咻！” 罗西想，“我的秘密还是安全的。” 
Just then Roxy spotted something under a shrub. "The treasure box!"
They ran over to see what was inside.
"Whew," Roxy thought. "My secret is still safe."
阳光咖啡厅里坐满了人。人们坐在位子上喝咖啡，吃面包。
一个女人站在柜台后面。“下一位。” 
Sunshine Coffee Shop was packed. People sat at tables, drinking coffee and eating baked goods.
A woman stood behind the counter. "I can help the next customer."
一个男人走向柜台。他点了一杯茶。“请再给我一个甜甜圈。” 
他坐下来，吃了一口甜甜圈。突然…….
“啊！” 
A man stepped up to the counter. He ordered a cup of tea. "I'll also have a donut, please."
He sat down and took a bite of his donut. Suddenly . . .
"Grargh!"
“呃！” 杰克看着盘子里的食物，皱起了眉头。“潘校长为什么非得换菜单呢？” 
午餐时间，罗西和她的朋友们在学校食堂里。今天是换新菜单的第一天。他们的盘子里装满了蔬菜和全麦食物。所有食物都是健康，有机的。
"Yuck!" Jack looked at the food on his tray and frowned. "Why did Principal Penn have to change the menu?"
It was lunchtime. Roxy and her friends were in the school cafeteria. Today was the first day with the new lunch menu. The kids' trays were full of vegetables and whole grains. All of the food was now healthy and organic.
特勒尔痛苦地说：“潘校长为什么要这样对我们？以前的菜单，除了牛肉汉堡， 都非常好吃！” 
“你们俩真幼稚。” 玛拉说，“午餐很好吃。” 玛拉吃了一口甘蓝沙拉，笑着说。 接着，她又吃了一些。
Terrell spoke in anguish. "Why did Principal Penn do this to us? Everything on the old menu was delicious, except for sloppy joes."
"You two are acting silly," Mara said. "This lunch is delicious." She took a bite of her kale salad and smiled. She ate some more.
特勒尔用怀疑的眼神看着午餐。他用叉子叉起一个小方块。“这是什么东西？” 
“是豆腐。” 玛拉说，“它是黄豆做的。味道不错。你应该试试。” 
Terrell looked at the lunch food suspiciously. He stuck his fork into a small cube and held it up. "What is this thing?"
"It's tofu," Mara said. "It's made from soybeans. It's good. You should try it."
特勒尔皱起了鼻子。“不了，谢谢。” 
豆腐从叉子上掉了下来。它掉在桌子上，又从桌子上弹到地上。 一个路过的同学踩碎了那块豆腐。它变得又平又黏，上面沾满了灰。杰克和特勒尔笑了。
Terrell wrinkled his nose. "No, thanks!"
The tofu fell off his fork. It bounced off the table and landed on the floor. A kid walking by stepped on the tofu. It was now flat and mushy, with bits of dirt on it. Jack and Terrell laughed.
“我喜欢新菜单。” 罗西说，“还有，潘校长不但要换菜单，她还想每个学生都变得更健康。所以，她延长了十分钟休息时间。” 
“这个改变好！” 杰克说。
"I like the new menu," Roxy said. "Also, this isn't the only thing Principal Penn changed. She wants everyone to be healthier. So she added ten more minutes to recess."
"Now that is a good change!" Jack said.
“是的。不过……” 特勒尔叹了一口气，“火箭女孩儿能把我们从甘蓝和豆腐中解救出来就好了。” 
罗西转了一下眼睛。“火箭女孩儿有更重要的事情要做，特勒尔。而且，火箭女孩儿说不定还很喜欢这些食物呢。” 
"Yeah, but . . ." Terrell sighed. "I wish Rocket Girl would save us from this kale and tofu."
Roxy rolled her eyes. "Rocket Girl has more important things to do, Terrell. And besides, maybe Rocket Girl actually likes this kind of food."
特勒尔怀疑地看了罗西一眼。“ 是吗？你怎么知道？” 
罗西愣住了。“嗯…….” 
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。
Terrell gave Roxy a suspicious look. "She does? How do you know?"
Roxy froze. "Um . . ."
Just then her watch beeped.
“我马上就回来。” 罗西跟朋友们说。她走到走廊，打开手表。
布洛姆市长看起来很害怕。
“发生了什么事情，市长？” 罗西问。
"I'll be right back," Roxy told her friends. She went into the hallway and opened the watch.
Mayor Bloom looked scared.
"What's wrong, Mayor?" Roxy asked.
“火箭女孩儿！发生了可怕的事情。” 布洛姆市长说，“ 饥饿僵尸们正在入侵美罗城！阳光咖啡厅里有一大群！” 
罗西咽了一口口水。“别担心，市长。我马上赶到！” 
"Rocket Girl! Something terrible is happening," Mayor Bloom said. "Hungry zombies are invading Metro City! There's a crowd of them at Sunshine Coffee Shop!"
Roxy gulped. "Don't worry, Mayor. I'm on my way!"
“我得马上赶到阳光咖啡厅。” 罗西想，“僵尸们正在害人！” 
罗西回到位子上。“我刚想起来了。我……嗯…….要去给潘校长帮忙！” 
"I have to get to Sunshine Coffee Shop," Roxy thought. "Zombies are hurting people!"
Roxy went back to the table. "I just remembered. I, uh, need to help Principal Penn!"
罗西快速跑过走廊。她打开门，飞上了天空。
人们站在阳光咖啡厅外面。罗西走近了才发现，他们不是普通人。他们的眼神空洞。他们的头发很乱。他们行走的方式很奇怪。
Roxy ran down the hall. She threw open the door and leaped into the sky.
People stood outside Sunshine Coffee Shop. When Roxy got closer, she saw they were not normal people. Their eyes were blank. Their hair was messy. And they moved in a strange way.
“僵尸！” 罗西说。
一个女人站在阳光咖啡厅的门口。她正拿着扫帚赶僵尸们。僵尸们的大嘴巴一张一合的。
“走开！” 女人吼道。
"Zombies!" Roxy said.
A woman was in the doorway of Sunshine Coffee Shop. She was waving zombies away with a broom. The zombies' mouths snapped open and shut.
"Get out of here!" the woman yelled.
罗西向下飞，推开了门前的僵尸们。她跟女人跑进了屋。女人锁上了身后的门。
Roxy swooped down and pushed the zombies away from the door. Then she ran in with the woman. The woman locked the door behind her.
“咻！” 女人用手擦了一下额头，“真是太可怕了！幸好你来了，火箭女孩儿！” 
“没事儿。” 罗西说。突然，她看到了史密斯侦探。他站在一个柜子旁边。柜子里只剩下几个甜甜圈。他的头发很乱。
"Whew!" The woman ran a hand across her forehead. "That was scary! I'm glad you're here, Rocket Girl."
"No problem," Roxy said. Suddenly she spotted Detective Smith. He stood up near a case with only a few donuts left. His hair was messy.
“啊！” 罗西大声喊道，“还有一个僵尸！” 
史密斯侦探皱起了眉头。“很有意思，火箭女孩儿！” 他用手整理了一下头发。“我早上忘了梳头了。” 
罗西指着窗外问。“是什么让那些人都变成了僵尸？” 
"Ahh!" Roxy cried. "It's another zombie!"
Detective Smith frowned. "Very funny, Rocket Girl." He tried to pat down his hair. "I forgot to brush my hair this morning."
Roxy pointed out the window. "What turned all those people into zombies?"
史密斯侦探挠挠头。他的头发更乱了。“我不太清楚。” 
女人指着柜子说。“是那些甜甜圈。” 
“你怎么知道的？” 罗西问。
Detective Smith scratched his head. His hair got messier. "I'm sure."
The woman pointed at the case. "It was those donuts."
"How do you know?" Roxy asked.
“刚才来了一个男人。” 她说，“他吃了一个甜甜圈以后变得很不正常。他想要咬其他客人，被我赶了出去。后来又有别的人吃了甜甜圈。他们身上也发生了同样事情。” 
"A man came in earlier," she said. "After he ate one of the donuts, he looked strange. He tried to bite another customer, so I chased him outside. Other people ate the donuts after that. The same thing happened to them."
史密斯侦探打开柜子。他拿出一个甜甜圈研究起来。“我觉得跟普通的甜甜圈一样啊。” 
“这种事情以前发生过吗？” 罗西问。
Detective Smith opened the case. He picked up a donut and studied it. "It looks like a regular donut to me."
"Did this ever happen before?" Roxy asked.
女人摇摇头。“一次也没有。我刚刚从一家新面包厂订了这些甜甜圈。这是我收到的第一批。” 
“这家面包厂叫什么名字？” 
“‘勒·斯威特面包厂’。” 女人说，“就在城外，山旁边。” 
The woman shook her head. "Never. I just started ordering these donuts from a new bakery. These are the first ones I got."
"What's the name of the bakery?"
"Le Sweet's," the woman said. "It's just outside the city, near the mountains."
“我去那里看看。” 罗西说。 她跑出咖啡厅，飞走了。
沿着街区，罗西看到乐购超市的门突然打开了。一大群僵尸从门里涌了出来。
"I'll go and check it out," Roxy said. She ran out the door and flew off.
Down the block she saw the door to Shop Well Supermarket fly open. A huge pack of zombies spilled out from the door!
罗西落到一辆卡车上。僵尸们跌跌撞撞地从乐购超市出来。他们的嘴上沾满了面包渣。罗西看到一个僵尸身上粘着勒·斯威特面包厂的包装纸。
Roxy landed on a truck. Zombies stumbled out of Shop Well Supermarket. Crumbs were stuck to their mouths. Roxy saw a Le Sweet wrapper stuck to one zombie.
罗西大吃 一惊。“那个僵尸不是演《大力士》的演员吗？” 
人们边跑边叫。
“啊！僵尸！” 一个老人大喊道。
三个十几岁的少年开始逃跑。其中一个拿着手机。“我要自拍……啊！” 
Roxy was surprised. "That zombie is the Mighty Man actor!"
People were running and shouting.
"Ahh! Zombies!" an old man cried.
Three teenagers started to race away. Then one held up his phone. "I'm going to take a selfie with—Ahh!"
“啊！” 大力士僵尸咯吱咯吱嚼着手机，然后吐了出来。 男孩儿跑去追朋友们。
罗西看到几个人躲在出租车上面。“火箭女孩儿，救救我们！” 僵尸们伸出手抓人。
"Grargh!" The Mighty Man chomped the phone and then spit it out. The boy ran after his friends.
Roxy saw several people huddled on top of a cab. "Rocket Girl, save us!" Zombies reached up, grabbing at the people.
一个老人对着僵尸们挥着他的拐杖。“离我们远一点，你们这些怪物！” 
嗖！罗西飞快地飞上天空。她用超级呼吸吹气。 那些僵尸摔倒后滚到了一起。
“快跑！” 罗西对人们说，“找个地方躲起来。我很快就回来。” 
An old man swung his cane at the zombies. "Get away from us, you monsters!"
Zoom! Roxy shot through the air. She blew her super breath. The zombies tumbled and rolled over each other.
"Run!" Roxy told the people. "Find somewhere to hide. I'll be back soon!"
罗西飞到勒·斯威特面包厂。里面，有两个巨大的烤箱在墙的一侧。机器发出很大的响声。装满甜甜圈的传送带慢慢地滚动着。 一台机器在甜甜圈上加糖霜，另一台机器把甜甜圈运到巧克力浆中。
Roxy flew to Le Sweet's Bakery. Inside, huge ovens lined one wall. Machines hummed loudly. Long belts filled with donuts rolled along slowly. One machine squirted icing onto donuts. Another machine dunked donuts into a tub of chocolate.
“我得把这些机器关上。它在生产甜甜圈，还有僵尸！” 她把所有机器都关上了。面包厂变得很安静。
"I have to shut this place down. It's making donuts—and zombies!" Roxy turned everything off. The bakery became still and silent.
过了一会儿，罗西听到了脚步声。一个戴着围裙和高高的白帽子的男人跑了进来。
“发生什么事了？” 他大声叫道。这时，他看到了罗西。“火箭女孩儿！” 
A second later Roxy heard footsteps. A man with an apron and a tall white hat hurried in.
"What happened?" he cried. Then he spotted Roxy. "Rocket Girl!"
“对不起，先生！” 罗西说，“你也许不知道。你的甜甜圈引起了很大麻烦。你知道……” 
“你以为你可以阻止我吗？” 那个男人生气地看着罗西。
“什么？” 罗西很困惑。
"Sorry, sir," Roxy said. "You might not know this. But your donuts are causing a big problem. You see—"
"You think you can stop me, do you?" The man glared at Roxy.
"Huh?" Roxy was confused.
那个男人接着说：“ 我叫皮特·勒·斯威特，我发明了一种特殊的甜甜圈配方。它太好吃了。所有的人都只想要吃它——我的甜甜圈！” 他大笑。“你阻止不了我，火箭女孩儿！” 
The man continued. "My name is Pete Le Sweet. I invented a special donut recipe. It's so good, everybody will be hungry for one thing—my donuts!" He laughed. "And you won't stop me, Rocket Girl!"
罗西眯起了眼睛。“你是有意把人变成僵尸的？而不是一个意外？” 
勒·斯威特扬起了一边的眉毛。“什么？僵尸？” 
罗西两手掐腰。“你的特殊配方糟透了。你的甜甜圈把人变成了僵尸！” 
Roxy narrowed her eyes. "You planned to turn people into zombies? It wasn't an accident?"
Le Sweet raised an eyebrow. "Huh? Zombies?"
Roxy put her hands on her hips. "Your special recipe stinks, Le Sweet. Your donuts are turning people into zombies!"
勒·斯威特耸耸肩。“只要我能多卖甜甜圈，管他呢！” 他把手放在拉杆上。“再见了，火箭女孩儿。” 
勒·斯威特拉了一下拉杆。巧克力酱洒出来，把罗西完全盖住了。
Le Sweet shrugged. "As long as I'm selling lots of donuts, who cares?" He put his hand on a lever. "Good-bye, Rocket Girl."
Le Sweet pulled the lever. Chocolate syrup rushed out, completely covering Roxy!
“呃！” 罗西在巧克力酱里挣扎。它又黏又重。
罗西慢慢站起来，然后转圈。她转得越来越快，就像龙卷风一样。巧克力酱被甩了出去，溅得到处都是。 
"Grr!" Roxy struggled in the chocolate syrup. It was thick and heavy.
Slowly she stood up. Then she spun around. She spun faster and faster, like a tornado. Drops of syrup flew off of her and splattered all over.
罗西很快就变干净了。她看了看四周。“ 勒·斯威特去哪里了？” 
罗西从一扇窗户飞了出去。“他在那儿！” 
勒·斯威特开着一辆送货车。车子飞快地开向城里。另外一辆送货车翻倒在地上。
Soon Roxy was clean. She looked around. "Where's Le Sweet?"
Roxy flew out a window. "There he is!"
Le Sweet was driving a delivery truck on the road below. The truck was zooming toward the city. A different delivery truck lay on its side.
罗西飞向第二辆送货车。司机站在车旁边。
“发生什么事了？” 罗西问。
司机举起两手。“勒·斯威特把我挤到路边！他抢走了我的送货区。他说我再也不能送全麦饼干了。从现在开始，人们都只吃勒·斯威特的甜甜圈。那个人疯了。” 
Roxy flew to the second truck. The driver stood next to it.
"What happened?" Roxy asked.
The driver threw his hands in the air. "Le Sweet ran me off the road! Then he stole my delivery route. He said I'd never deliver my whole-grain cookies again. From now on, people are only eating Le Sweet donuts. The man is crazy!"
“你的下一个送货区是哪里？” 罗西问。
“美罗城小学。” 男人说。
罗西咽了一口口水。“ 我们得马上去那儿，要快！” 罗西一只手抓着司机，另一只抓着送货车。嗖！罗西飞向天空。
"Where was your next delivery?" Roxy asked.
"Metro City Elementary School," the man said.
Roxy gulped. "We need to go there right now—fast!" She grabbed the driver with one hand. She grabbed the truck with the other hand. Zoom! Roxy shot through the sky!
司机笑了。“哇！” 
当罗西飞过美罗城的时候，她往下看去。她看到了演《大力士》的演员。他正在跟一个人自拍。
“咻！” 罗西想，“他现在看起来很正常。人们不会一直保持僵尸状态的。” 
The driver smiled. "Wow!"
As she flew over the city, Roxy looked down. She saw the Mighty Man actor. He was taking a selfie with someone.
"Whew," Roxy thought. "He looks fine now. People don't stay zombies forever!"
当孩子们正在食堂吃午饭的时候，一个男人走了进来。他手里拿着一摞盒子。
“我叫皮特·勒·斯威特。” 他说，“我来给大家 送免费甜甜圈了！” 
As the kids ate lunch in the cafeteria, a man walked in. He carried a stack of boxes.
"My name is Pete Le Sweet," he said. "I have free donuts for everyone!"
孩子们都拍手，欢呼起来。
勒·斯威特举起一个甜甜圈。“谁想要第一个？” 
“我！” 杰克跑过去。
勒·斯威特递给他一个甜甜圈。突然，食堂的门猛地被打开了。
Everyone clapped and cheered.
Le Sweet held up a donut. "Who wants the first one?"
"Me!" Jack ran over.
Le Sweet handed him the donut. Suddenly the cafeteria doors flew open.
“别吃那个！” 罗西大声喊道。
杰克吓得跳了起来。甜甜圈从他手里飞了出去。 它划过空中，刚好掉在勒·斯威特的嘴里。
“呃！啊！” 
"Don't eat that!" Roxy shouted.
Jack jumped. The donut flew out of his hand. It went up in the air . . . and landed right in Le Sweet's mouth!
"Gulp! Grargh!"
史密斯侦探冲了进来。
罗西笑了。“您可以把这个僵尸送进监狱了，侦探先生！” 
司机走了进来。“谁想吃饼干？” 
大家欢呼起来。
Detective Smith rushed in.
Roxy smiled. "You can take this zombie to jail, Detective!"
The driver stepped forward. "Who wants cookies?"
Everyone cheered.
“你错过了火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉在休息时间对罗西说。
“哦，真可惜。” 罗西说。
特勒尔怀疑地看了罗西一眼。“你总是错过火箭女孩儿。我想知道为什么。” 
"You missed Rocket Girl!" Mara said to Roxy during recess.
"Oh, that's too bad," Roxy said.
Terrell gave Roxy a suspicious look. "You always miss Rocket Girl. I wonder why."
“嗯……” 罗西不知道该怎么说 。
“你还错过了别的事情！” 杰克突然说，“一个奇怪的人吃了甜甜圈以后变成了僵尸！” 
罗西大笑起来。但是，特勒尔还是一幅很怀疑的表情。
"Uh . . ." Roxy didn’t know what to say.
"You missed something else too!" Jack said suddenly. "A weird guy ate a donut and turned into a zombie!"
Roxy laughed. But Terrell still had that suspicious look on his face.
一个狱警在美罗城监狱里巡逻。
“关灯！” 她大声喊道，“睡觉时间到了！” 
牢房里，普雷斯托嘟囔着爬上了床。 威格尔斯夫人和怪人博士在旁边的牢房里。
A guard walked through Metro City Prison.
"Lights out," she called. "It's bedtime!"
In his cell Mr. Presto grumbled and climbed into bed. Mrs. Wiggles and Dr. Odd were in nearby cells.
“我讨厌睡觉时间！” 威格尔斯夫人说。
狱警没有理坏人们。她走到一个拐角。突然，她大吃一惊。墙上有一个巨大的洞。
狱警大声喊道：“犯人逃走了！” 
"I hate bedtime!" Mrs. Wiggles said.
The guard ignored the villain. She walked around a corner. Then she gasped. There was a huge hole in the wall.
The guard shouted. "A prisoner escaped!"
“特勒尔去哪里了？” 杰克问。
罗西和玛拉在杰克家外面等他。
“他今天会迟到一会儿。” 罗西说，“ 我们先走吧！” 
"Where's Terrell?" Jack asked.
Roxy and Mara were waiting outside Jack's house.
"He's going to be a little late today," Roxy said. "Let's go first!."
三个朋友沿着人行道走着。
“特勒尔为什么会迟到呢？” 杰克问。
玛拉咯咯笑了。“他可能在家想办法找出火箭女孩儿到底是谁呢！” 
The three friends walked along the sidewalk.
"Why is Terrell going to be late?" Jack asked.
Mara chuckled. "He's probably at home, trying to figure out who Rocket Girl really is!"
杰克笑了。
罗西也笑了。“不是，他约了牙医。” 
他们很快到了学校。当他们快到教室的时候，罗西听到她的手表在响。
“我很快就进去。” 罗西说，“我得……嗯……去洗手间。” 
Jack laughed.
Roxy grinned. "No, he's at a dentist appointment."
Soon they arrived at school. As they reached their classroom, Roxy heard her watch beep.
"I'll be right in," Roxy said. "I have to, um, use the restroom."
罗西躲进一个拐角。
“布洛姆市长！” 她小声说，“一切都好吗？” 
市长看起来很困惑。“不是很好，火箭女孩儿！我觉得有人从美罗城监狱逃走了。” 
Roxy ducked around a corner.
"Mayor Bloom," she whispered. "Is everything okay?"
The mayor looked confused. "I'm not sure, Rocket Girl. I think someone escaped from Metro City Prison."
“谁？” 罗西问。
“我不知道。” 布洛姆市长说，“狱警们查了一整夜牢房。所有的犯人都在。” 
罗西挠了挠头。“我不明白，市长。那您为什么说有人逃走了？” 
"Who?" Roxy asked.
"I don't know," Mayor Bloom said. "The guards spent the night checking cells. All the prisoners are still there."
Roxy scratched her head. "I don't understand, Mayor. Why do you think someone escaped?"
“监狱墙上有一个大洞。” 布洛姆市长说，“很让人怀疑。” 
“好的，市长！” 罗西说，“我马上赶到！” 
突然，学校的门猛地被打开了。轰！空中传来很大的嗡嗡声。
"There's a big hole in the prison wall," Mayor Bloom said. "It's very suspicious."
"Okay, Mayor," Roxy said. "I’m on my way."
