Suddenly the school doors flew open. Shwoom! A loud humming sound filled the air.
罗西合上了手表。 她感到有一股无形的力量在拉她。老师们和学生们呼啦一下飞走了，好像被吸尘器吸走了一样。罗西用她超级力量在地上站稳了。
Roxy closed her watch. She felt an invisible force pulling on her. Teachers and students flew by, as if a vacuum was pulling them. Using her super strength, Roxy kept her feet planted on the floor.
玛拉和杰克飞走了。
“啊！” 玛拉尖叫着。
“救命啊！” 杰克大声喊道。
书、铅笔、纸从书包里掉了出来。走廊里一片混乱。很快，所有人都不见了。
“哎呀！” 罗西想，“怎么回事啊？” 
Mara and Jack flew by.
"Ahh!" Mara screamed.
"Help!" Jack shouted.
Books, pencils, and papers dropped from backpacks. The hallway was a mess. A moment later everyone was gone.
"Yikes!" Roxy thought. "What's going on?"
“嗯？” 特勒尔说，“发生了什么事？” 
他站在美罗城小学前面。路上到处都是纸和书。门大开着。
"Huh?" Terrell said. "What happened?"
He was standing in front of Metro City Elementary School. Papers and books were all over the street. The doors were wide open.
特勒尔跑进了学校。他看到罗西跑进了走廊尽头的洗手间。特勒尔沿着走廊跑过去。
过了一会儿，洗手间的门哐地打开，火箭女孩儿跑了出来。
Terrell ran to the school. At the far end of the hallway, he saw Roxy dart into a restroom. Terrell hurried down the hallway.
A second later the restroom door banged open, and Rocket Girl burst out!
特勒尔大吃了一惊。“罗西？” 
罗西咽了一口口水。特勒尔知道了她的秘密。
她深吸了一口气。“嗯……嗨，特勒尔。” 
特勒尔睁大了眼睛。“我早就知道了，罗西！我早知道你是火箭女孩儿！” 
Terrell was surprised. "Roxy?"
Roxy gulped. Terrell knew her secret!
She took a deep breath. "Um, hi, Terrell."
Terrell's eyes were wide. "I knew it, Roxy! I knew you were Rocket Girl!"
“是的！” 罗西说得很慢，“不过，你听好了。你不能告诉任何人，知道吗？只有另外两个人知道。潘校长和布洛姆市长。” 
特勒尔一只手按在胸口上。“我保证保密！” 他看了看四周，“这里发生了什么事？” 
"Yes," Roxy said slowly. "But listen, you can't tell anyone, okay? Only two other people know—Principal Penn and Mayor Bloom."
Terrell placed his hand over his heart. "I promise to keep it a secret." He looked around. "What happened here?"
罗西皱起了眉头。 “我正在和布洛姆市长打电话。突然间，有什么东西把所有的孩子和老师都吸走了。我不知道那是什么。” 
Roxy frowned. "I was talking to Mayor Bloom. Suddenly something sucked away all the kids and teachers. But I don't know what it was."
“你为什么和布洛姆市长打电话？” 特勒尔问。
“美罗城监狱发生了一件奇怪的事情。” 罗西说，“我现在还不能告诉你。我得马上赶到那里去。” 
"Why were you talking to Mayor Bloom?" Terrell asked.
"Something odd happened at Metro City Prison," Roxy said. "I can't tell you about that right now. I have to get there right away."
“好的！” 特勒尔说，“我留在这里，也许还能找到一些线索。” 
罗西点点头。“好主意。如果你需要我，你可以打电话到我的手表上。” 
罗西给了特勒尔火箭女孩儿的特殊号码 。他把号码存进了自己的手机里。
"Okay," Terrell said. "Maybe I can stay here and look for clues or something."
Roxy nodded. "Good idea. If you need me, call me on my watch."
Roxy gave Terrell the special number for Rocket Girl. He put it into his phone.
罗西到了美罗城监狱。她看到大楼的一侧有一个大洞。她从洞里飞进监狱。
史密斯侦探吓了一跳。“火箭女孩儿！你吓了我一跳！” 
“对不起，侦探先生。” 罗西说，“我很急。除了这个洞，早上还发生了别的事情。” 
Roxy arrived at Metro City Prison. She saw a big hole in the side of the building. She flew through it and into the prison.
Detective Smith jumped. "Rocket Girl! You startled me!"
"Sorry, Detective," Roxy said. "I'm in a rush. Not just this hole, but something else happened this morning."
“还发生了什么事？” 史密斯侦探问。
罗西告诉了他学校发生的事件。
他摸了摸下巴。“嗯……两个非常奇怪的事件。” 
“您觉得这两件事件有关联吗？” 
侦探叹了一口气。“我不知道。” 
"What else happened?" Detective Smith asked.
Roxy told him about the event at school.
He rubbed his chin. "Hmm . . . Two very weird events."
"Do you think they are connected?" Roxy asked.
The detective sighed. "I have no idea."
“我也不知道。” 罗西说。
突然，威格尔斯夫人从床上坐起来。“我讨厌睡觉时间！” 
罗西转动了一下眼睛。“现在是早上，威格尔斯夫人。不是睡觉时间。” 
罗西看了看四周。“布洛姆市长说所有的犯人都在这儿。” 
"Me neither," Roxy said.
Suddenly Mrs. Wiggles sat up in bed. "I hate bedtime!"
Roxy rolled her eyes. "It's morning, Mrs. Wiggles. It's not bedtime."
Roxy looked around. "Mayor Bloom said all the prisoners are still here."
史密斯侦探点了点头。“狱警已经数过几次犯人了。所有人都在。” 
罗西摇了摇头。“那是谁弄出的这个洞？为什么这么做呢？” 
罗西仔细看了一下那个洞。“洞的内部表面非常光滑。” 
Detective Smith nodded. "The guards have counted the prisoners several times. Nobody is missing."
Roxy shook her head. "Then who made this hole? And why?"
Roxy looked more closely at the hole. "The surface inside the hole is perfectly smooth."
史密斯侦探点点头。“看不到一点儿墙壁的碎块。太奇怪了。” 
“我讨厌睡觉时间！” 威格尔斯夫人再次说道。
罗西转过头去。“现在不是……” 
Detective Smith nodded. "There aren't any chips or broken bits of wall. It's very odd."
"I hate bedtime!" Mrs. Wiggles said again.
Roxy turned around. "It's not—"
“我讨厌睡觉时间！我讨厌睡觉时间！” 威格尔斯夫人的耳朵里冒出一小股烟。
“好奇怪啊！” 罗西想。她用眼睛发射的x射线看威格尔斯夫人。在这个坏人的身体里面，她看到了齿轮和弹簧。
罗西大吃了一惊。“那不是威格尔斯夫人！那是一个机器人！” 
"I hate bedtime! I hate bedtime!" A tiny puff of smoke drifted from Mrs. Wiggles' ear.
"That's strange," Roxy thought. Using her x-ray vision, she looked at Mrs. Wiggles. Inside the villain, Roxy saw gears and springs.
Roxy was surprised. "That's not Mrs. Wiggles! It's a robot!"
史密斯侦探看着威格尔斯夫人机器人。“这么说，真正的威格尔斯夫人逃走了！但是，她是怎么弄出这个洞的？太光滑了，好像是用……” 
罗西大吃一惊。“魔术！” 
史密斯侦探扬起一边的眉毛。“嗯？” 
Detective Smith looked at the Mrs. Wiggles robot. "So the real Mrs. Wiggles escaped! But how did she make that hole? It's so smooth, as if it was made with—"
Roxy was surprised. "Magic!"
Detective Smith raised an eyebrow. "Huh?"
罗西用眼睛发射的x射线看普雷斯托。魔术师也是一个机器人！是谁制造了机器人？
罗西转过来去看另外一个犯人。“怪人博士！”  她用眼睛发射的x射线看到怪人博士也是一个机器人。
Using her x-ray vision, Roxy looked at Mr. Presto. The magician was also a robot! And who made the robots?
Roxy spun toward another prisoner. "Dr. Odd!" With her x-ray vision, she saw that Dr. Odd was a robot too.
罗西咬了咬嘴唇。“太可怕了。学校里所有的人都不见了。至少有三个犯人逃走了!” 
史密斯侦探拿出了手机。“我来找一下怪人博士总部的地址。他们也许去那里了。” 
Roxy bit her lip. "This is terrible. Everyone from school is gone. And now at least three villains have escaped!"
Detective Smith pulled out his phone. "I'll find the address of Dr. Odd's headquarters. Maybe they went there."
“或者是去了威格尔斯夫人的空糖果工厂。” 罗西说。
就在这时，她的手表响了。“布洛姆市长？” 
“不。我是‘火箭男孩儿’。” 
罗西转动了一下眼睛。“你好，特勒尔。” 
"Or to Mrs. Wiggles' empty candy factory," Roxy said.
Just then her watch beeped. "Mayor Bloom?"
"Nope. This is Rocket Boy!"
Roxy rolled her eyes. "Hi, Terrell."
特勒尔的声音听起来很兴奋。“我想我找到了学校所有的人了！ 我顺着掉落的铅笔，纸和书走。我被引到了糖果工厂。” 
“哇！” 罗西说，“威格尔斯夫人肯定跟学校发生的事件也有关联。我马上去那里，特勒尔。” 
Terrell sounded excited. "I think I found everyone from school! I followed a trail of pencils, papers, and books. It led me to the candy factory."
"Whoa!" Roxy said. "Then Mrs. Wiggles is definitely involved in the stuff at school too. I'll be right there, Terrell!"
史密斯侦探收起了手机。“好的，火箭女孩儿，我觉得……火箭女孩儿？” 
罗西向糖果工厂飞去。特勒尔等在外面。“这里，罗西！” 
“嘘！” 罗西说，“当我是火箭女孩儿的时候，不要用我的真名。” 
Detective Smith put away his phone. "Okay, Rocket Girl, I think—Rocket Girl?"
Roxy flew to the candy factory. Terrell was waiting outside. "Hey, Roxy!"
"Shh!" Roxy said. "Don't use my real name when I'm Rocket Girl."
“哦，对。” 特勒尔说，“对不起。” 
罗西看到楼上有一扇打开的窗户。她飞快地飞了进去。
下面，孩子们和老师们都聚在工厂的地板上。威格尔斯夫人站在台子上。她手里拿着一根长长的甘草糖绳。
"Oh, right," Terrell said. "Sorry."
Roxy spotted an open window upstairs. She shot inside.
Below, kids and teachers were gathered on the factory floor. Mrs. Wiggles stood on a platform. She held a long licorice rope.
罗西没有看到普雷斯托和怪人博士。
“赶紧告诉我！谁是火箭女孩儿？” 威格尔斯夫人对人群说。
没有人回答。
Roxy didn't see Mr. Presto or Dr. Odd.
"Tell me now! Who is Rocket Girl?" Mrs. Wiggles said to the crowd.
Nobody answered.
威格尔斯夫人跺了跺脚。“我知道你们中有一个是火箭女孩儿！她是个孩子。也就是说，她在上学。告诉我，她现在在哪里？” 
“我们不会告诉你任何事情！” 潘校长大声喊道。
“对！” 杰克喊道 。
Mrs. Wiggles stamped her foot. "I know one of you is Rocket Girl! She's a kid. That means she goes to school. Now tell me where she is!"
"We won't tell you anything!" Principal Penn shouted.
"Yeah!" Jack cried.
罗西从人群中飞过。“我就在这儿，威格尔斯夫人！” 
“火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉喊道。
威格尔斯夫人恶狠狠地看着罗西。
罗西飞快地飞向坏人。
Roxy flew over the crowd. "I'm right here, Mrs. Wiggles!"
"Rocket Girl!" Mara cried.
Mrs. Wiggles gave Roxy an evil look.
Roxy shot toward the villain.
就在这时，普雷斯托从角落里出来了。“一，二，三，变！” 
罗西突然到了工厂的另外一个房间。
门开了。威格尔斯夫人走了进来。她的脸上带着邪恶的微笑。
Just then Mr. Presto stepped out of a corner. "One, two, three, change!"
Roxy was suddenly in another room in the factory.
A door opened, and Mrs. Wiggles stepped in. She had an evil smile.
一个很大的机器人撞开了墙壁。罗西看到怪人博士在机器人里面。
噗！ 普雷斯托出现了。
罗西咽了一口口水。“我被坏人们包围了！” 
A big robot smashed through a wall. Roxy saw Dr. Odd inside the robot.
Poof! Mr. Presto appeared.
Roxy gulped. "I'm surrounded by villains!"
威格尔斯夫人笑了。“真高兴看到你，火箭女孩儿。我们的原计划是要把你吸出学校。” 
普雷斯托笑了。“那个计划失败了。不过，幸好你还是来了。” 
Mrs. Wiggles grinned. "We're so happy to see you, Rocket Girl. Our plan was to suck you out of school."
Mr. Presto lauched. "That didn't work. But luckily you showed up anyway."
“你们想要什么？” 罗西问。
怪人博士咯咯的笑了。“我们想要除掉你，永远地！” 他向罗西发射了一枚能量弹。嗖！
“哇！” 罗西跳开了。
普雷斯托挥着他的魔术棒。“变！” 
"What do you want?" Roxy demanded.
Dr. Odd cackled. "We want to get rid of you—once and for all!" He fired an energy blast at Roxy. Ba-zoom!
"Whoa!" Roxy jumped.
Mr. Presto waved his wand. "Change!"
一面砖墙出现了。 砰！
“啊！” 罗西跌倒了。
咚！咚！机器人冲向罗西。一只沉重的脚向罗西踩下去。罗西抓住那只脚。她用力把机器人往后一扔。哐当！大楼震动了。
“啊！” 怪人博士喊道。
A brick wall appeared. Bam!
"Oof!" Roxy collapsed.
Stomp, stomp! The robot rushed toward Roxy. A heavy foot came down on her. Roxy grabbed the foot. She flipped the robot backward. Crash! The building shook.
"Gah!" Dr. Odd cried.
潘校长看到墙在震动。她看了看四周。没有一个人看管他们。“所有人都回学校！” 
老师们和学生们赶紧出去了。
Principal Penn saw the wall shake. She looked around. No one was guarding them anymore. "Everyone, back to school!"
The teachers and students hurried outside.
普雷斯托再一次挥动着魔术棒。
嗞！罗西眼睛发射出激光。但是，普雷斯托在被激光击中之前就已经不见了。
罗西觉得自己被甘草糖绳紧紧捆住了。
“抓住你了！” 威格尔斯夫人大声喊道。

Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams. But Mr. Presto vanished before they struck.
Roxy felt the licorice rope wrap around her.
"Got you!" Mrs. Wiggles shouted.
罗西挣扎着说道：“我讨厌甘草糖！” 
嗖！一发能量弹把罗西打倒了。
特勒尔在外面听到了里面的声音。“罗西很危险！” 他从窗口爬了进去。

Ba-zoom! An energy blast knocked Roxy over.
Outside, Terrell heard the noise. "Roxy's in trouble!" He climbed through a window.
普雷斯托举起了魔术棒。呼！罗西用她的超级呼吸吹气。魔术棒从普雷斯托的手里飞了出去。
特勒尔抓住了它！
罗西笑了。“特勒尔！” 
“别动！” 特勒尔用魔术棒指着魔术师。
Mr. Presto raised his wand. Whoosh! Roxy used her super breath. The wand flew from his hand.
Terrell caught it!
Roxy smiled. "Terrell!"
"Don't move!" Terrell pointed the wand at the magician.
普雷斯托举起了双手。“不要对我念咒语！” 
威格尔斯夫人丢下甘草糖绳，向门口跑去。“你绝对抓不到我！” 
罗西很快挣脱了绳子。她挥起甘草糖绳，抓住了威格尔斯夫人。
Mr. Presto held up his hands. "Don't cast a spell on me!"
Mrs. Wiggles dropped the licorice rope and ran for the door. "You'll never catch me!"
Roxy quickly freed herself. She swung the licorice rope and caught Mrs. Wiggles.
“不要！” 坏人喊道。
罗西听到了沉重的脚步声。怪人博士正向特勒尔跑去。
“拿回我的魔术棒！” 普雷斯托对着怪人博士大声喊道。
嗞！罗西的眼睛发射出激光。机器人爆炸了。怪人博士倒在地上，呻吟着。
"No!" the villain cried.
Roxy heard heavy footsteps. Dr. Odd was running toward Terrell.
"Get my wand!" Mr. Presto yelled to Dr. Odd.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams. The robot exploded. Dr. Odd lay on the floor, moaning.
罗西赶紧把坏人们用甘草糖绳绑了起来。然后，她转向特勒尔。
“谢谢你帮我！你做好飞的准备了吗？” 
特勒尔的脸亮起来了。
Roxy quickly tied up the villains with the licorice rope. Then she turned to Terrell.
"Thanks for the help! Ready to fly?"
Terrell's face lit up.
罗西一只手抓着特勒尔。一只手拎着被绑着的坏人们。
“哇！” 当罗西在美罗城上空飞的时候，特勒尔笑了。他们把犯人送进了监狱。然后，特勒尔和罗西回到了学校。
Roxy held Terrell with one hand. She held the bundled villains with the other.
"Whoa!" Terrell laughed as he and Roxy soared over Metro City. They dropped off the villains at prison. Then he and Roxy returned to school.
“罗西，特勒尔！” 玛拉说，“你们错过了所有的事情！坏人们绑架了学校所有的人！” 
“是火箭女孩儿救了我们！” 杰克说。
“真的吗？” 罗西做出吃惊的样子。
“我不相信我们错过了那些！” 特勒尔说。他看着罗西。
两人咯咯笑起来。
"Roxy, Terrell!" Mara said. "You missed everything! Villains kidnapped everyone from school."
"Rocket Girl saved us!" Jack said.
"Really?" Roxy pretended to be surprised.
"I can't believe we missed that!" Terrell said. He glanced at Roxy.
The two friends chuckled.
美罗城中央银行看上去非常忙碌。
“我要取钱。” 一个顾客说。
银行柜员在电脑上输入了信息，现金抽屉打开了。
“啊！” 柜员说，“抽屉里没钱了。请稍等一会儿！我到保险库里去拿。” 
Metro City Central Bank looked very busy.
"I need to withdraw some money," a customer said.
The bank teller typed the customer's information into a computer. A drawer popped open.
"Ah!" the bank teller said. "There's no more money in the drawer. Please wait here. I'll get it from the safe."
他走向保险库，开了锁，打开了门。
银行柜员大吃一惊，说：“钱都不见了！” 
“哇！” 玛拉说，“土星环太美了！” 
罗西和朋友们在学校的电脑室里。
He went over to the safe, unlocked the door, and opened it.
The bank teller gasped. "All the money is gone!"
"Wow!" Mara said. "Saturn's rings are amazing."
Roxy and her friends were in the computer center at school.
他们正在做一个科学研究课题。
“我想在土星环上跑圈。” 杰克说。
马拉翻了个白眼。
“杰克，你不能在土星环上跑圈，它不是固体的，而是由飘浮在行星周围的冰块和石块组成的。” 
They were doing research projects for science.
"I'd like to run around Saturn on its rings," Jack said.
Mara rolled her eyes.
"You can't run on Saturn's rings, Jack. They're not solid. They're made of chunks of ice and rock that float around the planet."
特勒尔看了过来。“我正在研究第一次登月，你完全可以在月球上跑，只不过你需要一套宇航服。” 
罗西也点了点头。“而且月球上没什么重力，你可以跳得很高。” 
Terrell looked over . "I'm researching the first moon landing. You could definitely run on the moon. You'd need a spacesuit though."
Roxy nodded. "Plus, there isn't much gravity on the moon, so you could jump really high."
杰克站了起来。“地球，我是宇航员杰克。我刚降落在月球上，现在要试一下‘月球跳’！” 杰克使劲儿跳了起来。
罗西，玛拉和特勒尔都笑了起来。
艾普卡特老师走了过来。“杰克，你选好主题了吗？” 
Jack stood up. "Earth, this is Astronaut Jack. I just landed on the moon. I'm going to try moon jumping now!" Jack jumped as high as he could.
Roxy, Mara, and Terrell laughed.
Teacher Cotterwalked over. "Jack, did you pick a topic for your project yet?"
杰克挠了挠头。“我大概会研究外星人吧！” 
艾普卡特老师叹了口气。“请你选一个严肃点儿的主题。还有，别再跳了。” 
“好的，老师。” 杰克又坐下了。

Jack scratched his head. "I might research aliens!"
Miss Cottersighed. "Please pick something more serious . And stop jumping."
"Okay, Teacher Jack sat back down.
"Roxy, which topic did you pick?" Terrell asked.
“嗯，” 罗西说，“我选了水星。不过，它不是很有趣。” 
 特勒尔想了一会儿。“我有个想法！火箭女孩儿！” 
"Well," Roxy said. "I picked the planet Mercury. But it's not very interesting."
Terrell thought for a moment. "I have an idea! Rocket Girl!"
罗西强忍着不笑。她知道特勒尔在开玩笑。“特勒尔，太有意思了。不过，火箭女孩儿有比帮我更重要的事情要做。” 
特勒尔摇了摇头。“不，我是说你应该写‘火箭女孩儿’！她可以在宇宙飞行，对吧？说不定她的速度跟彗星一样快呢！” 
Roxy tried not to laugh. She knew Terrell was kidding. "Very funny, Terrell. But Rocket Girl has more important things to do than help me."
Terrell shook his head. "No, I meant you should write about Rocket Girl. She can fly through space, right? And she's probably as fast as a comet!"
玛拉咯咯地笑了起来。“特勒尔，你太搞笑了！” 
“这比我那外星人的想法还要蠢。” 杰克说。
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。
“我很快就回来。” 她小声对特勒尔说，“是布洛姆市长的电话。”

"It's even sillier than my alien idea." Jack said.
Just then Roxy's watch beeped.

“我的玩偶也不见了！” 另外一个女人说。
"A very special doll," a man said. He wore a bright green suit. "I spent a lot of money on it. It's from Europe."
"My dolls are more than a hundred years old," a woman said, wiping a tear from her eye. "And now they're gone!"
"My dolls are gone too!" another woman said.
史密斯侦探拿出笔记本。“有人看到小偷了吗？” 
穿绿色西服的男人吸了吸鼻子。“没有，当时我们在另外一个房间里吃午饭。” 
女人点了点头。“我听到一声巨响，好像是玻璃被打碎了。我们跑进来后......” 她开始哭起来。
Detective Smith took out his notebook. "Did anyone see the thief?"
The man in the green suit sniffed. "No. We were eating lunch in another room."
The woman nodded. "I heard a loud crash, like glass being smashed. We ran in here, and . . . " She started to cry.
男人拍了拍她的肩膀。“贝蒂，没事儿的。火箭女孩儿会帮我们找到玩偶的。” 他看着罗西说，“对吧？” 
“我尽力。” 罗西没想到这些人会这么喜欢他们的玩偶。
The man patted her shoulder. "It's okay, Betty. Rocket Girl will help us find our dolls." He looked at Roxy. "Right?"
"I'll do my best." Roxy couldn't believe how much these people liked their dolls.
“我也听到小偷的声音了。” 另外一个女人说，“当时，我正在出口附近。我听到有人说‘我很坏，很坏，很坏！’。” 
史密斯侦探挠了挠头。“我大概知道谁是小偷了。在我侄子的生日派对上，有一个叫查克的表演者，他有一个很大的玩偶，表演得很差劲。他说了同样的话，‘我很坏，很坏，很坏！’。” 
"I heard the thief," another woman said. "I was near the exit at that time. I heard someone say, 'I am bad, bad, bad!'"
Detective Smith scratched his head. "I might know who the thief is. A performer named Chuck was at my nephew's birthday party. He had a large doll and was terrible. He said the same thing: 'I am bad, bad, bad.'"
“如果查克表演得很差劲的话，” 罗西说，“说不定他会去做小偷。” 
“我有他的名片，” 史密斯侦探从口袋里掏出名片一看，“他就住在附近，我们去看看！” 
"If Chuck was terrible," Roxy said, "maybe he became a thief instead."
"I have his business card." Detective Smith pulled the card from his pocket and looked at it. "He lives just around the corner. Let's go and have a look!"
罗西和史密斯侦探来到查克的家里。门开着，他们走了进去。
“查克在吗？” 史密斯侦探问。
他们听到呜呜的声音。罗西冲到衣柜前，打开一看，里面有一个被绑着的男人！
Roxy and Detective Smith arrived at Chuck's home. The door was open, so they went in.
"Chuck?" Detective Smith called.
They heard a muffled voice. Roxy rushed to the closet and opened it. A man was tied up!
史密斯侦探赶紧解开了他的绳子。
“谢谢！” 查克说，“你们来得太好了。它太坏了，完全失控了！” 
“哦？” 罗西挠了挠头说，“我们以为是你偷走了玩偶，才来这里的。” 
Detective Smith quickly untied him.
"Thank you!" Chuck said. "I'm so glad you're here. It's evil and out of control!"
"Huh?" Roxy scratched her head. "We're here because we thought you robbed the doll show."
查克摇了摇头。“不是我做的，是它做的！” 
“谁？” 史密斯侦探问。
“还能是谁？” 查克说，“我的玩偶查克斯！” 
Chuck shook his head. "I wouldn't do that. It was him!"
"Who?" Detective Smith asked.
"Who do you think?" Chuck said. "My doll Chuckles!"
“查克斯是个玩偶，” 罗西对查克说，“玩偶不可能犯罪。” 
史密斯侦探点了点头。“说得对！” 
“请相信我！” 查克说，“查克斯的背上有个特别的电脑芯片，本来是想让他说话搞笑，却没想到会让它变得那么坏。” 
"Chuckles is a doll," Roxy said to Chuck. "A doll can't commit a crime."
Detective Smith nodded. "Good point."
"Please believe me!" Chuck said. "Chuckles has a special computer chip in his back, and it was supposed to make him talk and be funny. I didn't expect him to become so evil."
史密斯侦探的电话响了。“喂？天啊！我们马上出发！” 他挂断了电话，说：“有人正在都会玩具店偷玩偶。” 
“是查克斯！” 查克说。
罗西咽了一口口水。“我的朋友们在那里！” 
Detective Smith's phone rang. "Hello? Oh no! We're on our way!" He hung up. "Someone is robbing Downtown Toys."
"Chuckles!" Chuck said.
Roxy gulped. "My friends are there!"
罗西飞进了都会玩具店。特勒尔从柜子的后面偷偷探出头。 他向罗西做了一个 “安静” 的手势，然后指了指收银台。
罗西看到一个大玩偶站在收银台上。“那应该就是查克斯了。” 
Roxy flew into Downtown Toys. Terrell peeked out from behind a shelf. He held a finger to his lips. Then he pointed toward the cash registers.
Roxy saw a big doll standing on a cash register. "That must be Chuckles."
几个玩偶正在从收款机里拿钱，它们把钱装进了袋子里。
这些玩偶看上去很旧，很贵。“它们是展会上的玩偶，” 罗西想，“也许是查克斯让它们复活的！” 
Several other dolls were taking money from the cash registers. They stuffed the money into bags.
The dolls looked old and valuable. "Those are the dolls from the doll show," Roxy thought. "Maybe Chuckles made them come to life!"
查克斯哈哈大笑。“我会变得很有钱，有钱，有钱！” 
“不，你不会的！” 罗西大声说。
“火箭女孩儿！” 查克斯看向其它的玩偶，“给我打！” 玩偶们扔下钱袋，冲向罗西。
Chuckles laughed. "I'm going to be rich, rich, rich!"
"No, you're not!" Roxy shouted.
"Rocket Girl!" Chuckles looked at the other dolls. "Attack!" The dolls dropped the money bags and rushed toward Roxy.
“呃哦！” 当罗西被玩偶们抓住时说，“这些玩偶很贵，我不能弄坏它们！” 
查克斯举起钱袋。“我该走了，走了，走了！” 
罗西差点儿踩到了一个玩偶。“啊！” 她摔倒时，撞倒了糖果柜子。柜子挡住了出口。
"Uh-oh!" Roxy said as dolls grabbed her. "These dolls are valuable. I can't break them."
Chuckles grabbed the money bag. "It's time for me to go, go, go!"
Roxy almost stepped on one doll. "Ah!" She stumbled and knocked over a candy display. The candy display blocked the entrance.
“啊！” 查克斯说，“我得走后门了。” 它跑掉了。
罗西好不容易推开了身边的玩偶。她飞快地看了一下四周，在收款机下面有个柜子。 她抓起玩偶们，把它们放进了柜子里，关上了门。
"Gah!" Chuckles said. "I'll go to the back door." He ran off.
Roxy managed to pull the dolls off her. Quickly she looked around. There was a cabinet under a cash register. She scooped up the dolls and stuffed them in the cabinet. Then she closed the door.
突然，罗西的手表响了。“特勒尔？” 
“我抓住那个大玩偶了！” 特勒尔说，“我们在玩偶区。” 
“放我走，小孩儿！” 查克斯在后面大喊。
“我马上到！” 罗西飞向玩偶区。货架上摆着一盒盒的玩偶。
Suddenly Roxy's watch beeped. "Terrell?"
"I caught the big doll!" Terrell said. "We're in the doll department."
"Let me go, kid!" Chuckles yelled in the background.
"I'll be right there!" Roxy flew to the doll department. Boxes of dolls lined the shelves.
特勒尔正用力地抓着查克斯。罗西跑过去，把玩偶按在了地上。“抓住你了！” 她说。
“玩偶们，复活吧！” 查克斯大喊。
所有的玩偶盒子开始晃动起来。 
“天啊！” 特勒尔说。
一个塑料小拳头从盒子里伸了出来。一只小脚从另外一个盒子里伸了出来。很快，所有的玩偶都从盒子里出来了。
Terrell was struggling with Chuckles. Roxy rushed over and pinned the doll to the floor. "Got you!" she said.
"Dolls, alive!" Chuckles shouted.
All the doll boxes shook.
"Oh dear," Terrell said.
A plastic fist popped out from one box. A tiny foot broke out from another box. Soon all the dolls were out of their boxes.
“给我打！” 查克斯大喊。
愤怒的玩偶们冲向罗西和特勒尔。玩偶们打的打，踢的踢。
“啊！” 特勒尔说。
一只只塑料小手抓住了罗西。
查克斯从罗西手里逃了出来，哈哈大笑起来。
“我很坏，很坏，很坏！” 
"Attack!" Chuckles yelled.
Angry dolls dived onto Roxy and Terrell. The dolls punched and kicked.
"Ah!" Terrell cried.
Tiny plastic hands grabbed at Roxy.
Chuckles slipped from her grip and laughed. "I am bad, bad, bad!"
更多愤怒的玩偶跳到了罗西和特勒尔的身上。 
查克斯咯咯地笑着说：“再见，火箭女孩儿！” 
“你跑不掉的！” 罗西大声说。
“不，我会的。” 查克斯说，“我已经从查克手里跑出来了。因为他不会挣钱，所以我离开了。我会和更多的玩偶一起去偷钱，偷钱，偷钱！” 查克斯跑出了玩具店。
More angry dolls piled onto Roxy and Terrell.
Chuckles giggled. "Good-bye, Rocket Girl!"
"You won't get away!" Roxy shouted.
"Yes, I will," Chuckles said. "I got away from Chuck. He didn't make much money, so I left. Now I'll steal money, money, money with more dolls!" Chuckles ran out of the store.
“呃！” 罗西用力推玩偶，又有一些玩偶跳到了她和特勒尔的身上。
“火箭女孩儿，快点儿想想办法啊！” 特勒尔说。
“我有办法了。” 罗西盯着头上的玩偶说。
她的眼睛发射出橘色的光束，玩偶们开始熔化。很快，地板上到处都是熔化的塑料堆。 
"Grr!" Roxy pushed away some of the dolls. Other dolls jumped onto her and Terrell.
"Rocket Girl, do something!" Terrell said.
"I have an idea," Roxy stared at the dolls on top of her.
Orange beams radiated from her eyes. The dolls began to melt. Soon a puddle of melted plastic covered the floor.
“干得好！” 特勒尔说。
杰克和玛拉跑了过来。“火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉说。
“我该走了！” 罗西说。嗖！
罗西很快找到了查克斯。它打开一辆出租车的门，把司机拉了出来，自己跳了进去，然后迅速地开走了。
"Well done!" Terrell said.
Jack and Mara ran over. "Rocket Girl!" Mara said.
"I have to go!" Roxy said. Zoom!
Soon Roxy found Chuckles. He opened a taxi door, pulled out the driver, and jumped in. Then he quickly drove the taxi away.
司机挥着拳头。“坏玩偶！” 
出租车开上了人行道。“啊！” 一个男人跳起来躲开了。
哐！查克斯开着车把水果摊撞飞了。“好玩儿，好玩儿，好玩儿！” 
罗西拦住出租车，把查克斯抓了出来。玩偶咬了罗西一口。
The driver shook his fist. "Rotten doll!"
The taxi swerved onto the sidewalk. "Ahh!" A man jumped out of the way.
Bam! Chuckles drove through a fruit stand. "This is fun, fun, fun!"
Roxy stopped the taxi and grabbed Chuckles. The doll bit her.
“啊！” 罗西松开了手。
“嘎嘣，嘎嘣，嘎嘣！” 查克斯跑了。
嗞！罗西眼睛里发射的激光射中了查克斯的木腿，腿开始冒烟了。
"Ouch!" Roxy pulled her hand away.
"Chomp, chomp, chomp!" Chuckles ran away.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy's eye laser beams hit Chuckles' wooden leg. The leg started to smoke.
查克斯咽了一口口水。“这个很坏，很坏，很坏！” 
一个女人拿着水瓶，查克斯抢过水瓶，往自己的腿上倒水。“现在好多了！” 它说。
罗西赶紧跑过去抓住查克斯。
Chuckles gulped. "This is bad, bad, bad!"
A woman was holding a water bottle. Chuckles grabbed the bottle and poured the water on his leg. "Much better!" he said.
Roxy hurried over and grabbed Chuckles.
“放开我！” 玩偶直踢腿，罗西把它按倒在地上。
罗西找到了电脑芯片，并把它拿了出来，查克斯不动了。罗西擦了一下额头说：“咻！” 
"Let me go!" The doll kicked, and Roxy flipped him over on the ground.
Roxy found the computer chip and ripped it out. Chuckles stopped moving. Roxy wiped her brow. "Whew!"
那些珍贵的玩偶们不再是活的了。罗西把它们带回了会展中心。
穿绿西服的男人笑了。“火箭女孩儿，你是我的英雄！” 
罗西把查克斯送到了查克那里。
The valuable dolls weren't alive anymore. Roxy brought them back to the convention center.
The man in the green suit smiled. "You're my hero, Rocket Girl!"
Roxy brought Chuckles to Chuck.
“我把芯片拿出来了。” 罗西说。
“火箭女孩儿，谢谢你！” 查克说，他假装是查克斯在说话，“火箭女孩儿，你真了不起！” 
“呃！” 罗西说，“是你的嘴巴在动。” 
"I took out the chip," Roxy said.
"Thanks, Rocket Girl," Chuck said. He pretended Chuckles was talking. "You're super, Rocket Girl!"
"Um," Roxy said, "your lips are moving."
罗西在都会玩具店里找到了朋友们。
“罗西，可惜当时你不在！” 杰克说，“这里出现了坏玩偶。” 
特勒尔咧嘴笑了。“不过已经被火箭女孩儿搞定了。” 
“哇！” 罗西转向玛拉说，“你给蒂娜的礼物选好了吗？” 
“还没有，” 玛拉说，“不过我知道不能给她买什么！玩偶！” 
At Downtown Toys, Roxy found her friends.
"Roxy, what a shame that you weren't here!" Jack said. "There was an evil doll!"
Terrell grinned. "But Rocket Girl stopped it."
"Wow." Roxy turned to Mara. "Did you pick a gift for Dina yet?"
"Nope," Mara said. "But I know what I'm not getting for her! A doll!"
“我们的新房子看上去真是太棒了！” 一个女人说。
她丈夫点了点头。“我想快点儿进去看看。” 
一个穿工作服，戴安全帽的大个子男人站在旁边。“进去吧！” 他说，“你们会喜欢的。” 
"Our new house looks amazing!" a woman said.
Her husband nodded. "I can't wait to go inside."
A big man in overalls and a hard hat stood nearby. "Go in," he said. "You're going to love it."
夫妻俩走了进去，女人大吃一惊。“所有东西都是歪的！” 
男人挠了挠头。“建筑工人做得太差了！” 
当他转身要出去的时候，地板裂开了。夫妻俩尖叫着掉进了黑暗中。
The couple went in. The woman gasped. "Everything is crooked!"
The husband scratched his head. "The builder did a terrible job!"
As he turned to go back outside, the floor opened up. The couple screamed and tumbled into darkness.
“呃，这几天一直下雨，好烦啊！” 玛拉说。
罗西和朋友们走在上学的路上。天上堆满乌云，雨轻轻地下着。
“我也是，” 罗西说，“感觉好像已经下了几个星期了。我想看到太阳。” 
"Ugh! It has been raining for days, I'm so annoyed" Mara said.
Roxy and her friends were on their way to school. The sky was filled with gray clouds, and rain was falling lightly.
"Me too," Roxy said. "It feels like it's been raining for weeks. I want to see the sun."
“我喜欢下雨。” 杰克抬起头，张开嘴，他用舌头接住了几滴雨。
特勒尔擦着眼镜上的雨水。“我也讨厌一整天都下雨，” 他说，“这就意味着......” 
"I like the rain." Jack looked up and held his mouth open. He caught some raindrops on his tongue.
Terrell wiped raindrops off his glasses. "I hate when it rains all day long," he said. "It mean . . . "
“得在室内休息！” 玛拉抱怨说。
“室内休息很没劲。” 杰克说。他踩了一下水坑，水花溅得到处都是。“太无聊了！” 
"Indoor recess!" Mara complained.
"Indoor recess stinks," Jack said. He stomped in a puddle. Water splashed everywhere. "It's so boring!"
雨下大了，朋友们走得更快了。大雨滴落在他们的雨伞上。
“学校今天安静了，” 玛拉说，“施工终于结束了。” 
Rain fell harder, and the friends walked more quickly. Heavy raindrops drummed against their umbrellas.
"It will be quiet in school today," Mara said. "The construction work is finally done."
过去的三个星期，学校里每天都有工人。潘校长说，楼太旧了，需要修理。
特勒尔转头看着罗西。“我希望火箭女孩儿今天什么也不用做。” 
Workers had been at school every day for the past three weeks. Principal Penn had said the building was old and needed some repairs.
Terrell looked at Roxy. "I hope Rocket Girl doesn't have to do anything today."
玛拉看过来问：“为什么？” 
特勒尔耸耸肩。“下雨呢！在雨里打坏人一定会很难。” 
杰克笑了。“怎么会呢！火箭女孩儿超级厉害，一点儿雨算什么。” 
Mara looked over. "Why?"
Terrell shrugged. "It's raining! It must be hard to fight villains in the rain."
Jack laughed. "No way! Rocket Girl is super tough, so rain wouldn't bother her."
罗西飞快地看了特勒尔一眼，笑了。“我同意特勒尔的话。火箭女孩儿应该也不想打坏人的时候被淋湿。” 
当他们到学校的时候，罗西的手表响了。她悄悄地离开朋友们，站在了大楼的旁边。
“布洛姆市长，” 她说，“有什么事吗？” 
Roxy shot a quick look at Terrell and smiled. "I agree with Terrell. Rocket Girl probably doesn't want to get soaked while fighting villains."
When they reached the school, Roxy's watch beeped. She sneaked away from her friends and stood close to the building. "Mayor Bloom," she said. "What's wrong?"
市长看上去很担心。“火箭女孩儿， 我也不确定！我给史密斯侦探打电话，但他一直不接，别的警官也不接。我担心他们出事了。” 
“您别担心，市长，” 罗西说，“我会查清楚的。” 
The mayor had a worried look on his face. "I'm not sure if anything is wrong, Rocket Girl. I tried to call Detective Smith, but he didn't answer his phone. I can't reach any other police officers either. I'm worried that something happened to them."
"Don't worry, Mayor," Roxy said. "I'll find out what's going on."
“史密斯侦探不见了，” 罗西想，“我得去一下警察总局。” 
她对朋友们喊道：“别等我，我......嗯......掉东西了！” 罗西跑了。
警察总局的停车场空荡荡的。
“警车都去哪里了？” 罗西说，“人又都去哪里了？” 
"Detective Smith is missing," Roxy thought. "I have to get to police headquarters."
She called to her friends. "Don't wait for me. I . . . um . . . dropped something!" Roxy ran off.
The parking lot at police headquarters was empty.
"Where are all the police cars?" Roxy said. "And where is everyone?"
当罗西进去后，她惊讶地睁大了眼睛。墙是歪的，地板是斜的。
“这里发生什么事了？” 罗西说，“怎么像游乐园里的趣味屋！” 
When she went inside, Roxy opened her eyes wide in surprise. All the walls were crooked, and the floors were slanted.
"What happened in here?" Roxy said. "It's like a fun house at an amusement park!"
走廊一边挂满了镜子。一面镜子让罗西看起来又高又瘦，另外一面镜子让她的头显得特别大。
罗西进了休息室。咖啡机开着，饼干放在柜子上，广播里播放着音乐，就是一个人也没有。
A hallway was lined with mirrors. One mirror made Roxy look tall and skinny. Another one made her head look enormous.
Roxy made her way to the break room. The coffeemaker was on, and cookies sat on the counter. Music played on a radio, but nobody was there.
罗西挠了挠头。“真奇怪。” 
咔嚓！扑通！罗西脚下的地板开始倾斜，她滑进了黑暗中。
“啊！” 罗西落在地板上。
“是火箭女孩儿吗？” 史密斯侦探问。
Roxy scratched her head. "This is odd."
Click! Ba-doom! The floor tilted under Roxy's feet, and she slid down into darkness.
"Ah!" Roxy landed on the floor.
"Rocket Girl?" Detective Smith asked.
通过夜光视力，罗西发现自己在一个水泥房里。侦探站在罗西的旁边，别的警官也都在这里。
罗西咧嘴笑了。“你们是在玩儿捉迷藏吗？” 
Using her night vision, Roxy found herself in a concrete room. The detective stood near Roxy, other police officers were here too.
Roxy grinned. "Are you all playing hide-and-seek?"
史密斯侦探看上去很恼火。“火箭女孩儿，现在不是开玩笑的时候。我们从昨天起就被困在这里了！” 
罗西咽了一口口水。“哦！对不起！这栋楼里发生了什么事？怎么看上去像一个趣味屋。” 
Detective Smith looked annoyed. "Rocket Girl, this is no time for jokes. We've been stuck down here since yesterday!"
Roxy gulped. "Oh! Sorry! What happened to the building? It's like a fun house."
“我们雇了一个建筑工人修理这栋大楼，” 史密斯侦探叹了口气，“很明显他做得太差了。我们现在连大楼都不能用了。” 
“建筑工人是谁？” 罗西问。
“杰克·哈默，” 史密斯侦探说，“我们再也不会雇他了。” 
"We hired a builder to make some improvements to this building." Detective Smith sighed. "Obviously he did a terrible job. We can't even use the building now."
"Who is the builder?" Roxy asked.
"Jack Hammer," Detective Smith said. "We won't hire him again."
一位警官走了过来。“我们怎么从这里出去呢？” 她问。
罗西哈哈大笑。“这个很容易。” 罗西飞起来把警官们带到了休息室。
史密斯侦探拿起一块饼干，咬了一口。
A police officer walked over. "How will we get out of here?" she asked.
Roxy laughed. "That's easy." Roxy flew the police officers up to the break room.
Detective Smith grabbed a cookie and took a bite.
女警官看到电话机的灯在闪。“啊！” 她说，“我们有留言。” 她按了第一条留言。
“喂？我很担心我的朋友布兰达和丹·杜雷。昨天他们搬了新家，在十水坑街上。我打了电话，也敲了门，但都没人应。” 
A female police dispatcher saw a light flashing on the phone. "Yikes!" she said. "We have messages." She played the first message.
"Hello? I'm worried about my friends Brenda and Dan Dooley. They moved into their new house yesterday. It's at Ten Puddle Lane. I tried calling and knocking on their door, but there's no answer."
其他打电话的人也留了类似的留言。有些人还打了好几次。
史密斯侦探咽下最后一口饼干。“天啊！” 
Other people had called with similar messages. Some of them had called several times.
Detective Smith swallowed the last bite of his cookie. "Oh boy!"
“糟了，” 史密斯侦探说，“城里有很多人都被困在了自己的房子里。我们先去布兰达和丹·杜雷的家。他们住在......” 
“十水坑街！” 罗西已经飞走了。
史密斯侦探抱怨说：“火箭女孩儿从来不......” 
"This is bad," Detective Smith said. "People all over the city are trapped in their houses. We'll go to Brenda and Dan Dooley's house first. They live at . . ."
"Ten Puddle Lane!" Roxy took off.
Detective Smith groaned. "Rocket Girl never…"
一位警官跑了进来。“我们的警车被偷了。” 
史密斯侦探再次抱怨起来。
罗西按了杜雷家的门铃，没人应。于是她走了进去。“有人吗？” 
“咔嚓！” 地板开始移动，罗西跳到空中。扑通！地板裂开了。罗西飞了下去。
A police officer ran in. "Our police cars were stolen!"
The detective groaned again.
Roxy rang the Dooley's doorbell, but no one answered. So she entered the house. "Anybody home?"
"Click!" The floor moved, and Roxy jumped up. Ba-doom! The floor opened. Roxy flew down.
“是火箭女孩儿，太好了！” 杜雷先生说，“手机在这里没有信号。” 
罗西把他们夫妻俩带离了黑房间。
杜雷夫人大吃一惊。“我们的家具都去哪儿了？” 
"Rocket Girl, thank goodness!" Mr. Dooley said. "Phones can't get a signal down here."
Roxy carried the couple out of the dark room.
Mrs. Dooley gasped as they flew through the house. "Where's our furniture?"
“我们的电视不见了！” 杜雷先生说。
罗西把他们带到院子里。“你们在地下被困了多久？” 
“是从昨天开始的，” 杜雷先生说，“我们的建筑工人建好了房子，他让我们进去看看，所有的东西都糟透了。随后地板裂开了，我们就滑进了那个房间。” 
"Our TV is gone!" Mr. Dooley cried.
Roxy brought them to the yard. "How long were you trapped down there?"
"Since yesterday," Mr. Dooley said. "Our builder finished working on the house. He told us to take a look. Everything looked awful. Then the floor opened up, and we slid down into that room."
“建筑工人是谁？” 罗西问。
“他叫杰克·哈默。” 杜雷夫人说。
杜雷先生皱起了眉头。“我们再也不雇他了，我还要在网上给他差评。” 
“杰克·哈默把别人也困了起来。” 罗西说，“我得抓住他。” 
"Who was the builder?" Roxy asked.
"His name is Jack Hammer," Mrs. Dooley said.
Mr. Dooley frowned. "We won't hire him again. I'm going to give him a bad online review too!"
"Jack Hammer trapped other people," Roxy said. "I have to catch him."
杜雷先生在手机里找到杰克·哈默。他把地址给了罗西。
罗西找到了杰克·哈默的办公室，它在一家旧工厂里。一个大个子男人坐在桌子后面，他穿着工作服，戴着安全帽。
“杰克·哈默！” 罗西大喊。
Mr. Dooley looked up Jack Hammer on his phone. He gave the address to Roxy.
Roxy arrived at Jack Hammer's office. It was in an old factory. A big man sat behind a desk. He wore overalls and a hard hat.
"Jack Hammer!" Roxy shouted.
男人站了起来。“火箭女孩儿，你好啊！” 
罗西皱起了眉头。“你为什么把人关在房子里？” 
杰克·哈默哼了一声。“你以为呢？我想偷东西啊，不仅仅是房子！最近，我还在警察总局和学校里干活呢！” 
The man stood up. "Hello, Rocket Girl."
Roxy frowned. "Why are you trapping people in their houses?"
Jack snorted. "Why do you think? I want to steal stuff. And it's not just houses! Recently, I worked on police headquarters and a school!"
罗西很恼火。“哪个学校？” 
“美罗城小学。” 杰克·哈默看了看他的手表，“现在我正要去那里呢！” 
Roxy was angry. "What school?"
"Metro City Elementary." Jack Hammer looked at his watch. "I am heading over there now!"
“呃！” 罗西冲向坏人。他迅速跳进了一扇门里。罗西追了过去，发现自己到了一个又大又空的房间里。
“啊？” 房间开始旋转，罗西被摔到墙上。“啊！” 
"Grr!" Roxy rushed toward the villain. He stepped quickly through a door. Roxy burst through and found herself in a large, empty room.
"Huh?" The room spun, and Roxy was thrown against a wall. "Ah!"
房间停止转动以后，罗西跑到了另一扇门里。她的周围都是镜子，镜子里都是她自己。
罗西咽了一口口水。“我被困在可怕的趣味屋了！” 
罗西听到杰克·哈默的笑声。“火箭女孩儿，你再也出不来了！” 
When the room stopped spinning, Roxy ran through another door. Mirrors surrounded her. Her reflection was everywhere.
Roxy gulped. "I'm stuck in an evil fun house!"
Roxy heard Jack Hammer laugh. "You'll never get out, Rocket Girl!"
罗西走了一步。砰！她撞到了镜子上。所有镜子里的自己都在揉头。“呃！我被困在大型镜子迷宫里了！” 
“是的，说得对！” 杰克·哈默出现在镜子里。
Roxy took a step. Bam! She hit a mirror. All of her reflections rubbed their heads. "Ugh! I'm stuck in an enormous mirror maze!"
"Yes, you are!" Jack Hammer appeared in the mirrors.
嗞！罗西的眼睛发射出激光。砰！砰 ！激光从镜子上反射回来。 当激光经过罗西的头顶时，她躲开了。 
杰克·哈默哈哈大笑。“火箭女孩儿，再见了！” 
Whiz-hoo! Roxy fired her eye laser beams. Ping! Ping! The beams bounced off the mirrors. Roxy ducked as they passed by her head.
Jack Hammer laughed. "So long, Rocket Girl!"
罗西不停地撞到镜子上。几分钟过去了，她还在迷宫里。
“我怎么才能从这里出去呢？” 罗西想。她很快有了主意。她吹了一口冷气。镜子上结满了霜，随后出现了裂缝。然后，咔嚓！镜子碎了。
Roxy banged into mirrors again and again. After a few minutes, she was still in the maze.
"How will I get out of here?" Roxy thought. Then she had an idea. She blew her freeze breath. The mirrors filled with frost, cracks crept along the glass. And then, smash! The mirrors shattered.
罗西看到了出口的标志。“太棒了！” 
当罗西赶到美罗城小学的时候，学校里空荡荡的。
她给特勒尔打了个电话，然后用超级听力听到了铃声。罗西向铃声跑去，叹了口气。手机在他们教室，在特勒尔的包里，但是特勒尔不在那里。
Roxy saw an exit sign. "Yes!"
Metro City Elementary School was empty when Roxy arrived.
She called Terrell's phone. Using her super hearing, she heard it ringing. Roxy rushed to the phone and sighed. The phone was in their classroom inside Terrell's backpack, but Terrell wasn't there.
罗西在学校里一边到处走，一边用她的超级听力去听。她听到了体育馆下面有人说话。罗西用手劈开地板，发现在地板下面有一个巨大的漏斗。罗西跳进去，沿着一条又长又弯的滑梯滑了下去。
最下方有一个巨大的房间，所有人都被困在了里面。
Walking through the school, Roxy used her super hearing. She heard voices under the gym. Roxy punched through the floor and found an enormous funnel beneath the floor. Roxy jumped in and went down a long, twisting slide.
At the bottom there was a big empty room, and everyone was trapped inside.
“火箭女孩儿！” 特勒尔说。
“咻！” 潘校长擦了擦额头，“你终于找到我们了！” 
罗西把所有的人都带到安全的地方。“现在我得找到杰克·哈默。” 
罗西在学校找到了那个建筑工人。他正在把学校的电脑往面包车上搬。
"Rocket Girl!" Terrell said.
"Whew!" Principal Penn wiped her brow. "Finally, you found us!"
Roxy brought everyone back to safety. "Now I have to find Jack Hammer."
Roxy spotted the builder at school. He was loading school computers into a van.
“住手！” 罗西大喊。
“才不呢！” 杰克·哈默对着罗西开了一钉枪。
“啊！” 罗西的眼睛发射出激光。
杰克·哈默躲开了。 激光被安全帽弹开，射碎了玻璃。
"Stop right there!" Roxy shouted.
"Never!" Jack Hammer fired a nail gun at Roxy.
"Ah!" Roxy fired her eye laser beams.
Jack Hammer ducked. The beams bounced off his hard hat and shattered a window.
“哈哈！” 坏人钻进面包车里逃走了。
罗西追上了他，跟着面包车飞。罗西使用了她的热感视力。面包车的门熔化了。
“喂！” 杰克·海默大叫。
罗西的眼睛发射的激光击破了轮胎。面包车滑进水坑，停了下来。
"Ha-ha!" The villain hopped into his van and took off.
Roxy shot after him, flying alongside the van. Roxy used her heat vision. The van's doors melted.
"Hey!" Jack Hammer yelled.
Roxy zapped the tires with her eye laser beams. The van slid through a puddle and stopped.
杰克·哈默想要打开车门。“天啊！我......” 
“被困住了！” 罗西笑了。
罗西把杰克·哈默送进了监狱，然后去了杰克·哈默的大楼。被偷来的东西都在那里。最后，她回到了学校。
Jack Hammer tried to open the door. "Oh no! I'm . . . "
"Trapped!" Roxy smiled.
Roxy took Jack Hammer to jail. Next she flew to Jack Hammer's building. All the stolen items were there. Finally she returned to school.
“室内休息怎么样啊？” 罗西问朋友们。
“非常好！” 玛拉说。
“是的！” 杰克说，“体育馆下面有个大滑梯！” 
罗西和特勒尔飞快地看了对方一眼，笑了。
"How was indoor recess?" Roxy asked her friends.
"It was great!" Mara said.
"Yeah!" Jack said. "There's a big slide under the gym!"
Roxy and Terrell shot each other a quick look and smiled.
“天气真好啊！” 一个女人跟邻居们在一起，他们正在公寓的楼顶上开派对。
一个男人笑了。“拿掉那个臭烘烘的鹰巢，真是太让人高兴了。” 
另外一个邻居也笑了。“我们的公寓楼变得更好了。” 
"Nice weather!" A woman was with her neighbors. They were having a party on the roof of their apartment building.
A man smiled. "I'm glad we got rid of that smelly hawk's nest."
Another neighbor grinned. "Our apartment building is much nicer now."
啁！啁！一个长着翅膀的黑影从天上俯冲下来。
“啊！” 那个女人尖叫起来。
“好酷啊！” 杰克说，“秃鹫！” 
罗西和朋友们在美罗城的猛禽中心。那里有很多关在大笼子里的猛禽。
Kee, kee! A winged figure swooped down from the sky.
"Ahh!" The woman screamed.
"Cool!" Jack said. "Vultures!"
Roxy and her friends were at the Metro City Raptor Center. The center had lots of raptors locked up in large cages.
有个女人走了过来。她的胸卡上写着 “罗宾” 。
“这些是土耳其秃鹫，” 罗宾说，“秃鹫是猛禽的一种。猛禽是猎取其它动物的鸟。” 
“那它们为什么在这里呢？” 玛拉问。
A woman walked over. She wore a name tag that read Robin.
"Those are turkey vultures," Robin said. "Vultures are a type of raptor. Raptors are birds that hunt other animals."
"Why are they here?" Mara asked.
“这些秃鹫受伤了，” 罗宾说，“我们在帮它们康复。我们很快就会把它们放出去的。” 
罗宾带着大家来到另一个大笼子前面。“这只鸟叫佩里，它是一只游隼。佩里的一只翅膀断了，我们认为那是车撞的。” 
"Those vultures got injured," Robin said. "We helped them get better. Soon we'll release them."
Robin led everyone to the front of another large cage. "This is Perry. It's a peregrine falcon. Perry's wing is broken. We think it got hit by a car."
“真是太惨了。” 杰克说。
“开车的人竟然没有停下来，” 罗宾的眼睛闪着怒火。“人们需要善待鸟类，尤其是猛禽类。它们是视力极好的猎人。秃鹫还能通过清理动物尸体来改善环境呢！” 
"That's awful," Jack said.
"The person driving the car didn't even stop." Robin's eyes flashed with anger. "People need to be nice to birds, especially raptors. They are great hunters with amazing eyesight. Vultures even help the environment by cleaning up dead animals!"
“我的窗外就有一个鸟巢，” 特勒尔说，“我喜欢看小鸟宝宝。” 
“不过，有的人不喜欢鸟巢！” 罗宾看上去非常生气，“在美罗城公园附近的公寓楼上，有一个非常漂亮的鸟巢。公寓楼里那些黑心居民竟然把它拿掉了！” 
"There's a bird's nest outside my window," Terrell said. "I love looking at the baby birds."
"However, some people don't like nests!" Robin looked very angry now. "There was a beautiful hawk's nest on an apartment building near Metro City Park. The building's horrible residents had the nest removed!"
“他们真坏！” 杰克说。
罗宾突然抬头看向天空。 一只大鸟正在头顶上盘旋。“我马上回来。” 罗宾匆忙离开了。
“有点奇怪啊！” 玛拉说。
杰克耸耸肩。
"They are horrible," Jack said.
Suddenly Robin looked up. A large bird was flying overhead. "I'll be right back." Robin hurried away.
"That was strange," Mara said.
Jack shrugged.
“鹰巢被人拿掉了，真让人难过，” 罗西说，“我很喜欢鹰。” 
“我也是。” 杰克说，“为什么没有人阻止这件事呢？” 
“火箭女孩儿肯定能阻止那些人。” 特勒尔说。
"It's sad that the hawk's nest was removed," Roxy said. "I love hawks."
"Me too," Jack said. "Why didn't anyone stop that?"
"Rocket Girl could have stopped them," Terrell said.
马拉翻了个白眼。“特勒尔，我敢肯定火箭女孩儿有更重要的事情要做。” 
罗西和特勒尔互相看了看，笑了。
罗西的手表响了。她悄悄地离开了朋友们。
“布洛姆市长？有什么事吗？” 
Mara rolled her eyes. "I'm sure Rocket Girl has more important things to do, Terrell."
Roxy and Terrell looked at each other and grinned.
Roxy's watch beeped. She stepped away from her friends.
"Mayor Bloom? Is something wrong?"
“火箭女孩儿，我需要你的帮忙。” 市长看起来很生气，“工人们打算砍掉美罗城公园的一些树，但是他们刚刚被袭击了，他们的设备也被弄坏了。” 
“别担心，市长，” 罗西说，“我马上过去！” 
"Rocket Girl, I need your help." The mayor looked annoyed. "Workers are trying to cut down some trees in Metro City Park, but they were just attacked, and all their equipment was destroyed."
"Don't worry, Mayor," Roxy said. "I'm on my way!"
“我得去一下美罗城公园，” 罗西想，“有人袭击了那里的工人。” 
罗西看着朋友们。“我很快回来。我......嗯......我想再看看猫头鹰！” 
"I have to get to Metro City Park," Roxy thought. "Someone just attacked workers there."
Roxy looked at her friends. "I'll be right back. I . . . um . . . want to look at the owls again!"
罗西赶到美罗城公园时，看到了一些工人。草地上有断了的锯子和绳子。附近停着一辆卡车，它的轮胎也瘪了，窗户也被打碎了，车上的起重机也断了。
“哇！” 罗西想，“为什么会有人这么干呢？” 
When Roxy landed in Metro City Park, she saw some workers. Broken saws and rope lay in the grass. A bucket truck was parked nearby. Its tires were flat, and its windows were smashed. Its crane was bent.
"Wow," Roxy thought. "Why would someone do this?"
史密斯侦探正看着几棵树。树上停着几只秃鹫。
“这么说，侦探先生，” 罗西笑着说，“这些秃鹫知道是谁袭击的工人吗？” 
史密斯侦探抱怨说：“很有意思，火箭女孩儿。这些树是工人们打算要砍掉的。” 
Detective Smith was looking at some trees. Vultures were perched on the branches.
"So, Detective," Roxy said with a grin. "Do the vultures know who attacked the workers?"
Detective Smith groaned. "Very funny, Rocket Girl. Those are the trees the workers were going to cut down."
一个工人向史密斯侦探和罗西走了过来。“我叫厄尔，” 他说，“是这里的主管。” 
“这里发生了什么事？” 史密斯侦探问。
厄尔挠了挠头。“我们是来砍树的，但是后来一个飞人袭击了我们。” 
A worker walked over to Detective Smith and Roxy. "I'm Earl," he said. "I'm the supervisor."
"What happened here?" Detective Smith asked.
Earl scratched his head. "We came here to cut down those trees, but then a flying person attacked us.”
“你们为什么要砍树呢？” 罗西问。
“秃鹫总是站在那些树上，” 厄尔说，“附近的居民们不喜欢秃鹫。” 
罗西不明白。“秃鹫怎么了？它们只是鸟而已。” 
厄尔耸耸肩。“居民们觉得秃鹫很可怕。” 
"Why were you cutting down the trees?" Roxy asked.
"Vultures perch in them," Earl said. "Residents near here don't like vultures."
Roxy was confused. "What's wrong with vultures? They're just birds."
Earl shrugged. "The residents say the vultures are creepy."
“呃，有人能帮我吗？” 一个声音说。
罗西抬头一看。一个工人在高高的树上。他脚下的草地上有一根绳子。
“卡尔！” 厄尔说，“我忘了你还在树上！” 
卡尔看上去很恼火。“那个坏鸟人把我的绳子咬断了，现在我被困在这里了！” 
"Um, can someone help me?" a voice said suddenly.
Roxy looked up. A worker was high up in a tree. A rope lay in the grass below him.
"Carl!" Earl said. "I forgot you were up there!"
Carl looked annoyed. "That bird villain snapped my rope. Now I'm stuck up here!"
“等一下！” 罗西飞向卡尔，把他安全地带了下来。
“火箭女孩儿，你是最棒的！” 卡尔说。
史密斯侦探拿出笔记本。“你们能描述一下那个坏人吗？” 
"Hold on!" Roxy flew up to Carl and brought him safely down.
"You're the best, Rocket Girl," Carl said.
Detective Smith took out his notepad. "Can you describe the villain?"
厄尔点了点头。“好的。她看上去像一只鹰，有一双大翅膀和一个鹰脸面具。” 
卡尔也点了点头。“她叫自己‘雷鹰’。” 
Earl nodded. "Yeah. She looked like a hawk, and she had really big wings and a hawk mask."
Carl nodded too. "She called herself Thunderhawk."
史密斯侦探想了一会儿。“跟袭击屋顶派对的应该是同一个人，派对是在那里举行的，” 他指着附近的一栋楼，“居民们说他们刚拿掉了一个鹰巢。” 
“嗯，” 罗西想，“罗宾非常爱鸟，特别是猛禽。说不定她知道谁是雷鹰。” 她给特勒尔打了电话。
Detective Smith thought for a while. "This must be the same person who attacked people at the roof party. The party was over there." He pointed at a nearby building. "The residents said they had just gotten rid of a hawk's nest."
"Hmm," Roxy thought. "Robin cares about birds, especially raptors. Maybe she knows who Thunderhawk is." She called Terrell.
“嗨，火箭女孩儿。” 特勒尔说。
“特勒尔，我要回一趟猛禽中心。” 罗西说，“我需要跟罗宾谈谈。” 
“罗宾不在这里。” 特勒尔说，“她再也没有回来过。” 
"Hey, Rocket Girl," Terrell said.
"I'm coming back to the Raptor Center, Terrell," Roxy said. "I need to talk to Robin."
"Robin's not here," Terrell said. "She never came back."
“哇！” 罗西想，“我觉得罗宾可能就是雷鹰。” 她看向史密斯侦探。“侦探先生，” 罗西说，“我想......” 
史密斯侦探的电话响了。“喂？天啊！我马上就过去！” 
史密斯侦探看着罗西。“雷鹰在美罗城动物园。你要跟我说什么？” 
“没什么。” 罗西说。嗖！罗西飞走了。
"Wow," Roxy thought. "I think maybe Robin is Thunderhawk." She looked over at Detective Smith. "Detective," Roxy said, "I think . . . "
The detective's phone rang. "Hello? Oh no! We'll be right there!"
Detective Smith looked at Roxy. "Thunderhawk is at Metro City Zoo. What were you going to tell me?"
"Never mind," Roxy said. Zoom! Roxy flew off.
罗西到动物园时，人们在四处奔跑。
“大鹰人来了！” 
“快逃命啊！” 
When Roxy arrived at the zoo, people were running in every direction.
"There's a big hawk person!"
"Run for your lives!"
罗西看到了雷鹰。她在禽类馆的楼顶上。她有一双大翅膀，带着鹰脸面具。
“那肯定是罗宾。” 罗西想。“雷鹰！” 她叫道。
Roxy spotted Thunderhawk. The villain was on top of the bird building. She had large wings and a hawk mask.
"That's definitely Robin," Roxy thought. "Thunderhawk!" she shouted.
罗宾看了过来。“火箭女孩儿，走开！我要放了这些鸟！” 她在屋顶砸了一个洞，鸟都飞了出去。
“你不能那样做！” 罗西喊道。
“鸟不应该在笼子里！” 罗宾喊道，“它们是自由的！” 
Robin looked over. "Go away, Rocket Girl! I'm freeing these birds!" She smashed a hole in the building's roof and birds flew out.
"You can't do that!" Roxy shouted.
"Birds shouldn't be in cages!" Robin cried. "They should be free!"
“雷鹰，你很快就要失去自由了，” 罗西说，“你会进监狱的！” 
罗西像箭一样飞向罗宾。她伸手去抓罗宾。罗宾跳起来，罗西没有抓住。
“飓风！” 罗宾喊道。她扇动起了巨大的翅膀。
"You won't be free for much longer, Thunderhawk," Roxy said. "You're going to jail!"
Roxy shot toward Robin like an arrow. She reached out to grab Robin. Robin leaped, but Roxy missed her.
"Hurricane wind!" Robin shouted. She flapped her huge wings.
呼-呼-呼啦！一阵强风刮了过来。罗西想站稳，但是风太大了。
她向后跌倒在地上，把大猩猩展示馆的围栏撞破了。
Whoo-whoo-whoosh! A strong wind blew. Roxy tried to stay where she was, but the wind was too strong.
She tumbled backward, crashing through the fence of a gorilla exhibit.
“啊！” 罗西坐起来看了看四周。一只大猩猩正看着她，然后大猩猩从展示馆里跑了出去。
“呃哦！” 罗西说。 她听到了人们的尖叫声。
“大猩猩跑出来了！” 
“快逃命啊！” 
"Ah!" Roxy sat up and looked around. A gorilla looked at her, then it ran out of the exhibit.
"Uh-oh!" Roxy said. She already heard people screaming.
"A gorilla's loose!"
"Run for your lives!"
罗西从展示馆里爬了出来。罗宾向尖叫的人群扑来扑去。
“我得阻止罗宾，” 罗西想，“但是大猩猩逃走了！” 
罗西在大猩猩后面飞。她看到一个管理员正在靠近大猩猩。
Roxy crawled out of the exhibit. Robin swooped over the crowd of screaming people.
"I have to stop Robin," Roxy thought. "But that gorilla is on the loose!"
Roxy flew after the gorilla. She saw a zookeeper approaching the gorilla.
管理员看了罗西一眼。“火箭女孩儿，别担心！我会带大猩猩回展示馆的。请你一定要阻止那个坏人！” 
罗西在动物园上空飞。“罗宾去哪儿了呢？” 她想。
The zookeeper glanced up at Roxy. "Don't worry, Rocket Girl! I'll take the gorilla back to the gorilla exhibit. Just stop that villain, please!"
Roxy flew over the zoo. "Where did Robin go?" she thought.
就在这时，罗西看到了奔跑的动物群。大象、犀牛，以及别的动物到处追赶人群！
罗西听到了笑声。罗宾飞远了。“火箭女孩儿，但愿你能抓回所有的动物！” 
Then she saw a stampede. Elephants, rhinos, and other animals were chasing people all over the place!
Roxy heard laughter. Robin was flying away. "Good luck catching all those animals, Rocket Girl!"
罗西帮忙把动物抓了回去。“现在我得去找罗宾了。” 她想。
罗西飞向猛禽中心。她看到了特勒尔、玛拉和杰克，但是没有看到罗宾。罗西飞到了主楼的顶层。透过窗子，罗西看到了罗宾。她仍然是鹰的打扮。
Roxy helped put the animals back. "Now I have to find Robin," she thought.
Roxy flew to the Raptor Center. She spotted Terrell, Mara, and Jack. But Robin wasn't in sight. Roxy landed on top of the main building. Peeking through a window, Roxy saw Robin. She still wore her hawk disguise.
罗西从窗户跳了进去。“我抓住你了，雷鹰！” 
罗宾大吃一惊。她的脸变得很凶。她展开了翅膀。“飓风！” 
嗖！罗西向坏人冲了过去。她们撞破了墙壁，跌倒在地上。
Roxy leaped through the window. "I've got you, Thunderhawk!"
Robin gasped. Then her face had a nasty look. She raised her wings. "Hurricane—"
Zoom! Roxy charged at the villain. They crashed through the wall and landed on the ground below.
“火箭女孩儿！” 玛拉叫道。
罗西和罗宾打斗的时候，特勒尔焦急地看着。
最后，罗西把罗宾按在地上。“雷鹰，投降吧！” 
罗宾大叫起来。“啁！啁！” 
罗西不明白。“你在干什么？” 
"Rocket Girl!" Mara cried.
As Roxy and Robin wrestled, Terrell watched anxiously.
Finally Roxy pinned Robin to the ground. "Give up, Thunderhawk!"
Robin let out a cry. "Kee, kee!"
Roxy was confused. "What are you doing?"
罗宾没理她。“啁！啁！” 突然，好多猛禽一起冲了下来。它们用爪子抓罗西。
“嘿！” 罗西挥着双手保护自己，“怎么回事啊？” 
罗宾溜走了。“我可以跟鸟对话。我保护它们，所以它们也保护我。” 
Robin ignored her. "Kee, kee!" All of the sudden, many raptors swooped down. They clawed at Roxy.
"Hey!" Roxy waved her arms to protect herself. "What's going on?"
Robin slipped free. "I can speak to birds. I protect them, so they protect me."
罗西想要赶走这些猛禽。“我不想伤害这些鸟。” 她想。
“火箭女孩儿！” 特勒尔大声说，“用你的超级呼吸！” 
罗西看到特勒尔站在一个打开的大笼子旁边。呼！她吹了口气。她的超级呼吸把鸟都吹进了笼子里。特勒尔把门关上了。
Roxy tried to shoo away the raptors. "I don't want to hurt these birds," she thought.
"Rocket Girl!" Terrell cried. "Use your super breath!"
Roxy saw that Terrell was standing near a large open cage. Whoosh! She blew. Her super breath swept the birds into the cage. Terrell threw the door shut.
罗宾飞走了。
嗞！罗西的眼睛发射出激光，烧断了罗宾的翅膀。
“啊！” 罗宾从天上掉了下来。
罗西赶紧飞过去接住了她。
“火箭女孩儿！” 罗宾说，“你救了我！” 
Robin flew off.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy's eye laser beams burned Robin's wings.
"Ahh!" Robin fell from the sky.
Roxy flew fast and caught her.
"Rocket Girl!" Robin said. "You saved me!"
罗西把罗宾带到了地上。
“我也爱鸟，” 罗西说，“不过， 你还是得接受惩罚。” 
罗宾低下了头。“我只是想帮助鸟类。” 
“我有一个主意。” 罗西说。
Roxy brought Robin down to the ground.
"I care about birds too," Roxy said. "But you still have to be punished."
Robin hung her head. "I just wanted to help birds."
"I have an idea," Roxy said.
首先，罗西和雷鹰去拜访了布洛姆市长。罗宾向他说明了秃鹫对环境的好处。
“那好，” 市长说，“我们不会再砍公园的树了。” 
接着，她们去了公寓楼。罗宾告诉居民们秃鹫是多么神奇的鸟类。
First, Rocket Girl and Thunderhawk visited Mayor Bloom. Robin told him how vultures help the environment.
"Very well," the mayor said. "We won't cut down the trees in the park."
Next, they visited the apartment building. Robin told the residents how amazing hawks are.
居民们听了都很难过。一个女人说：“我们很抱歉拿掉了那个鹰巢。” 之后，罗宾答应罗西不再惹麻烦了。“我会赔偿所有的损失。” 
The people looked upset. "We’re very sorry about getting rid of the nest," a woman said. After that, Robin promised Roxy she wouldn't cause any more trouble. "I'll pay for all the damage."
第二天，罗西和朋友们来到了美罗城公园。
“真酷！” 杰克看着树上的秃鹫说。
罗西笑了。她抬头看了看公寓楼。 一只鹰正在建造一个新巢。
The next day Roxy and her friends were in Metro City Park.
"Cool!" Jack said when he saw vultures in the trees.
Roxy smiled. She looked up at the apartment building. A hawk was starting to build a new nest.
都会钻石店老板克朗先生拐进了西街。“真是一个美好的早晨啊！” 他说。
吧唧！克郎先生踩到一个软软的东西。他低头一看，地上到处都是垃圾。他的鞋底上粘着一个烂香蕉。
Mr. Crown, the owner of Downtown Diamonds, turned onto West Street. "It's a lovely morning," he said.
Squish! Mr. Crown's foot sank into something soft. He looked down. Garbage was everywhere. A rotten banana was stuck to the bottom of his shoe.
“这条街太脏了！” 他说。
当他走到自己商店的时候，他愣住了，商店玻璃都被打碎了。他往里一看，大吃一惊。“我的钻石都不见了！” 
"This street is filthy!" he said.
When he arrived at his store, he froze. The windows of the store were all smashed. He looked in and gasped. "My diamonds are gone!"
“呃！” 
“呃，杰克！” 玛拉说，“太恶心了！” 
杰克耸耸肩。“对不起！” 
罗西正在和朋友们吃午餐。杰克刚喝完冰茶。
“有人要吃苹果吗？” 特勒尔问。
"Burp!"
"Eww, Jack!" Mara said. "That's gross!"
Jack shrugged. "Sorry!"
Roxy and her friends were at lunch. Jack had just finished his iced tea.
"Does anyone want my apple?" Terrell asked.
玛拉拿起一个橙子。“我跟你换。” 
罗西吃完最后几口墨西哥卷饼。“墨西哥卷饼真好吃。” 她说。
特勒尔看着自己吃剩的披萨，叹了口气。“我应该买墨西哥卷饼的，披萨太难吃了。” 
Mara held up an orange. "I'll trade you."
Roxy ate the last few bites of her taco. "These tacos are so good," she said.
Terrell looked at the pizza he left and sighed. "I should have gotten tacos. This pizza tastes terrible."
杰克端着盘子站了起来。“我吃完了，我们出去休息吧！” 
他们去扔垃圾，退餐盘。特勒尔看到一个巨大的垃圾桶。上面写着 “清洁工垃圾回收公司” 。
“另外那家‘聪明兄弟垃圾回收公司’怎么了？” 玛拉问。
Jack stood up with his tray. "I'm done. Let's go out to recess!"
They went to throw out their trash and return their lunch trays. Terrell saw a large trash can. Trashman's Trash Pickup was stamped on the side.
"What happened to the other trash company, Smart Brothers' Garbage Pickup?" Mara asked.
罗西看了一下四周。“回收箱和堆肥箱呢？” 
“管他呢？” 杰克把垃圾、冰茶瓶和食物残渣都扔进了垃圾桶。“现在扔垃圾更简单了，不用分类了！” 
玛拉皱起了眉头。“杰克，很多东西都可以回收利用，食物还可以堆肥呢！” 
Roxy looked around. "And what happened to the recycling and compost bins?"
"Who cares?" Jack dumped his trash, iced tea bottle, and food scraps into the trash can. "Dumping trash is so easy now. No need to separate everything!"
Mara frowned. "A lot of things can be recycled, Jack. And food can be composted!"
特勒尔点了点头。“没错，我们如果不给东西分类，它们就会被送进垃圾填埋场，一直堆在那里，对环境不好。” 
杰克叹了口气。“你们说得对！” 
特勒尔、玛拉和罗西去扔垃圾的时候，罗西笑了。“我知道怎么处理所有的垃圾了！” 
Terrell nodded. "That's right. And if we don't sort everything, it goes to a landfill, and the garbage just sits there. It's not good for the environment."
Jack sighed. "You're right!"
As Terrell, Mara, and Roxy threw away their trash, Roxy smiled. "I know how to get rid of all the trash!"
“怎么处理？” 特勒尔问。
罗西哈哈大笑。“火箭女孩儿可以用她的热视力，把垃圾都烧光。” 
特勒尔笑了。“罗西，你太搞笑了。火箭女孩儿有比烧垃圾更重要的事情要做。” 
"How?" Terrell asked.
Roxy laughed. "Rocket Girl can use her heat vision and burn the trash up!"
Terrell smiled. "That's ridiculous, Roxy. Rocket Girl has more important things to do than burn trash."
杰克笑了。“特勒尔说得对！” 
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。罗西走进走廊，打开手表。布洛姆市长出现在屏幕上。在他身后，罗西看到废纸篓里装满了垃圾。
Jack laughed. "Terrell's right!"
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. Roxy stepped into the hallway and turned on her watch. Mayor Bloom appeared on the screen. Behind him, Roxy saw a wastepaper basket overflowing with trash.
“布洛姆市长，” 罗西说，“您有什么事吗？” 
“火箭女孩儿，我们需要你的帮助，” 市长说，“美罗城电子商城刚刚被盗了！” 
“别担心，市长。” 罗西说，“我马上过去！” 
"Mayor Bloom," Roxy said. "What's wrong?"
"We need your help, Rocket Girl," the mayor said. "Metro City Electronics has just been robbed!"
"Don't worry, Mayor," Roxy said. "I'm on my way!"
罗西的朋友们从学校食堂里出来了。
“我得去一下美罗城电子商城。” 罗西想。
“我要去一下医务室。” 她对朋友们说，“我......嗯......有点儿不舒服。可能是墨西哥卷饼引起的！” 罗西迅速跑开了。
Roxy's friends came out of the cafeteria.
"I must get to Metro City Electronics," Roxy thought.
"I'm going to the nurse," she said to her friends. "I… um… don't feel well. Maybe it was the tacos!" Roxy hurried away.
“唉，” 玛拉说，“希望罗西没事。” 
“她应该没事的。” 特勒尔说。
罗西看到史密斯侦探在美罗城电子商城前面。她还看到了垃圾，街上和人行道上到处都是。
"Gee," Mara said. "I hope Roxy is okay."
"She's probably fine," Terrell said.
Roxy spotted Detective Smith in front of Metro City Electronics. She also saw trash. It was all over the sidewalk and street.
罗西降落在地上。“侦探先生，您不能乱扔垃圾哦！” 
史密斯侦探皱起了眉头。“很有意思，火箭女孩儿。这个星期没有人收垃圾，所以到处都是垃圾。” 
“为什么呢？” 罗西问。
Roxy landed. "Detective, you shouldn't litter!"
Detective Smith frowned. "Very funny, Rocket Girl. No one picked up the trash this week, so it's piling up everywhere."
"Why?" Roxy asked.
史密斯侦探耸耸肩。“ ‘聪明兄弟’不接电话，所以布洛姆市长就请了一家新的公司来收垃圾。我想是新公司漏掉了一些街道吧！” 
就在这时，一辆垃圾车飞快地开了过去，车身上写着 “清洁工垃圾回收公司” 。
Detective Smith shrugged. "The Smart Brothers stopped answering their phones. So Mayor Bloom hired a new company to pick up the trash. I guess the new company forgot some streets."
Just then a garbage truck zoomed by. Trashman's Trash Pickup was written on the side.
“那个就是新公司，” 史密斯侦探说，“我相信它很快就会来收这些垃圾的。” 
罗西和史密斯侦探走进了美罗城电子商城。
一位职员跑了过来。“你们来了，真是太好了。有人盗了我们仓库的很多东西。” 
"That's the new company," Detective Smith said. "I'm sure it'll pick up the garbage soon."
Roxy and Detective Smith went into Metro City Electronics.
An employee hurried over. "I'm glad you're here. Someone stole a bunch of things from our warehouse."
她领着罗西和侦探穿过摆满了电视、扬声器和其它电子产品的货架。他们穿过一扇门，进到了一个大仓库里。罗西看到很多货架都是空的。
“强盗是从那扇门闯进来的。” 那位职员指着仓库后面破碎的门说。
She led Roxy and the detective past shelves filled with TVs, speakers, and other electronics. They went through a door and entered a big warehouse. Roxy noticed that many shelves were empty.
"The robber broke in through that door." The employee pointed to a door in the back of the warehouse.
门外是一条小巷子，巷子里堆满了垃圾。垃圾箱里装满了垃圾袋、腐烂的食物，以及其他垃圾。
史密斯侦探捏住了鼻子。“希望‘清洁工垃圾回收公司’赶快把垃圾收走！” 
Outside the door was an alley, and trash filled the alley. A dumpster overflowed with bags, rotting food, and other garbage.
Detective Smith hold his nose. "I hope Trashman's Trash Pickup starts picking up garbage soon!"
罗西点了点头。“我也是这么想的。不过，现在我们要先抓住强盗。” 她转向职员，“你看到强盗了吗？” 
职员摇摇头。“我正在接待一位顾客。后来我来这儿给顾客找电视。这时，我才看到门坏了，货架也空了。” 
Roxy nodded. "I hope so too. But right now we need to catch the robber first." She turned to the employee. "Did you see the robbers?"
The employee shook her head. "I was helping a customer. Then I came back here to look for a TV for the customer. Then I saw the doors were broken and the shelves were empty."
呜！一辆大卡车飞快地开了过去。包装纸和碎报纸在空中飞舞。
史密斯侦探又抱怨起来。“又是那辆垃圾车！它为什么不来收垃圾呢？” 
Vroom! A big truck rumbled down the alley. Wrappers and scraps of newspaper fluttered through the air.
Detective Smith groaned again. "That was the garbage truck again! Why didn't it pick up this trash?"
罗西看着卡车经过拐角。“我也不知道。不过我开始怀疑它了。” 
这时，他们听到了一个声音。“有人偷了我的车！” 
Roxy watched the truck turn the corner. "I don't know, Detective. But I'm starting to think it's suspicious."
Just then they heard a voice. "Someone stole my car!"
“有人的车被偷了！” 罗西飞出了小巷子。
一个男人手里拿着车钥匙，看上去很恼火。“现在我怎么去上班呢？那辆车花了我很多钱的！” 
史密斯侦探跑了出来。
"Someone's car was stolen!" Roxy flew out of the alley.
A man held a car key. He looked furious. "How will I get to work now? I paid a lot of money for that car!"
Detective Smith ran over.
“是谁偷了你的车？” 罗西问，“你看到小偷了吗？” 
“没有，” 男人说，“不过我看见了他的卡车！” 
史密斯侦探拿出了笔记本。“什么样的卡车？” 
"Who stole your car?" Roxy asked. "Did you see the thief?"
"No," the man said. "But I saw his truck!"
Detective Smith took out his notepad. "What does it look like?"
“是一辆垃圾车，” 男人说，“上面写着 ‘清洁工垃圾回收公司’。” 
罗西不明白。“小偷在垃圾车里，他是怎么偷你的车的呢？” 
"It's a garbage truck," the man said. "It says Trashman's Trash Pickup on it."
Roxy was confused. "The thief was in a garbage truck. So how did he steal your car?"
“卡车上有一只带爪子的大手臂。” 男人说。他伸出手臂演示了一下爪子是怎么动的。“爪子抓住了我的车，把它装进了卡车后面。” 
男人踢了一脚掉在人行道上的咖啡杯，“清洁工做事太差劲了，垃圾没收走，却把我的车收走了！” 
"The truck has a big arm with a claw," the man said. He held out his arm to show how the claw worked. "The claw grabbed my car and put it in the back of the truck!"
The man kicked a coffee cup lying on the sidewalk. "Trashman stinks at his job. He didn't pick up any of this trash, but he picked up my car!"
“嗯，” 史密斯侦探说，“说不定美罗城电子商城也是清洁工盗的。” 
罗西点了点头。“我们要查清楚。” 
史密斯侦探找到了 “清洁工垃圾回收公司” 的地址，“公司的总部在城北。” 
"Hmm," Detective Smith said. "Maybe Trashman robbed Metro City Electronics too."
Roxy nodded. "We should find out."
Detective Smith looked up the address for Trashman's Trash Pickup. "The headquarters is just north of the city."
“我去看看！” 罗西飞走了。
不一会儿，罗西降落在一栋大楼前。她走进了一个非常大的房间，周围都是一堆堆的垃圾。罗西听到了什么声音，一个男人正在搬运箱子。
"I'll go check it out!" Roxy flew off.
Moments later Roxy landed in front of a huge building. She entered an enormous room. Piles of trash surrounded her. Roxy heard a sound. A man was carrying a box.
他的旁边停着几辆豪车。他穿着一件又脏又破的夹克，头发和胡子乱七八糟的。
“清洁工！” 罗西叫道。
Some nice cars were parked near him. He wore a filthy, ripped jacket, his hair and beard stuck out in all different directions.
"Trashman!" Roxy shouted.
男人把箱子扔到了地上。“火箭女孩儿，你......咳......咳！” 男人咳嗽起来，“你来这里做什么？” 
罗西两手叉腰。“你不去收垃圾，一直在偷东西！” 
The man dropped the box on the ground. "Rocket Girl, you . . . ahugh . . . ahugh!" The man coughed. "What are you doing here?"
Roxy put her hands on her hips. "You've not been picking up trash, you have been stealing things!"
男人双臂交叉。“那又怎么样？我受够了那些垃圾。我决定要偷些好东西。” 
罗西很恼火。“你要去的地方什么好东西也带不了，是监狱！” 
Trashman folded his arms. "So what? I'm tired of all this trash. I decided to steal some nice things!"
Roxy was angry. "You won't be able to take any nice things where you're going, jail!"
清洁工哈哈大笑，再次咳嗽起来。“不可能！我要把你和垃圾一起扔出去！” 他走到墙边，拉下了开关。
哐当！罗西头顶上的门打开了。然后，哗啦啦！成吨的垃圾砸在她身上。
“哈哈！咳......咳!” 清洁工跑出了门。“火箭女孩儿，再见！” 
Trashman laughed and then coughed again. "No way! I'm putting you out with the trash!" He stepped over to the wall and pulled a lever.
Clank! Doors opened above Roxy's head. Then, shwoompf! Tons of trash crashed down on her.
"Ha-ha! Ahugh . . . ahugh!" Trashman ran out the door. "So long, Rocket Girl!"
恶心的垃圾堆在罗西身上。“呃！” 罗西擦去脸上发霉的番茄酱，“真是太恶心了！呃！” 
罗西刚把身上的垃圾推开，就又有更多的垃圾掉在她身上。
Disgusting garbage piled up on top of Roxy. "Yuck!" Roxy wiped moldy tomato sauce off her face. "This is gross! Bleck!"
Roxy pushed garbage away from herself. More garbage fell down onto her.
“啊！” 罗西发起火来。她的眼睛发射出橙色的光束。垃圾受热后突然起火了，罗西赶紧从垃圾堆里跳了出来。她看着被火烧掉的垃圾。
"Grr!" Roxy grew angry. Orange beams radiated from her eyes. The garbage heated up and then burst into flames. Roxy quickly burst out of the pile. She watched the trash burning down by the fire.
“现在我得去找清洁工了。” 罗西想。她飞出大楼，飞上了天空。她低头一看，几辆警车在追一辆垃圾车。
“那是清洁工！” 罗西跟上了垃圾车。
"Now I have to find Trashman," Roxy thought. She flew out of the building and up into the sky. Looking down, she saw police cars chasing a garbage truck.
"That's Trashman!" Roxy kept up with the garbage truck.
清洁工看到了警车。“垃圾炮弹！” 他按下了一个按钮，一颗巨大的垃圾球从卡车后面发射了出去。砰！垃圾爆炸了，警车被撞毁了。
Trashman saw the police cars. "Garbage bombs!" He pushed a button, and a huge ball of garbage fired out from the back of the truck. Boom! The garbage exploded, and the police cars crashed.
“哈哈！” 清洁工那乱七八糟的头发晃来晃去。“咳......咳! 哈哈！” 
“清洁工真坏！” 罗西想，“他不仅偷东西，还乱扔垃圾！” 
砰！砰！更多垃圾炮弹爆炸了。一只破袜子掉在了一个男人头上。他对着垃圾车举起拳头。“乱扔垃圾的家伙！” 
"Ha-ha!" Trashman's messy hair waved wildly. "Ahugh… ahugh! Ha-ha!"
"Trashman is terrible!" Roxy thought. "He doesn't just steal, he litters too!"
Boom! Boom! More garbage bombs exploded. A ripped sock landed on a man's head. He shook his fist at the garbage truck. "Litterbug!"
罗西追上了卡车。砰！一颗垃圾炮弹在罗西的脸上爆炸了。
“呃！” 罗西擦了擦脸。突然，咔嚓一声，卡车的爪子抓住了罗西。罗西想要挣脱，爪子抓得更紧了。罗西用力一翻，卡车翻了，滑行了一段停下了。
Roxy caught up to the truck. Boom! A garbage bomb exploded in her face.
"Grr!" Roxy wiped her face. Suddenly, snap—the truck's claw grabbed Roxy. Roxy struggled, but the claw squeezed more tightly. Roxy twisted with all her might. The truck flipped, and slid to a stop.
清洁工从卡车里爬了出来。“火箭女孩儿，你是永远......咳......抓不住我的！” 
罗西用她的超级力量，慢慢把爪子打开了。她把爪子从卡车上扯了下来。嗖！她追上了清洁工。咔嚓！罗西用爪子抓住了那个坏人。
Trashman crawled out of the truck. "Rocket Girl, you'll never . . . ahugh . . . catch me!"
Roxy used her super strength. Slowly she forced the claw to open. She ripped it from the truck. Zoom! She shot after Trashman. Snap! Roxy caught the villain with the claw.
罗西笑了。“我抓住你了！” 
清洁工哼了一声。他开始咳嗽。罗西把他送进了监狱。
“火箭女孩儿，谢谢你！” 史密斯侦探说，“我们找到了‘聪明兄弟’。清洁工把他们关了起来。布洛姆市长让他们马上开始收垃圾。” 
Roxy grinned. "Got you!"
Trashman groaned. He started to cough. Roxy brought him to jail.
"Rocket Girl, thanks," Detective Smith said. "We found the Smart Brothers. Trashman locked them up. Mayor Bloom asked them to start picking up trash right away."
“太好了！” 罗西说，“我要回家洗澡！” 
第二天，罗西在学校里碰到了朋友们。大厅里有一个垃圾桶，上面写着 “聪明兄弟垃圾回收公司” 。
"Good!" Roxy said. "I'm going home to take a shower!"
The next morning Roxy met her friends at school. A trash can stood in the lobby. Smart Brothers' Garbage Pickup was written on the side.
“罗西，你昨天是生病回家了吗？” 玛拉问。
“是的，” 罗西说，“但是你知道吗？我昨天回家路上看到了火箭女孩儿。她在打坏人，还烧了垃圾！” 
“好酷啊！” 杰克说。
特勒尔笑了。
"Roxy, did you go home sick yesterday?" Mara asked.
"Yep," Roxy said. "But guess what. I saw Rocket Girl on my way home yesterday. She was fighting a villain and burning up trash!"
"Cool!" Jack said.
Terrell smiled.
“巴斯特，我们出去走走吧！” 一个男人说。他给狗拴上了牵引绳。他们出去了。男人的前院里长了一棵又大又可怕的植物。
“天啊！” 男人说，“这棵奇怪的植物是从哪里来的？” 
他走近了一点。突然，植物张开了大嘴。
"Let's go for a walk, Buster," a man said. He put a leash on his dog. They went outside. A big, creepy plant grew in the man's front yard.
"Oh my!" he said. "Where did that strange plant come from?"
He stepped closer. Suddenly the plant opened a large mouth.
“天啊！” 男人大喊。
咕咚！
“今天是星期五，我太高兴了！” 玛拉说。
罗西和朋友们走在放学回家的路上。
"Oh no!" the man cried out.
Gulp!
"I'm so glad it's Friday," Mara said.
Roxy and her friends were walking home from school.
“是啊。” 杰克说，“今天考了三场考试，实在是太累了。” 
突然，特勒尔的手一指。“那是什么？” 大家看过去。一棵很可怕的植物长在一栋房子旁边。
“哇！” 玛拉说，“它看起来好像是从另外一个星球来的。” 
"Me too," Jack said. "I can't believe we had three exams today, I'm so tired."
Suddenly Terrell pointed. "What is that?" Everyone looked. A creepy plant was growing next to a house.
"Wow," Mara said. "It looks like something from another planet."
“我家后院也有一棵这样的植物，” 杰克说，“不过比这大得多。我妈妈也不知道那是什么。我们有一个菜园，但是从来没有种过那样的东西。” 
"There's also a plant like that in my backyard," Jack said. "It's a lot bigger though. My mom was also wondering what it is. We have a vegetable garden, but we didn't plant anything like that."
罗西边走边仔细地看着那棵树，“这到底是什么植物呢？” 
特勒尔笑了，“也许是外星植物！” 他举起双手，看起来像两只爪子。“玛拉，小心！外星植物要追上你了！” 
Roxy looked at the plant closely as she walked. "What kind of plant is it?"
Terrell laughed. "Maybe it's an alien plant!" He held out his arms to look like claws. "Look out, Mara! The alien plant is coming after you!"
玛拉翻了个白眼。“特勒尔，你太搞笑了 。” 
杰克接着往前走。“快走吧！” 他说，“到了我家，我给你们看那棵植物。” 
很快，他们到了杰克家。杰克说得对，他家院子里的植物非常大。它藤蔓弯曲，花苞也很大。
Mara rolled her eyes. "You're ridiculous, Terrell."
Jack kept walking. "Come on," he said. "When we get to my house, I'll show you my plant."
A moment later they got to Jack's house. Jack was right, the plant in his yard was huge. It had twisting vines and large bulbs.
“啊！” 玛拉说，“你应该把它砍了。” 
杰克挠了挠头。“我不敢靠近它。” 接着他又笑着说，“也许我可以请火箭女孩儿砍了它。” 
特勒尔和玛拉都笑了。
"Yikes!" Mara said. "You should probably cut that down."
Jack scratched his head. "I'm afraid to get close to it." Then he laughed. "Maybe I can get Rocket Girl to cut it down."
Terrell and Mara laughed.
“我们去仔细看看吧！” 特勒尔说。
就在这时，罗西的手表响了。她等到朋友们都走进了杰克家的后院。
“布洛姆市长，” 她小声说，“有什么事吗？” 
"Let's take a closer look!" Terrell said.
Just then Roxy's watch beeped. She waited while her friends walked into Jack's backyard.
"Mayor Bloom," she whispered. "What's wrong?"
布洛姆市长看上去很着急。“火箭女孩儿，我这里出了点儿问题。我的助理今天没来上班，办公室其他的人也没来。” 
罗西摸了摸下巴。“也许他们只是想休一天假呢！” 
Mayor Bloom looked anxious. "I have a problem, Rocket Girl. My assistant never came to work today. Neither did anyone else in my office."
Roxy rubbed her chin. "Maybe they just wanted the day off."
市长摇了摇头。“不会的，他们喜欢上班，而且史密斯侦探说一直有人给警察局打电话，他们认识的人也失踪了。” 
“别担心，市长，” 罗西说，“我马上过去！” 
The mayor shook his head. "No, they love coming into work. And Detective Smith told me people keep calling the police station, people they know are missing too."
"Don't worry, Mayor," Roxy said. "I'm on my way!"
“我得去布洛姆市长的办公室，” 罗西想，“有人失踪了。” 
罗西跑进了杰克家的后院。“喂，朋友们，” 她说，“我要......” 
杰克、玛拉和特勒尔都不在。
“他们去哪儿了呢？” 罗西说。她耸了耸肩，“他们可能去杰克家里了吧！” 
"I need to go to Mayor Bloom's office," Roxy thought. "People are missing."
Roxy ran into Jack's backyard. "Hey, guys!" she said. "I need to . . . "
Jack, Mara, and Terrell weren't there.
"Where are they?" Roxy said. She shrugged. "They probably went into Jack's house!"
当罗西到市长办公楼的时候，她大吃一惊。“又一棵植物！” 
这棵植物非常大。弯曲的藤蔓爬到了大楼的另一侧，一个个大花苞好像在晃动，花苞下面挂着几个大豆荚。
When Roxy arrived at the mayor's building, she gasped. "Another plant!"
This plant was enormous. Its twisting vines crept up the side of the building. It had several large bulbs that seemed to move. Large pods hung from under the bulbs.
罗西来到布洛姆市长的办公室，市长不在。罗西发现窗户破了。“他去哪儿了呢？” 她想。
罗西飞向警察总局。大楼的旁边也长了一棵植物。“这些植物是从哪里来的呢？” 罗西想。
Roxy went into Mayor Bloom's office. The mayor wasn't there. Roxy noticed the window was broken. "Where did he go?" she thought.
Roxy flew over to police headquarters. Another plant was growing up the side of that building. "Where did all these plants come from?" Roxy thought.
史密斯侦探在他的办公室里，正在看电脑。
“嗨，侦探先生！” 罗西说，“我刚看到您......嗯......外面的花园。您应该除草了！” 
Detective Smith was in his office. He was looking at something on his computer.
"Hey, Detective!" Roxy said. "I just saw your . . . um . . . garden outside. You really need to do some weeding!"
史密斯侦探翻了个白眼。“很有意思，火箭女孩儿。我真的不知道那是什么植物。太可怕了，我不喜欢。” 
“那您在看什么呢？” 罗西问，“动画片吗？” 
Detective Smith rolled his eyes. "Very funny, Rocket Girl. I have no idea what that plant is. It's very creepy. I don't like it."
"So, what are you watching?" Roxy asked. "Cartoons?"
史密斯侦探抬头看着她。“你今天开了很多玩笑啊！这是一段监控录像。” 他往旁边移动了一下让罗西也来看。
“有几个人在西街和河道的十字路口附近失踪了。这是那里的监控拍下来的。” 
Detective Smith looked up at her. "You're making a lot of jokes today. This is a security video." He moved over so Roxy could get a look.
"Several people went missing near the corner of West Street and River Drive, this video is from a camera there."
罗西看到从十字路口开过的汽车和卡车，人们沿着人行道走。突然，一个女人抬起头来，用手指着什么东西。录像没有声音。
Roxy watched cars and trucks drive through the intersection. People walked along the sidewalk. Suddenly a woman looked up and pointed at something. The video didn't have sound.
不过罗西看得出女人很害怕。别的人也抬头向上看。他们尖叫着跑开了。这时一根藤蔓向镜头移过来，紧接着录像变黑了。
“真奇怪。” 罗西说。
But Roxy could tell the woman was scared. Other people looked up. They screamed and ran off. Then a vine moved close to the camera. After that the video went black.
"That was weird," Roxy said.
史密斯侦探向窗外看去，那棵大型植物的花苞挡住了太阳。 他挠了挠头。“我不喜欢那些植物。它们到底是从哪儿来的呢？” 
罗西的手表响了，她很快接了起来。“是布洛姆市长吗？” 
Detective Smith looked out the window. The giant plant's bulbs blocked the sun. He scratched his head. "I don't like those plants. Where did they come from anyway?"
Roxy's watch beeped. She quickly answered it. "Mayor Bloom?"
“火箭女孩儿！” 是特勒尔，“你还记得杰克家后院的植物吧？” 
罗西叹了口气。“当然记得。不过我现在很忙，有什么事吗？” 
“出大事了！” 特勒尔说，“那棵植物把我们吃掉了。” 
"Rocket Girl!" It was Terrell. "Remember that plant in Jack's backyard?"
Roxy sighed. "Of course I remember it. I'm busy right now, though. What's wrong?"
"A lot is wrong!" Terrell said. "That plant ate us."
罗西咽了一口口水。“特勒尔，你没事吧？” 
特勒尔清了清嗓子。“我还行，但是被困在植物里面了。我们正在看它的时候，一个花苞突然打开了，看起来像一张大嘴。它吃掉了杰克，另外一张嘴吃掉了玛拉。我还没来得及跑，它就抓住了我。” 
Roxy gulped. "Terrell, are you okay?"
Terrell cleared his throat. "I'm fine, but I'm trapped inside the plant. We were looking at it when one of the bulbs opened. It looked like a big mouth. It ate Jack. Another mouth ate Mara. Before I could run away, the plant caught me."
“特勒尔，别担心！” 罗西说，“我马上过去！” 
“你快点儿来，” 特勒尔说，“我开始感到......” 他打了个哈欠，“好困啊！” 
罗西关上手表。“对了，侦探先生，我需要......” 
咔嚓！一根藤蔓打破窗户，抓住了侦探。
"Don't worry, Terrell!" Roxy said. "I'll be there right away!"
"Come quickly," Terrell said. "I'm beginning to feel . . . " He yawned. "Sleepy!"
Roxy closed her watch. "Listen, Detective, I need to . . . "
Smash! A vine shattered the window and grabbed the detective.
“啊！” 史密斯侦探想要挣脱，“火箭女孩儿，帮帮......” 
咕咚！那棵植物把侦探吞了进去。
“啊！” 罗西尖叫起来。又有一根藤蔓伸进了办公室。罗西从走廊逃走了。她从窗户飞了出去。
"Grr!" Detective Smith tried to wriggle free. "Rocket Girl! Help . . . "
Gulp! The plant swallowed the detective.
"Ahh!" Roxy screamed. Then another vine reached into the office. Roxy escaped down the hallway. She flew out through a window.
“天啊！” 罗西喊道。到处都是巨大的植物。藤蔓扫来扫去，张着嘴要吃人。每张嘴下面都有几个豆荚，豆荚在晃动。
“呃！” 罗西说，“豆荚里面有人！” 
“植物在吃人！” 一位老太太大喊。
"Oh no!" Roxy cried. Giant plants were everywhere. Vines whipped back and forth. Mouths snapped at people. There were several pods under each mouth, and the pods wiggled.
"Whoa," Roxy said. "There are people in those pods!"
"The plants are eating people!" an old woman shouted.
“快逃命啊！” 一个男人喊道，“不要让植物......” 咕咚！一张大嘴抓住了他。
嗞！罗西的眼睛发射出激光射中了植物的嘴，男人跳了出来。“火箭女孩儿，谢谢你！” 他沿着街道逃跑，但就在这时，咕咚！另外一棵植物又抓住了他。
"Run for your lives!" a man cried. "Don't let the plants . . . " Gulp! A giant mouth grabbed him.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy's eye laser beams blasted the plant's mouth, and the man jumped out. "Thanks, Rocket Girl!" He ran down the street. But then, gulp! Another plant got him.
“呃！” 罗西握紧拳头说，“我要怎么阻止植物吃人呢？” 
罗西听到有人在笑。一艘小型宇宙飞船飞了过来。宇宙飞船的顶部打开了。一个女人坐在里面，操纵着控制器。
"Ugh!" Roxy made a fist. "How can I stop these plants from eating people?"
Roxy heard someone laughing. A small spaceship floated nearby. The top of the spaceship opened. A woman sat inside, operating the controls.
罗西睁大了眼睛。“维妮！” 
“火箭女孩儿，你好啊！” 那个坏女人脸上带着可恶的笑，“再次见到我你很吃惊吗？” 
“我以为你永远消失了！” 罗西说。
Roxy's eyes went wide. "Vinnie!"
"Hello, Rocket Girl." The villain had an evil smile. "Are you surprised to see me again?"
"I thought you were gone forever!" Roxy said.
维妮突然变得很恼火。“在你把我推进虫洞以后，我真就差点儿永远消失了！” 她咬着牙说，“不过幸运的是我降落在了一个安全的星球上。我还在那里交了很多新朋友！” 
All of the sudden, Vinnie got angry. "After you pushed me through that wormhole, I was almost gone!" She gritted her teeth. "But luckily I landed on a safe planet. And while I was there, I made some new friends!"
“你是说那些植物？” 罗西问。
维妮点了点头。“它们在豆荚里存储生物，然后吸收这些生物的能量。” 
“你为什么要这么做呢？” 罗西问。
"The plants?" Roxy asked.
Vinnie nodded. "They store living things in their pods. Then they feed off the living things' energy."
"Why are you doing this?" Roxy asked.
“我要报仇！” 维妮生气地说，“我差点儿就永远消失在太空中了。现在我这些植物要毁掉美罗城的所有人，也包括你，火箭女孩儿！” 
罗西突然感到自己被藤蔓紧紧地缠住了。接着，咕咚！
"I want revenge!" Vinnie snapped. "I could have been lost in space forever! Now my plants will destroy every person in Metro City, including you, Rocket Girl!"
Roxy suddenly felt a vine wrap tightly around her. And then, gulp!
罗西滑到了植物的豆荚里。
“啊！” 罗西喊，“这里又热又黏!” 
最后，她不动了。“我现在肯定是在豆荚里。” 罗西说。她想动一下手脚，但是没有空间。
Roxy slid inside the plant's pod.
"Ah!" Roxy cried. "It's so hot and sticky in here!"
Finally she stopped moving. "I must be in a pod now," Roxy said. She tried to move her arms and legs. But there was no room.
“我最好......出去。我......开始......” 她打了一个大哈欠，“好困啊！” 
罗西摇了摇头。“我不能睡！” 她对自己说。她想用眼睛发射激光，但是豆荚里没有足够的空间。
“也许我的热视力能有用。” 罗西想。
"I better . . . get out. I'm . . . getting . . ." She let out a big yawn. "Sleepy!"
Roxy shook her head. "I can't fall asleep!" She told herself. She tried firing her eye laser beams. But there wasn't enough room in the pod.
"Maybe my heat vision will work," Roxy thought.
热视力对植物没有用。豆荚里面反而越来越热了。
罗西又试了一下冷呼吸，她听到了咔嚓的声音，豆荚的内部变成了灰色。
“太棒了！” 罗西大声说，“我的冷呼吸杀死了植物！” 她更用力地吹，豆荚枯死了。
The heat vision didn't have any effect on the plant. Instead the inside of the pod grew hotter.
Roxy tried her freeze breath next. She heard a crackling sound. The inside of the pod became gray.
"Yes!" Roxy cried. "My freeze breath killed the plant!" She blew harder. The pod withered and died.
罗西在豆荚上打了一个洞。“我出来啦！” 
植物上面还有别的豆荚。罗西看到豆荚在动，有人在里面。她对着整棵植物吹冷气，那棵巨大的植物死掉了，人们从豆荚里爬了出来。
Roxy punched a hole through the pod. "I'm out!"
The plant had many other pods. Roxy saw the pods wiggling. People were in them. She blew her freeze breath all over the plant. Soon the giant plant was dead. People climbed out of the pods.
“火箭女孩儿，谢谢你！” 一个男人说。
“不用谢！” 罗西说。她看到维妮坐着宇宙飞船飞走了。维妮正朝虫洞飞去。
"Thank you, Rocket Girl!" a man said.
"No problem!" Roxy said. Then she saw Vinnie fly off in her spaceship. Vinnie was zooming toward a wormhole!
“维妮要从那个虫洞逃走了！” 罗西说，“我不能让她逃走！” 。罗西急忙向那个坏女人飞了过去。藤蔓向她伸过来，花苞向她张开了大嘴。罗西躲来躲去。
嗞！罗西的眼睛发射出激光，打中了维妮的宇宙飞船。宇宙飞船冒起了烟，在虫洞附近掉了下来。
"Vinnie is going to escape through that wormhole!" Roxy said. "I can't let her get away!" Roxy shot toward the villain. Vines reached for her. Giant bulbs snapped at her. Roxy zigzagged to avoid them.
Whiz-hoo! Roxy's eye laser beams hit Vinnie's spaceship. The spaceship smoked, and it crashed near the wormhole.
维妮跳出宇宙飞船，向虫洞跑去。她回头看了看罗西。“火箭女孩儿，再见啦！我要回到......” 一张大嘴向她张开。咕咚！
罗西大笑。“太省事了！” 她看了看四周，“现在我只需要消灭掉植物就可以救出人们了。” 
Vinnie jumped out of the spaceship and ran toward the wormhole. She looked over her shoulder at Roxy. "Good-bye, Rocket Girl! I'm going back to . . . " A mouth snapped. Gulp!
Roxy laughed. "That was easy!" She looked around. "Now I just need to destroy all the other plants, and then I can save everyone."
罗西很快把史密斯侦探放了出来。
“火箭女孩儿，谢谢你！” 侦探说，“被植物吃掉的感觉太可怕了！” 
罗西把一个晃动的豆荚放在他面前。“你可以把这个放进监狱了。” 她咧嘴一笑，“维妮在里面呢！” 
A little later Roxy freed Detective Smith. "Thanks, Rocket Girl," the detective said. "Being eaten by that plant was terrible!"
Roxy placed a wiggling pod in front of him. "You can put this in a jail cell." She grinned. "Vinnie is inside!"
罗西回到了杰克家的后院。“嗨，朋友们！我可以看看那棵奇怪的植物吗？” 
杰克摇了摇头。“那棵植物死了，你都错过了！那棵植物吃掉了我们！” 
Roxy returned to Jack's backyard. "Hey, guys! Can I see that strange plant now?"
Jack shook his head. "The plant is dead. You missed everything! The plant ate us!"
特勒尔点了点头，笑着说：“是火箭女孩儿救了我们！” 
罗西摇了摇头。“你们真会开玩笑。” 
“是真的！” 玛拉说。
罗西只是笑了笑。
Terrell nodded, smiling. "Rocket Girl saved us!"
Roxy shook her head. "That's ridiculous, guys."
"It's true!" Mara said.
Roxy just laughed.
